# cs.CV [[Back]](#toc)

### [1] [MatPhaseBench: A Semantics-Guided Benchmark for Materials Phase Diagrams Understanding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02934)
*Hanwen Wang,Sihan Liang,Zhiwei Liu,Yangang Wang,Wei Yan,Yuqin Liu,Zongguo Wang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出 MatPhaseBench——一个面向材料相图（phase diagram）的高质量、高可靠性基准测试（benchmark），用于评估视觉语言模型（VLM）在复杂科学图像理解上的能力。实验表明，当前 VLM 仍远落后于专家水平，仅停留在浅层视觉感知，缺乏基于热力学机制（thermodynamic mechanism）的深层推理和领域知识。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 材料相图是材料科学中的核心知识表征，但现有 VLM 在需要深层机制解释的逻辑复杂图像上缺乏系统评估，相图为此提供了具有挑战性的测试场景。

Method: MatPhaseBench 从 3681 篇经典材料科学期刊论文中筛选出 200 个高质量图-文对，覆盖 189 个材料体系和 70 种元素；采用三项关键策略：面向复杂科学图像理解、全面的图文对齐（image-text alignment）、高质量人工监督文本采集。

Result: 当前 VLM 远落后于专家理解水平，主要局限于表面视觉感知，缺乏基于热力学机制的深度推理，领域意识和专家分析经验有限，在复合或多图设置中区分细粒度差异的能力较差。

Conclusion: MatPhaseBench 构成了一个具有挑战性的研究级基准，为复杂科学图像理解、相图分析及可信赖的多模态人工智能（multimodal AI）在科学中的应用提供了基础平台。

Abstract: Materials phase diagrams are a core knowledge representation in materials science, encoding temperature,composition, phase stability, and phase transformation pathways, with their full understanding requiring thermodynamic mechanism analysis and scientific reasoning. Although VLMs have shown promise in scientific image understanding, their systematic evaluation on such logically complex images demanding deep mechanistic interpretation remains limited, and phase diagrams provide a challenging testbed for this purpose. We introduce MatPhaseBench, a high-quality, high-reliability benchmark for complex scientific image understanding, focused on materials phase diagrams. MatPhaseBench is constructed from 3681 papers in classical materials science journals, from which 200 high-quality diagram-text pairs were selected, covering 189 material systems and 70 elements. The benchmark has three key features: (1)targeting complex scientific image understanding-it moves beyond simple objective tests to open-ended tasks requiring deep comprehension; (2)comprehensive image-text alignment-semantic information associated with images is fully preserved during literature mining and matching; (3) high-quality human-supervised text acquisition-all descriptions undergo strict manual validation. Experimental results show that current VLMs remain substantially behind expert-level understanding: they are largely limited to surface visual perception, lack deep reasoning grounded in thermodynamic mechanisms, have limited domain awareness and expert analytical experience, and perform poorly in distinguishing fine-grained differences in composite or multi-diagram settings. Overall, MatPhaseBench constitutes a challenging research-grade benchmark, providing a foundational platform for complex scientific image understanding, phase diagram analysis, and trustworthy multi-modal AI in science.

</details>

# cond-mat.supr-con [[Back]](#toc)

### [2] [Theoretical investigation of power absorbed by superconductors with Rashba spin-orbit coupling in the presence external time-dependent perturbation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02812)
*Reza Afzali,Bahman Takrim,Amir Hossein Asghari*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文通过Bogoliubov准粒子态之间的跃迁研究了超导体在外界含时扰动下的吸收功率，推导了包含超导相干因子（coherence factor）的跃迁矩阵元，并将其应用于包含关联跳跃（correlated hopping）和Rashba自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）的Hubbard模型超导体。数值计算表明，超导能隙、准粒子谱变化以及Rashba自旋-轨道耦合对归一化吸收功率有显著影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究超导体在外界含时扰动（如超声或电磁波）下的吸收响应机制，理解超导能隙（superconducting gap）、准粒子激发谱（quasiparticle spectrum）以及自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）等因素对吸收过程的调控作用。

Method: 基于Bogoliubov准粒子态之间的跃迁推导吸收功率的表达式，引入超导相干因子（coherence factor）描述跃迁矩阵元；将该形式应用于包含关联跳跃和Rashba自旋-轨道耦合的Hubbard模型超导体，通过数值计算获得准粒子能量、态密度（density of states）、化学势以及温度依赖的超导能隙，进而评估归一化吸收功率。

Result: 吸收响应强烈受超导能隙和准粒子谱变化的影响；Rashba自旋-轨道耦合通过改变态密度来调制吸收；关联跳跃过程、相互作用强度以及自旋-轨道耦合强度均对超导系统的超声和电磁吸收起重要作用。

Conclusion: 跳跃过程、相互作用强度和自旋-轨道耦合在超导系统的超声及电磁吸收中扮演关键角色，为理解相关实验现象提供了理论依据。

Abstract: The absorbed power in superconductors driven by a time-dependent external perturbation is investigated through transitions between Bogoliubov quasiparticle states. The transition matrix element contains the superconducting coherence factor, which determines the role of the gap, excitation spectrum, and external frequency in the absorption process. The formulation is applied to a Hubbard-model superconductor including correlated hopping and Rashba spin-orbit coupling. In this model, numerical calculations are used to obtain the quasiparticle energies, density of states, chemical potential, and temperature-dependent superconducting gap. The normalized absorbed power is then evaluated for different values of temperature, interaction strength, correlated hopping parameter, and spin-orbit coupling strength. The results show that the absorption response is strongly affected by the superconducting gap and by changes in the quasiparticle spectrum. Rashba spin-orbit coupling changes the density of states and therefore modifies the absorption. These results show that hopping processes, interaction strength, and spin-orbit coupling play important roles in the ultrasonic and electromagnetic absorption of superconducting systems.

</details>


### [3] [When Repulsion Creates Pairing: A New Perspective on Unconventional Superconductivity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03022)
*Patrick Navez*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个基于Kohn-Luttinger机制的铜氧化物超导理论形式，认为库仑相互作用的动态屏蔽（dynamic screening）来源于氧轨道空穴的超交换动力学（superexchange dynamics），并由此推导出与实验半定量一致的温度-掺杂相图。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管库仑排斥定律和泡利统计（Pauli statistics）不利于形成束缚态，但在多体相互作用和谷势景观（valley potential landscapes）下，电子或空穴之间仍可能存在吸引力，这让人联想到奇异超导材料。特别是1965年Kohn和Luttinger指出，动态屏蔽（dynamic screening）可在特定条件下导致有效吸引以形成库珀对（Cooper pairs）。本文旨在将这一形式推广到铜氧化物（cuprates）中。

Method: 方法上，本文针对铜氧化物体系提出一种形式化框架（formalism），其中屏蔽来自$CuO_2$平面氧轨道中虚空穴的超交换动力学（superexchange dynamics）。该框架受BCS理论启发。

Result: 基于该理论，推导出了温度-掺杂相图（temperature-doping phase diagram）的一些预测，涵盖赝能隙（pseudo-gap）、奇异金属（strange metal）、反铁磁性（antiferromagnetism）、超导态和正常态等区域。

Conclusion: 预测结果与观测结果在半定量水平上（semi-quantitative agreement）一致。这表明基于Kohn-Luttinger机制的动态屏蔽思路可能是理解铜氧化物超导现象的一个有效途径。

Abstract: Despite the repulsive Coulomb law and the Pauli statistics that do not favor bound states, attraction between electrons or holes is nevertheless possible in the context of many body interaction and of valley potential landscapes, reminiscent of exotic superconducting materials. In particular, in 1965, Kohn and Luttinger published a note revealing that the dynamical screening of the repulsive Coulomb interaction leads, under certain conditions, to an effective attraction necessary for the formation of Cooper pairs. We propose such a formalism adapted to the cuprates, where the screening arises from the superexchange dynamics of virtual holes in the oxygen orbitals of the $Cu O_2$ plane. Inspired from the Bardeen-Copper-Schrieffer (BCS) theory, we can derive some predictions for the temperature-doping phase diagram (pseudo-gap, strange metal, antiferromagnetism, superconducting, and normal states) in semi-quantitative agreement with observations.

</details>


### [4] [Josephson effects in the spin-triplet superconductor/altermagnet/spin-triplet superconductor junctions: the detection of the intrinsic $\bf{d}$-vector](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03685)
*Ya-Ting Han,Li-Juan Chen,Wen-Ting Liu,Qiang Cheng,Qing-Feng Sun*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文利用格林函数方法，研究了自旋三重态超导体/交变磁体/自旋三重态超导体结中的约瑟夫森效应，发现结的电流-相位关系强烈依赖于自旋三重态超导体中d-矢量的方向和交变磁体的取向角，并且通过旋转d-矢量可实现0-π跃迁；该交变磁约瑟夫森结能有效避免磁场对d-矢量的负面影响，可作为检测本征d-矢量的可行方案，并有望用于量子器件设计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索自旋三重态超导体与交变磁体（altermagnet）构成的约瑟夫森结中的物理特性，特别是d-矢量方向的检测问题，以解决现有研究中磁场对d-矢量产生负面影响的弊端。

Method: 采用格林函数方法（Green's function method），对自旋三重态超导体/交变磁体/自旋三重态超导体结进行理论建模，系统分析电流-相位关系、临界电流随各参数的变化。

Result: 发现结中的电流-相位差关系强烈依赖于自旋三重态超导体中d-矢量（d-vector）的方向和交变磁体的取向角（orientation angle）；在给定取向角下，旋转d-矢量可实现0-π跃迁（0-π transition）；临界电流随d-矢量方向、取向角和交变磁体强度的变化被系统揭示。

Conclusion: 交变磁约瑟夫森结能有效避免磁场对d-矢量的负面影响，可作为检测本征d-矢量的可行方案，且结中观测到的0-π跃迁在量子器件设计中具有潜在应用价值。

Abstract: We study the Josephson effects in the spin-triplet superconductor/altermagnet/spin-triplet superconductor junctions using the Green's function method. It is found that the current-phase difference relationships in the junctions strongly depend on the direction of the $\bf{d}$-vectors in the spin-triplet superconductors and the orientation angle of the altermagnet. For the given orientation angle, the $0$-$π$ transition can be obtained when the $\bf{d}$-vector is rotated. The variations of the critical current of the junctions with the direction of the $\bf{d}$-vector, the orientation angle and the strength of altermagnetism are systematically investigated. These Josephson effects can provide the distinguishable information about the direction of the $\bf{d}$-vector. Compared to the existing research, the proposed altermagnetic Josephson junctions can effectively avoid the negative influence of the magnetic field on the $\bf{d}$-vector and can serve as a feasible scheme for the detection of the intrinsic $\bf{d}$-vector. The obtained $0$-$π$ transition in the junctions can also have potential applications in the design of quantum devices.

</details>


### [5] [Tuning Superconductivity by Isovalent Antimony Substitution in PrFeAs(O,F)](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03712)
*Priya Singh,Konrad Kwatek,Tatiana Zajarniuk,Taras Palasyuk,Cezariusz Jastrzębski,Michał Wierzbicki,Tomasz Cetner,Andrzej Szewczyk,Shiv J. Singh*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 在氟掺杂铁基超导体PrFeAsO0.7F0.3中，用等价Sb替代As位导致超导转变温度从约48 K逐渐降低，并在中等Sb掺杂时出现上临界场和涡旋钉扎能的增强，但整体临界电流密度因晶粒间连接性差而较低，体系从电子调控的超导态向无序主导的机制发生交叉转变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究在氟掺杂铁基超导体PrFeAsO0.7F0.3中，用等价的锑（Sb）替代砷（As）位点对超导电性及相关物理性质的影响，并理解从电子调控超导态向无序主导机制的交叉转变行为。

Method: 采用结构分析、拉曼光谱（Raman spectroscopy）、密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）、输运测量、磁输运测量以及磁性测量等多种手段，系统研究PrFeAs1-xSbxO0.7F0.3 (x = 0 到 1.0) 系列样品。

Result: 超导转变温度从母体的约48 K逐渐下降，在x ≤ 0.3时降至约44 K，更高Sb浓度时因无序增强和第二相形成而迅速抑制；拉曼光谱和DFT表明Sb替代导致晶格膨胀和与pnictogen相关的振动模式明显软化；中等掺杂时上临界场（upper critical field）和涡旋激活能（vortex activation energy）增强，但临界电流密度（critical current density）因晶粒间连接性差而较低。

Conclusion: 在等价位取代的铁基超导体中，存在从电子调控超导态向无序主导机制的交叉转变；中等Sb掺杂可增强涡旋钉扎，但总体超导性能受限于晶粒间连接性。

Abstract: We investigate the effects of isovalent Sb substitution at the As site in fluorine-doped PrFeAs1-xSbxO0.7F0.3 (x = 0 to 1.0) through structural, Raman spectroscopy, density functional theory (DFT), transport, magnetotransport, and magnetic measurements. The superconducting transition temperature decreases gradually from ~48 K for the parent compound to ~44 K up to x = 0.3, followed by a rapid suppression at higher Sb concentrations due to increasing disorder and secondary phase formation. Raman spectroscopy and DFT reveal lattice expansion and pronounced softening of pnictogen related vibrational modes upon Sb substitution. Magnetotransport measurements up to 9 T show enhanced upper critical fields and increased vortex activation energy for moderate Sb doping, indicating stronger vortex pinning. However, the critical current density remains low because of poor intergranular connectivity. The results demonstrate a crossover from an electronically tuned superconducting state to a disorder-dominated regime in isovalently substituted iron pnictides.

</details>


### [6] [Evidence of the Cooper-Pair Field with Gaussian Memory Kernel in Unconventional Superconductors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03937)
*Udomsilp Pinsook*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文发展了一个动力学超导对场描述，将库珀通道的Hubbard–Stratonovich场 Δ 视为具有记忆效应的Bogoliubov对场，而非静态序参量。通过与反节点选择性集体场耦合及高斯系综平均，得到记忆因子 exp[-t²/(2τ_g²)]，并解析出从 p=-1/2, 1/2, 1, 3/2 等共振代数前因子层级。该框架包含赝能隙记忆通道和凝聚体辅助相干通道，超导转变主要重排对场谱权重。数值结果与Bi₂Sr₂CaCu₂O₈₊δ 实验数据可比。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有超导对场理论通常将 Hubbard–Stratonovich 场 Δ 处理为静态序参量，难以同时描述赝能隙（pseudogap）与超导凝聚体之间的动力学关联。作者旨在发展一个包含记忆效应的动力学对场描述，以统一理解超导转变中谱权重的重排机制。

Method: 从标准对场有效作用量出发，将 Δ 与反节点（antinode）选择性集体场或自生场耦合。假设这些模式的系综分布近似为高斯分布，通过系综平均导出高斯记忆因子。采用抛物线柱函数（parabolic-cylinder functions）表达频域响应，并推导出共振代数前因子层级。

Result: 得到记忆因子 exp[-t²/(2τ_g²)]；解析出共振代数前因子（algebraic prefactors）p = -1/2, 1/2, 1, 3/2, … 构成的层级结构，由高斯包络截断其发散增长。超导相变后出现与 |Δ₀(T)|² 成正比的凝聚体辅助相干通道，且反节点间隙或赝能隙充当动量空间谱腔（momentum-space spectral cavity），筛选出可发展为电荷密度波（charge-density-wave）不稳定的涨落波矢 Q_a。

Conclusion: 超导转变主要将对场谱权重从非相干赝能隙记忆通道重排至相干Bogoliubov记忆通道。Raman、ARPES、隧道谱及掺杂依赖的ARPES数据可被视为同一高斯记忆对连续谱（Gaussian-memory pair continuum）的互补投影。数值结果与Bi₂Sr₂CaCu₂O₈₊δ 近年实验吻合。

Abstract: We develop a dynamical description of the superconducting pair field in which the Cooper-channel Hubbard--Stratonovich field $Δ$ is treated as a memory-dressed Bogoliubov pair field rather than as a purely static order parameter. Starting from the standard pair-field effective action, we couple $Δ$ to antinode-selected collective or self-generated fields. An ensemble of such modes produces a distribution of local Bogoliubov frequencies; when this distribution is approximately Gaussian, ensemble averaging gives the memory factor $\exp[-t^2/(2τ_g^2)]$. In cuprate superconductors, the antinodal gap or pseudogap restricts the active electronic phase space and acts as a momentum-space spectral cavity. It selects fluctuation wavevectors $\mathbf Q_a$ that may become charge-density-wave-like instabilities in an ordered limit, but behave as a reservoir of local collective fields in the fluctuating regime. The same framework admits resonant algebraic prefactors, so that threshold and forced-oscillator responses generate the hierarchy $p=-1/2,1/2,1,3/2,\ldots$, while the Gaussian envelope cuts off secular growth and converts these branches into finite spectral components. The resulting picture contains a robust pseudogap memory channel and, below $T_c$, an additional condensate-assisted coherent channel proportional to $|Δ_0(T)|^2$. Thus the superconducting transition primarily reorganizes pair-field spectral weight between incoherent pseudogap memory and coherent Bogoliubov memory. The frequency-domain response is expressed in terms of parabolic-cylinder functions, and comparisons with Raman, ARPES, tunneling, and doping-dependent ARPES scaling suggest that these probes are complementary projections of the same Gaussian-memory pair continuum. We compare our numerical results with the recent experimental data on Bi$_2$Sr$_2$CaCu$_2$O$_{8+δ}$.

</details>


### [7] [Full Gate-Voltage Control of a Parity-Protected Superconducting Qubit with an Altermagnetic Josephson Junction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04097)
*Guo-Liang Guo*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于门控超导体-交变磁体-超导体（superconductor-altermagnet-superconductor）约瑟夫森结的宇称保护（parity-protected）超导量子比特，通过化学势电控调节两自旋通道的干涉，在0-π转变点实现第二约瑟夫森谐波主导的双阱势，从而在无需磁通偏置的条件下获得长相干时间（估计可达数十毫秒）的全电控可扩展量子比特方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有宇称保护超导量子比特虽具有本征长相干时间，但多数实现方案依赖磁通偏置（magnetic-flux biasing），这会引入磁通噪声、增加控制开销并限制可扩展性。因此，需要一种无需磁通偏置、可全电学控制的宇称保护量子比特方案。

Method: 提出一种基于门控可调的交变磁体-超导体约瑟夫森结的宇称保护量子比特。交变磁体（altermagnet）具有动量依赖的自旋分裂和零净磁化，可在无外磁场条件下提供自旋依赖功能。在该结中，两自旋通道获得相反的相位偏移，产生两个约瑟夫森通道，其干涉通过化学势（chemical potential）进行电学调控。在调谐至0-π转变点时，第一约瑟夫森谐波被强烈抑制，第二谐波主导，形成具有两个近似简并对库珀对宇称（Cooper-pair parity）相反态的双阱势。

Result: 对于与实际gatemon兼容的参数，估计相干时间可达数十毫秒级别，同时保持全门控的量子比特操作。

Conclusion: 交变磁体约瑟夫森结为实现受保护的超导量子比特提供了一条有前景的路径，其控制方式为局域、可扩展且全电学（local, scalable, and all-electrical control）。

Abstract: Parity-protected superconducting qubits offer intrinsically long coherence, but many current implementations require magnetic-flux biasing, which introduces flux noise, control overhead, and limited scalability. Here we propose a parity-protected qubit based on a gate-tunable superconductor-altermagnet-superconductor Josephson junction. Altermagnets are compensated magnets with momentum-dependent spin splitting and zero net magnetization, providing spin-dependent functionality without external magnetic fields. In the proposed junction, the two spin sectors acquire opposite phase shifts, generating two Josephson channels whose interference is controlled electrically by the chemical potential. At the tuned $0$-$π$ transition, the first Josephson harmonic is strongly suppressed while the second harmonic dominates, yielding a double-well potential with two nearly degenerate states of opposite Cooper-pair parity. For realistic gatemon-compatible parameters, we estimate coherence times of up to tens of milliseconds while maintaining fully gate-controlled qubit operations. These results establish altermagnetic Josephson junctions as a promising route toward protected superconducting qubits with local, scalable, and all-electrical control.

</details>


### [8] [Vortex-Number-Controlled Josephson Diode Polarity in Corbino Junctions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04104)
*Linghao Huang,Jing Wang*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文证明，在Corbino约瑟夫森结中，约瑟夫森二极管效应的极性可通过涡旋数（vortex number）确定性调控，该机制源于结构化空间不均匀性（structured spatial inhomogeneity）的普遍后果。通过求解连续安德烈夫谱问题，发现涡旋数选择性过滤局域不均匀性的特定空间傅里叶谐波，从而重塑高阶约瑟夫森电流谐波的幅度与相对相位，最终导致临界电流不对称性的反转。数值模拟证实了该机制的稳健性，并指出涡旋宇称依赖的二极管极性反转并非马约拉纳物理（Majorana physics）的专属特征，而是可在Corbino结中由几何与结构不均匀性普遍产生。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索约瑟夫森二极管效应（Josephson diode effect）极性可控性的物理机制，特别是涡旋数在其中的决定性作用，并澄清该效应与马约拉纳物理之间的关联。

Method: 求解连续安德烈夫谱问题（Andreev spectral problem），识别涡旋数对局域不均匀性空间傅里叶谐波的选择性滤波机制；结合有效一维边缘模型和完整二维晶格模型进行数值模拟验证。

Result: 涡旋数通过选择性过滤特定空间傅里叶谐波，改变高阶约瑟夫森电流谐波（higher-order Josephson current harmonics）的幅度和相对相位，进而反转临界电流不对称性（critical-current asymmetry）。两种数值模型均确认了该机制的稳健性。

Conclusion: 涡旋宇称依赖的二极管极性反转并非马约拉纳物理的排他性特征，而是Corbino约瑟夫森结中由几何与结构不均匀性普遍导致的涌现现象。

Abstract: We demonstrate that the polarity of the Josephson diode effect in Corbino Josephson junctions can be deterministically controlled by the vortex number, which arises as a generic consequence of structured spatial inhomogeneity. By solving the continuum Andreev spectral problem, we identify a mechanism in which the vortex number selectively filters specific spatial Fourier harmonics of the local inhomogeneity. This harmonic selection reshapes the amplitudes and relative phases of higher-order Josephson current harmonics, ultimately reversing the critical-current asymmetry. Numerical simulations of both an effective one-dimensional edge model and full two-dimensional lattice models confirm the robustness of this mechanism. Crucially, our results show that a vortex-parity-dependent reversal of diode polarity is not an exclusive signature of Majorana physics, but can emerge generically from geometric and structural inhomogeneities in Corbino junctions.

</details>


### [9] [Hall Coefficient Sign Reversal Driven by Orbital-Selective Oxygen-Vacancy Scattering in Nickelate Films](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04122)

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文通过DFT+CDMFT导出的关联多轨道准粒子模型结合半经典玻尔兹曼输运框架中的T矩阵氧空位散射处理，发现氧空位散射的轨道选择性和能谷分辨特性是超导双层镍酸盐薄膜中霍尔系数符号反转的微观起源，而单纯的多带补偿效应不足以解释该现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超导双层镍酸盐薄膜的霍尔测量（Hall measurements）显示符号反转现象，但仅凭刚性带电子掺杂（rigid-band electron doping）无法解释，因此需要揭示其微观机制。

Method: 将DFT+CDMFT导出的关联多轨道准粒子模型（correlated multi-orbital quasiparticle model）与半经典玻尔兹曼输运框架（semiclassical Boltzmann transport framework）中的T矩阵（T-matrix）氧空位散射处理相结合。

Result: 多带补偿（multiband compensation）本身不足以解释符号反转：面内氧空位（in-plane vacancies）选择性地抑制由d_{x^2-y^2}轨道主导的输运通道并使霍尔系数R_H过零，而内顶氧空位（inner-apical vacancies）则使R_H更负。

Conclusion: 能谷分辨（pocket-resolved）和轨道选择性（orbital-selective）的氧空位散射是霍尔系数符号反转的微观起源，为镍酸盐薄膜中依赖氧化学计量比的输运行为提供了理论框架。

Abstract: Hall measurements in superconducting bilayer nickelate films show sign reversals that cannot be explained by rigid-band electron doping alone. We combine a DFT+CDMFT-derived correlated multi-orbital quasiparticle model with a $T$-matrix treatment of oxygen-vacancy scattering in a semiclassical Boltzmann transport framework. We find that multiband compensation is insufficient by itself: in-plane vacancies selectively suppress the transport channel dominated by the $d_{x^2-y^2}$ orbital and drive $R_H$ through zero, whereas inner-apical vacancies make $R_H$ more negative. These results identify pocket-resolved and orbital-selective oxygen-vacancy scattering as the microscopic origin of the Hall coefficient sign reversal and provide a framework for oxygen-stoichiometry-dependent transport in nickelate films.

</details>


### [10] [Pseudo-superconducting-diode effect in ferroelectric Josephson junctions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04398)
*Yaozu Tang,Nienke ten Haaf,Artem Bondarenko,Mazhar N. Ali,Yaroslav M. Blanter*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超导二极管效应（superconducting diode effect, SDE）允许超导电流的单向整流，但通常依赖外部磁场或复杂结构。本文试图在无磁场条件下，利用破缺反演对称性的铁电约瑟夫森结实现类似的非互易超导电流行为。

Method: 构建了一个耦合动力学模型：将依赖极化的电阻-电容-分路结（RCSJ）描述与朗道-哈拉特尼科夫-塔尼（Landau-Khalatnikov-Tani）铁电动力学方程相结合，用于模拟铁电约瑟夫森结中的电流-电压特性。

Result: 模拟结果表明，铁电体的极化翻转（polarization switching）能在正向和反向电流扫描中产生不对称的临界电流（critical current）与俘获电流（retrapping current），从而实现非互易性（nonreciprocity）。该非互易性可通过铁电参数和扫描协议高度调谐，并且在有限温度下依然保持鲁棒。

Conclusion: 该研究指出，铁电约瑟夫森结是实现无磁场非互易超导器件的有前景平台，为超导电子学中无需磁场的整流功能提供了一条新路径。

Abstract: The superconducting diode effect (SDE), characterized by unequal critical supercurrents in opposite current directions, enables supercurrent rectification. We propose a magnetic-field-free pseudo-superconducting-diode effect in ferroelectric Josephson junctions with broken inversion symmetry. Using a coupled dynamical model that combines a polarization-dependent RCSJ description with Landau-Khalatnikov-Tani ferroelectric dynamics, we show that ferroelectric polarization switching induces asymmetric critical and retrapping currents under current sweeps. The resulting nonreciprocity is highly tunable via ferroelectric parameters and the sweep protocol and remains robust at finite temperatures. Our work identifies ferroelectric Josephson junctions as a promising platform for magnetic-field-free nonreciprocal superconducting devices.

### [11] [Superconductivity on the verge of metal-insulator transition in Cu$_{1-x}$Zn$_x$Ir$_2$S$_4$ probed by $μ$SR](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04628)
*K. M. Kojima,M. Miyazaki,M. Hiraishi,A. Koda,R. Kadono,C. Baines,Y. Tsuchiya,H. S. Suzuki,H. Kitazawa*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文通过μ子自旋旋转与弛豫（μSR）实验研究了Zn替代Cu诱导的超导电性Cu$_{1-x}$Zn$_x$Ir$_2$S$_4$（$x=0.3,0.4$），发现超流密度的温度/磁场依赖性与完全能隙的$s$波配对（fully gapped $s$-wave pairing）一致。常态势电阻率较高，表明超导处于“脏极限”（dirty limit），平均自由程远小于相干长度（$\ell \ll ξ_0$），电子散射抹平了潜在的各向异性。研究提示Zn替代诱导的超导与高压下CuIr$_2$S$_4$中发现的超导可能存在联系。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用μ子自旋旋转与弛豫（muon spin rotation and relaxation, $μ$SR）技术测量了Cu$_{1-x}$Zn$_x$Ir$_2$S$_4$（$x=0.3, 0.4$，$T_{\rm c} \approx 3$ K和2.5 K）样品的超流密度（superfluid density）的温度依赖性和磁场依赖性。

Result: 超流密度的温度/磁场依赖性符合完全能隙的$s$波配对（fully gapped $s$-wave pairing）。常态势电阻率较高（10$^{-3}$-10$^{-2}$ $Ω\:$cm），表明超导处于脏极限（dirty limit），即平均自由程远小于相干长度（$\ell \ll ξ_0$）。强电子散射（electron scattering）使与非常规配对机制相关的潜在各向异性（anisotropy）被抹平。

Conclusion: Zn替代诱导的超导电性呈现常规的完全能隙$s$波配对行为，脏极限下的强电子散射抑制了各向异性。这一特征可能与高压（>18 GPa）下CuIr$_2$S$_4$中发现的超导存在关联，因为后者也被认为存在强电子散射。

Abstract: The thiospinel CuIr$_2$S$_4$ undergoes a metal-insulator transition below $\approx$230 K, which is suppressed by substitution of Cu with Zn (Cu$_{1-x}$Zn$_x$Ir$_2$S$_4$) to induce superconductivity for $0.2\lesssim x\lesssim0.8$. We show that the temperature/field dependence of superfluid density in samples with $x = 0.3$ and 0.4 ($T_{\rm c} \approx 3$ K and 2.5 K) investigated by muon spin rotation and relaxation ($μ$SR) is consistent with a fully gapped $s$-wave pairing. Meanwhile, the relatively high resistivity (10$^{-3}$-10$^{-2}$ $Ω\:$cm) in their normal state suggests that the superconductivity is in the "dirty limit" where the mean free path is much shorter than the coherence length ($\ell \ll ξ_0$). This indicates that the potential anisotropy associated with unconventional pairing mechanisms expected under the strong electron correlations is smeared out by the electron scattering. Based on these observations, we discuss potential link between the Zn substitution-induced superconductivity and that recently discovered in CuIr$_2$S$_4$ under high pressure ($>18$ GPa) where the existence of strong electron scattering is also suggested.

### [12] [$H-T$ Phase diagram of CeRh$_{2}$As$_{2}$: Refinement of the parity-switch scenario](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04928)
*Changhee Lee,P. M. R. Brydon*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该论文通过考虑非对称能带结构（nonsymmorphic band structure）和共存的反铁磁序（antiferromagnetic order），解释了CeRh₂As₂中高场超导相异常的初始斜率与近乎垂直的热力学相边界，弥补了单纯宇称翻转（parity-switch）图像与实验相图之间的偏差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: CeRh₂As₂的超导电性因其磁场下的一级相变而受到关注。虽然多重超导（superconducting, SC）相和一级相变看似支持局部非中心对称晶体结构（locally non-centrosymmetric crystal structure）所导致的强Rashba自旋-轨道耦合（Rashba spin-orbit coupling）的宇称翻转（parity-switch）图像，但实验相图与这一简单图像存在明显偏差：热力学测量显示高场SC相的相边界近乎垂直，而输运测量表明其初始斜率比低场SC相更陡。因此需要新的理论解释这些不一致之处。

Method: 论文结合了非对称能带结构分析与共存反铁磁序的唯象理论。通过分析布里渊区边界X点附近狄拉克节点（Dirac node）和II型Van Hove鞍点（type-II Van Hove saddle points）处对称性强制的电子结构，探究层间跳跃振幅增加导致的各向异性增强；同时引入包含共存反铁磁性的唯象理论来解释热力学相边界行为。

Result: 发现对称性强制的电子结构在狄拉克节点和II型Van Hove鞍点附近随层间跳跃振幅增加而变得更加各向异性，这种各向异性能带结构自然地解释了奇宇称（odd-parity）SC相异常的初始斜率。同时，共存反铁磁序导致的场增强奇宇称超导电性（field-enhanced odd-parity superconductivity）抑制了Pauli去配对（Pauli depairing），从而解释了近乎垂直的热力学相边界。

Conclusion: CeRh₂As₂中超导相图的异常特征可通过非对称能带结构与共存反铁磁序的联合效应得到统一理解，这超越了单纯的宇称翻转图像，为理解局域非中心对称超导体中的复杂相行为提供了新的理论框架。

Abstract: The superconductivity of CeRh$_2$As$_2$ has drawn attention due to its first-order transition in magnetic fields. At first glance, the multiple superconducting (SC) phases as well as the first-order transition appear consistent with the parity-switch scenario, which emphasizes the role of strong Rashba spin-orbit coupling enabled by the locally non-centrosymmetric crystal structure. However, experimental phase diagrams exhibit notable deviations from this simple picture: thermodynamic measurements reveal a nearly vertical phase boundary of the high-field SC phase despite the orbital depairing effect, while transport measurements show that the initial slope of the high-field SC phase is steeper than that of the low-field SC phase. Here, we show that these discrepancies can be understood by considering the combined effects of nonsymmorphic band structure and coexisting antiferromagnetic order. We demonstrate that the symmetry-enforced electronic structure around the Dirac node and type-II Van Hove saddle points near the X point in the Brillouin zone boundary becomes more anisotropic with increased interlayer hopping amplitude, and this anisotropic band structure naturally accounts for the anomalous initial slope of the odd-parity SC phase. Meanwhile, a phenomenological theory incorporating coexisting antiferromagnetism explains the nearly vertical thermodynamic phase boundary as a consequence of field-enhanced odd-parity superconductivity enabled by the over-suppression of Pauli depairing.

</details>

### [13] [Becoming, Duration, and the Evolving Block Universe](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03415)

TL;DR: 本文探讨了“两个时间问题”（the two-times problem），即生物与意识系统的定向时间与基础物理学时间之间的关系。作者指出，演化块宇宙（Evolving Block Universe）模型解释了物理时间的方向及其多尺度涌现至大脑时间的过程，但未能解释物理时间如何与时间流逝的主观体验相联系。文章主张柏格森的“绵延”（durée）——即对 lived time 的连续质性体验——标志着这一层级结构到达其极限的第一人称层面，从而将物理时间与 lived time 之间的剩余缺口定位于认识论（epistemological）层面。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决“两个时间问题”，即解释定向、有向的生物与意识系统时间与基础物理学时间之间的关系，并指出已有模型（如演化块宇宙）在解释主观时间体验方面的不足。

Method: 采用概念分析与哲学论证方法，通过引入柏格森的“绵延”（durée）概念，论证其作为第一人称层面的时间体验，是物理时间层级结构（从物理时间到大脑时间）的极限。

Conclusion: 演化块宇宙模型虽能解释物理时间方向及其向大脑时间的多尺度涌现，但无法解释时间流逝的主观体验；柏格森的“绵延”作为第一人称层面的 lived time，标志着这一层级结构的终点，从而将两类时间之间的差距定位于认识论层面。

Abstract: The two-times problem asks how the directed, oriented time of biological and conscious systems relates to the time of fundamental physics. The Evolving Block Universe, in which spacetime grows along Ricci eigenlines through an irreversible quantum dynamics, explains the direction of physical time and its multi-scale emergence up to brain time. It does not explain how this physical time is related to the experience of temporal passage. We argue that Bergson's durée, the continuous qualitative experience of lived time, marks the first-person level beyond brain time at which this hierarchy reaches its limit. This locates the remaining gap between physical time and lived time at the epistemological level.

### [15] [Observational Constraints on Kazakov-Solodukhin Quantum-Deformed Black Holes from M87$^*$ and Sgr A$^*$ Shadows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02631)
*A. Errehymy,Y. Khedif,M. Daoud,B. Turimov,S. Usanov,Z. Yasakov,Z. Avezmuratova*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本论文系统分析了Kazakov-Solodukhin量子变形黑洞时空，该模型通过单一变形参数η将量子修正引入经典Schwarzschild解。研究表明，该模型通过消除经典奇点、引入最小长度尺度、降低Hawking温度以及修正光子动力学和弱场偏转角等特征，在理论上具有吸引力且在观测上可检验。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索一种既保留广义相对论（general relativity）正确极限（η→0），又能引入强场区域量子修正的黑洞时空模型，以解决经典Schwarzschild解中的奇点（singularity）问题。

Method: 基于Kazakov-Solodukhin量子变形（quantum-deformed）黑洞时空，采用单一变形参数η对经典Schwarzschild解进行修正，通过分析曲率不变量、视界结构、热力学性质、光子动力学以及弱场偏转角等特征来刻画模型特性。

Result: 曲率不变量在最小半径r=η附近保持有限，有效消除了经典奇点；视界位置和质量-半径关系发生变化；表面引力降低导致Hawking温度下降和蒸发过程减缓，增强了黑洞的热力学稳定性（thermodynamic stability）；光子球位置偏移，强引力透镜特征改变；阴影保持圆形但尺寸依赖于η；弱场偏转角获得正比于η²的二次修正。

Conclusion: 该量子变形黑洞模型同时满足理论上的奇点消解和观测上的可检验性，观测约束可通过阴影半径偏差不等式|R_sh(η)−R_obs| ≤ ΔR_obs施加对变形参数η的上限。

Abstract: We explore the Kazakov-Solodukhin quantum-deformed black hole spacetime, characterized by a single deformation parameter \( η\) that encodes quantum corrections to the classical Schwarzschild solution. The model preserves the correct general-relativistic limit as \( η\to 0 \), while introducing significant and physically meaningful deviations in the strong-field regime. A central and remarkable feature of the geometry is the regularization of the classical singularity: curvature invariants remain finite near the minimal radius \( r = η\), effectively replacing the divergent core with a smooth and well-behaved region. This behavior naturally introduces a minimal length scale into the spacetime structure, offering a geometrically motivated resolution of the singularity problem. The deformation modifies the horizon structure, shifts the event horizon location, and alters the mass-radius relation. It also reduces the surface gravity, leading to a lower Hawking temperature and a slower evaporation process, thereby enhancing the thermodynamic stability of the black hole. Photon dynamics are correspondingly affected, resulting in a displaced photon sphere and modified strong-lensing characteristics. While the shadow remains perfectly circular due to spherical symmetry, its size depends sensitively on \( η\). Observational constraints can be expressed through \( \left| R_{sh}(η) - R_{obs} \right| \leq ΔR_{obs}, \) which places an upper bound on the deformation parameter. In the weak-field limit, the deflection angle acquires a quadratic correction proportional to \( η^2 \), ensuring consistency with precision tests while allowing potentially detectable deviations in strong-gravity observations. These features make the model both theoretically appealing and observationally testable.

</details>


### [16] [Interacting Holographic Dark Energy in $f(Q)$ Gravity: Cosmological Evolution and Gravitational Wave Signatures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02792)
*N. Amiriborkhani,Alireza Amani,M. A. Ramzanpour*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在修正引力 \(f(Q)\) 框架下研究了一种相互作用的全息暗能量（interactive Holographic Dark Energy, HDE）模型。通过哈勃参数的幂律参数化重构场方程，并利用观测数据约束模型参数，分析了暗能量在宇宙历史中的动力学行为。结果表明，晚期宇宙中暗能量自然趋近于宇宙学常数行为，而在过去则呈现不同的动力学演化。声速稳定性分析表明模型在当前时期具有良好的经典稳定性。引力波传播分析显示，\(f(Q)\) 引力修正及物质与暗能量的相互作用会对张量扰动产生可观测的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在全息暗能量模型的基础上，将其置于修正引力 \(f(Q)\) 的理论框架中，以探索暗能量与物质之间相互作用对宇宙演化和引力波传播的影响，从而构建一种能够描述宇宙加速膨胀并具备观测检验能力的理论模型。

Method: 采用哈勃参数（Hubble parameter）的幂律参数化（power parameterization）来重构场方程；利用 \(H(z)\) 观测数据对模型参数进行约束；基于声速（speed of sound）进行经典稳定性分析；在宇宙学背景下研究张量扰动（tensor perturbations）的演化以分析引力波传播。

Result: 暗能量在晚期宇宙中自然趋近于宇宙学常数（cosmological constant）行为，而在过去则遵循不同的动力学演化；声速稳定性分析表明模型在当前时期具有良好的经典稳定性；物质与暗能量的相对密度参数与观测约束兼容；\(f(Q)\) 引力修正及相互作用对张量扰动的演化产生区别于标准宇宙学场景的信号。

Conclusion: 相互作用的全息暗能量在 \(f(Q)\) 引力框架下能够为宇宙加速膨胀提供一致的理论描述，并为引力波（gravitational waves）的宇宙学观测后果研究提供可行的分析框架。

Abstract: In this paper, an interactive Holographic Dark Energy (HDE) model is studied in the framework of modified gravity \(f(Q)\). By adopting a power parameterization for the Hubble parameter, the field equations are reconstructed and the evolution of the universe at the background level and tensor perturbations are investigated. Then, using observational data \(H(z)\), the model parameters are constrained and the dynamical behavior of dark energy throughout the history of the universe is analyzed. Also, the study of the evolution of energy density, pressure and the Equation of State (EoS) parameter of dark energy shows that dark energy in the late universe naturally tends to a region close to the cosmological constant behavior, while in the past it followed a distinct dynamical evolution. Stability analysis based on the speed of sound also indicates that the model has good classical stability around the present era. In addition, the compatibility of the current values of the relative density parameters of matter and dark energy with the observational constraints confirms the ability of the model to reproduce the main features of the observed universe. Next, the propagation of gravitational waves in the cosmological context of the model is investigated. The results show that the corrections due to \(f(Q)\) gravity and the interaction between matter and dark energy can affect the evolution of tensor perturbations and produce signatures distinct from the standard scenario. Overall, the findings of this study indicate that the interactive HDE in the gravitational framework \(f(Q)\) can provide a consistent framework for describing the cosmic acceleration and studying the cosmological consequences of gravitational waves.

</details>


### [17] [Distinguishing wormholes via Einstein rings and global curvature](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02889)
*M. B. Cruz,C. R. Muniz,R. M. P. Neves,Jonathan A. Rebouças*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了嵌入弯曲FLRW宇宙中的静态Ellis-Bronnikov虫洞的引力透镜性质，推导了弱场透镜方程，发现虫洞爱因斯坦环半径与宇宙学距离呈立方标度关系（区别于史瓦西黑洞的平方根行为），并分析了该效应作为区分虫洞与黑洞透镜的几何诊断工具的潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有引力透镜研究主要针对黑洞或致密天体，而虫洞作为一种假设性的时空拓扑结构，其透镜特征尚缺乏系统分析。本文旨在建立虫洞透镜的唯象模型，并寻找能够将其与黑洞透镜从根本上区分开来的几何诊断方法。

Method: 采用曲率依赖的宇宙学距离，推导嵌入FLRW背景中的静态Ellis-Bronnikov虫洞的弱场透镜方程。通过解析与数值方法分析爱因斯坦环半径的标度行为、红移演化以及空间曲率的不对称响应。

Result: 虫洞爱因斯坦环半径与宇宙学距离呈立方标度关系，而非黑洞的平方根行为；透镜信号在红移演化上呈现质的差异；局部虫洞几何与FLRW背景的耦合产生对空间曲率的不对称响应，该响应在中间红移处反转；虫洞的透镜效率显著低于同等尺度的史瓦西黑洞，微角秒级爱因斯坦环需要宏观尺度的喉部半径。

Conclusion: 虫洞透镜信号提供了一种模型无关的几何诊断方法，可区分虫洞与黑洞引力透镜；若宇宙中存在虫洞族群，其透镜特征可作为探测奇异时空拓扑与宇宙全局几何的灵敏且互补的探针。

Abstract: In this work, we investigate the gravitational lensing properties of a static Ellis-Bronnikov wormhole embedded in a curved Friedmann-Lemaître-Robertson-Walker (FLRW) universe. By employing curvature-dependent cosmological distances, we derive the corresponding weak-field lens equation and demonstrate that the wormhole Einstein ring radius follows a characteristic cubic scaling with cosmological distances, in sharp contrast to the square-root behavior found for Schwarzschild black holes. This distinct scaling leads to a qualitatively different redshift evolution of the lensing signal, providing a model-independent geometric diagnostic to discriminate between wormhole and black hole lensing scenarios. Numerical analysis reveals that the interplay between the local wormhole geometry and the FLRW background produces an asymmetric response to spatial curvature that inverts at intermediate redshifts, exhibiting a non-negligible sensitivity even under tight modern constraints such as those from DESI 2024. We also find that Ellis-Bronnikov wormholes are substantially less efficient gravitational lenses than Schwarzschild black holes of comparable physical scale, implying that microarcsecond-scale Einstein rings require macroscopic throat radii. These results suggest that, should a population of cosmological wormholes exist, their lensing signatures could provide a sensitive, complementary probe of both exotic spacetime topology and the global geometry of the Universe.

### [18] [Decoherence Effects on Primordial Black Holes and Scalar-Induced Gravitational Waves](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02935)
*Waqas Ahmed*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文利用高斯量子失谐（Gaussian quantum discord）诊断原初黑洞（PBH）产生过程中标量扰动的量子-经典转变（quantum-to-classical transition），并展示退相干（decoherence）通过协方差抑制因子 \(Q_{\rm dec}\) 同时影响PBH丰度和标量诱导引力波（SIGW）谱，其中SIGW谱的修正标度关系为 \(\Omega_{\rm GW}^{\rm eff}\simeq Q_{\rm dec}^2\Omega_{\rm GW}^{\rm class}\)。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 原初黑洞（primordial black holes, PBHs）由暴涨真空中的量子涨落（quantum fluctuations）产生，这自然要求用量子信息（quantum-information）的语言描述产生PBH的标量扇区。现有框架缺乏对残余量子关联（residual quantum correlations）的定量诊断。

Method: 将每个动量对 \((\bm k,-\bm k)\) 建模为双模高斯态（two-mode Gaussian state），在纯压缩极限下分析量子失谐（quantum discord）随压缩参量（squeezing parameter）的快速增长行为；在退相干混合态情形中，利用Lindblad开系统描述（Lindblad open-system description）建立高斯损失通道，引入协方差生存因子 \(Q_{\rm dec}(k)\) 并区分其与量子失谐的作用。

Result: 纯压缩极限下，低阈值量子失谐自动满足；退相干情形下，协方差抑制因子 \(Q_{\rm dec}\) 通过经典坍缩方差（classical collapse variance）影响PBH丰度，并通过 \(Q_{\rm dec}(ku)Q_{\rm dec}(kv)\) 因子直接修正辐射主导时期卷积积分中的SIGW谱，给出标度关系 \(\Omega_{\rm GW}^{\rm eff}\simeq Q_{\rm dec}^2\Omega_{\rm GW}^{\rm class}\)。

Conclusion: 量子失谐和退相干提供了刻画PBH产生过程中量子-经典转变（quantum-to-classical transition）的可控方案，最清晰的印记出现在标量诱导引力波（scalar-induced gravitational waves）中。

Abstract: Primordial black holes (PBHs) form when large primordial curvature perturbations re-enter the Hubble radius and exceed the classical collapse threshold. These perturbations originate as quantum fluctuations of the inflationary vacuum, motivating a quantum-information description of the PBH-producing scalar sector. We develop a conservative extension of the standard PBH and scalar-induced gravitational-wave (SIGW) framework in which Gaussian quantum discord is used as a diagnostic of residual quantum correlations, not as a new PBH-formation criterion. We describe each \((\bm k,-\bm k)\) pair as a two-mode Gaussian state and show that, in the pure squeezed limit, discord grows rapidly with the squeezing parameter, so low discord thresholds are automatically satisfied for strongly squeezed modes. The nontrivial regime is the mixed state produced by decoherence. Using a Lindblad open-system description, we motivate a Gaussian loss channel for the scalar covariance matrix and distinguish the discord from a covariance-survival factor \(Q_{\rm dec}(k)\). If the decoherence channel suppresses the scalar two-point covariance, PBH abundance can be affected through the classical collapse variance, while the SIGW spectrum is modified more directly by the factors \(Q_{\rm dec}(ku)Q_{\rm dec}(kv)\) inside the radiation-era convolution. For a narrow scalar peak and slowly varying \(Q_{\rm dec}\), this gives the benchmark scaling \(Ω_{\rm GW}^{\rm eff}\simeq Q_{\rm dec}^2Ω_{\rm GW}^{\rm class}\). Thus quantum discord and decoherence provide a controlled way to characterize the quantum-to-classical transition of PBH-producing perturbations, with the clearest imprint appearing in scalar-induced gravitational waves.

</details>


### [19] [Black holes in f(R) theory of gravity with compact extra dimensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03034)
*Arkady Popov,Sergey Rubin*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文在 $f(R)$ 引力框架下研究 $D=4+n$ 维时空中的静态球对称解，发现额外维紧致化为恒定半径的 $n$ 球时，四维度规对应施瓦西–德西特（Schwarzschild–de Sitter）时空，但宇宙学常数过大。通过引入非最小耦合量子场的真空极化效应，可在半经典近似下获得渐近平坦的四维施瓦西解，并讨论有效普朗克质量与额外维半径的径向依赖性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在高维 $f(R)$ 引力中，静态球对称解通常导致四维有效宇宙学常数（cosmological constant）过大，与观测不符。因此需要引入量子真空极化（vacuum polarization）效应来修正这一矛盾，以获得与观测兼容的渐近平坦解。

Method: 在 $D=4+n$ 维 $f(R)$ 引力中构造静态球对称度规，额外维假设为恒定半径的 $n$ 维紧致球面。求解场方程得到精确解后，引入非最小耦合（nonminimally coupled）量子场的真空极化效应，采用半经典（semiclassical）方法修正引力方程。

Result: 精确解的四维部分对应施瓦西–德西特度规，额外维半径 $L_0$ 与四维宇宙学常数满足关系 $\Lambda_4 = (n-1)/L_0^2$，该值通常过大。引入量子真空极化后，可获得渐近平坦的四维施瓦西解作为极限情形，此时额外维半径由量子场真空期望值（vacuum expectation value）决定。有效四维普朗克质量（Planck mass）和额外维半径均表现出径向坐标依赖性。

Conclusion: 高维 $f(R)$ 引力中的经典解需要量子真空极化效应才能与观测相符；量子修正后的解可实现额外维的稳定化并得到渐近平坦四维时空，但有效引力耦合和额外维结构在径向上并非恒定的。

Abstract: We study static, spherically symmetric solutions in $f(R)$ gravity within a $D = 4+n$-dimensional spacetime, where the extra dimensions form a compact $n$-sphere of constant radius. We derive an exact solution in which the four-dimensional part of the metric corresponds to the Schwarzschild - de Sitter metric, while the extra dimensions are stabilized at a constant radius $L_0$. A consistency condition relates the size of the internal space to the effective four-dimensional cosmological constant $Λ_4 = (n-1)/L_0^2$, which is generally too large to be compatible with observations. To overcome this issue, we include the vacuum polarization effects of quantized matter fields nonminimally coupled to curvature. Using the semiclassical approach, we obtain an asymptotically flat four-dimensional Schwarzschild solution as a limiting case, where the size of the extra sphere is determined by the vacuum expectation values of the quantum fields. Finally, we discuss the dependence of the effective four-dimensional Planck mass and the extra-dimensional radius on the radial coordinate.

</details>


### [20] [Conformal symmetries and MOTS stability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03128)
*Abbas M. Sherif*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文证明了在温和能量条件下，与时空中过去指向共形 Killing 矢量场（conformal Killing vector field）的积分曲线相交的 MOTS（marginally outer trapped surface，边际外陷表面）是严格稳定的（strictly stable），并会光滑演化至类空视界（spacelike horizon）。同时给出了基于矢量场散度正负的稳定性判据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解 MOTS 在广义相对论（General Relativity）中的稳定性与演化行为，是研究黑洞视界（black hole horizon）形成与动力学的核心问题之一。本文旨在建立 MOTS 在共形 Killing 场存在条件下的稳定性条件及其与未来类空视界的关系。

Method: 采用微分几何与广义相对论的框架，在时空中选取一类由 2-曲面 $\mathcal{S}$ 构成的类空叶状结构（spacelike foliation），并考虑与过去指向共形 Killing 矢量场（该场位于 $\mathcal{S}$ 的法空间内）的积分曲线相交的 MOTS，通过分析散度条件与能量条件推导稳定性结论。

Result: 1. 在温和能量条件下，与过去指向共形 Killing 矢量场积分曲线相交的 MOTS 是严格稳定的，并且会光滑演化成类空视界。2. 若矢量场散度在 $\mathcal{S}$ 上的限制非负，则 $\mathcal{S}$ 不稳定；若该限制为负且 $\mathcal{S}$ 是 2-球面，则 $\mathcal{S}$ 必定严格稳定。

Conclusion: MOTS 的稳定性与其在共形 Killing 场下的几何条件直接相关，稳定解可演化为类空视界，为黑洞视界动力学提供了新的理论判据。

Abstract: Let $\{Σ_t\}$ be a spacelike foliation of a spacetime $\mathcal{M}$, and suppose each $Σ_t$ is foliated by 2-surfaces $\mathcal{S}$ with spacelike unit normal in $Σ_t$. We show that under mild energy conditions, a MOTS $\mathcal{S}$ that intersects integral curves of past-pointing conformal Killing vector field lying in the normal space of $\mathcal{S}$ is strictly stable and evolves smoothly to a spacelike horizon. We also show that if the restriction of the divergence of the vector field to $\mathcal{S}$ is non-negative, $\mathcal{S}$ is unstable, and if negative and $\mathcal{S}$ is a 2-sphere, $\mathcal{S}$ must be strictly stable.

</details>


### [21] [Odd-parity ringdown gravitational waves of a spherically symmetric black hole with perfect fluid accretion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03231)
*Rikuto Ohashi,Yasutaka Koga,Hiroyuki Nakano,Kota Ogasawara,Chul-Moon Yoo*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文研究了在稀薄稳态球对称完美流体吸积（accretion）过程中增长的史瓦西黑洞（Schwarzschild black hole）的奇宇称环波（odd-parity ringdown）。在吸积率的一阶近似下，通过时域直接计算波形，发现频率虚部与实部之比可以抵消黑洞增长引起的长期变化和红移因子，从而纯粹反映环境信息；而频率的时间依赖性则反映吸积率，二者共同构成两组可观测物理量，有望通过多模式测量约束黑洞周围环境。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 黑洞的环波（ringdown）信号是探测强场引力的干净探针，但真实黑洞周围可能存在物质分布，导致背景时空动力学演化，环波频率也随时间变化。现有模型通常假设静态时空，忽视了环境物质对环波频率的影响。因此，有必要研究存在吸积过程时环波频率的行为，并从观测角度提取环境信息。

Method: 研究采用奇宇称（odd-parity）分析，针对通过稀薄稳态球对称完美流体吸积而增长的史瓦西黑洞。在吸积率的一阶微扰框架下，直接在时域（time domain）计算动力背景上的环波波形（ringdown waveform）。由于奇宇称物质扰动与度规扰动（metric perturbation）解耦，波模式可纯粹由张量模式（purely tensorial mode）描述。

Result: 频率虚部与实部的比值可以同时抵消由黑洞质量增长引起的长期变化（secular variation）和红移因子（redshift factor），使其偏离史瓦西背景值的部分纯粹反映周围环境。另一方面，频率的时间依赖性反映吸积率（accretion rate），可定义与之相关的第二组可观测量。

Conclusion: 测量上述两组可观测量，并跨多个准正则模式（quasinormal modes）进行联合分析，可能为约束黑洞周围的物质环境提供重要信息。

Abstract: The ringdown waves from a black hole offer a clean probe of strong-field gravity, but a matter distribution that may be present around a realistic black hole renders the background spacetime dynamical and the ringdown frequencies time-dependent. We study the odd-parity ringdown of a Schwarzschild black hole that grows through the dilute, steady, spherically symmetric accretion of a perfect fluid. Working to first order in the accretion rate, we compute the ringdown waveform directly in the time domain on this dynamical background. Since the odd-parity matter perturbation decouples from the metric perturbation, the wave mode can be described by a purely tensorial mode on the accreting background. In particular, the ratio of the imaginary to the real part of the frequency cancels both the secular variation caused by the growth of the black hole and the redshift factor, so that its deviation from the Schwarzschild value purely reflects the surrounding environment. The time dependence of the frequency, on the other hand, reflects the accretion rate and allows us to define a second observable tied to it. We argue that measuring these observables across multiple modes may provide significant information to constrain the surrounding environment of the black hole.

</details>


### [22] [Dark energy genesis: modeling dissipative effects in primordial cosmology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03272)
*Pietro Pellecchia,Alejandro Perez,Salvatore Ribisi*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文提出，量子引力中的离散结构可导致平滑有效区域的耗散效应，并基于单模引力（unimodular gravity）构建了一个有效宇宙学模型，其中变宇宙学常数（varying cosmological constant）源于耗散。通过引入“量子引力缺陷”（quantum gravity defects）作为隐藏自由度充当物质场的有效热浴，并借鉴Caldeira-Leggett模型研究欧姆热浴（Ohmic bath）情形，结果表明耗散可以从无暗能量的原初宇宙出发，产生一个小的正宇宙学常数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子引力（quantum gravity）的各种方法中，时空几何被认为是从普朗克尺度（Planck scale）的更为基本的离散结构中涌现出来的。这些离散结构的存在可能导致平滑有效区域中的耗散效应（dissipative effects），然而如何在引力理论中系统描述此类非守恒效应仍是一个开放问题。

Method: 论文在单模引力框架下发展了一种有效宇宙学模型（effective cosmological model），允许宇宙学常数因耗散而变动。为描述这一过程，引入了隐藏自由度——称为量子引力缺陷——作为物质场的有效热浴（effective bath）。具体地，借鉴描述布朗运动（Brownian motion）的Caldeira-Leggett模型，研究欧姆热浴情形下的耗散动力学，推导出物质能量密度（matter energy density）的扩散方程（diffusion equation）。

Result: 结果表明，从一个没有暗能量（dark energy）的原初宇宙（primordial universe）出发，耗散机制能够产生一个小的正宇宙学常数（small positive cosmological constant）。

Conclusion: 论文通过将量子引力缺陷作为隐藏自由度引入单模引力框架，论证了耗散效应可以自然地导致宇宙学常数的动态生成，为非保守引力效应提供了一种新的有效描述路径。

Abstract: In various approaches to quantum gravity, spacetime geometry is understood to emerge from more fundamental discrete structures at the Planck scale. As sometimes posited, their presence could lead to dissipative effects in the smooth effective sector. In this paper, we develop the idea of non-conservation in gravity, by introducing an effective cosmological model within unimodular gravity, in which a varying cosmological constant arises as a consequence of dissipation. We show that this requires to incorporate hidden degrees of freedom -- termed quantum gravity defects -- that act as an effective bath for the matter fields. To illustrate the viability of the framework, we study the case of an Ohmic bath inspired by the Caldeira-Leggett model for Brownian motion, leading to a diffusion equation for the matter energy density. The results show that, starting from a primordial universe with no dark energy, dissipation can account for the generation of a small positive cosmological constant.

</details>


### [23] [Reconstructing $f(R)$ gravity from Viaggiu Holographic Dark Energy under Hubble, Event Horizon and Granda Oliveros cutoffs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03308)
*Arushi Jhunjhunwala,Sayani Maity*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在Viaggiu全息暗能量（VHDE）框架下重构了$f(R)$引力理论，通过VHDE与曲率诱导能量密度的对应关系，对哈勃视界、未来事件视界以及Granda Oliveros截断三种红外截断分别推导出显式的$f(R)$形式。通过宇宙学参数、稳定性条件和局部引力约束的分析，验证了所构造模型无鬼影（ghost）和无快子（tachyonic）不稳定性，表明VHDE启发的$f(R)$引力模型是解释晚期宇宙加速膨胀的一致且灵活的几何框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有$f(R)$引力模型需要从全息暗能量视角获得更系统的理论重构，而Viaggiu全息暗能量（VHDE）由于考虑了宇宙学视界动力学导致的熵修正，为建立更自洽的全息暗能量与修正引力之间的对应关系提供了新契机。

Method: 在VHDE框架下建立全息暗能量与曲率诱导能量密度之间的对应关系（correspondence），分别采用哈勃视界（Hubble horizon）、未来事件视界（future event horizon）和Granda Oliveros截断三种不同的红外截断（infrared cutoff），推导出相应的$f(R)$显式形式，并通过状态方程（equation of state）和减速参数（deceleration parameter）等宇宙学参数进行图形化分析。

Result: 所重构的$f(R)$模型成功描述了宇宙从减速膨胀到加速膨胀的转变；稳定性条件和局部引力约束检验表明模型不存在鬼影和快子不稳定性。

Conclusion: VHDE启发的$f(R)$引力模型是一个一致且灵活的几何框架（geometric framework），能够有效解释晚期宇宙的加速膨胀。

Abstract: This work explores the reconstruction of $f(R)$ gravity within the framework of newly proposed Viaggiu holographic dark energy (VHDE), which incorporates entropy corrections due to the dynamical nature of cosmological horizons. By implementing a correspondence between VHDE and curvature-induced energy density, we generate explicit forms of $f(R)$ for different infrared cutoffs, namely the Hubble horizon, future event horizon, and Granda Oliveros cutoff. The resulting models are analyzed graphically through the cosmological parameters such as the equation of state and deceleration parameter, revealing a successful description of the transition from decelerated to accelerated expansion. The viability of the reconstructed models is further examined through stability conditions and local gravity constraints, that yields the nature of the models as free from ghost and tachyonic instabilities and demonstrates VHDE-inspired $f(R)$ gravity model as a consistent and flexible geometric framework for explaining the late-time cosmic acceleration of the Universe.

### [24] [Black Hole Memory Burden and its Signatures in Gravitational Waves from Mergers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03560)
*Gia Dvali,Michael Zantedeschi,Sebastian Zell*

TL;DR: 本文研究黑洞（black hole）的“快速记忆负担”（swift memory burden）效应如何由坍缩源特征决定，发现该记忆负担可远超其前身星的信息含量；极端情况下（如双粒子碰撞形成的黑洞）呈现最大记忆负担。研究进一步推导了恒星坍缩形成黑洞的界限，并量化了记忆负担对引力波（gravitational waves）准正则模频率偏移的影响，表明引力波观测可探测黑洞信息存储机制及其形成历史。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索黑洞“快速记忆负担”（swift memory burden）效应如何受其坍缩形成源特征的影响，并理解该效应对引力波（gravitational waves）观测的潜在可探测信号。

Method: 通过理论分析，研究不同类型坍缩源（尤其是双粒子碰撞与恒星坍缩）形成黑洞的记忆负担（memory burden）特征；推导恒星坍缩情形下的界限，并计算记忆负担对黑洞准正则模（quasinormal modes）频率偏移的定量影响。

Result: 黑洞的记忆负担可显著超过其前身星的信息含量；双粒子碰撞形成的黑洞呈现最大记忆负担；记忆负担会引发引力波（gravitational waves）准正则模的频率偏移。

Conclusion: 引力波（gravitational waves）观测能够探测黑洞的信息存储机制及其形成历史，从而检验快速记忆负担（swift memory burden）效应的理论预言。

Abstract: Swift memory burden (MB) implies that the information stored in a black hole (BH) can modify its classical dynamics when the BH is perturbed. This influences the gravitational waves (GWs) emitted during BH mergers. In this paper, we investigate how the BH memory load is determined by the features of the collapsing source. We show that the memory load can vastly exceed the information content of its progenitor. An extreme example is a BH formed in a two-particle collision, which exhibits maximal MB. We then derive bounds for BHs formed through stellar collapse and examine the impact of swift MB on BH quasinormal modes, quantifying the MB-induced frequency shift of GWs. These findings imply that GW observations probe the fundamental mechanisms of BH information storage as well as their formation history.

### [25] [Generalized Unruh temperature for dynamical thin-shell wormholes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03577)
*Francisco S. N. Lobo,Manuel E. Rodrigues*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文统一了动力学薄壳虫洞中两种有效温度概念——喉部局域加速度温度与类霍金粒子产生温度——通过广义Unruh恒等式建立等价关系，并在Schwarzschild-Schwarzschild虫洞中给出解析表达与量子通量，揭示了壳温度与Tolman温度在准视界附近的发散同源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 动力学薄壳虫洞中存在两种独立定义的有效温度（加速度温度与粒子产生温度），但二者之间的关系尚未明确。本文旨在统一这两个温度概念，并建立其内在联系。

Method: 通过对虫洞两侧结条件（junction）的加速度标度取平均定义热力学壳温度；利用每个渐近宇宙的剥离函数（peeling function）定义有效粒子产生温度；在渐近指数型零射线映射（asymptotically exponential null-ray maps）下推导出广义Unruh恒等式（generalized Unruh identity），证明两种温度等价。

Result: 在Schwarzschild-Schwarzschild虫洞的对称与非对称构型中，给出了类霍金谱（Hawking-like spectra）、重整化量子通量（renormalized quantum fluxes）及准视界极限（quasi-horizon limits）的显式解析表达式。证明壳温度在准视界附近的发散与局域Tolman温度（local Tolman temperature）的发散同源，均来自视界处的无限引力蓝移（infinite gravitational blueshift）。

Conclusion: 该结果提供了无视界动力学时空中加速度、粒子产生与温度的统一诠释，将Hawking效应与Unruh效应之间的概念联系从稳态黑洞扩展到更一般的动力学场景。

Abstract: We unify two independent notions of effective temperature in dynamical thin-shell wormholes: the local acceleration temperature of the throat and the Hawking-like particle-creation temperature governed by the peeling of null rays. The effective acceleration scale, obtained by averaging over both sides of the junction, defines the thermodynamic shell temperature, while peeling functions for each asymptotic universe yield an effective particle-creation temperature. For asymptotically exponential null-ray maps, we derive the generalized Unruh identity that equates these two temperatures. Applied to Schwarzschild-Schwarzschild wormholes, the formalism yields explicit analytical expressions for the Hawking-like spectra, renormalized quantum fluxes, and quasi-horizon limits in both symmetric and asymmetric configurations. The divergence of the shell temperature near the quasi-horizon is shown to mirror the divergence of the local Tolman temperature, both originating from the infinite gravitational blueshift at a horizon. These results provide a unified interpretation of acceleration, particle creation, and temperature in horizonless dynamical spacetimes, extending the conceptual link between the Hawking and Unruh effects beyond stationary black holes.

</details>


### [26] [Additional Observational Signatures of Asymmetric Thin-Shell Wormholes within 4D Einstein-Gauss-Bonnet Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03673)
*J. Song,X. G. Lan*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过Visser的剪切-粘贴构造（cut-and-paste construction）研究4D爱因斯坦-高斯-邦内特（Einstein-Gauss-Bonnet）非对称薄壳虫洞的光学外观，发现其图像中存在额外的光子环（photon rings）和透镜带（lensing bands），这些特征在对应黑洞中不存在，且额外环的尺寸随高斯-邦内特耦合常数$α$增大而增大，为区分和表征薄壳虫洞时空提供了可靠判据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索4D爱因斯坦-高斯-邦内特非对称薄壳虫洞（asymmetric thin-shell wormhole）的光学外观，寻找能够区分虫洞与黑洞的观测特征。

Method: 采用Visser的剪切-粘贴构造（cut-and-paste construction）构建非对称薄壳虫洞；计算不同高斯-邦内特耦合常数$α$下的光子球半径（photon sphere radius）和临界碰撞参数（critical impact parameter）；分析有效势（effective potential）和光子运动（photon motion）；假设光学薄吸积盘（optically thin accretion disk）为唯一光源进行成像模拟。

Result: 虫洞的有效势、光线路径和方位角（azimuthal angle）与两个时空的质量比（mass ratio）密切相关；非对称薄壳虫洞图像出现额外的光子环和透镜带，这些特征在4D爱因斯坦-高斯-邦内特黑洞中不存在；额外环的尺寸随$α$增大而增大，与黑洞情况相反；质量比和喉半径（throat radius）显著调节这些额外光子环的形态。

Conclusion: 额外出现且异常明亮的光子环为区分和表征薄壳虫洞时空（thin-shell wormhole spacetime）提供了可靠判据。

Abstract: In this paper, we study the optical appearance of a 4D Einstein-Gauss-Bonnet asymmetric thin-shell wormhole. Using Visser's cut-and-paste construction, we determine the photon sphere radius and critical impact parameter for different values of the Gauss-Bonnet coupling $α$. We then investigate the effective potential and photon motion inside the wormhole spacetime. It is found that the effective potential, light ray paths, and azimuthal angle are closely tied to the mass ratio of the two spacetimes. Considering an optically thin accretion disk as the only light source, we find that the asymmetric thin-shell wormhole's images exhibit additional photon rings and lensing bands that are absent for a 4D Einstein-Gauss-Bonnet black hole. Furthermore, the size of these extra rings increases with $α$, contrary to the black hole case. Such exceptionally bright rings provide a reliable criterion for distinguishing and characterizing a thin-shell wormhole spacetime. We also verify that the mass ratio and throat radius significantly tune the morphology of these extra photon rings.

### [27] [Equatorial periodic orbits and gravitational waveforms in Bardeen black holes surrounded by perfect fluid dark matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03714)
*Sohan Kumar Jha*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文研究了完美流体暗物质（PFDM）包围的Bardeen黑洞（BPFDM黑洞）中非线性电动力学（NED）与暗物质对粒子轨道动力学和引力波波形的联合影响，揭示了NED和暗物质在约束轨道与极端质量比旋进（EMRI）波形中的可区分特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究暗物质（dark matter）与非线性电动力学（non-linear electrodynamics, NED）之间的相互作用，通过分析Bardeen黑洞在完美流体暗物质（perfect fluid dark matter, PFDM）背景下的轨道动力学与引力波信号，寻找暗物质和NED在强引力系统中的可观测特征。

Method: 首先计算控制粒子轨迹的有效势（effective potential），通过对势施加合适条件，研究暗物质和NED对边际束缚轨道（marginally bound orbit, MBO）和最内稳定圆轨道（innermost stable circular orbit, ISCO）的影响。利用$(z,w,v)$分类法（taxonomy）系统组织周期轨道，结合有理数$q$分析周期轨道特征。最后采用数值"Kludge"方法计算以BPFDM黑洞为中心天体的极端质量比旋进（EMRIs）发射的引力波波形。

Result: 暗物质和NED参数（磁荷$g$和暗物质参数$\b$）对边际束缚轨道（MBO）、最内稳定圆轨道（ISCO）以及周期轨道的能量、角动量和有理数$q$均有显著影响；引力波波形中亦呈现出暗物质和NED的独特信号特征。

Conclusion: 非线性电动力学（NED）和暗物质（DM）在黑洞轨道动力学与引力波波形中留下了可区分的特征信号，这为通过引力波观测探测暗物质属性和检验非线性电动力学理论提供了潜在途径。

Abstract: To probe the interplay between dark matter (DM) and non-linear electrodynamics (NED), we consider the Bardeen black hole (BH) surrounded by perfect fluid dark matter (PFDM). We first compute the effective potential governing the particle trajectory, and then, by imposing suitable conditions on the potential, examine the effects of DM and NED on the marginally bound orbit (MBO) and innermost stable circular orbit (ISCO). In this study, we confine the particle's trajectory to the equatorial plane. We then investigate periodic orbits around the Bardeen BH surrounded by PFDM (BPFDM BH), considering the rational number $q$ associated with each periodic orbit. We use the $(z,w,v)$ taxonomy, which is widely used to systematically organize periodic orbits. We examine the variation of $q$ with energy and angular momentum, and also the variation of the angular momentum and energy required for a specific $(z,w,v)$ configuration with the magnetic charge $g$ and DM parameter $\b$. Finally, with the help of the numerical "Kludge" method, we examine gravitational waveforms emitted from EMRIs where the central supermassive BH is modeled as a BPFDM BH. Our study reveals distinct signatures of NED and DM on orbital dynamics and gravitational waveforms.

### [28] [Radiated Energy Spectrum, Radiated Angular Distribution and Non-linear Memory from the One-loop Gravitational Bremsstrahlung Waveform](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03879)
*Donato Bini,Thibault Damour,Stefano De Angelis,Andrea Geralico*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文在单圈精度的频域引力波波形基础上，推导了广义相对论两体散射中辐射引力波的频谱、角分布及非线性记忆效应的多极展开，将相关计算结果推进至后闵可夫斯基阶$G^4$（辐射能量）和$G^5$（记忆效应），并在质心系中达到7.5后牛顿阶精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在近期获得的两体无自旋大质量粒子散射的频域引力波波形（后闵可夫斯基（post-Minkowskian）单圈阶，即$G^2+G^3$）基础上，进一步系统推导更高阶的引力波辐射量，包括频谱、角分布及非线性记忆效应，以扩展已有的理论结果。

Method: 基于单圈精度的频域引力波波形$h(ω, θ,φ) \sim G^2 + G^3$，依次推导谱引力波辐亮度（spectral gravitational-wave radiance）$dE^{\rm gw}/(dωdΩ)$、辐射引力波能谱（radiated GW energy spectrum）$dE^{\rm gw}/dω$及辐射引力波角分布（radiated GW angular distribution）$dE^{\rm gw}/dΩ$至$G^4$阶；从角分布进一步推导非线性记忆（non-linear memory）的多极展开（multipole expansion）至$G^5$阶。全部计算均在质心系（center-of-mass frame）中进行。

Result: 获得了至$G^4$阶的引力波辐射频谱与角分布，以及至$G^5$阶的非线性记忆多极展开；所有结果在质心系中达到了分数7.5后牛顿（post-Newtonian, PN）精度。

Conclusion: 该工作系统拓展了后闵可夫斯基框架下两体散射引力波辐射的理论预测，为后续更高精度引力波波形建模提供了重要参考。

Abstract: The frequency-domain gravitational waveform emitted by the scattering of two non-spinning massive particles has recently been derived at next-to-leading, \textit{i.e.} one-loop, post-Minkowskian order, $h(ω, θ,φ) \sim G^2 + G^3$. Building on this one-loop-accurate frequency-domain gravitational waveform, we successively derive the spectral gravitational-wave (GW) radiance, $dE^{\rm gw}/(dωdΩ)$, the radiated GW energy spectrum, $dE^{\rm gw}/dω$, and the radiated GW angular distribution, $dE^{\rm gw}/dΩ$, up to order $G^4$ included. We deduce from the radiated angular distribution the multipole expansion of the non-linear memory up to order $G^5$ included, thereby extending previous results. We work in the center-of-mass frame, and our results reach the fractional 7.5PN accuracy. For completeness, we include the tree-level information (considered in the center-of-mass frame).

</details>


### [29] [Identifying lensed gravitational waves with physics-informed posterior learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03885)
*Tian-Yang Sun,Xiao Guo,Jing-Fei Zhang,Xin Zhang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种物理信息驱动的后验学习（physics-informed posterior learning）方法，用于区分引力波透镜多镜像信号与非关联的多并合事件。该方法利用几何光学一致性约束，结合模拟训练的后验分布与波形特征，在1%虚警率下将探测效率从20.8%提升至35.2%，并将所需网络信噪比从45.3降低至33.5，表明物理一致性可成为密集引力波目录中机器学习搜索的指导原则。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 引力波引力透镜效应可用于探测致密透镜体、暗物质子结构及宇宙学距离，但当无关的双星并合事件在同一分析窗口内重叠时，识别透镜事件极其困难。现有方法无法有效区分真正的透镜多像信号与时间上重合的非关联并合事件。

Method: 开发了物理信息驱动的后验学习（physics-informed posterior learning）方法，利用透镜在几何光学近似下的物理一致性——透镜可改变振幅、到达时间和莫尔斯相位偏移（Morse phase offset），但保留源信号的本征相位演化。方法包括两步：首先推断基于模拟训练的公共探测器帧啁啾质量（detector-frame chirp mass）和对称质量比（symmetric mass ratio）的近似后验分布，然后将后验样本与直接波形特征融合。训练采用通用多像模拟，而点质量、奇异等温球（singular-isothermal-sphere）、奇异等温椭球（singular-isothermal-ellipsoid）及剪切扰动透镜则留作透镜族外推评估。

Result: 基于观测动机的双黑洞种群，融合排序方法在1%参考虚警率阈值下将探测效率从20.8%提升至35.2%；实现50%探测效率所需的网络信噪比从45.3降至33.5，对应信噪比等效距离尺度扩大1.35倍。性能提升受限于部分源一致的高信噪比非关联多并合事件，以及对非关联多并合群体校准的需求。

Conclusion: 物理一致性可成为密集引力波目录中机器学习搜索的指导原则。该方法在区分透镜多像信号与非关联多并合事件方面具有显著优势，但性能仍受限于高信噪比干扰事件及群体校准精度。

Abstract: Gravitational lensing of gravitational waves can probe compact lenses, dark matter substructure, and cosmological distances, but identifying lensed events is difficult when unrelated binary mergers overlap in the same analysis window. We develop physics-informed posterior learning for ranking lensed multi-image signals against unrelated multiple-merger events. The method exploits the geometric-optics consistency that lensing can change amplitudes, arrival times, and Morse phase offsets while preserving the intrinsic phase evolution of the source. We infer a simulation-trained approximate posterior for the common detector-frame chirp mass and symmetric mass ratio, and fuse posterior samples with direct waveform features. Training uses generic multi-image simulations, while point-mass, singular-isothermal-sphere, singular-isothermal-ellipsoid, and shear-perturbed lenses are reserved for held-out lens-family evaluation. For the observationally motivated binary-black-hole population, the fusion ranking raises the detection efficiency from $20.8\%$ to $35.2\%$ at a $1\%$ reference false-positive-rate threshold calibrated on the corresponding unrelated multiple-merger sample. It lowers the network signal-to-noise ratio needed for $50\%$ detection efficiency from 45.3 to 33.5, which corresponds to a 1.35 times larger signal-to-noise-ratio-equivalent distance scale. The gain is limited by loud unrelated multiple-merger events that are partly source consistent, and by the need to calibrate the unrelated multiple-merger population. These results suggest that physical consistency can become a guiding principle for machine learning searches in dense gravitational-wave catalogs.

</details>


### [30] [Semiclassical regularity of compact trapped regions: From dynamical horizons to inner extremality](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03916)
*Raúl Carballo-Rubio,Francesco Di Filippo,Stefano Liberati,Matt Visser*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究永恒黑洞内部视界（inner horizon）的半经典不稳定性，发现在动力学演化时空中，由于内视界不再是柯西视界（Cauchy horizon），重整化应力-能量张量（RSET）保持有限；但在非极端内视界情况下，RSET随时间指数增长，仅当陷获区域永恒存在时才出现发散；而内极端（inner-extremal）几何中，指数增长被替换为温和得多的幂律增长，因此这类时空可能成为经典和半经典意义上亚稳态黑洞内部的自然候选者。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典非极端内视界同时存在质量膨胀（mass-inflation）不稳定性和半经典不稳定性（重整化应力-能量张量发散）；内极端几何虽可避免经典质量膨胀，但在静态设定下仍存在RSET的奇异行为。本文旨在探讨动力学情形下内视界的半经典稳定性是否与静态情形具有质的区别。

Method: 考虑描述紧凑陷获区域（compact trapped region）在有限时间内形成与蒸发的动力学时空，采用s-波波里亚科夫近似（s-wave Polyakov approximation），计算内真空态（in-vacuum state）下应力-能量张量的期望值。

Result: 动力学情形下，由于内视界不再是柯西视界，RSET在全时空保持有限。对于一般非极端内视界，RSET在内视界处随时间指数增长，发散仅出现在陷获区域永恒存在的渐近极限中。对于内极端几何，指数增长被替换为弱得多的幂律增长（power-law growth）。

Conclusion: 在动力学演化时空中，内极端几何的半经典不稳定性显著弱于非极端情形，这类时空可作为经典和半经典意义上亚稳态黑洞内部的自然候选者。

Abstract: In eternal black-hole spacetimes, inner horizons are Cauchy horizons and are generically unstable. For non-extremal inner horizons, this includes both the classical mass-inflation instability and a semiclassical instability associated with divergences in the renormalized stress-energy tensor (RSET). Inner-extremal geometries, for which the inner-horizon surface gravity vanishes, evade classical mass inflation, but in stationary settings still suffer from singular behavior of the RSET. In this work, we show that the dynamical case is qualitatively different. Considering spacetimes describing the formation and evaporation of a compact trapped region in finite time, and working in the $s$-wave Polyakov approximation, we compute the expectation value of the stress-energy tensor in the in-vacuum state. Given that in this case the inner horizon is not a Cauchy horizon, the RSET remains finite everywhere. For generic non-extremal inner horizons, however, the RSET grows exponentially in time at the inner horizon, with a divergence emerging only in the asymptotic limit of an ever-lasting trapped region. For inner-extremal geometries this exponential growth is replaced by a considerably milder power-law growth. Such spacetimes may therefore be considered natural candidates for classically and semiclassically meta-stable black-hole interiors.

</details>


### [31] [On the structure of black hole interior in a model of scalar quasi-particles within the GR framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03938)
*S. Bondarenko*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出一个由非线性自相互作用标量场描述的无奇点黑洞内部模型。该模型包含三层结构：核心（负能量AdS区域）、过渡层（零引力超曲面）、外壳（正能量热激发层）。通过Israel匹配连接各层，求解静态爱因斯坦方程得到各层的度规与质量函数，并建立两温度热力学。黑洞形成与霍金蒸发被描述为准静态热力学循环。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有黑洞内部模型通常存在奇点问题，因此需要构建一个有效且无奇点（singularity-free）的黑洞内部描述，克服经典广义相对论中奇点不可避免的困难。

Method: 采用一个具有非线性自相互作用势（non-linear self-interaction potential）的标量场（scalar field）来描述黑洞内部。将内部划分为三层——核心（core）、过渡层（transition layer）和外壳（crust）——每层由局域准粒子密度及势的极值点确定。通过Israel匹配条件在过渡层处连接核心与外壳，并求解静态爱因斯坦方程（static Einstein equations）得到各层的度规（metric）和质量函数（mass function）。

Result: 获得了外壳的边界状态方程（edge equation of state）、零引力超曲面（null-gravity surface）对于普通物质和有效负质量物质的线性稳定性条件（linear stability condition），以及连接动能激发与负温度基态的两温度热力学（two-temperature thermodynamics）。核心为AdS型负能量密度区域，模拟准粒子凝聚体；外壳为位于零势阱之上的正能量热激发层。

Conclusion: 该框架将核心与外壳统一在同一个场描述中，强调了负能量AdS核心及负温度概念在黑洞内部描述中的关键作用。在这一图景下，黑洞的形成与霍金蒸发（Hawking evaporation）表现为一个近似绝热（adiabatic）热力学引擎的准静态循环，以负能量核心为工作物质。

Abstract: We propose an effective, singularity-free model of the black hole interior described entirely by a scalar field with a non-linear self-interaction potential. The interior consists of three layers -- a core, a transition layer, and a crust -- each fixed by the local quasi-particle density and the corresponding extremum of the potential of the field. The crust is a layer of massive, positive-energy thermal excitations above the zero-potential well, beneath a genuine Schwarzschild horizon at $r = 2GM_{\rm ADM}$. The core is an AdS-type region of negative energy density, it simulates a condensate of quasi-particles which carry zero classical kinetic energy and form a negative potential well governed by a negative inverse temperature parameter. The two regions are joined through Israel matching across the transition layer, which sits at an approximately null-gravity hypersurface of maximal regular matter density and where both the sign of the energy density and the type of thermal excitations change. Solving the static Einstein equations, we obtain the metric and mass functions of each layer, the edge equation of state of the crust, the linear stability condition of the null-gravity surface for ordinary and effectively negative mass matter, and the two-temperature thermodynamics linking the kinetic excitations to the negative temperature ground state. The framework unifies core and crust within a single field description and highlights the role of the negative energy AdS core and the associated negative temperature notion in describing black hole interior. In this picture the formation and Hawking evaporation of a black hole appear as a quasi-static cycle of an almost adiabatic thermodynamic engine, with the negative energy core as the working substance.

### [32] [Transient Dynamical Wormholes with Decaying Radial Energy Flux](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04041)
*Allah Ditta,Phongpichit Channuie*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在广义相对论（general relativity）框架下研究了一类形状函数随时间变化的可穿越虫洞（traversable wormhole）。几何演化通过爱因斯坦场方程的非对角分量与径向能量流（radial energy flux）直接耦合，从而实现了非静态构型。模型由静态背景加上随时间衰减的瞬态项构成，满足喉部存在、外扩条件和渐近平坦性等可穿越虫洞标准。零能量条件（null energy condition）在喉部附近被违背，但违背程度随时间降低；总奇异物质（exotic matter）体积积分在晚期趋于常数。在适当参数下，系统对小扰动保持稳定且扰动随时间衰减。该模型通过能量输运（energy transport）驱动虫洞演化，逐步过渡到静态构型，为动力学虫洞提供了物理动机清晰的框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 广义相对论中的可穿越虫洞通常基于静态几何构造，然而真实物理场景（如天体演化或宇宙学环境）要求虫洞几何具有时间依赖性。现有动力学虫洞研究多依赖宇宙学尺度因子（cosmological scale factor）驱动演化，缺乏由内部能量输运机制驱动的自然描述。本文旨在提出一种由径向能量流直接驱动几何演化的动力学虫洞模型，以弥合静态理想化与真实动力学之间的差距。

Method: 通过允许虫洞的形状函数（shape function）随时间变化，将几何演化与爱因斯坦场方程中非对角分量所描述的径向能量流直接联系起来。求解场方程得到精确解，几何形式为静态背景加随时间衰减的瞬态项。在此基础上，分别检验可穿越虫洞的标准条件（喉部、外扩条件和渐近平坦性）、能量条件的违背情况（含零能量条件及其体积积分度量）、以及系统对小扰动的稳定性。

Result: 获得了满足喉部存在、外扩条件和渐近平坦性的精确动力学解。零能量条件在喉部附近被违背，但违背程度随时间减小；奇异物体的体积积分在晚期趋于常数。在适当参数下，小扰动随时间衰减，系统保持线性稳定。径向能量流的物理来源可与零流体（null fluid）物质源对应。

Conclusion: 该模型描述了一个由能量输运控制演化的虫洞时空，并逐步过渡到静态构型，为广义相对论及扩展引力理论中更现实的动力学虫洞研究提供了简单且物理动机清晰的框架。与基于宇宙学尺度因子的传统方法形成互补，并指出了径向能量流可能的物质起源。

Abstract: We investigate a class of time-dependent traversable wormholes within the framework of general relativity by allowing the shape function to vary with time. In this setting, the evolution of the geometry is directly connected to a radial energy flux through the off-diagonal component of the Einstein field equations, providing a natural mechanism for non-static configurations. We obtain exact solutions in which the geometry consists of a static background supplemented by a transient term that diminishes with time. The resulting spacetime satisfies the standard conditions required for a traversable wormhole, including the presence of a throat, the flaring-out condition, and asymptotic flatness. An analysis of the energy conditions indicates that the null energy condition is violated in the vicinity of the throat, although the degree of violation decreases as the system evolves. This feature is examined further through a volume integral that measures the total amount of exotic matter, demonstrating that it approaches a constant value at late times. We also study the response of the system to small perturbations and find that, for a suitable choice of parameters, the configuration remains stable with perturbations decaying over time. We discuss how this flux-driven mechanism relates to the alternative and extensively studied approach in which wormhole evolution is instead carried by a cosmological scale factor, and we identify possible physical origins of the assumed radial flux in terms of null-fluid matter sources. Overall, the model describes a wormhole spacetime whose evolution is controlled by energy transport, leading to a gradual transition toward a static configuration. This framework offers a simple and physically motivated approach to dynamical wormholes and may be useful for exploring more realistic scenarios in both general relativity and extended theories of gravity.

### [33] [Where Thermodynamics Meets Geometry: Critical-Radius Coincidences in Confining-NED Black Holes with Barrow Entropy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04173)
*Erdem Sucu,İzzet Sakallı*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文研究爱因斯坦引力与非线性电动力学（含夸克-反夸克禁闭相互作用）耦合下的静态球对称黑洞。度量在Reissner-Nordström基础上增加由ζ控制的对数修正，通过Hamilton-Jacobi隧穿法得到Hawking温度，引入Barrow熵考虑量子引力涨落。核心发现是四重巧合：峰值Hawking温度、热容发散、Joule-Thomson反转与径向潮汐力零点均位于同一半径r₊处。EHT对Sgr A*的观测给出ζ≲0.7的约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将夸克-反夸克禁闭相互作用的非线性电动力学模型引入黑洞物理，探索禁闭项对黑洞热力学（thermodynamics）和几何结构（geometry）的影响，并借助Event Horizon Telescope（EHT）观测数据给出参数约束。

Method: 采用爱因斯坦引力耦合非线性电动力学（nonlinear electrodynamics）构造含对数修正的度量；利用Hamilton-Jacobi隧穿法（Hamilton-Jacobi tunneling method）计算Dirac费米子的Hawking温度；通过Barrow熵（Barrow entropy）引入量子引力涨落；在扩展相空间（extended phase space）中计算内能、自由能、压强、热容、等温压缩系数和Joule-Thomson系数。

Result: 热容给出依赖于变形指数Δ的稳定区域；等温压缩系数在整个分析域内为负，表明无van der Waals临界性的力学刚性相。核心结果为四重巧合：峰值Hawking温度、热容发散、Joule-Thomson反转与径向潮汐力零点均位于由A''(r₊)=0定义的同一半径r₊处；极值视界与角向潮汐力零点由A'(r_h)=0给出。EHT观测对Sgr A*给出ζ≲0.7（Q/M=0.5时）的约束。

Conclusion: 禁闭项对测地偏离（geodesic deviation）产生可观测修正；完整的临界点分析可简化为关于度量函数A(r)的两个标量方程；观测约束留出了一个有限参数窗口，值得进一步研究。

Abstract: We study a static, spherically symmetric black hole obtained from Einstein gravity coupled to a nonlinear electrodynamics model with a quark--antiquark confinement interaction. The metric extends Reissner--Nordström by a logarithmic correction controlled by $ζ$, modifying both horizon structure and the near-singularity regime. The Hamilton--Jacobi tunneling method for Dirac fermions yields the Hawking temperature; the $ζ$-dependent terms suppress the small-horizon divergence and signal a remnant. Quantum-gravitational fluctuations are incorporated through Barrow entropy with deformation index $Δ$. Within the extended phase space we compute the internal energy, free energy, pressure, heat capacity, isothermal compressibility, and Joule--Thomson coefficient. The heat capacity locates $Δ$-dependent stability regions; the compressibility stays negative across the domain analysed here, marking a mechanically rigid phase with no van der Waals criticality in this branch. The central result is a quadruple coincidence: the peak Hawking temperature, the heat-capacity divergence, the Joule--Thomson inversion, and the zero of the radial tidal force all sit at one radius $r_\star$ defined by $A''(r_\star)=0$, while the extremal horizon and the angular tidal-force zero coincide via $A'(r_h)=0$. These reduce the full critical-point analysis to two scalar equations on $A(r)$. Geometric tidal accelerations are mapped against the thermodynamic critical curves. Event Horizon Telescope observations of Sgr~A* translate into a constraint $ζ\lesssim 0.7$ at $Q/M=0.5$, leaving a finite window open. The confinement term induces observable corrections to geodesic deviation.

### [34] [Tests of general relativity using analytic derivatives of parametrized post-Einsteinian gravitational waveforms within the Fisher-matrix framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04238)
*Jie Wu,Mengfei Sun,Jin Li*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在参数化后爱因斯坦（parametrized post-Einsteinian）框架下，基于频域旋近波形推导了Fisher矩阵形式中的波形导数解析表达式，从而无需有限差分即可稳定高效地计算Fisher矩阵。将该方法应用于天基、地面及多波段引力波观测配置，并结合多种双黑洞族群模型，系统揭示了非广义相对论效应约束随后牛顿阶数、探测器类型和源族群变化的清晰趋势，并展示了不同探测器之间的互补性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超越广义相对论（general relativity, GR）的引力检验是探索强场高动力学区域基础物理的关键。现有Fisher矩阵计算依赖有限差分方案，存在数值系统误差和计算效率问题，亟需一种解析且稳定的方法以支持大规模参数研究。

Method: 在参数化后爱因斯坦（parametrized post-Einsteinian, ppE）框架下，利用频域旋近波形推导了波形导数的解析表达式，将其嵌入Fisher矩阵形式中，避免了有限差分数值方案。该方法适用于天基、地面及多波段探测器配置，并与不同双黑洞种群模型结合进行系统分析。

Result: 结果显示，非GR效应的约束能力随后牛顿（post-Newtonian, PN）阶数、探测器类型和源种群呈现清晰且系统的变化趋势。天基与地面探测器之间表现出互补性，尤其对于低频旋近阶段积累的效应。解析方法大幅降低了计算成本，并避免了步长选择带来的数值系统误差。

Conclusion: 该解析方法适合大规模参数研究，可为未来引力波观测约束非GR效应及环境影响的探测能力提供稳健预报，凸显了即将部署的探测器网络在精密引力检验中的科学潜力。

Abstract: Testing gravity beyond general relativity (GR) is essential for probing fundamental physics in the strong-field and highly dynamical regime accessed by gravitational-wave (GW) observations. In this work, we derive analytic expressions for waveform derivatives in the Fisher-matrix formalism within the parametrized post-Einsteinian framework, using the frequency-domain inspiral waveform. These analytic derivatives enable stable and efficient Fisher-matrix calculations without relying on finite-difference schemes. We apply this method to a wide range of detector configurations, including space-based, ground-based, and multiband observations, and combine it with different binary black hole population models. Our results reveal clear and systematic trends in the constraints on non-GR effects as functions of post-Newtonian order, detector type, and source population. They also demonstrate the complementarity between space- and ground-based detectors, particularly for effects that accumulate during the low-frequency inspiral. The analytic approach substantially reduces computational cost and avoids numerical systematics associated with step-size choices, making it well suited for large-scale parameter studies. These results provide robust forecasts for the capability of future GW observations to constrain a broad class of non-GR effects and environmental influences, highlighting the scientific potential of upcoming detector networks for precision tests of gravity.
