### [35] [Rigidity and the interpretation of mass with a positive cosmological constant](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04291)
*Eneko Aranguren,Raül Vera*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文针对正宇宙学常数Λ>0情形，构造了一族满足强能量条件和主能量条件的正则静态恒星解，其外部Schwarzschild-de Sitter区域的质量参数可正、可零、可负，从而否定了Λ=0时质量刚性定理（positive mass theorem）向Λ>0的直接推广。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验在正宇宙学常数Λ>0的条件下，质量参数是否仍具有Λ=0情形下由正质量定理（positive mass theorem）所保证的刚性（rigidity）性质，即外部真空区域不可与满足能量条件的规则完美流体区域共存于零质量构型中。

Method: 构造一族显式的正则静态球对称恒星构型（regular static stellar configurations），使其满足主能量条件（dominant energy condition）和强能量条件（strong energy condition），且不含表面层（surface layers）；外部分别对接Schwarzschild-de Sitter或de Sitter区域，通过调整内解参数实现质量参数的正、零、负取值。

Result: 成功构造出质量参数可正、可零、可负的静态解族；其中零质量情形对应的外部真空区恰好退化为de Sitter时空，使得de Sitter区域与规则完美流体共存，这与Λ=0情形下Minkowski区域无法与满足能量条件的完美流体区域共存形成鲜明对比。

Conclusion: 与Λ=0正质量定理相关联的静态球对称刚性原理（rigidity principle）在Λ>0时不再成立，正宇宙学常数从根本上改变了质量参数的刚性特征。

Abstract: We provide an explicit counterexample to the rigidity properties underlying the interpretation of mass in the presence of a positive cosmological constant $Λ$. Specifically, we construct a family of regular static stellar configurations satisfying the dominant and strong energy conditions, and containing no surface layers, for which the mass parameter of the outer Schwarzschild-de Sitter region can be positive, zero, or negative. The zero-mass configuration is precisely the one for which the outer vacuum region becomes exactly de Sitter, yielding a spacetime in which a de Sitter domain coexists with regular perfect-fluid matter. This contrasts sharply with the $Λ=0$ case, where a Minkowski domain cannot coexist with perfect-fluid regions satisfying the energy conditions. These results show that the static, spherically symmetric realization of the rigidity principle associated with the positive mass theorem for $Λ=0$ does not carry over to $Λ>0$.

</details>


### [36] [Complete Quantum Stress Tensor Inside a Four Dimensional Schwarzschild Black Hole: A Divergent Focusing Source](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04386)
*Shun Jiang,Jie Jiang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文首次计算了四维史瓦西黑洞内部无质量最小耦合标量场的完整重整化应力-能量张量（RSET），覆盖Unruh态与Hartle-Hawking态，从视界到接近时空类奇点（r/M≃10⁻⁴），同时获得了真空极化〈Φ²〉_ren，并发现主导紫外源是局部真空极化应力而非输运的霍金通量，该源在奇点附近满足零能量条件但违背主导能量条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 四维黑洞内部的完整重整化应力-能量张量（RSET）长期无法获得，导致半经典反作用所需的局部源项未知，尤其是在类空奇点（spacelike singularity）附近这一空白更为突出。本文以史瓦西（Schwarzschild）黑洞内部为具体实例，首次填补了这两个空白。

Method: 采用角分裂重整化方案（angular-splitting renormalization scheme）结合高阶大ℓ渐近减除（high-order large-ℓ asymptotic subtraction），计算了从事件视界（event horizon）到r/M≃10⁻⁴范围内⟨T^a_b⟩_ren的所有独立分量，并同时获得了相应的真空极化〈Φ²〉_ren。

Result: 张量通过了协变守恒（covariant conservation）和迹恒等式（trace identity）的交叉检验。在类空奇点附近，Unruh态与Hartle-Hawking态趋近同一守恒标度解，且Unruh通量相对于对角混合分量被(r/M)^4抑制。主导紫外源是局部真空极化应力（vacuum-polarization stress）而非输运的霍金通量。极限张量违背主导能量条件（dominant energy condition）但满足零能量条件（null energy condition）。

Conclusion: 在固定背景史瓦西RSET层面，半经典主导源并不支持量子去聚焦（quantum defocusing）平滑奇点的直观认识，反而在局部Raychaudhuri方程中提供了发散的聚焦源。然而，要获得真正的全局结论，需要求解反作用后的半经典几何（semiclassical geometry）。

Abstract: We compute the complete renormalized stress-energy tensor (RSET) of a massless minimally coupled scalar field throughout the interior of a four-dimensional Schwarzschild black hole, in both the Unruh and Hartle--Hawking states. The complete RSET inside four-dimensional black holes has long been unavailable, leaving the local source term required for semiclassical backreaction unknown. This gap is even sharper near spacelike singularities. Taking the Schwarzschild interior as a concrete example, we close both gaps for the first time. Using an angular-splitting renormalization scheme together with a high-order large-$\ell$ asymptotic subtraction, we determine all independent components of $\langle T^a{}_{b}\rangle_{\rm ren}$ from the event horizon down to $r/M\simeq10^{-4}$, and simultaneously obtain the corresponding vacuum polarization $\langleΦ^2\rangle_{\rm ren}$. The tensor passes the cross-checks of the covariant conservation and the trace identity. Near the spacelike singularity, the Unruh and Hartle--Hawking states approach the same conserved scaling solution, \ba M^4\langle T^a{}_{b}\rangle_{\rm ren} \simeq \left(\frac{r}{M}\right)^{-6}τ^a{}_{b},\nn \ea while the state-dependent Unruh flux is suppressed by $(r/M)^4$ relative to the diagonal mixed components. The leading ultraviolet source is therefore a local vacuum-polarization stress rather than transported Hawking flux. The limiting tensor violates the dominant energy condition but satisfy the null energy condition. Thus, at the level of the complete fixed-background Schwarzschild RSET, the leading semiclassical source does not support the intuition that quantum defocusing smooths the singularity; instead, it supplies a divergent focusing source in the local Raychaudhuri equation. A genuine global conclusion, however, requires solving the backreacted semiclassical geometry.

Abstract: Modified theories of gravity based on the symmetric teleparallel framework have recently attracted considerable attention as viable alternatives to General Relativity. In this context, f(Q) gravity, in which the gravitational interaction is encoded in the nonmetricity scalar Q, provides a consistent geometrical formulation that differs from the standard curvature-based description. In this work, we investigate the structure of neutron stars within a family of f(Q) gravity models by employing realistic equations of state, namely FPS, SLy, ENG and MPA1. Using the covariant formulation of f(Q) gravity, we derive the corresponding Tolman-Oppenheimer-Volkoff equations and apply them to model compact stellar configurations. Numerical integration of the field equations provides the mass-radius relations and the maximum masses supported by each equation of state, enabling a direct comparison with current observational constraints. Furthermore, we analyze the behavior of the nonmetricity scalar both inside and outside the stellar object, providing additional insight into the gravitational structure of compact stars in this framework.

### [38] [Beyond the Bounce: Multiple Tidal Sign Reversals and Turning-Point Bifurcations in Multi-Horizon Black Holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04642)
*Mohammad Ali S. Afshar,J. Sadeghi*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了爱因斯坦引力耦合非线性电动力学（NED）下的多视界黑洞解中中性测试粒子的径向运动与潮汐力，发现NED场导致径向和角向潮汐力分量出现多次零交叉，从而在拉伸和压缩潮汐区域之间产生连续转变；径向运动方程中存在由反弹点（bounce-back points）界定的经典禁戒区域，阻止粒子进入潮汐力发散的区域；在超极端条件下，禁戒区域可能延伸至事件视界之外，阻止远方静止释放的粒子穿越视界。此外，研究还识别出与潮汐力零交叉、额外视界及反弹点出现相关的临界电荷值满足层级次序，表明潮汐力结构的变化先于视界构型的相应改变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非线性电动力学（NED）对多视界黑洞时空结构及粒子动力学的影响尚未被充分理解，特别是NED如何修正经典史瓦西（Schwarzschild）和赖斯纳-诺德斯特洛姆（Reissner-Nordstrom, R-N）时空中的径向测地运动和潮汐力分布，是本研究关注的核心问题。

Method: 研究聚焦于三视界和四视界黑洞构型，通过分析非线性电动力学修正下的径向运动方程和潮汐力分量（径向与角向）的零交叉行为，并与经典Schwarzschild和R-N时空进行对比，系统考察NED对因果结构、径向测地运动及潮汐力剖面的影响。

Result: NED场导致径向和角向潮汐力分量出现多次零交叉，引起拉伸与压缩潮汐区域间的连续转变。径向运动方程中存在由反弹点界定的经典禁戒区域，阻止粒子进入潮汐力发散区域；在超极端（super-extremal）条件下，该禁戒区域可能延伸至事件视界之外，阻止远方静止释放的粒子穿越视界。与潮汐力零交叉、额外视界和反弹点相关的临界电荷值满足层级次序，且潮汐力结构的变化先于视界构型的改变。

Conclusion: 非线性电动力学能够通过禁戒区域、多重潮汐转变和视界结构变化的联合效应，实质性地修正多视界黑洞时空中性粒子的经典动力学行为。

Abstract: We investigate the radial motion and tidal forces experienced by neutral test particles in multi-horizon black hole solutions arising from Einstein gravity coupled to nonlinear electrodynamics (NED). Focusing on the three- and four-horizon configurations, we examine how nonlinear electromagnetic corrections modify the causal structure, radial geodesic motion, and tidal-force profiles in comparison with the Schwarzschild and Reissner-Nordstrom (R-N) spacetimes.
  Our analysis shows that the NED field gives rise to multiple zero crossings in both the radial and angular tidal-force components, leading to successive transitions between stretching and compressive tidal regimes. More importantly, the radial equation of motion contains classically forbidden regions bounded by bounce-back points. For the class of trajectories considered in this work, these forbidden regions prevent particles from entering the spacetime domain where the tidal forces become divergent. In the super-extremal regime admitted by these solutions, the forbidden region may extend beyond the event horizon, preventing particles released from rest at sufficiently large distances from crossing the horizon.
  We further identify a systematic ordering of the critical charge values associated with the appearance of tidal-force zero crossings, additional horizons, and bounce-back points. For both the three- and four-horizon configurations, these critical values satisfy a hierarchical ordering, indicating that changes in the tidal-force structure precede the corresponding modifications of the horizon configuration.
  These results demonstrate that nonlinear electrodynamics can substantially modify the classical dynamics of neutral particles in multi-horizon black hole spacetimes through the combined effects of forbidden regions, multiple tidal transitions, and changes in the horizon structure.

### [39] [Constraining inflationary models via de-Sitterization of Bianchi Cosmologies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04701)
*Apurba Samanta,Rahul Kothari*

Main category: gr-qc

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 本文针对比安奇宇宙（Bianchi Universe）模型，引入一个具有一般势（general potential）的均匀暴胀场（inflaton field），并设定该场需满足的特定判据。通过理论分析证明在该判据下，无需引入宇宙学常数即可实现德西特化（de Sitterization）。进一步将该判据应用于约束暴胀模型（inflation models），并给出具体示例进行说明。

Result: 结果表明，对于比安奇宇宙（Bianchi Universe），一个满足特定判据的均匀暴胀场（inflaton field）足以实现德西特化（de Sitterization），即从各向异性初始几何演化到各向同性的最终状态，且该过程不依赖宇宙学常数。此外，该判据可用于约束具体的暴胀模型（inflation models）。

Conclusion: 比安奇宇宙（Bianchi Universe）的德西特化（de Sitterization）可以在没有宇宙学常数的条件下，仅通过满足特定判据的均匀暴胀场（inflaton field）实现。这一发现不仅拓展了实现宇宙各向同性的理论路径，还提供了一种约束暴胀模型（inflation models）的新判据。

Abstract: Our Universe is isotropic and homogeneous when we observe it on $\gtrsim$ Mpc length scales. It is desirable that present state of the Universe has no dependence on its initial geometry. In case of Bianchi Universes, i.e., anisotropic but homogeneous Universe, this has already been demonstrated via cosmological constant in a process that we call \textit{de Sitterization}. In this letter, we show that for Bianchi Universe, the same state can be achieved by a homogeneous inflaton field with a general potential and satisfying a criterion without the need of a cosmological constant. More importantly, we show that the same condition can constrain models of inflation and explain our idea with examples.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在R平方f(R)引力（$f(R)=R+aR^{2}$，其中$a$是控制标量自由度有效质量尺度的正参数）框架下构建静态和均匀旋转的费米子-玻色子星模型。费米子部分采用零温表格化状态方程（tabulated equation of state）的理想流体描述，玻色子部分由自相互作用复玻色子场表示。

Abstract: Fermion-boson stars are compact equilibrium configurations composed of ordinary fermionic matter and a bosonic dark component interacting only through gravity. We construct static and uniformly rotating fermion-boson stars within the framework of $R$-squared $f(R)$ gravity, characterized by the functional form $f(R)=R+aR^{2}$, where $a$ is a positive parameter governing the effective mass scale from the scalar degree of freedom. The fermionic sector is modeled as a perfect fluid described by a tabulated equation of state at zero temperature, while the bosonic component is represented by a self-interacting complex bosonic field. Our results show that the scalar degree of freedom modifies the spatial distribution of both the bosonic field and the fermionic pressure, enlarges the domain of admissible equilibrium solutions, and increases the maximum supported masses relative to general relativity. Our models remain compatible with current astrophysical and gravitational-wave constraints, suggesting that fermion-boson stars in $R$-squared gravity offer a promising framework to investigate the combined effects of dark bosonic matter, rotation, and strong-field modifications of gravity in compact objects.

### [41] [Measurability of Quadrupole Deviations from Kerr in Binary black hole Mergers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04762)
*Song Li,Wen-Biao Han*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文利用超越广义相对论的全波形模型Ψ_FD，对LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA合作组观测到的五个双黑洞并合事件的黑洞四极矩与Kerr黑洞的偏差进行了可测量性研究。高信噪比事件GW230814和GW250114的结果与Kerr预言一致，未发现对无毛定理（no-hair theorem）的可观测偏离。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用超越广义相对论的全波形模型Ψ_FD，对五个双黑洞并合事件（含GWTC-4新增的高信噪比事件GW231226、GW230814和GW250114）进行贝叶斯参数估计。分别执行全波形（full-waveform）、旋近（inspiral）和旋近后（post-inspiral）三段分析，以获取四极矩偏差后验分布。

Result: 早先低信噪比事件轻微倾向于非零四极矩偏差，但新加入的高信噪比事件GW231226、GW230814和GW250114的结果与Kerr预言（ΔQ/Q=0）日趋一致。其中最高信噪比的两个事件GW230814和GW250114的四极矩偏差与零在误差范围内一致；其全波形、旋近与旋近后分析的后验分布均集中于ΔQ/Q≈0附近。

Abstract: We investigate the measurability of black hole quadrupole deviations from Kerr using five binary black hole mergers observed by the LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA Collaboration with the beyond-general-relativity full-waveform model $Ψ_{\mathrm{FD}}$. While earlier lower-SNR events mildly favored nonzero quadrupole deviations, the newly included high-SNR GWTC-4 events GW231226, GW230814, and GW250114 yield results increasingly consistent with the Kerr prediction. In particular, GW230814 and GW250114, the two highest-SNR events in our sample, yield deviations consistent with zero. We further perform separate inspiral and post-inspiral analyses and find both the posterior distributions centered close to $ΔQ/Q=0$ for GW230814 and GW250114. Overall, the full-waveform, inspiral, and post-inspiral results for GW230814 and GW250114 reveal no observable departure from the no-hair theorem within the sensitivity of the current data and the $Ψ_{\mathrm{FD}}$ framework. Although the limited number of events prevents a definitive conclusion, future detections of additional high-SNR binary black hole mergers will enable increasingly stringent and robust tests of the Kerr nature of black holes.

### [42] [Chaotic particle dynamics near a traversable wormhole throat](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04799)
*Xin Zhao,Xing-Kun Zhang,Ya-Peng Hu,Yu-Sen An*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究可穿越虫洞（traversable wormhole）喉部附近测试粒子在外界简谐势（harmonic potential）作用下的非线性动力学。一维径向微扰分析表明粒子在平衡位置局部线性稳定，但在二维和高能情况下系统呈现非线性响应并引发大尺度混沌。当粒子被限制在虫洞一侧时，庞加莱截面（Poincare section）在极高能量下仍保留KAM环面（KAM tori），这与黑洞事件视界（event horizon）导致的混沌不同。通过另一组形状函数验证了该相空间结构的普适性，为基于混沌动力学识别强场天体物理中的黑洞模拟体（black hole mimickers）提供了新判据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索可穿越虫洞这一理论天体在强引力场中的非线性动力学行为，揭示其与黑洞在动力学机制上的差异，为区分黑洞与虫洞提供新的理论判据。

Method: 采用测试粒子在虫洞喉部附近受外界简谐势影响的动力学模型，分别进行一维径向微扰分析和二维高能情形下的数值模拟，通过庞加莱截面分析相空间结构，并更换形状函数验证结果的普适性。

Result: 一维情形下粒子在平衡位置局部线性稳定；二维高能情形下系统呈现非线性响应并产生大尺度混沌。粒子被限制在虫洞一侧时，极高能量下庞加莱截面仍保留KAM环面，与黑洞事件视界导致的混沌行为截然不同，且该相空间结构在不同形状函数下具有普适性。

Conclusion: 该研究阐明了可穿越虫洞独特的非线性动力学机制，基于混沌动力学（chaotic dynamics）提出了识别黑洞模拟体的新判据，为强场天体物理观测中的天体辨识提供了理论依据。

Abstract: This study investigates the nonlinear dynamics of a test particle near the traversable wormhole throat under an external harmonic potential. One-dimensional radial perturbation analysis shows that the particle is locally linearly stable at the equilibrium position. However, for two-dimensional and high-energy cases, the system exhibits a nonlinear response, leading to large-scale chaos. The analysis indicates that, if the particle is confined on one side of the wormhole, the Poincare section will still retain Kolmogorov-Arnold-Moser (KAM) tori under extremely high-energy conditions, which is distinct from the chaos caused by the event horizon in the black hole. By studying another set of shape functions, the universality of this phase space structure is confirmed. This research clarifies the unique nonlinear dynamical mechanism of a traversable wormhole. It provides a new criterion, based on chaotic dynamics, for identifying black hole mimickers in strong-field astrophysical observations.

</details>


### [43] [A stepping stone toward detecting gravitational wave memory: a cumulative analysis with the full $(\ell=2, m=0)$ spherical harmonic using events from GWTC-4.0 and GWTC-5.0](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04909)
*Maria Rosselló-Sastre,Sascha Husa,Yumeng Xu,Jorge Valencia,Joan Llobera-Querol,Antoni Ramos-Buades*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文使用贝叶斯模型选择（Bayesian model selection）方法，检验引力波事件中是否存在 (ℓ=2,m=0) 球谐模态（spherical harmonic mode）。基于IMRPhenomTHM_20波形模型，对GWTC-4.0和GWTC-5.0目录中的双黑洞（binary black hole）信号进行分析，发现累积对数贝叶斯因子（log₁₀ℬ）=1.38±0.79支持该模态的存在，并评估了未来检测引力波记忆（gravitational wave memory）的前景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究已将多个引力波事件识别为双黑洞并合，但对(ℓ=2,m=0)模态（包含振荡分量和位移记忆分量）的系统性贝叶斯检验尚不充分。本文旨在填补这一空白，为最终检测引力波记忆提供自然的过渡步骤。

Method: 采用贝叶斯模型选择（Bayesian model selection）方法，使用准圆形、无进动的IMRPhenomTHM_20波形模型作为信号模型，该模型包含(2,0)模态的振荡贡献和位移记忆贡献。对GWTC-4.0目录中的所有双黑洞信号以及选定的GWTC-5.0事件进行分析，并针对进动候选事件GW241127_061008使用包含进动的IMRPhenomTPHM_20模型进行额外检验。

Result: 对于GWTC-4.0目录，累积对数贝叶斯因子为log₁₀ℬ=1.38±0.79，支持(2,0)模态的存在。包含振荡分量后，该模态的信噪比（signal-to-noise ratio, SNR）和证据均高于仅检验引力波记忆的情形。经过约7.5个月的O4a观测，记忆信噪比达SNR_memory=0.89⁺⁰·²⁹₋₀·₁₁。对GW241127_061008的分析未发现进动模型下(2,0)模态的额外证据。乐观估计需要约N_events=166⁺⁸²₋₅₅个事件才能获得决定性统计证据。

Conclusion: 当前引力波数据为(2,0)模态提供了初步但非决定性的观测支持。获得决定性统计证据需要更大的事件目录和更全面的波形系统误差研究（waveform systematics study）。本文结果为未来检测引力波记忆提供了量化评估和前景展望。

Abstract: We perform Bayesian model selection to test for the presence of the $(\ell=2,m=0)$ spherical harmonic mode in gravitational wave events that have previously been identified as binary black hole mergers. As our signal model we use the quasi-circular, non-precessing IMRPhenomTHM_20 waveform model, which includes the oscillatory and displacement memory contributions. Including the oscillatory component of the (2,0) mode increases the signal-to-noise ratio and evidence for this mode, compared to testing only for the presence of gravitational wave memory. Our analysis thus constitutes a natural stepping stone toward detecting gravitational wave memory. We perform our analysis for the binary black hole signals identified in the GWTC-4.0 catalog, and for selected GWTC-5.0 events. In our Bayesian model comparison we find a cumulative $\log_{10}\mathcal{B}=1.38\pm0.79$ in favor of the presence of the (2,0) mode for the GWTC-4.0 catalog. We also stack the signal-to-noise ratio of the full (2,0) mode and of its individual contributions, obtaining results consistent with previous studies and reaching $\mathrm{SNR}_{\mathrm{memory}} = 0.89^{+0.29}_{-0.11}$ after approximately 7.5 months of O4a observations. In addition, we study the precessing candidate GW241127_061008, and find no additional evidence for the (2,0) mode when precession is included in IMRPhenomTPHM_20. Overall, our results provide an assessment of the observational support for the (2,0) mode in current gravitational wave data and allow us to discuss prospects for its future detection. We find that decisive statistical evidence will likely require a larger catalog, with an optimistic estimated number of events of $N_{\mathrm{events}} = 166^{+82}_{-55}$, based on the specific assumptions adopted in this work. We also expect that decisive evidence will require a more extensive waveform systematics study.

</details>


### [44] [Emergent cosmology and gravity from quantum time?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05020)
*Ovidiu Cristinel Stoica*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出，通过将量子态平方振幅解释为内禀时间（intrinsic time）的概率密度，可以从平稳量子态（stationary quantum states）的宏观可观测量（macroscopic observables）中恢复出内禀动力学，并自然地涌现出曲率（curvature），无需预设引力理论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索宏观可观测量如何从平稳量子态中恢复内在动力学，并检验曲率是否可以从内禀时间视角自然涌现，从而为引力的涌现提供新的理论可能性。

Method: 将波函数的平方振幅（squared amplitude）解释为内禀时间各确定值的概率密度，从而在时间方向上诱导出曲率；若不存在唯一的时间方向，则曲率在所有时空维度中从平稳波函数的可变振幅中涌现。

Result: 从四维欧几里得空间（four-dimensional Euclidean space）中的球对称平稳解中，无需预设引力即可涌现出弗里德曼-勒梅特-罗伯逊-沃克（Friedmann-Lemaître-Robertson-Walker, FLRW）宇宙学模型。若时间方向不唯一，曲率在所有时空维度中均从波函数振幅中涌现。

Conclusion: 该发现为广义相对论（general relativity）或其修正理论从内禀时间可观测量（intrinsic time observables）中涌现提供了新的可能性。

Abstract: Macroscopic observables allow the recovery of intrinsic dynamics from stationary quantum states. I show that, by interpreting the squared amplitude as the probability density for each definite value of intrinsic time, a curvature emerges in the time direction. For example, from the perspective of intrinsic quantum time, the Friedmann-Lemaître-Robertson-Walker cosmological model emerges from spherically symmetric stationary solutions in four-dimensional Euclidean space, without presupposing gravity. If there is no unique direction of time, curvature emerges in all spacetime dimensions, without presupposing gravity, from the variable amplitude of the stationary wavefunction alone. This opens a new possibility that general relativity or some modification of it emerges from intrinsic time observables.

</details>


### [45] [Leading weak-field magnetic corrections to charged scalar quasinormal modes of Kerr black holes in the Melvin--Kerr geometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05074)
*Haryanto M. Siahaan*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在梅尔文-克尔（Melvin–Kerr）几何中计算了弱外部磁场对克尔黑洞带电标量拟正规模（quasinormal mode, QNM）谱的领头阶磁修正。在O(bq)截断下，带电克莱因-戈登方程可分离，径向问题通过有效质量替换化为有质量标量克尔形式。磁修正完全由该替换传递，表现为不同自转扇区复数频率实部的线性移动，符号与|m|相关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有研究广泛探讨了无磁场克尔黑洞的拟正规模，但实际天体物理环境中黑洞常处于外部磁场中。本文旨在定量计算弱磁场对克尔黑洞带电标量扰动QNM谱的领头阶修正，并揭示其物理机制。

Method: 采用梅尔文-克尔度规描述带磁场黑洞；选择规范使电磁势时间分量在大半径处为零；在O(bq)截断下分离带电克莱因-戈登方程；通过有效质量替换μeff²≡μ²+2qbm将径向问题映射为有质量标量克尔形式；采用参数形变的Dolan连分数格式求解；设置中间克尔区域(r+≪r≪b⁻¹)的外向边界条件。

Result: 无磁场骨干在a≤0.5M下以10⁻⁶精度复现Dolan的表格谱。对于ℓ=1、μM∈{0,0.3}、a/M∈{0.3,0.5}、qM=0.1、bM≤10⁻²，频率实部Re(Mω)的磁偏移在两个自转扇区符号相反：m=+1向上、m=-1向下，且与qb成线性关系。偏移大小可由无磁场斜率∂Re(Mω)/∂(μM)²定量复现。ℓ=2的结果确认了该图像。

Conclusion: 弱磁场对克尔黑洞QNM的领头阶磁修正完全通过有效质量替换μeff²≡μ²+2qbm传递，不产生额外的有限半径修正。磁偏移的大小和符号随自转扇区变化，可由无磁场下关于质量平方的导数定量解释。由于梅尔文-克尔时空渐近非平坦，所得谱并非完整磁化时空的全局QNM，而是克尔振铃模式在弱场下的偏离。

Abstract: We compute the leading magnetic corrections to the charged-scalar quasinormal-mode (QNM) spectrum of a Kerr black hole immersed in a weak external magnetic field, working in the Melvin--Kerr geometry and in the gauge in which the time component of the electromagnetic potential vanishes at large radius. Within the controlled $\mathcal{O}(bq)$ truncation, the charged Klein--Gordon equation separates and the radial problem takes the massive-scalar Kerr form under the effective-mass substitution $\mueff^{2}\equivμ^{2}+2qbm$, applied to the asymptotic mass exponent and to the spheroidicity parameter. This gives a parameter-deformed Dolan continued-fraction scheme, with no further finite-radius correction at the order retained. Since the Melvin--Kerr spacetime is not asymptotically flat, the resulting spectrum is not the exact global QNM spectrum of the full magnetized spacetime: the modes are weak-field deviations of Kerr ringdown modes, defined by outgoing boundary conditions in the intermediate Kerr-like region $r_{+}\ll r\ll b^{-1}$. The unmagnetized backbone reproduces Dolan's tabulated spectra at the $10^{-6}$ level for $a\le 0.5M$. For $\ell=1$, $μM\in\{0,0.3\}$, $a/M\in\{0.3,0.5\}$, $qM=0.1$, and $bM\le 10^{-2}$, the magnetic shift in $\Re(\Mw)$ is opposite in sign between the two rotating sectors of equal $|m|$: upward for $m=+1$, downward for $m=-1$, and linear in $qb$. The sign and sector-dependent magnitude of each shift are quantitatively reproduced by the unmagnetized slope $\partial\Re(\Mw)/\partial(μM)^{2}$ evaluated per sector, confirming that the magnetic effect is fully transmitted through the master substitution. Effective-potential diagnostics and an extension to $\ell=2$ confirm the picture.

</details>


### [46] [Structure of Anisotropic Magnetized Neutron Stars in f(R,T) Gravity with Realistic Equation of State](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05333)
*M. Savari,G. H. Bordbar,J. Sedaghat,A. Sheykhi*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在f(R,T)修正引力框架下，结合AV18核子-核子势导出的精确状态方程（EoS），研究了耦合参数、磁场及各向异性参数对中子星结构的影响。结果表明，该理论框架能够解释质量间隙（2.5–5 M☉）内的致密天体，其理论计算结果与LIGO/Virgo/KAGRA及NICER的观测数据（如GW170817、GW190814等）一致。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用基于AV18核子-核子势（nucleon-nucleon potential）的精确状态方程（EoS），在f(R,T)修正引力框架下计算中子星结构。通过求解史瓦西半径（Schwarzschild radius）、致密性（compactness）、引力红移（gravitational surface redshift）及Kretschmann标量（Kretschmann scalar），并与LIGO/Virgo/KAGRA及NICER的观测数据进行比较，从而约束理论参数。

Result: 在f(R,T)引力下，部分位于质量间隙内的致密天体可以被解释为中子星候选体。通过调节f(R,T)理论参数及各向异性参数，成功再现了GW170817、PSR J0952-0607和PSR J0740+6620的质量与半径，以及GW190814和GW200210-092254次级成分的质量。

Conclusion: f(R,T)修正引力框架下的理论结果与现有观测约束一致，表明该理论能够有效描述质量间隙中的致密天体，拓展了中子星模型的理论边界。

Abstract: In this study, within the framework of f(R,T) modified gravity, we investigate the influence of coupling parameter, magnetic field and anisotropy parameter on the neutron star structure. This work employs an accurate equation of state (EoS), derived from realistic microscopic calculations based on the AV18 nucleon-nucleon potential, to compute the structure of this compact object. Here, determination of Schwarzschild radius, compactness, gravitational surface redshift and Kretschmann scalar within the f(R, T) gravity, confirms that our theoretical results are consistent with the observational constraints. While established physical EoSs within the framework of Einstein gravity have successfully characterized a broad range of compact objects, they remain inadequate in explaining certain massive objects residing within the mass gap (2.5 to 5 Msun). We show that some compact objects residing in the mass gap interpreted as candidates of neutron stars within the framework of f(R, T) gravity. Finally, we compare our results with the observational data from LIGO/Virgo/KAGRA and NICER, setting the parameters of the f(R, T) theory and anisotropy to successfully reproduce the masses and radii of the GW170817, PSR J0952-0607 and PSR J0740+6620 and the masses of the secondary components of GW190814 and GW200210-092254.

### [47] [Neural-Network Inverse Design of SRF Cavities and Transmons for Bosonic Quantum Computation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02289)
*Joseph Yaker,Jovan Markovic,Alessandro Reineri,Doga Murat Kurkcuoglu,Silvia Zorzetti*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出两种深度神经网络（DNN）方法，分别用于三维超导射频（SRF）腔体和transmon量子比特的逆向设计，能够从目标器件行为直接生成候选几何设计，精度分别达到约5%（腔体）和约2%（transmon），是传统迭代仿真方法的高效替代方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 三维超导射频（SRF）腔体与transmon量子比特耦合的体系在玻色量子信息处理中具有重要应用前景，但其逆向设计（inverse design）是一个一对多（one-to-many）问题，且耦合强度对transmon几何结构及其在腔体电磁场中的位置极为敏感。随着系统规模扩大和设计参数空间增长，传统迭代仿真的计算成本变得难以承受。

Method: 采用两种深度神经网络（deep neural network, DNN）方法，分别处理设计堆栈（design stack）中不同层级的问题：第一种方法生成能够产生目标腔体观测量的SRF腔体几何结构；第二种方法生成能够产生目标量子比特-腔体参数——即耦合率（coupling rate, $g$）、量子比特频率（qubit frequency, $\nu_q$）和反非谐性（anharmonicity, $\alpha$）——的transmon量子比特设计。

Result: 通过端到端重仿真（end-to-end re-simulation）验证，第一种方法恢复的腔体候选设计与目标之间的匹配精度约为5%，第二种方法的transmon候选设计匹配精度约为2%。两种方法均能直接从目标器件行为映射到候选设计。

Conclusion: 这两种DNN方法为传统迭代仿真研究提供了一种快速替代方案，能够高效地将期望的器件行为直接映射为候选几何设计，适用于超导量子信息处理系统中日益复杂的设计需求。

Abstract: Three-dimensional superconducting radio-frequency (SRF) cavities provide exceptionally long-lived electromagnetic modes and, when coupled to nonlinear elements such as transmon qubits, become promising architectures for bosonic quantum information processing. The inverse design of such systems, i.e., recovering device geometries that produce specified electromagnetic and coupling targets, is generally a one-to-many problem. The qubit-cavity coupling strength depends sensitively on both the transmon geometry and its position within the cavity's electromagnetic field. As these systems scale up and their design parameter spaces grow, the cost of conventional iterative simulation becomes prohibitive. We present two deep neural network (DNN) approaches that address this inverse-design problem at complementary levels of the design stack. The first proposes SRF cavity geometries that produce target cavity observables. The second proposes transmon qubit designs that produce target qubit-cavity parameters -- the coupling rate, qubit frequency, and anharmonicity $(g, ν_q, α)$. The recovered candidate designs match the targets to within $\sim$5\% (cavity) and $\sim$2\% (transmon), confirmed by end-to-end re-simulation. Both approaches map desired device behavior directly to candidate designs, a fast alternative to the iterative simulation studies usually required.

</details>


### [48] [Krylov-Lie Algebras for Variational Quantum Algorithms: Geometric, Depth-Aware Insights into Expressivity and Trainability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02626)
*Anžej Margeta-Cacace*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文引入Krylov代数（Krylov algebras）作为变分量子算法（VQA）损失景观理论的新框架，在有限深度几何下更准确地描述可达流形，推导出加权非Haar方差公式，并表明非Haar贡献可能缓解贫瘠高原（barren plateaus）问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于动态李代数（dynamical Lie algebras）、Jordan代数Wishart系统、近似t-designs和Haar随机电路的景观理论忽略了真实ansätze的有限深度几何（finite-depth geometry），在浅层区域（shallow-depth regime）适用性不足，而该区域VQA的训练可行性最高。

Method: 提出Krylov代数的概念，即由有限生成子集作用于一个或多个种子向量（seed vectors）所生成的Krylov张成空间（Krylov span）诱导出的代数结构；利用Krylov-Lie代数和群对VQA可达流形进行数值稳健且几何保真的近似，并推导出规范不变测度（canonical invariant measures）来计算期望值和方差。

Result: 推导出加权非Haar方差公式，该公式以通常的Lie代数Haar公式为特例，并将非Haar效应分离为显式修正项；证明“足够深的电路ensemble必然收敛到Haar”这一启发式论断在缺乏额外假设时一般不成立，并识别出具体的障碍；在自然且必要的遍历性条件下恢复了收敛性。

Conclusion: 非Haar贡献通过重新加权损失景观的可见扇区（visible sectors）可能缓解贫瘠高原，暗示VQA的可训练性可能优于近期文献的普遍预期。

Abstract: Variational quantum algorithms (VQAs) are a leading approach to near-term quantum computation, but their utility is limited by barren plateaus and other pathologies in their loss landscapes. Existing landscape theories based on dynamical Lie algebras, Jordan-algebraic Wishart systems, approximate t-designs, and Haar-random circuits are foundational, but they often neglect the finite-depth geometry of realistic ansätze and are therefore poorly suited to the shallow-depth regime, where VQAs are poor approximators of 2-designs and trainability is most feasible. This thesis introduces Krylov algebras, algebraic structures induced by the Krylov span of a finite generator set acting on one or more seed vectors, as a framework for VQA landscape theory. We show that VQA reachable manifolds can be approximated in a numerically robust, geometrically faithful way by Krylov-Lie algebras and groups, and that these structures induce canonical invariant measures for computing expectation values and variances under general sampling measures. In particular, we derive weighted non-Haar variance formulas that recover the usual Lie-algebraic Haar formulas as a special case while isolating non-Haar effects into explicit correction terms. We also show that the common heuristic that sufficiently deep circuit ensembles must converge to Haar fails in general without additional hypotheses, identify concrete obstructions to naive Haar convergence, and recover convergence under natural necessary and sufficient ergodic conditions. Lastly, our formulas further imply that non-Haar contributions may mitigate barren plateaus by reweighting the visible sectors of the loss landscape, suggesting that VQAs may be more trainable than recent literature has posited.

</details>


### [49] [Encoding matroids into quantum states](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02736)
*Nathan Ferreira,Alison A. Silva,Giuliano G. La Guardia,Fabiano M. Andrade*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文基于图态（graph states）和超图态（hypergraph states）的公理化框架，引入了一类新的多体量子态——拟阵态（matroid states），建立了基于电路和独立集两种构造方式，并揭示了图态、拟阵态与超图态之间的层级关系，表明拟阵论可作为描述多体量子态的天然组合语言。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多体量子态的高效表示是量子信息论中的基础问题，而现有图态与超图态的公理化构造已展现出在刻画纠缠方面的价值。本文旨在将这一公理化方法推广到更一般的组合结构——拟阵（matroid），从而拓展多体量子态的描述框架。

Method: 本文提出两种拟阵态的构造方式：第一种基于拟阵的电路（circuits）定义，第二种基于独立集（independent sets）定义。两种方法均引入满足局域性（locality）、对称性（symmetry）和交换性（commutativity）的全局算子，这些算子与拟阵的组合结构相关联。

Result: 建立了图态、拟阵态与超图态之间的层级关系，证明任意图态可通过施加合适的拟阵态族获得，且这些拟阵态对应的算子是图态稳定子群（stabilizer subgroup）的生成元。

Conclusion: 拟阵论为多体量子态的高效描述提供了一种自然的组合语言，为量子纠缠及相关组合结构的研究开辟了新视角。

Abstract: Efficient representations of multipartite quantum states play a fundamental role in quantum information theory, providing both conceptual insight and practical tools for characterizing entanglement. Motivated by the axiomatic framework for graph states [Phys. Rev. A 85, 062313 (2012)] and its subsequent extension to hypergraph states [Phys. Rev. A 87, 022311 (2013)], we introduce an axiomatic construction of \emph{matroid states}, a new family of multipartite quantum states associated with matroids. Our constructions are based on a set of axioms analogous to those that define graph and hypergraph states, yielding a consistent quantum representation of arbitrary matroids. Two ways of constructing matroid states are proposed: the first is defined in terms of circuits, and the second in terms of independent sets. In both approaches, we establish the existence of universal global operators that satisfy desirable properties such as locality, symmetry, commutativity, and are associated with the combinatorial structure of matroids. Furthermore, we establish a hierarchy connecting graph, matroid, and hypergraph states within a unified framework. Additionally, we show how to obtain an arbitrary graph state by applying suitable families of matroid states, whose corresponding operators are the generators of the stabilizer subgroup of the graph state. These results identify matroid theory as a natural combinatorial language for the efficient description of multipartite quantum states and open new perspectives for the investigation of quantum entanglement and related combinatorial structures.

</details>


### [50] [Superposed circular motion Unruh effect in (3+1) dimensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03468)

Result: 在四种几何场景中：(a) 同心垂直叠放轨迹中，探测器响应与单一圆形轨迹的近似热响应仅存在微小偏差；(b) 共面水平偏移轨迹；(c) 静态中心点与周围圆形轨迹中，有效温度显著降低且随能隙（energy gap）变化更大；(d) 同心共面圆形轨迹中呈现上述两类特征。

Abstract: Using a recently-introduced quantum control model for Unruh-DeWitt detectors in superpositions of classical trajectories, we investigate the response of a detector interacting with a massless scalar quantum field in (3+1) dimensions along a superposition of circular trajectories. We present numerical results for the transition probability and effective temperature of such a detector in four distinct geometric scenarios: (a) concentric, vertically-stacked trajectories, (b) planar, horizontally-displaced trajectories, (c) static central point and surrounding circular trajectory, and (d) concentric, planar circular trajectories. For Gaussian switching functions that are much broader than the acceleration timescale, in case (a) we find only minor deviations from the well-known, effectively thermal response of a single circular trajectory, whereas in case (c) we find a significant reduction in the effective temperature and greater variation with energy gap. We conclude with a discussion of a potential analogue implementation in ultracold atom systems.

### [51] [Driving collective RPA modes by a time-dependent Dyson map](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03493)
*Andreas Fring,Marta Reboiro*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了一个含时非厄米（non-Hermitian）的Schütte-Da Providência模型推广，利用含时Dyson映射构造厄米对应，通过随机相位近似（RPA）简化费米子部分，将动力学映射为两个含时谐振子支路，并分析了非绝热跃迁与参数共振行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将传统上描述玻色子模与集体粒子-空穴激发耦合的Schütte-Da Providência模型推广到含时非厄米情形，以探索非厄米动力学中集体激发与非绝热跃迁的物理机制。

Method: 采用含时Dyson映射（time-dependent Dyson map）构造非厄米模型的厄米对应；利用随机相位近似（RPA）约化集体费米子部分；在瞬时基下进行一阶含时微扰论计算，并与精确Lewis-Riesenfeld跃迁振幅进行对比。

Result: 动力学被映射为两个具有瞬时RPA频率 $W_\pm(t)$ 的含时谐振子分支；一阶微扰论中主导跃迁为 $n\to n+2$，振幅正比于 $\dot W_j/W_j$，表明其为纯非绝热效应；Dyson映射的不同分量提供不同驱动机制——标度参数调节有效耦合，压缩参数通过移动边界贡献起作用；两种机制均诱导出参量共振峰和边带结构。

Conclusion: 含时非厄米模型中，非绝热效应驱动集体跃迁，且Dyson映射的标度与压缩分量可作为独立的调控手段，产生参量共振及边带等可观测特征。

Abstract: We study a time-dependent non-Hermitian generalisation of the Schütte-Da~Providência model describing a bosonic mode coupled to collective particle-hole excitations. Using a time-dependent Dyson map, we construct a Hermitian counterpart and reduce the collective fermionic sector by means of the random phase approximation (RPA). The resulting dynamics is mapped to two time-dependent harmonic-oscillator branches with instantaneous RPA frequencies $W_\pm(t)$. We determine the corresponding stability regions and compute transition probabilities between instantaneous oscillator states. In first-order instantaneous-basis perturbation theory the leading transition $n\to n+2$ is proportional to $\dot W_j/W_j$, showing that it is purely nonadiabatic and absent in the time-independent case. We compare this result with exact Lewis-Riesenfeld transition amplitudes within the RPA approximation. Numerical examples show that different components of the Dyson map provide distinct driving mechanisms: the scaling parameter modulates the effective coupling, while the squeezing parameter acts through a moving-boundary contribution. In both cases the induced collective transitions exhibit parametric-resonance peaks and sideband structures.

### [52] [Algebra of quantum mechanics via classical phonons. I: The Schrodinger equation as the Newtonian equation of motion and quantum observables as classical averages](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03897)
*Emmanuel Giner*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过经典声子模型——Frenkel-Kontorova模型，形式化地推导出单粒子无自旋的薛定谔方程。从一维耦合谐振子晶格出发，在连续极限下得到实值场的Klein-Gordon方程；通过引入混合位移场和速度场的复变量变换，并分离快慢时间尺度，在非相对论极限下将Klein-Gordon方程改写为薛定谔方程。该复变换还可将总能量、动量等经典可观测量对应为量子可观测量。当模型中引入摩擦力时，对应的Klein-Gordon方程可改写为含非厄米哈密顿量的薛定谔方程。研究说明，量子代数和复值波函数可经由经典动力学精确重现，但仅限于非相对论框架，未涉及测量问题、量子化或相对论效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索经典声子模型能否在数学形式上严格导出量子力学的核心方程（薛定谔方程），从而揭示量子代数与复值波函数的经典根源。

Method: 基于一维耦合谐振子晶格的Frenkel-Kontorova模型，取连续极限得到实值场的Klein-Gordon方程；再引入混合位移场与速度场的复变量变换，并结合快慢时间尺度分离，在非相对论极限下将Klein-Gordon方程转化为薛定谔方程。

Result: 成功从经典声子模型形式化推导出单粒子无自旋薛定谔方程，且经典可观测量（总能量、动量）可通过复变换映射为量子可观测量。引入摩擦力后，可获得含非厄米哈密顿量的薛定谔方程。

Conclusion: 经典声子动力学可通过适当的复变量变换精确重现量子代数和复值波函数形式，但当前工作局限于非相对论、无自旋情形，未涵盖测量问题、量子化及相对论效应；相对论情形及对易子与泊松括号的联系将在后续工作中探讨。

Abstract: The Schrodinger equation for a single spinless particle is formally obtained via a classical phonon model, namely the Frenkel-Kontorova model. Starting from a one-dimensional lattice of coupled harmonic oscillators, we show that the continuous limit of the corresponding Newtonian equation of motion yields the Klein-Gordon equation for a real-valued field. By introducing a complex-valued change of variables mixing the real-valued displacement and velocity fields, and by separating fast and slow time scales, the Klein-Gordon equation is written as the Schrodinger equation within the non-relativistic limit. This complex change of variable also allows to rewrite classical global observables of the phonon field, such as the total energy or momentum, as the corresponding quantum observables. Additionally, we show that when a friction force is incorporated into the classical model, the corresponding Klein-Gordon equation can be rewritten as a Schrodinger equation with a non-Hermitian Hamiltonian. While the global approach is limited here to the non-relativistic regime and does not address the measurement problem, quantization or relativistic effects, it nonetheless illustrates how quantum algebra and complex-valued wave functions can be exactly reproduced using classical dynamics. The relativistic regime for a spinless particle and the link between commutators and Poisson brackets is addressed in the second part of this series.

### [53] [Algebra of quantum mechanics \textit{via} classical phonons. II: Klein-Gordon dynamics, the Heisenberg formalism, the Dirac canonical commutation rule and the Poincaré algebra through the continuous Poisson bracket formalism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03909)
*Emmanuel Giner*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文表明，通过经典哈密顿形式论（Hamiltonian formalism）应用于同一声子（phonon）模型，可以恢复无自旋单粒子的相对论性量子力学（relativistic quantum mechanics）特征，包括Klein-Gordon场、泊松括号（Poisson brackets）、海森堡形式论（Heisenberg formalism）与庞加莱群（Poincaré group）等结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在系列第一部分已基于牛顿运动方程从经典声子模型导出单粒子薛定谔方程（Schrödinger equation）与非相对论量子可观测量；本文进一步探索同一模型在经典哈密顿形式论下能否恢复相对论性量子力学的特征，从而将经典与相对论量子理论更紧密地联系起来。

Method: 基于经典声子模型，定义经典可观测量之间的连续泊松括号（continuous Poisson brackets），用以描述实值Klein-Gordon场的动力学（Ehrenfest关系）与运动常数；引入非局域复值变量变换（non-local complex-valued change of variables），将实值Klein-Gordon方程重写为类薛定谔方程形式，并将经典可观测量转化为量子期望值；进一步将经典泊松括号重写为厄米算符（hermitian operators）的对易子（commutators），建立经典泊松括号与海森堡形式论的严格等价性；最后利用泊松括号恢复1+1维庞加莱群变换及其代数。

Result: 建立了经典哈密顿形式论与相对论性量子力学（Klein-Gordon场）之间的严格对应关系：经典泊松括号等价于厄米算符的对易子；经典可观测量可表示为量子期望值；庞加莱群代数及其洛伦兹不变内积（Lorentz invariant inner product）与粒子质量的Casimir不变量（Casimir invariant）得以恢复。

Conclusion: 同一经典声子模型不仅可导出非相对论量子力学，亦可通过哈密顿形式论系统性地恢复无自旋粒子的相对论性量子力学结构，表明经典声子模型可作为统一描述非相对论与相对论量子现象的底层经典框架。

Abstract: In the first part of this series we have shown how the Schrodinger equation for a single particle and the corresponding non relativistic quantum observables can be obtained from a purely classical phonon model through the Newtonian equations of motion. In this work we focus instead on how the classical Hamiltonian formalism applied to the same phonon system allows to recover the feature of relativistic quantum mechanics for a single spinless particle. Using the classical nature of the phonon model, we naturally define continuous Poisson brackets between classical observables, which allows to recover the dynamics of such observables, i.e. the Ehrenfest relations associated to real-valued Klein-Gordon fields. The Poisson brackets also permits to obtain the generic form of constants of motions, thus generalizing the concept of inner products and momentum on Klein-Gordon fields. We then connect the formalism of real-valued classical functionals with that of hermitian operators and complex-valued wave functions. This is done through the introduction of a non-local complex-valued change of variables which allows to rewrite the real-valued Klein-Gordon equation in a form akin to the Schrodinger equation, and the classical observables as quantum expectation values. Then, we show how this change of variables allows to rewrite the classical Poisson brackets as commutators of hermitian operators. This points out the strict equivalence between the Heisenberg formalism and the formalism of classical Poisson bracket. Eventually, we illustrate how the Poisson brackets allows to recover the transformations of Poincaré group in 1+1 dimension together with its algebra. The latter makes the link between the Lorentz invariant inner product of Mostafazadeh and the Casimir invariant associated to the mass of particle.

### [54] [False vacuum decay in long-range interacting quantum systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03274)
*Valerio Pagni,Laura Batini,Nicolò Defenu*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文将混合场伊辛链（mixed-field Ising chain）中的假真空衰变（false-vacuum decay）建模为具有分数阶空间动能项 $\sim |q|^\sigma$ 的空间非局域欧几里得 $\phi^4$ 理论，其中 $\sigma = \alpha - 1$。研究表明，非局域反弹（bounce）解在时空上各向异性并产生代数尾部，改变了传统薄壁图像，且长程效应主要体现为亚主导修正项，对主导指数无影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解具有 $1/r^\alpha$ 长程相互作用的量子系统中的假真空衰变机制，特别是超越标准薄壁近似的非局域效应如何影响气泡 nucleation 和衰变寿命。

Method: 将问题映射为空间非局域欧几里得 $\phi^4$ 理论，其空间动能项为分数阶形式 $\sim |q|^\sigma$（$\sigma = \alpha - 1$）；结合薄壁论证（thin-wall arguments）与完整非局域鞍点方程（nonlocal saddle）的数值求解。

Result: 非局域反弹解在时空上各向异性，并发展出代数空间尾部（algebraic spatial tails）。对于 $0<\sigma<1$，寿命指数 $B \sim h^{-1/\sigma}$；对于 $1<\sigma<2$，主导项恢复 Coleman 标度 $B \sim h^{-1}$，长程效应体现在亚主导项 $\sim h^{\sigma-2}$ 中。

Conclusion: 可调长程相互作用从根本上重塑气泡 nucleation 过程，改变量子模拟器中的假真空衰变行为；代数尾部不改变主导薄壁指数，但通过亚主导修正项产生可观测效应。

Abstract: We formulate false-vacuum decay in a mixed-field Ising chain with $1/r^α$ interactions as a spatially nonlocal Euclidean $φ^4$ theory featuring a fractional spatial kinetic term $\sim |q|^σ$, where $σ=α-1$. The nonlocal bounce is anisotropic in space-time and develops algebraic spatial tails, challenging the standard thin-wall picture of a compact droplet. Combining thin-wall arguments with numerical solutions of the full nonlocal saddle, we show that these tails preserve the leading thin-wall exponents, manifesting instead in subleading corrections. For $0<σ<1$, the lifetime exponent scales with the energy bias $h$ of the metastable state as $B\sim h^{-1/σ}$; for $1<σ<2$, the leading Coleman scaling $B\sim h^{-1}$ is recovered, while long-range effects are retained in the subdominant term $\sim h^{σ-2}$. Our results show that tunable long-range interactions fundamentally reshape bubble nucleation and alter false-vacuum decay in quantum simulators.

### [55] [A Lie-Jordan Geometric Formulation of Lindblad Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04052)
*Leonel Bixano,Victor Alberto Cruz-Barriguete,Guillermo López-Alvarez,V. G. Ibarra-Sierra,José Luis Cardoso,Alejandro Kunold*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文基于李-乔丹几何（Lie-Jordan geometry）构建了有限维开放量子动力学的形式化框架。核心成果是识别出一个与基无关的三线性通用耗散映射（universal trilinear dissipative map），其分量仅由李-乔丹结构张量（Lie-Jordan structure tensors）决定。物理耗散子（physical dissipator）通过将该张量与林德布拉德算子（Lindblad operators）和科萨科夫斯基矩阵（Kossakowski matrix）的展开系数缩并得到，从而实现代数普适结构与模型依赖物理信息的分离。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有开放量子系统的超算子（superoperator）形式化缺乏一个与基无关且能够清晰分离代数结构与模型依赖信息的几何框架。本文旨在基于前期工作（arXiv:2606.26477）的代数框架，发展一种李-乔丹几何表述，从而以张量和仿射几何的语言统一刻画有限维开放量子动力学。

Method: 在希尔伯特-施密特算子空间（Hilbert-Schmidt operator space）中引入正交归一埃尔米特基（orthonormal Hermitian basis），利用结构张量 \(C_{μν}{}^λ\)（对易子）和 \(B_{μν}{}^λ\)（反对易子）编码李-乔丹代数结构。在此基础上构造了一个与基无关的三线性通用耗散映射 \(\mathcal D(X,Y)Z=XZY-\frac12\{YX,Z\}\)，其分量仅由结构张量决定。物理耗散子通过该通用张量与林德布拉德算子和科萨科夫斯基矩阵的展开系数缩并得到。此外，利用组合 \((B+C)\) 和 \((B-C)\) 生成内部左、右输运（left and right transports），将基本耗散映射表达为左-右双模作用（left-right bimodule action）加有序乔丹修正（ordered Jordan contribution）的形式。

Result: 通用耗散映射满足与基无关的迹保持（trace preservation）和埃尔米特共轭保持（Hermitian-conjugation preservation）恒等式，由此得出完整耗散子的迹保持性、埃尔米特性保持性以及在埃尔米特希尔伯特-施密特基中分量表示的实性。还推导了该映射的希尔伯特-施密特伴随（Hilbert-Schmidt adjoint），并针对具有纯退相（pure dephasing）和振幅阻尼（amplitude-damping）通道的量子比特（qubit）进行了实例展示。

Conclusion: 该构造为 arXiv:2606.26477 中导出的通用超算子结构提供了张量和仿射几何解释，同时保持代数部分与模型依赖部分的明确分离。这为有限维开放量子系统的形式化描述提供了一种兼具几何直观性和代数普遍性的框架。

Abstract: We develop a Lie-Jordan geometric formulation of finite-dimensional open quantum dynamics, building on the algebraic framework introduced in our previous work (arXiv:2606.26477). The Hilbert-Schmidt operator space is endowed with an orthonormal Hermitian basis, in which the commutator and anticommutator are encoded by the structure tensors \(C_{μν}{}^λ\) and \(B_{μν}{}^λ\). Within this formulation, the von Neumann and Gorini-Kossakowski-Lindblad-Sudarshan equations admit a direct component representation. Our central result is the identification of a basis-independent universal trilinear dissipative map, \( \mathcal D(X,Y)Z=XZY-\frac12\{YX,Z\}, \) whose components define a universal operator-space tensor depending only on the Lie-Jordan structure tensors. The physical dissipator is obtained by contracting this tensor with the expansion coefficients of the Lindblad operators and the Kossakowski matrix, thereby separating the universal algebraic structure from the model-dependent physical information. We further show that the combinations \((B+C)\) and \((B-C)\) generate internal left and right transports, allowing the elementary dissipative map to be expressed as a left-right bimodule action corrected by an ordered Jordan contribution. The universal map satisfies basis-independent trace and Hermitian-conjugation identities, from which trace preservation, Hermiticity preservation of the complete dissipator, and the reality of its component representation in a Hermitian Hilbert-Schmidt basis follow. We also derive its Hilbert-Schmidt adjoint and illustrate the formalism for a qubit with pure dephasing and amplitude-damping channels. This construction provides a tensorial and affine-geometric interpretation of the universal superoperator structure derived in arXiv:2606.26477 while keeping the algebraic and model-dependent sectors explicitly separated.

</details>


### [56] [Frozen-Tree Sampling Refutes Quantum Advantage of Random Circuit Sampling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04054)
*Sangchul Oh*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种高效的经典“冻结树采样算法（frozen-tree sampling algorithm）”，该算法利用Haar随机量子态的标度不变性（conditional scale invariance），能在O(n)时间内采样n量子比特的比特串。其输出分布与随机量子电路在统计上完全一致，因此任何仅基于样本的统计检验都无法区分经典采样与量子电路采样，从而对随机电路采样的量子优势声称提出挑战。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随机电路采样（random circuit sampling）被广泛认为是经典难以模拟的任务，并因此成为展示量子优势（quantum advantage）的主要基准。本文旨在质疑这一前提，试图证明该任务实际上存在高效的经典算法。

Method: 提出冻结树采样算法，利用Haar随机量子态的条件标度不变性（conditional scale invariance）实现经典高效采样；该算法以O(n)的时间复杂度生成n量子比特的比特串。

Result: 冻结树采样器输出的概率p_F(x)与随机量子电路输出的概率p_C(x)统计上完全等同，二者均为同一狄利克雷分布（Dirichlet distribution）的独立实例。因此，任何仅基于样本的统计检验都无法区分经典冻结树采样器与量子随机电路。

Conclusion: 随机电路采样的量子优势经不起推敲：其计算困难性并不在于从狄利克雷分布中采样（这可以经典高效实现），而在于识别具体的电路实现（circuit realization）。

Abstract: Random circuit sampling of bitstrings from a Haar-random quantum state is widely believed to be classically intractable, and has therefore been implemented as a primary benchmark for demonstrating quantum advantage. Here, we challenge this premise by proposing an efficient classical frozen-tree sampling algorithm that exploits the conditional scale invariance of Haar-random quantum states [Oh, arXiv:2602.19448]. The frozen-tree sampler draws bitstrings of $n$ qubits in $O(n)$ time per sample. Moreover, its output probability $p_F(x)$ is statistically identical to the probability $p_C(x)$ of a random quantum circuit, since both are independent instances of the same Dirichlet distribution. Consequently, no statistical test acting on samples alone can distinguish the classical frozen-tree sampler from a quantum random circuit. The claimed quantum advantage of random circuit sampling therefore does not withstand scrutiny: its hardness lies not in sampling from the Dirichlet distribution, which is classically efficient, but in identifying a specific circuit realization.

</details>


### [57] [Wei-Norman approach for non-Hermitian driven spin-$S$ systems and its application to defect freezing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04075)
*Mingwei Meng,Chen Sun*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过Wei-Norman方法，将一般非厄米时变驱动下自旋-S系统的演化算符矩阵元用闭合解析形式（雅可比多项式）表达，并应用于研究$\mathcal{PT}$对称SSH模型中的缺陷冻结现象，揭示了该现象仅出现在穿过$\mathcal{PT}$对称性破缺区域（即经过高阶例外点）的动量扇区，且激发密度在非厄米参数的临界值处出现奇异性。

Method: 采用Wei-Norman方法（Wei-Norman approach），对于受一般非厄米时变驱动（non-Hermitian time-dependent drive）的自旋-S系统，将演化算符的矩阵元用雅可比多项式（Jacobi polynomials）表示为闭合解析形式，并通过对应自旋-1/2模型加以表达。

Conclusion: 本工作丰富了多能级非厄米系统中非绝热动力学的解析工具库，为跨越高阶例外点的缺陷冻结现象提供了定量且可检验的理论预测，并指出这些预测可能在电路网络（electric circuit networks）和光子晶格（photonic lattices）等平台上被实验验证。

Abstract: In the theoretical study of nonequilibrium non-Hermitian systems, obtaining exact analytical solutions for their nonadiabatic dynamics is highly desirable yet often challenging. In this work, we identify a class of non-Hermitian quantum systems where this difficulty can be substantially reduced. Employing the Wei-Norman approach, we show that for a spin-$S$ subject to a general non-Hermitian time-dependent drive, the matrix elements of the evolution operator can be expressed in closed analytical forms (via Jacobi polynomials) in terms of the corresponding spin-$1/2$ model. This approach is straightforward and accessible to nonspecialists in Lie algebra. As an application, we investigate a specific nonequilibrium non-Hermitian phenomenon known as defect freezing, i.e., the existence of excitations in the adiabatic limit, in spin-$S$ extensions of the $\mathcal{PT}$-symmetric Su-Schrieffer-Heeger model under linear quenches. We derive exact analytical expressions for the momentum-resolved excitation probabilities and the total excitation densities. Our results reveal that defect freezing occurs exclusively in momentum sectors that traverse the $\mathcal{PT}$-symmetry-broken region -- and thus pass through a pair of higher-order exceptional points (EPs) -- during the quench; notably, the excitation density exhibits a singularity at a critical value of the non-Hermiticity parameter. This work enriches the analytical toolkit for nonadiabatic dynamics in multi-level non-Hermitian systems and provides quantitative, testable predictions for defect freezing across higher-order EPs, possibly accessible on platforms such as electric circuit networks and photonic lattices.

### [58] [Matter-Field Exchange Generates Entanglement, Not Classical Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03429)
*Nicetu Tibau Vidal,Aditya Varna Iyer*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文分析Aziz和Howl提出的“经典引力介导纠缠”机制，指出该效应并非由经典引力自由度介导，而是来自量子物质场在两个干涉仪之间的交换传播（matter-field cross-talk），可通过使用不同物质种类或插入屏障予以消除。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验Aziz和Howl提出的混合理论（hybrid theory）中经典引力场能否诱导两个大质量系统间的纠缠，澄清该效应在BMV型纠缠见证（BMV-type witnesses）意义上的物理归属。

Method: 在微扰量子场论（perturbative QFT）框架内分析Aziz-Howl机制，追踪纠缠项的传播子（propagator）结构，并考察后选择（postselection）对最终子空间的投影效应。

Result: 该不可分离项依赖于同一量子物质场在两个干涉仪之间的交换传播子（cross-propagator）；若使用不同且不可相互转换的物质场，该交叉传播子消失，纠缠图（entangling diagram）亦消失；效应还依赖于投影到包含原始局域N粒子分支态（branch states）的受限子空间。

Conclusion: Aziz-Howl机制是经典背景下物质扇区的串扰效应（matter-sector cross-talk effect），而非经典引力介导的纠缠；可通过使用不同物质种类或在干涉仪间插入屏障来消除该效应。

Abstract: Aziz and Howl have argued that a hybrid theory with quantum matter and a classical gravitational field can generate entanglement between two massive systems. In their construction, the branch-dependent contribution appears at fourth order through propagators of the quantum matter field in a fixed classical gravitational potential. We analyse this mechanism within the same perturbative QFT framework and show that the effect should not be interpreted as classical gravity mediating entanglement in the sense relevant to BMV-type witnesses. The non-separable term relies on a quantum-matter exchange channel between the two interferometers and is present only when the two systems are modelled as excitations of the same matter field. If distinct, non-interconverting matter fields describe the systems, the corresponding cross-propagator is absent and the Aziz-Howl entangling diagram vanishes. The effect relies on coherent propagation amplitudes of the quantum matter field between the two interferometers, together with postselection onto the original localised branch subspace. Moreover, the inference of entanglement is made after projecting the full QFT evolution onto a restricted final subspace containing the original localised $N$-particle branch states. This projection removes precisely the sectors that would record matter-field contamination, mode deformation, or exchange between the two interferometers. We therefore argue that the Aziz-Howl mechanism is a matter-sector cross-talk effect in a classical background, not entanglement mediated by classical gravitational degrees of freedom. Having identified the channel responsible for the Aziz-Howl contribution, we predict that it can be eliminated by using distinct, non-interconverting matter species in the two interferometers, or by inserting a barrier that suppresses matter-field propagation between them.

Furthermore, we explore the thermal properties of the system by employing the partition function. Numerical results are presented to provide a comprehensive analysis of the system behavior under the considered effects. ### [60] [Contraction and Expansion Values of Quantum Channels](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04950)
*Ruben Ibarrondo,Mikel Sanz*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了收缩值（contraction values）和扩张值（expansion values）两条单调序列，用以细化量子信道（quantum channel）的迹距离（trace distance）收缩系数，揭示了其与s-数理论（s-numbers）的联系，并建立了主要结构性质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 迹距离的收缩系数（contraction coefficient）是量化量子信道退化状态可区分性的核心工具，但它作为极值比率只刻画信道的最优行为，即使对强噪声信道也往往平凡，且单一标量难以描述收缩在信道复合下的累积效应。

Method: 作者引入收缩值和扩张值两条单调序列，通过无迹厄米算子（traceless Hermitian operators）子空间上的极小-极大变分原理（min-max variational principle）定义，并证明其等价于信道限制在无迹算子上的Gel'fand数或Bernstein数，从而将其纳入Pietsch的s-数理论框架。

Result: 该序列具有操作意义，可解释为两种态区分博弈（state-discrimination games）；在信道复合下能提供收缩系数无法给出的界限；作者建立了其主要结构性质，并对单量子比特信道、d维振幅阻尼信道（amplitude damping channels）以及直和信道（direct-sum channels）进行了计算或估计。

Conclusion: 收缩值和扩张值比单一的收缩系数更精细地刻画了信道在迹距离下的行为，且通过s-数理论为信道复合下的界限分析提供了理论支撑。

Abstract: The contraction coefficient of the trace distance is a central tool in quantum information, quantifying how strongly a quantum channel degrades the distinguishability of states. However, being an extremal ratio, it captures only the most optimistic behaviour of the channel and is often trivial, even for very noisy channels. Moreover, a single scalar is poorly suited to describe how contraction accumulates under channel composition. In this work we introduce the \emph{contraction and expansion values}, two monotone sequences that refine the contraction and expansion coefficients in the same way singular values refine the operator norm. They arise from a min--max variational principle over subspaces of traceless Hermitian operators, admit an operational interpretation in terms of two state-discrimination games, and are shown to coincide with the Gel'fand or Bernstein numbers of the channel restricted to traceless operators. This identification places the sequences within Pietsch's theory of $s$-numbers and yields, in particular, bounds under channel composition that the contraction coefficient alone cannot provide. We establish their main structural properties and compute or estimate them for single-qubit channels, $d$-dimensional amplitude damping channels, and direct-sum channels.

Abstract: Matrix Brownian motion provides a powerful framework for studying crossover ensembles in quantum chaos and quantum transport, as well as thermalization and information scrambling in many-body dynamics. Here, we develop a unified diagrammatic framework to characterize Brownian ensembles for orthogonal and symplectic random matrices, which describe systems with particle-hole symmetry. We compute polynomial averages up to fourth order and construct an orthogonally invariant interpolation for the disconnected $\mathrm{SO}^-(q)$ sector of the orthogonal group. Here, we extend the framework of geometric modulation to multi-level systems and show that both transition and survival intensities can be modulated. ### [65] [Semiclassical Langevin dynamics of long-range dissipative time crystals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03486)
*Reyhaneh Khasseh,Rosario Fazio,Angelo Russomanno*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文发展了一种半经典朗之万方法（semiclassical Langevin approach），用于研究耗散时间晶体（dissipative time crystals）中的有限尺寸效应（finite-size effects），揭示了系统尺寸与时间晶体鲁棒性之间的标度关系，并验证了该方法在超越精确林德布拉德模拟（exact Lindblad simulations）的区间内的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 耗散时间晶体系统在有限尺寸下的行为尚不清楚，现有的精确林德布拉德模拟受限于系统规模，需要发展一种能够跨越更大尺寸范围的有限尺寸探测方法，以量化时间晶体鲁棒性及其与系统尺寸的关系。

Method: 采用半经典朗之万方法（semiclassical Langevin approach），分别分析了两类自旋模型：一是具有幂律林德布拉德算符（power-law Lindblad operators）的自旋-1/2模型，二是具有局域耗散与长程哈密顿相互作用的自旋-1模型（后者使用盖尔曼变量（Gell-Mann variables）表述）。通过有限尺寸标度分析，考察振荡衰减、偏差时间及主导傅里叶峰行为。

Result: 在自旋-1/2模型中，发现有限尺寸振荡随时间指数衰减，其衰减率在长程区间内随系统尺寸呈代数下降，标度指数可作为时间晶体鲁棒性的直接诊断。在自旋-1模型中，稳定性的偏差时间与主导傅里叶峰均随系统尺寸呈幂律标度，当相互作用幂律指数低于某一阈值时表现出时间晶体行为，该阈值与累积展开（cumulant expansion）结果一致。

Conclusion: 半经典朗之万动力学是一种有效的有限尺寸探测工具，能够在超越精确林德布拉德模拟的区间内对耗散时间晶体进行定量分析，其揭示的标度行为可推广至更广泛的长程耗散系统。

Abstract: We develop a semiclassical Langevin approach to study finite-size effects in dissipative time-crystalline spin systems. For a spin-$1/2$ model with power-law Lindblad operators, we find finite-size oscillations exponentially decaying in time, and their decay rate decreases algebraically with system size in the long-range regime. The scaling exponent of this decay time provides a direct diagnostic of the robustness of the time-crystalline, and we find that this robustness extends beyond the range of power-law dissipation exponents where the system dynamics is mean-field in the thermodynamic limit. We also apply our approach to a spin-one model with local dissipation and long-range Hamiltonian interactions, formulating it in terms of Gell-Mann variables. In this case, finite-size stability is quantified through the deviation time from the mean-field behavior and the behavior of the dominant Fourier peak. We find that both quantities scale as a power law with the system size -- marking thereby a time-crystal behavior -- when the exponent of the power-law interaction is below a certain threshold, that turns out to be in agreement with previous cumulant-expansion findings. Our results show that semiclassical Langevin dynamics provides a useful finite-size probe of dissipative time crystals in regimes beyond exact Lindblad simulations.

### [66] [Thermalization hierarchy from irreducible degrees of freedom](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03535)
*Pedro Fittipaldi de Castro,Wladimir A. Benalcazar*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文揭示了量子多体系统中键代数（bond algebra）与交换子代数（commutant algebra）表示维数 $D_\lambda$ 控制热化（thermalization）层级结构的机制，从精确量子多体疤痕（$D_\lambda=1$）到体率遍历态（大$D_\lambda$）连续插值，并引入不可约自由度（irreducible degrees of freedom, IDOF）作为该层级结构的微观解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子多体系统的希尔伯特空间分解为对称性扇区（symmetry sectors）不足以刻画其动力学孤立子空间的精细结构；已有研究仅认识到低键不可约表示维数（bond-irrep dimension）$D_\lambda$的子空间倾向于违背本征态热化假说（eigenstate thermalization hypothesis, ETH），但$D_\lambda$在全谱动力学子空间中的连续控制作用尚未阐明。

Method: 以SU(2)对称的自旋-1/2链为范例，计算各扇区内平均本征态纠缠熵（entanglement entropy）与$\mathrm{log} \ D_\lambda$的定量关系；引入不可约自由度（IDOF）作为键代数扇区内多体态独立可变空间坐标数，以微观解释$D_\lambda$的物理意义及热化层级结构；通过选择性破缺对称性同时保留特定键代数扇区，嵌入具有指定纠缠水平的非热本征态。

Result: $\mathrm{log} \ D_\lambda$能够定量解释每个扇区内平均本征态纠缠熵，建立起从$D_\lambda=1$的精确量子多体疤痕到$D_\lambda$大值时的体率遍历态之间的热化层级；通过对称性破缺可在遍历谱中嵌入具有预设纠缠水平的非热本征态族，将受限谱生成代数（restricted spectrum-generating algebra）从单个态塔推广至整个动力学子空间。

Conclusion: 键代数表示维数$D_\lambda$是控制量子多体系统热化行为的连续参数，其对数与纠缠熵定量相关；不可约自由度的概念为热化层级提供了微观基础；该方法可推广用于工程化设计具有特定纠缠特性的非热本征态族。

Abstract: The decomposition of the Hilbert space of a quantum many-body system into the irreducible representations of its bond and commutant algebras yields a finer structure of dynamically isolated subspaces than the mere decomposition into symmetry sectors. While it has been recognized that subspaces associated with low bond-irrep dimensions $D_λ$ tend to violate the eigenstate thermalization hypothesis (ETH), here we show that $D_λ$ controls thermalization continuously across the full spectrum of dynamical subspaces. Using SU(2)-symmetric spin-1/2 chains as a paradigmatic example, we demonstrate that $\mathrm{log} \ D_λ$ quantitatively accounts for the average eigenstate entanglement entropy within each sector, establishing a thermalization hierarchy that interpolates from exact quantum many-body scars at $D_λ=1$ to volume-law ergodic states at large $D_λ$. To make this concrete, we introduce the notion of irreducible degrees of freedom (IDOF), defined as the number of independently-varying spatial coordinates parametrizing a many-body state within a given bond-algebra sector, which provides a microscopic interpretation of $D_λ$ and of the resulting thermalization hierarchy. Finally, we show that by selectively breaking symmetries while preserving chosen bond-algebra sectors, one can embed families of nonthermal eigenstates at prescribed entanglement levels into an otherwise ergodic spectrum, generalizing restricted spectrum-generating algebras from towers of individual states to entire dynamical subspaces.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 本文采用广义克利福德电路（generalized Clifford circuits），并将基于克利福德电路增强矩阵乘积态（CAMPS）的密度矩阵重整化群（DMRG）方法扩展到自旋-1系统。

Conclusion: 广义Kramers-Wannier变换提供了一条从对称性保护拓扑序（symmetry-protected topological order）到对称性破缺（symmetry breaking）的新的幺正路径（unitary route），这与Kennedy-Tasaki变换截然不同。

Abstract: Disentangling transformations play a central role in the classical simulation of quantum many-body systems, yet their analytic structure and underlying mechanism remain largely unexplored. Here, we study the structure of the disentangler in the Haldane phase of spin-1 systems using generalized Clifford circuits. To this end, we extend the Clifford-circuit-augmented matrix product states (CAMPS)-based density-matrix renormalization group (DMRG) method to spin-1 systems. Within this framework, we find that the local disentanglers optimized for the Haldane phase implement the generalized Kramers--Wannier (KW) transformation, and we analytically verify its optimality for the Affleck--Kennedy--Lieb--Tasaki (AKLT) state. Beyond reducing entanglement, the KW transformation maps the Haldane phase to a phase with spontaneously broken $\mathbb{Z}_{2}$ symmetry. This mapping is distinct from the Kennedy--Tasaki transformation and provides a new unitary route from symmetry-protected topological order to symmetry breaking.

### [68] [Orthogonality Edges in Strong-Coupling Quantum Work Statistics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03950)
*Atta ur Rahman,Muhammad Noman,S. M. Zangi,Saeed Haddadi*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究驱动量子系统在红外奇异库（infrared singular reservoir）耦合下的功分布（work distribution）阈值结构，以偏置自旋-玻色子模型（spin-boson model）的突然偏置翻转为例，展示了从准粒子（quasiparticle）型阈值线到多体边缘（many-body edge）的转变机制，并利用数值方法分析了有限隧穿效应下的阈值分辨与交叉行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索强耦合红外奇异库对驱动量子系统功分布阈值结构的深远影响，揭示从准粒子型阈值到多体边缘的转变机制，并澄清在偏离静态边界极限时阈值的新奇行为及其诊断分歧。

Method: 采用独立玻色子极限下的精确解对红外分类进行分析；使用基于位移基矢的对数离散化库精确对角化（displaced-basis exact diagonalization of logarithmically discretized baths）方法，结合 z-交错谱（z-interleaved spectra）和 z-平均重叠（z-averaged overlaps）提取累积连续谱指数和弹性重叠指数。

Result: 超欧姆（super-Ohmic）库可保留有限弹性阈值权重，而欧姆（Ohmic）和亚欧姆（sub-Ohmic）库通过边界正交性（boundary orthogonality）消灭弹性线；在欧姆不动点，同一指数控制弹性残留和低功连续谱的消失；有限隧穿下两个诊断指数出现分离（θ_C > θ_Z），且该分离对拟合窗口、截断、谱大小和留一交叉检验均稳健；时间域特征函数提供了兼容但不具决定性的诊断；相同阈值边缘控制Jarzynski型指数平均的采样成本。

Conclusion: 指数分离应解释为偏离静态边界不动点（static-boundary fixed point）的有限能量交叉（finite-energy crossover），而非新渐近不动点的证据；阈值边缘结构在低温下对稀有低功事件的采样成本有关键影响。

Abstract: Strong coupling to a reservoir can do more than shift, broaden, or dress the work peaks of a driven quantum system. When the reservoir is infrared singular, a sudden change of a local control parameter can alter the boundary condition seen by infinitely many low-energy modes, converting a quasiparticle-like threshold line into a many-body edge. We demonstrate this mechanism for the inclusive work distribution of the biased spin-boson model under a sudden bias inversion. In the independent-boson limit, the problem is exactly solvable and gives a sharp infrared classification: a super-Ohmic bath can retain a finite elastic threshold weight, whereas Ohmic and sub-Ohmic baths extinguish the elastic line through boundary orthogonality. At the Ohmic fixed point, the same exponent controls both the vanishing elastic residue and the low-work continuum. We then ask how this edge is resolved away from the static-boundary limit. Using displaced-basis exact diagonalization of logarithmically discretized baths, we find that finite tunnelling leaves an edge-like continuum over the accessible energy window, while separating two operational diagnostics of the threshold: the cumulative-continuum exponent extracted from $z$-interleaved spectra lies above the elastic-overlap exponent extracted from $z$-averaged overlaps, $θ_C>θ_Z$. We interpret this separation as a finite-energy crossover away from the static-boundary fixed point, not as evidence for a new asymptotic fixed point. The separation survives fitting-window variation, oscillator-cutoff checks, spectrum-size checks, and leave-one-$z$-out tests, while time-domain characteristic functions provide a compatible but non-decisive diagnostic. Finally, the same threshold edge controls the sampling cost of Jarzynski-type exponential averages, making rare low-work events increasingly important at low temperature.

### [70] [Controlling many-body quantum chaos in a dissipative optical cavity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04455)
*Filippo Ferrari,Francesca Orsi,Ekaterina Fedotova,Óscar Rios Alves,Michał Zdziennicki,Jean-Philippe Brantut,Vincenzo Savona*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究超冷费米子腔量子电动力学（cavity QED）平台中，在可控无序和长程相互作用下，由腔光子损耗和原子自发辐射两种耗散源驱动的非平衡动力学，揭示二者在结构上的本质差异及其对多体量子混沌可观测性的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 论文在典型的腔QED设置中引入可控无序和长程相互作用，从理论上分析驱动-耗散动力学，分别考察腔光子损耗和原子自发辐射两种耗散通道的结构，并基于实验现实参数推导定量约束条件。

Result: 腔光子损耗简化为单个退相干通道（dephasing channel），而原子自发辐射在实验相关区域内产生一组非局域退相干通道（nonlocal dephasing channels）。腔诱导的退相干保留了可积分动力学与混沌动力学在线性依赖于密度矩阵的可观测量上的区分特征，而自发辐射则抑制这些特征。纠缠熵（entanglement entropy）等探测多体态结构的量则受两种耗散机制的强烈影响。

Abstract: Cavity quantum electrodynamics (QED) with ultracold fermions provides a promising platform for realizing many-body quantum chaos through disordered, photon-mediated long-range interactions. Such setups are inherently open and are therefore subject to dissipation arising from cavity photon loss and atomic spontaneous emission. In this article, we study the driven-dissipative dynamics of a typical cavity QED setting including controllable disorder and long-range interactions. We find that the two dissipation sources have qualitatively different structures. Cavity loss reduces to a single dephasing channel, whereas spontaneous emission in the experimentally relevant regime generates a collection of nonlocal dephasing channels. Cavity-induced dephasing preserves signatures distinguishing integrable from chaotic Hamiltonian dynamics in observables that depend linearly on the density matrix, while spontaneous emission suppresses these signatures. By contrast, quantities that probe the structure of the many-body state, such as the entanglement entropy, are strongly affected by both dissipation mechanisms. Assuming experimentally realistic parameters, we derive quantitative constraints for the observation and control of many-body quantum chaos in cavity-QED platforms.

*Ling-Feng Zhang,Wing Chi Yu*

Abstract: We investigate phase transitions in the extended Su-Schrieffer-Heeger (SSH) model with next-nearest-neighbor hoppings and an imaginary staggered chemical potential. In the presence of small non-Hermiticity, exceptional points emerge in pairs from the gap-closing momenta near the topological phase boundaries of the Hermitian limit. Utilizing the Krylov spread complexity and entanglement entropy, we analyze two dynamical protocols: (i) preparing the non-Hermitian ground state via a unitary transformation, and (ii) evolving the system under the non-Hermitian Hamiltonian. We show that the spread complexity, and long-time spread complexity as well as entanglement entropy can effectively signal phase transitions in the first and second protocols, respectively. To unravel the detailed structure of the transitions, we introduce the momentum-resolved complexity that identifies the characteristic modes and tracks their evolution with the driving parameter. In the regime where the system possesses a purely imaginary spectrum, we further identify dynamical phases based on the saturation behavior of the spread complexity. The entanglement entropy is also found to exhibit similar saturation behavior, thereby providing a more experimentally accessible probe of the dynamical phases.
