### [72] [Sector-memory obstruction to probe-level bath emergence in finite programmable qubit environments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04791)
*Gaurav Sarmah,Ramakrishna Podila*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过数值模拟与量子硬件实验，研究了在电荷守恒约束下有限量子环境能否使局域探针弛豫到吉布斯态（Gibbs state）。结果表明，尽管每个固定电荷扇区（fixed-charge sector）内部可达到近最大混合态，但全局吉布斯拟合误差显著，表明扇区约束下的平衡不足以产生扇区无关的吉布斯态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索有限量子环境是否能在不充当正则热库（canonical bath）的情况下使局域探针弛豫，并定量刻画这种约束性平衡与标准热化之间的区别。

Method: 在激发数守恒（excitation-number-conserving）动力学下，将探针量子比特（qubit）与N个环境量子比特耦合，利用Haar随机纯态在完整固定电荷扇区内进行精确模拟，并构造电荷守恒的Floquet电路（包含Rz相位门和XX+YY交换门），在理想与噪声Qiskit仿真以及IBM Fez量子处理器上实施有限深度实验。

Result: 扇区分辨的晚期布居（sector-resolved late-time population, p_e^{(q)}）接近最大混合扇区基准值p_e^{(q)}=q/(N+1)，但全局Gibbs拟合误差Δ_G^{global}显著（N=4时约0.558）。对称性破缺扫描（bath R_x(ε)旋转）降低诊断指标但增加电荷泄漏，无法在可达到深度内消除扇区排序。

Conclusion: 在约束扇区内的平衡不足以使探针达到扇区独立的单一吉布斯态，这表明有限量子环境的热化需要超越扇区约束的额外机制。

Abstract: Finite quantum environments can relax local probes without acting as canonical baths. We study this distinction for a probe qubit coupled to a programmable bath of ($N$) qubits under excitation-number-conserving dynamics. The conserved charge partitions the Hilbert space into sectors. We characterize probe-level bath emergence using the sector-resolved late-time population ($p_e^{(q)}$), the sector-memory variance ($M_N$), and a global Gibbs-fit error ($Δ_G^{\mathrm{global}}$). Exact simulations with Haar-random pure states in each complete fixed-charge sector yield sector-dependent populations close to the maximally mixed-sector benchmark ($p_e^{(q)}=q/(N+1)$), producing a nonzero Gibbs obstruction. We then construct charge-preserving Floquet circuits using ($R_z$) phases and ($XX+YY$) exchange gates, validate them with ideal and noisy Qiskit simulations, and implement finite-depth experiments on IBM Fez. For ($N=4$) and ($ε=0$), the hardware data give ($M_N \simeq 0.044$), ($Δ_G^{\mathrm{global}} \simeq 0.558$), and charge preservation near 0.90 after readout mitigation. A paired symmetry-breaking scan using bath ($R_x(ε)$) rotations reduces both diagnostics while increasing charge leakage, but does not erase sector ordering over the accessible depths. These results show that equilibration within constrained sectors is insufficient to produce a single sector-independent Gibbs state for the probe.

</details>


### [73] [Canonical quantization of neurons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05000)
*Alexander He,Nana Liu,Mark M. Wilde*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文将经典神经元的能量函数替换为量子哈密顿量（Hamiltonian），通过矩阵泛函微积分（matrix functional calculus）对激活函数（activation function）进行量子化，从而构建出量子化神经元（quantized neuron），并开发了相应的混合量子-经典算法（hybrid quantum-classical algorithms）用于函数逼近与梯度估计。数值实验表明，该量化神经元在代表性学习任务中展现出比经典神经元更强的表达能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典机器学习中的神经元模型缺乏源自物理学基本原理的量子化方法，而正则量子化（canonical quantization）作为从经典哈密顿量构建量子模型的系统性手段，尚未被应用于神经网络的基本计算原语（computational primitive）。本研究旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 将神经元视为能量函数（energy function）与激活函数（activation function）的组合；用量子哈密顿量替代能量函数，并通过矩阵泛函微积分对激活函数进行量子化，得到可作用于输入量子态的激活可观测量（activation observable）。基于此开发混合量子-经典算法，训练与评估中分别利用Hadamard测试（Hadamard test）、哈密顿模拟（Hamiltonian simulation）和“单qumode之力”（power of one qumode）与薛定谔化（Schroedingerization）等量子算法。

Result: 数值实验结果显示，所提出的量化神经元在代表性学习任务上的表达能力优于对应的经典神经元。

Conclusion: 正则量子化为构建量子机器学习原语（quantum machine learning primitives）提供了一种原则性框架，并为设计适配量子数据的神经架构奠定了理论基础。

Abstract: Canonical quantization provides a systematic procedure for constructing quantum models from classical Hamiltonians. Here, we apply this principle to a fundamental computational primitive of machine learning: the neuron. Specifically, by viewing a neuron as a composition of an energy function and an activation function, we quantize this model by replacing the energy function with a quantum Hamiltonian and applying the activation function to it through matrix functional calculus. This results in an activation observable that can be measured on an input quantum state. We investigate the use of these quantized neurons for function approximation, where the objective is to learn an unknown observable from labeled quantum data. For this purpose, we develop hybrid quantum-classical algorithms for training and evaluation, including procedures for measuring the activation observable and estimating gradients of the squared loss error. Our algorithms for gradient estimation rely on basic primitives like classical random sampling, the Hadamard test, and Hamiltonian simulation, and those for measuring an activation observable rely on quantum algorithms known as the power of one qumode and Schroedingerization. Numerical experiments demonstrate that our quantized neurons exhibit enhanced expressive capabilities relative to corresponding classical neurons on representative learning tasks. Our work establishes canonical quantization as a principled framework for constructing quantum machine learning primitives and provides a foundation for developing neural architectures tailored to quantum data.

</details>


### [74] [Fragile single-cone Dirac quantum walks in two dimensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05112)
*C. W. J. Beenakker,J. Sánchez Férnan,J. Tworzydło*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文发现二维量子行走（quantum walk）相比一维情形在结构上更为脆弱。虽然局域两带量子行走可以存在未配对的狄拉克锥（Dirac cone），但其保护对称性不再是普通的在位对称性（on-site symmetry），而变为非对称性（non-symmorphic symmetry），涉及半格点平移，且会被一般空间不均匀性破坏。具体以Ho-Chalker网络模型为例，论证了该二维狄拉克量子行走可被势散射（potential scattering）打开能隙。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已知一维量子行走可对无质量狄拉克方程（massless Dirac equation）实现局部时空离散化，且没有费米子加倍问题（fermion doubling），并能保持连续理论的基对称性（手征对称性与时间反演对称性）。作者进而探索二维情形是否也能构造类似的拓扑稳定量子行走模型。

Method: 通过理论分析二维局域两带量子行走的对称性结构，指出其保护对称性非寻常（变为非对称性，即non-symmorphic symmetry），并结合Ho-Chalker网络模型的具体构造，分析势散射对其能隙的影响。

Result: 二维局域两带量子行走可以存在未配对的狄拉克锥，但保护该狄拉克锥的对称性不再是普通的在位对称性，而是涉及半格点平移的非对称性。这种非对称性容易被一般的空间不均匀性破坏。在Ho-Chalker网络模型的基础上，势散射可以使其能隙打开。

Conclusion: 二维情形下，量子行走对狄拉克方程的离散化在结构上比一维情形更为脆弱，因为保护对称性是非对称性的，会因空间不均匀性而被破坏，从而失去对狄拉克锥的拓扑保护。

Abstract: It is known that a one-dimensional (1D) quantum walk gives a local space-time discretization of the massless Dirac equation with a single quasi-energy cone (no fermion doubling at low energies), keeping the fundamental symmetries (chiral and time-reversal) of the continuum theory. We show that the analogous 2D construction is fundamentally more fragile. Local two-band quantum walks can have an unpaired Dirac cone, but the protecting symmetries then cease to be ordinary on-site symmetries: they become non-symmorphic, involving half-lattice translations, and are broken by generic spatial inhomogeneities. In particular, we demonstrate that the 2D Dirac quantum walk based on the Ho-Chalker network model can be gapped by potential scattering.

</details>


### [75] [Efficient classical simulation of two-dimensional long-range systems: Rydberg arrays and beyond](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05178)
*Jia-Lin Chan,Tao Xiang,Yantao Wu*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种将变分蒙特卡洛（VMC）对张量网络态（tensor network states）的局部能量计算复杂度从$O(N^3)$降至$O(N)$的新框架，使得能够对长程相互作用量子系统（如里德伯模拟器中的$10\times10$偶极XY模型）进行可扩展且精确的经典模拟，同时解决了张量网络VMC中从直积态（product state）演化时的病理问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在具有任意全连接两体相互作用的$N$位点量子系统中，变分蒙特卡洛（VMC）计算局部能量的开销通常高达$O(N^3)$，严重限制了经典模拟的可扩展性；此外，当前里德伯（Rydberg）和离子阱（ion-trap）模拟器等长程量子平台亟需可扩展的经典基准测试（benchmarking）工具，而现有方法难以处理此前文献[Chen et al., Nature 2023]中的十乘十偶极XY模型的绝热实时动力学。

Method: 提出一种新框架，将张量网络态下局部能量的变分蒙特卡洛（VMC）计算复杂度从$O(N^3)$降低到$O(N)$；同时作为独立的技术贡献，解决了张量网络VMC中从直积态（product states）演化时存在的病理问题。

Result: 成功实现了里德伯模拟器中$10\times10$偶极XY模型绝热实时协议的精确模拟，该模拟此前无法通过经典计算完成；还直接进行了基态VMC计算以与绝热态制备（adiabatic state preparation）进行比较。

Conclusion: 张量网络变分蒙特卡洛（tensor network VMC）是用于长程量子平台（如里德伯和离子阱模拟器）的强大经典模拟工具，能够满足当前对这些平台进行可扩展经典基准测试的迫切需求。

Abstract: In variational Monte Carlo (VMC) calculations of $N$-site quantum systems with arbitrary all-to-all two-body interactions, evaluating the local energy generally costs $O(N^3)$. We introduce a new framework that reduces this cost to $O(N)$ for tensor network states, capable of scalable and accurate computation of real-time dynamics and ground states. As a result, we obtain accurate simulations of the adiabatic real-time protocol of a $10\times10$ dipolar XY model realized in a Rydberg simulator [C. Chen et al., Nature 616, 691 (2023)], which was previously beyond the reach of classical simulation. Going beyond quantum experiments, we also directly perform ground state VMC to compare with the adiabatic state preparation. Our work demonstrates tensor network VMC as a powerful classical simulator for long-range quantum platforms such as Rydberg and ion-trap simulators, which are currently in urgent need of scalable classical benchmarking tools. As a separate technical contribution, we resolve the pathology of evolving from product states within of tensor network VMC.

</details>


### [76] [Quantum Computational Resources and Conformal Field Theory: Unifying Spins, Bosons, and Fermions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05343)
*Ryota Matsuda,Masahiro Hoshino,Yuto Ashida*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个统一度量——魔法Rényi熵（magic Rényi entropy, MRE），用于在自旋、玻色子和费米子系统中平等地量化计算资源（nonstabilizerness和non-Gaussianity），并通过共形场论分析揭示了临界多体态中这些计算资源的普适方面，发现其普适贡献由Affleck-Ludwig边界熵决定，且非高斯性可连续重整化该贡献或驱动边界相变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管量子纠缠（quantum entanglement）作为多体系统中量子资源（quantum resource）的范例已被广泛研究，且近期工作表明自旋系统中量子魔法（quantum magic）的共形场论分析揭示了与纠缠定性不同的普适特征，但在玻色子和费米子系统中，尚未建立类似于non-Gaussianity的计算资源统一表述。因此，需要一个统一的框架来平等处理自旋、玻色子和费米子中的计算资源。

Method: 引入统一度量魔法Rényi熵（magic Rényi entropy, MRE），将自旋中的nonstabilizerness与玻色子和费米子中的non-Gaussianity纳入同一框架；采用共形场论（conformal field theory, CFT）分析，将其普适贡献关联至Affleck-Ludwig边界熵；并利用边界重整化群流（boundary renormalization-group flows）描述非高斯性对普适贡献的重整化或边界相变（boundary phase transition）。

Result: CFT分析表明MRE的普适贡献以与系统大小无关的形式出现，由Affleck-Ludwig边界熵决定；非高斯性可连续重整化该贡献，或通过体诱导的边界重整化群流驱动边界相变。具体地，对Tomonaga-Luttinger液体描述的自旋less费米子交互系统的详细分析揭示，在Luttinger参数K=1/3和K=3处发生边界相变，数值计算验证了场论预测。

Conclusion: 这些结果为跨自旋、玻色子和费米子系统的多体魔法（many-body magic）提供了统一的场论理解，表明MRE可作为一种普适量度来捕捉临界多体态中计算资源的普适行为。

Abstract: Characterizing a quantum state through the lens of quantum resources provides an information-theoretic perspective on many-body systems. While quantum entanglement serves as the paradigmatic example of a quantum resource, recent studies have shown that quantum magic, a resource for universal quantum computation, can capture aspects of many-body states complementary to those described by entanglement. For instance, in spin systems, conformal field theory (CFT) analysis of the stabilizer Rényi entropy has revealed universal features of nonstabilizerness that are qualitatively distinct from entanglement. In bosonic and fermionic systems, however, a comparable formulation for their computational resource, non-Gaussianity, has yet to be established. In this work, we introduce a unified measure, the magic Rényi entropy (MRE), to quantify computational resources in spins, bosons, and fermions on an equal footing. This allows us to reveal common universal aspects of nonstabilizerness and non-Gaussianity in critical many-body states. In particular, our CFT analysis shows that the universal contribution to the MRE appears as the size-independent term determined by the Affleck-Ludwig boundary entropy. We find that non-Gaussianity can continuously renormalize this universal contribution or drive a boundary phase transition through bulk-induced boundary renormalization-group flows. As a concrete demonstration, we present a detailed CFT analysis of non-Gaussianity in interacting spinless fermions described by the Tomonaga-Luttinger liquid, showing boundary transitions at the Luttinger parameters $K=1/3$ and $K=3$. We perform numerical calculations that confirm our field-theoretical predictions. These results provide a unified field-theoretical understanding of many-body magic across spins, bosons, and fermions.

</details>

### [77] [Anisotropic magnetoresistance of 2D Rashba films with in-plane Zeeman field and short-range disorder](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02747)
*Igor Gornyi,Alexander Khaetskii*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文研究了具有面内塞曼场的二维Rashba薄膜在短程无序散射下的直流电导率，发现几何机制导致准经典电导率中不存在各向异性磁电阻（AMR），并基于面积不变性和密度Ward恒等式给出了严格证明。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探讨在具有面内塞曼场（in-plane Zeeman field）的二维Rashba体系中，短程标量无序（delta-correlated scalar disorder）是否会产生各向异性磁电阻（anisotropic magnetoresistance, AMR），并澄清其微观机制。

Method: 采用准经典（quasiclassical）电导率计算方法，结合密度Ward恒等式（density Ward identity）分析Born自能（Born self-energy）的标量性质及其与粒子密度对塞曼场导数的关系，并利用两条Rashba–Zeeman能带所围总面积对场不变这一几何性质，推导Kubo电导率（Kubo conductivity）的面内场无关性。

Result: 虽然面内塞曼场使两条螺旋费米轮廓（helicity Fermi contours）发生形变并旋转自旋织构（spin texture），但准经典电导率中并不出现AMR；Born自能为标量且与场无关，准粒子寿命保持各向同性；对角带内Kubo电导率仅取决于两条能带所围总面积，该面积与面内场无关，故电导率亦与场无关。

Conclusion: 在短程无序准经典框架下，点状非磁性杂质不会在该模型中产生AMR；若要产生AMR，必须引入超出该准经典短程无序机制的物理因素。

Abstract: We study the dc conductivity of a continuum two-dimensional Rashba film with an in-plane Zeeman field and delta-correlated scalar disorder. Although the field deforms the two helicity Fermi contours and rotates the spin texture, it does not produce anisotropic magnetoresistance in the leading quasiclassical conductivity. The mechanism is geometric. A density Ward identity fixes the spin-vector part of the Born self-energy to the derivative of the total particle density with respect to the field. This derivative vanishes, because the total area enclosed by the two Rashba-Zeeman sheets is independent of the in-plane field. The Born self-energy is therefore scalar and field independent, and the quasiparticle lifetime stays isotropic. The same area invariance controls transport: once the leading impurity ladder reduces the current vertex to the parabolic velocity, the diagonal intraband Kubo conductivity collapses onto the two-sheet occupied area and is field independent as well. The result settles the short-range-disorder quasiclassical problem: point-like nonmagnetic impurities do not produce AMR in this model. A nonzero AMR requires physics beyond this quasiclassical short-range-disorder mechanism.

</details>


### [78] [Electrically tunable interfacial thermal conduction via electronic structure engineering in ${Au}$/$Bi_{1-x}$$Sb_{x}$ topological insulators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02899)
*Min Young Kim,Joon Sang Kang,Jangwoo Ha,Hyungyu Jin,Sandy A. Ekahana,Pratik Saud,Chris Jozwiak,Eli Rotenberg,Aaron Bostwick,Jyoti Katoch,Joseph P. Heremans*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本研究通过 Au/BiSb 拓扑绝缘体（topological insulator）异质结提供了拓扑界面态（topological interface states）调控热传导的直接实验证据，并展示了通过电流注入可逆调控界面热导（interfacial thermal conductance）的能力，为主动热管理（active thermal management）开辟了基于界面电子结构工程（interface electronic structure engineering）的新路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统固体界面热传导的调控手段有限，缺乏对热流进行主动、可逆控制的机制。本研究旨在探索拓扑界面态在金属/拓扑绝缘体（metal/topological insulator）结中是否能够提供可电调谐的热传导能力，以满足日益高密度、高功率固态器件对主动热管理的需求。

Method: 实验上制备了 Au/Bi₈₉Sb₁₁ 和 Au/Bi₈₇Sb₁₃ 两种金属/拓扑绝缘体异质结，测量其界面热导（interfacial thermal conductance）随温度和偏压的变化行为。通过控制实验对比了平庸半金属（trivial semimetals）和绝缘插入层（insulating interlayers）体系，以确认效应的拓扑特异性（topological specificity）。

Result: 界面热导表现出与温度和偏压相关的独特行为。温度依赖来源于费米-狄拉克展宽（Fermi-Dirac broadening）驱动的拓扑界面态与体带态（bulk band states）之间的载流子再分布（carrier redistribution）；电偏压依赖则源于准费米能级移动（quasi-Fermi-level shifts）和 WKB 隧穿（WKB tunneling）进入邻近体带。控制实验证实该效应为拓扑界面态所特有。

Conclusion: 电可调谐界面热传导的实验发现表明，界面电子结构工程（interface electronic structure engineering）是实现主动热管理（active thermal management）的有效途径。该工作为替代传统依赖于结构变化的热控制方法提供了机械鲁棒性（mechanically robust）更高的方案，适用于日益高密度、高功率的固态器件。

Abstract: This work provides direct experimental evidence for the role of topological interface states in thermal conduction across a metal/topological insulator junction. It also shows that this conduction can be reversibly modulated by electrical current injection, offering a new approach toward active control of heat flow at solid-state interfaces. Specifically, the interfacial thermal conductance of ${Au}$/$Bi_{89}$$Sb_{11}$ and ${Au}$/$Bi_{87}$$Sb_{13}$ junctions demonstrates distinct temperature- and bias-dependent behavior. Both responses are attributed to carrier redistribution between topological interface and bulk band states, driven thermally by Fermi-Dirac broadening and electrically by quasi-Fermi-level shifts and WKB tunneling into nearby bulk bands. Control experiments using trivial semimetals and insulating interlayers further confirm the topological specificity of the effect. Such electrically tunable interfacial heat conduction positions interface electronic structure engineering as a promising route for active thermal management. In doing so, it lays the groundwork for a mechanically robust alternative to conventional structure-driven thermal control compatible with increasingly dense, high-power solid-state devices.

</details>


### [79] [Hall Shift Current and Nonlinear Anomalous Hall Effect in Gapped Dirac Fermion Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02953)
*Toshihito Osada*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该论文提出一种新的非线性反常霍尔效应（nonlinear anomalous Hall effect）机制，源于倾斜二维能隙狄拉克费米子系统中与朗道-齐纳隧穿（Landau-Zener tunneling）相关的侧跳位移（side-jump displacement），可解释有机狄拉克费米子系统α-(ET)2I3中观测到的非线性霍尔效应和非线性纵向输运现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有非线性反常霍尔效应通常由贝里曲率偶极子（Berry curvature dipole）的带内机制解释，但某些倾斜二维狄拉克费米子系统（如α-(ET)2I3）中观测到的非线性霍尔效应伴随非线性纵向输运现象无法完全由该机制说明，因此需要探索新的带间机制。

Method: 作者提出一种基于侧跳位移（side-jump displacement）的新机制，该位移与跨越质量隙（mass gap）的朗道-齐纳隧穿（Landau-Zener tunneling）相关，针对倾斜二维有能隙狄拉克费米子系统进行分析。

Result: 在轻掺杂且小能隙的倾斜狄拉克系统中，该带间机制（interband mechanism）能够对非线性反常霍尔效应产生贡献，与传统的由贝里曲率偶极子导致的带内机制（intraband mechanism）并存。

Conclusion: 该机制为有机狄拉克费米子系统α-(ET)2I3中观测到的伴随非线性纵向输运的非线性霍尔效应提供了可能的解释。

Abstract: We discuss a new mechanism for the nonlinear anomalous Hall effect in tilted two-dimensional gapped Dirac fermion systems. This mechanism originates from a side-jump displacement associated with Landau-Zener tunneling across the mass gap. In lightly doped tilted Dirac systems with a small gap, this interband mechanism can contribute to the nonlinear anomalous Hall effect in addition to the conventional intraband mechanism arising from the Berry curvature dipole. It provides a possible explanation for the nonlinear Hall effect accompanied by nonlinear longitudinal transport observed in the organic Dirac fermion system α-(ET)2I3 with an extremely small gap.

</details>


### [80] [Effects of Impurity Scattering on Orbital Hall Conductivity and Orbital Transport in Ru-based Alloys](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03076)
*Yumin Yang,Yanxu Chen,Wenqi Xu,Dahai Wei*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过Cu/Ti合金化调控Ru基非磁/铁磁双层膜中的杂质散射，发现Ru中轨道霍尔效应（orbital Hall effect）以对弱无序适度鲁棒的内禀机制为主，但轨道扩散长度（orbital diffusion length）在~14 nm基本不变，表明轨道输运并非简单由杂质散射主导，静态与动态无序通过不同微观通道影响轨道输运。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 杂质散射在轨道电流（orbital current）产生与输运中的作用远不如在传统自旋霍尔系统（conventional spin Hall systems）中那样明确，该研究旨在澄清这一未充分理解的问题。

Method: 通过Cu或Ti合金化调控Ru基非磁/铁磁双层膜中的杂质散射，结合自旋轨道转矩（SOT）测量和厚度依赖的漂移-扩散分析（drift-diffusion analysis），提取有效轨道霍尔电导率（effective orbital Hall conductivity）和轨道扩散长度。

Result: 多晶Ru中的轨道霍尔效应由内禀机制主导，对弱无序适度鲁棒但被强合金无序抑制；轨道扩散长度在所研究的杂质范围内几乎不变，约为14 nm；静态杂质与动态晶格无序通过不同的微观通道影响轨道输运。

Conclusion: 轨道输运并非简单地由杂质散射主导，静态与动态无序具有不同的影响机制。该结果为无序如何调控轨道产生与输运提供了新见解，并为开发高效轨道电子学（orbitronic）材料提供了实验指导。

Abstract: The role of impurity scattering in the generation and transport of orbital current remains less established than in conventional spin Hall systems. Here we investigate Ru-based nonmagnet/ferromagnet bilayers in which the impurity scattering is tuned by Cu or Ti alloying. According to SOT measurement and thickness-dependent drift-diffusion analysis, we extract the effective orbital Hall conductivity and the orbital diffusion length. We find that the orbital Hall effect in polycrystalline Ru is dominated by intrinsic mechanism that is moderately robust against weak disorder but suppressed by stronger alloy disorder. However, the orbital diffusion length remains nearly unchanged at approximately 14 nm over the investigated impurity range. This behavior indicates that orbital transport is not governed simply by an impurity scattering. Together with previous temperature-dependent measurements, our results show that static impurities and dynamic lattice disorder affect orbital transport through distinct microscopic channels. These results provide new insight into how disorder governs orbital generation and transport, and offer experimental guidance for developing high-efficient orbitronic materials.

### [81] [Substrate-Mediated Persistent Photodoping in WSe2/hBN Field-Effect Transistors Enabled by Defect States in SiO2](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03121)
*Sung-Ha Kim,Seong-Yeon Lee,Tae-Jeong Kim,Beomkyu Shin,Young-Jun Yu,Kenji Watanabe,Takashi Taniguchi,Soungmin Bae,Ki-Ju Yee*

TL;DR: 本工作通过实验与第一性原理计算相结合，揭示了WSe₂场效应晶体管中紫外光致掺杂（UV-induced photodoping）的起源主要来自SiO₂衬底中的缺陷态，而非hBN中的缺陷。SiO₂衬底充当电荷库，促进电荷转移和长期载流子俘获，而移除SiO₂层后光致掺杂效应被显著抑制。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于SiO₂/p-Si衬底上的WSe₂/hBN异质结构构建多层WSe₂ FET器件；开展波长依赖的光致掺杂测量（405 nm与640 nm激发）；对比有无SiO₂层时的光致掺杂行为；结合非晶SiO₂中缺陷态分布的分析与hBN缺陷的第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）。

Conclusion: SiO₂衬底中的缺陷态是WSe₂ FET器件中紫外光致掺杂与光栅控（photogating）行为的主要来源，而非hBN层中的缺陷。这一发现强调了衬底相关陷阱态在二维半导体器件光电响应中的主导作用。

Abstract: Photodoping plays an important role in determining the optoelectronic response of two-dimensional semiconductor devices; however, the origin of the responsible trap states remains unclear. In this work, we investigate UV-induced photodoping in multilayer WSe2 field-effect transistors (FETs) based on WSe2/hBN heterostructures on SiO2/p-Si substrates. Wavelength-dependent measurements reveal pronounced n-type photodoping under 405 nm illumination, whereas the effect is orders of magnitude weaker under 640 nm excitation and for p-type photodoping. Furthermore, when the SiO2 layer is removed, both n-type and p-type photodoping are strongly suppressed, demonstrating that the oxide layer is essential for persistent photodoping. Analysis of defect-state distributions in amorphous SiO2, together with first-principles calculations for hBN defects, shows that the experimental observations cannot be explained by defects in hBN. Instead, the results indicate that defect states in the SiO2 substrate act as charge reservoirs that facilitate charge transfer and long-term carrier trapping. These findings highlight the dominant role of substrate-related trap states in UV-induced photodoping and photogating behavior in WSe2 FET devices.

Abstract: Heteroatom substitution is a powerful route to tune the chemical and electronic properties of carbon nanomaterials. The electronic properties of the nanostructures were studied by scanning tunneling spectroscopy and density functional theory calculations. Our analyses revealed the presence of localized nitrogen-centered electronic states. In the gas phase where the nanostructures are in a neutral charge state, these states undergo spin polarization leading to an open-shell ground state. Upon adsorption on Au(111), the nanostructures exhibit electron transfer to the surface, which resulted in a closed-shell ground state. Our results demonstrate a straightforward and generally applicable route to synthesize graphitic nitrogen-substituted carbon nanomaterials with potential applications in spintronics, catalysis and energy storage.

### [84] [Many-body quantum chaos in excitonic spectra from first principles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03294)
*Daniel Hernangómez-Pérez,Rafael A. Molina*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过第一性原理GW-BSE计算，证明实际激子多体哈密顿量在无序驱动下可表现出随机矩阵普遍性所支配的量子混沌，并揭示了从规则动力学到完全混沌动力学的交叉过程，以及多体振子强度服从Porter-Thomas统计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索实际激子多体系统（excitonic many-body system）是否能够表现出量子混沌（quantum chaos）行为，以及无序（disorder）如何调控混沌动力学与多体遍历性（many-body ergodicity）。

Method: 基于第一性原理GW-Bethe-Salpeter方程（GW-BSE）计算构建真实的激子多体哈密顿量；以WS₂-石墨烯范德华异质结构为原型，引入晶格无序（lattice disorder）；分析能量分辨的谱关联（energy-resolved spectral correlations）及多体振子强度（oscillator strength）的统计涨落。

Result: 发现无序驱动系统从规则动力学经不完全混沌（non-ergodicity）向完全混沌（ergodic）的交叉；无序诱导的电子平带（electronic flat bands）催化谷混合（valley mixing），打破近似谷对称性（valley symmetry），使系统进入完全混沌遍历态；多体振子强度涨落服从Porter-Thomas统计；通过长程谱关联（long-range spectral correlations）估计出激子混合的Thouless时间（Thouless time）。

Conclusion: 激子（excitons）可作为高度可调谐的平台，用于在真实的二维材料中探测多体遍历性（many-body ergodicity）及其光谱学特征。

Abstract: We demonstrate that realistic excitonic many-body Hamiltonians obtained from first-principles GW-Bethe-Salpeter equation calculations can exhibit quantum chaos governed by random-matrix universality. Considering a prototypical van der Waals heterostructure (WS$_2$-graphene), with and without lattice disorder, we analyze their energy-resolved spectral correlations and identify a disorder-driven crossover from regular to complete chaotic dynamics. We show that while pristine samples exhibit incomplete chaos (non-ergodicity) due to an approximate valley symmetry that restricts excitonic mixing, the presence of disorder-induced electronic flat bands act as a catalyst for valley mixing to drive the system into a fully developed chaotic (ergodic) regime with reduced symmetry. Crucially, fluctuations in many-body oscillator strengths are shown to follow universal Porter-Thomas statistics, directly linking the underlying quantum chaos and experimentally accessible optical observables. Finally, by examining long-range spectral correlations, we estimate the Thouless time associated to excitonic mixing across the entire many-body bandwidth. Our results establish excitons as a highly tunable platform for probing many-body ergodicity and its spectroscopic signatures in realistic interacting 2D materials.

### [85] [Emergent $\mathbb{Z}$-type topology in a quasi-one-dimensional extended QWZ model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03401)
*Zebedeus F. Osseweijer,Lumen Eek,Cristiane Morais Smith*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文研究Qi-Wu-Zhang（QWZ）模型及其扩展模型中纳米带的零维拓扑端态，发现纳米带的实空间几何结构可导致额外手征对称性出现，使有效一维系统从D类提升至BDI类，并揭示了边缘 termination 和宽度奇偶效应对拓扑分类的重要影响。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 使用 Qi-Wu-Zhang（QWZ）模型及其包含长程耦合的扩展模型描述纳米带系统；通过分析纳米带的长度方向（long）和末端（end）终止方式，结合实空间几何中的轨道与空间变换，识别出具有手征对称性（chiral symmetry）的额外对称性；并推导有限宽度纳米带的拓扑相边界解析表达式，利用 $\mathbb{Z}_2$ 不变量和缠绕数（winding number）刻画杂化能隙相。

Result: 额外对称性的存在同时依赖于纳米带的长度方向和末端终止方式，且表现出关于纳米带宽度的奇偶效应（even-odd effect）；常规矩形纳米带是一个特殊的高对称性情况。在传统QWZ模型中，可得到有限宽度纳米带拓扑相边界的解析解；扩展QWZ模型支持具有多个拓扑端态和更高缠绕数的相，这些相可通过来自高陈数（higher-Chern-number）体相的多重边缘态杂化等机制产生。

Abstract: We investigate the emergence of zero-dimensional topological end states in nanoribbons described by the Qi-Wu-Zhang (QWZ) model and its extensions with longer-range couplings. While dimensional reduction from two to one dimension is often assumed to preserve the symmetry classification of the parent system, here an additional symmetry can emerge originating from the real-space geometry of the ribbon. This symmetry acts as a chiral symmetry, combining orbital and spatial transformations, and promotes the effective one-dimensional system from symmetry class D to class BDI. We demonstrate that the existence of such a symmetry depends both on the long and end termination of the ribbon and exhibits an even-odd effect with respect to ribbon width, revealing that the commonly studied rectangular ribbons constitute a special high-symmetry case. For the conventional QWZ model, we derive analytic expressions for the topological phase boundaries of finite-width nanoribbons and characterize the resulting hybridization-gap phases through ($\mathbb{Z}_2 $) and winding-number invariants. We further show that extended QWZ models with longer-range couplings support phases with multiple topological end states and higher winding numbers. These phases arise through distinct mechanisms, including the hybridization of multiple edge modes inherited from higher-Chern-number bulk phases. Our results demonstrate that both long and end termination can fundamentally alter the topological classification of confined Chern insulators, highlighting the interplay between crystalline geometry, emergent symmetries, and dimensional reduction.

### [86] [Evidence of length scale effect in contact electrification in conducting thin film heterostructures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03428)
*Paul C. Lou,Ravindra G. Bhardwaj,Anand Katailiha,W. P. Beyermann,Sandeep Kumar*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文实验证明在坡莫合金与重掺杂p-Si构成的异质结构系统中，由于挠曲电（flexoelectricity）介导的接触起电（contact electrification），会产生长度尺度效应（length scale effect）：材料厚度不同时，界面电荷扩散深度不同（400 nm厚样品中电荷穿透整个厚度，2 μm厚样品中仅扩散至界面以下51 nm），该效应还可诱导p-Si层发生金属-绝缘体转变（metal-insulator transition）。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 选用坡莫合金（permalloy）与重掺杂p-Si构成的异质结构系统，通过实验观测不同厚度（400 nm 和 2 μm）p-Si样品中接触起电引发的层间电荷转移与扩散深度。

Abstract: Contact electrification between two conducting materials is expected to exhibit length scale effect because the screening effect will diminish in conductors as a function of material dimensions. As a consequence, the interfacial charge accumulation will diffuse away from interface/surface to a critical penetration depth as a function of material dimension. This work experimentally demonstrates the length scale effect in a permalloy and degenerately doped p-Si heterostructure system due to the flexoelectricity mediated contact electrification. The contact electrification induced interlayer charge transfer is observed through the whole thickness in case of 400 nm thick p-Si samples. Whereas, the charge carrier diffuses to a depth of 51 nm from the interface in case of 2 um thick Si. The length scale effect also leads to metal-insulator transition in p-Si layers in both cases. These results present a new opportunity to tailor the physical properties in conducting materials using contact electrification.

</details>


### [87] [Graphene Electric Double-Layer Transistors for Enhanced-Sensitivity Label-Free Detection of Human Serum Albumin](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03491)
*Arslan Liaquat,Ghassem Baridi,Federico Rapuzzi,Daniele Goldoni,Vito Clerico,El Hadj Abidi,Yahya Moubarak Meziani,Mario Amado,Enrique Diez,Naveen Kumar,Camilia Coletti,Beatrice Cipriani,Hender Lopez,Giorgia Brancolini,Leonardo Martini,Luigi Rovati,Francesco Rossella*

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于石墨烯（graphene）电解质栅控场效应晶体管（EGFET）的免标记、实时人血清白蛋白（HSA）检测方法，在非法拉第（non-Faradaic）模式下利用电双层（EDL）的高界面电容将静电扰动转换为电导调制；结合布朗动力学（Brownian Dynamics）模拟揭示吸附取向与界面电荷分布机制，实现0.0087 mg mL⁻¹的检测限和可逆操作，为石墨烯生物电子器件中的无序介导输运机制提供了新见解。

Conclusion: 液栅石墨烯EGFET可作为定量蛋白质传感的有前景平台，并为石墨烯生物电子器件中无序介导的输运机制提供了深入理解。

Abstract: Accurate detection of human serum albumin (HSA) is essential for the early diagnosis and monitoring of renal and hepatic disorders. We present a graphene-based electrolyte-gated field-effect transistor (EGFET) for label-free, real-time quantification of HSA under non-Faradaic operation. Devices exploit the high interfacial capacitance of the electric double layer (EDL) to transduce electrostatic perturbations induced by albumin adsorption into measurable conductance modulation. Negatively charged HSA molecules induce systematic modulation of the graphene channel, producing a concentration-dependent displacement of the Dirac voltage consistent with p-type doping. To establish a molecular-level interpretation of the sensing response, Brownian Dynamics simulations show that HSA adsorbs onto graphene through multiple adsorption orientations associated with heterogeneous interfacial charge distributions and variable dipole alignments relative to the surface. Adsorption is energetically stabilized by van der Waals interactions. Analysis of transfer characteristics across concentrations ranging from 0.01 to 30mgmL-1 reveals a correlation between surface charge density and carrier transport modulation within the electric double layer. Optimized devices exhibit a limit of detection of 0.0087 mg mL-1 and a linear dynamic range extending to 10 mg mL-1. The response remains non-Faradaic under sub-volt operation with reversible and reproducible behavior. The use of an inverse-mobility analytical metric highlights the role of disorder-enhanced carrier scattering in signal amplification, enabling sensitive electrostatic detection while preserving reversible device operation. These results establish liquid-gated graphene EGFETs as a promising platform for quantitative protein sensing and provide insight into disorder-mediated transport mechanisms in graphene bioelectronic devices.

### [88] [Robustness of quantized Hall resistivity under cavity coupling at zero temperature](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03511)
*Juan Román-Roche,Jie Wang,Michael Ruggenthaler,Angel Rubio,Vasil Rokaj*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期实验发现电磁腔中的强光-物质耦合可通过形成朗道极化子（Landau polaritons）改变量子霍尔系统的输运性质，这引发了关于拓扑保护（topological protection）鲁棒性的疑问。早期理论虽表明霍尔电导率在有限温度和有限极化子寿命下可被修改，但实验主要探测的是电阻率张量，因此需要澄清两者在强耦合条件下的差异。

Method: 采用唯象模型（phenomenological model）研究量子霍尔系统在强光-物质相互作用下的电导率与电阻率行为，特别关注极化子展宽（polariton broadening）对两者的影响。

Result: 模型显示电导率与电阻率之间存在不对称性（asymmetry）：在零温下，霍尔电阻率（Hall resistivity）完全不受空腔诱导的极化子展宽引起的修正，且这一免疫性与光-物质耦合强度无关；而霍尔电导率则可能被修改。

Conclusion: 结果解释了为何在低温下通过霍尔电阻率探测偶数量子霍尔平台时，冯·克利青常数（von Klitzing constant）不出现重整化（renormalization）；同时阐明了耗散与强光-物质耦合在混合光-物质系统中的不同作用。

Abstract: Recent experiments have shown that strong light-matter coupling in electromagnetic cavities can modify transport properties of quantum Hall systems through the formation of Landau polaritons, prompting questions about the robustness of topological protection. While earlier theory demonstrated that the Hall conductivity can be modified at finite temperature and finite polariton lifetime (or finite broadening), experiments primarily probe the resistivity tensor. Our phenomenological model reveals an asymmetry between conductivity and resistivity in quantum Hall systems under strong light-matter interaction, showing that at zero temperature the Hall resistivity remains completely immune to cavity-induced modifications arising from polariton broadening, independent of the light-matter coupling strength. These results provide a deeper explanation for the absence of renormalization in the von Klitzing constant in experiments probing the even QH plateaus through the Hall resistivity at low temperature, and clarify the distinct roles of dissipation and strong light-matter coupling in hybrid light-matter systems.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于连续平移不变系统的对称性分析，引入二维狄拉克材料中的非均匀应变（nonuniform strain），通过长波赝规范场（pseudo-gauge field）提供横向动量转移，将OAM二向色性分解为非局域弹光张量（nonlocal elasto-optic tensor）与涡旋横向相位流（vortex transverse phase current）和应变场的重叠积分。

Conclusion: 连续平移不变系统无法产生OAM二向色性，即使考虑光学非局域性（optical nonlocality）和多极光-物质耦合（multipole light-matter coupling）也是如此；但二维狄拉克材料中的应变工程可有效绕过这一限制，实现可测量的OAM二向色性效应。

Abstract: Vortex light carries orbital angular momentum (OAM) in its transverse phase, unlike spin, which is encoded in polarization. We show that this phase cannot produce OAM dichroism in any continuously translation-invariant system, even when optical nonlocality and multipole light--matter coupling are included. Nonuniform strain in a two-dimensional Dirac material bypasses this no-go condition by supplying transverse momentum transfer through a long-wavelength pseudo-gauge field, so that the OAM dichroism factorizes into a nonlocal elasto-optic tensor and the overlap of the vortex transverse phase current with the strain field. For a micron-scale Gaussian bubble, the resonant OAM-odd conductivity reaches \(\sim10^{-3}e^2/\hbar\), within reach of differential optical measurements.

### [90] [Hybrid-order nonlinear topological phases](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03678)
*Yu-Peng Ma,Ming-Jian Gao,Jun-Hong An*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该论文通过提出辅助系统形式化方法（auxiliary-system formalism），解决了非线性系统中体-边界对应（bulk-boundary correspondence, BBC）不明确的问题，建立了多能带体-边界对应，并通过堆叠工程在三维体系中实现了不同阶数（first-order、second-order、third-order）的混合阶拓扑相。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 线性系统中的体-边界对应（bulk-boundary correspondence, BBC）已得到充分理解，但在非线性系统中，多能带拓扑（multigap topologies）使BBC变得模糊且拓扑描述困难，因此需要在非线性系统中建立明确的拓扑分类框架。

Method: 发展了一种辅助系统形式化方法（auxiliary-system formalism），用于对非线性特征值系统（nonlinear-eigenvalue systems）进行拓扑分类；通过将二维系统沿第三维堆叠（stacking），研究了均匀堆叠（uniform stacking）和二聚化堆叠（dimerized stacking）两种方式下的拓扑相实现。

Result: 在二维情形下，两个固定特征值可支持第一阶无间隙边界模式（first-order gapless boundary modes）和第二阶角模式（second-order corner modes）。均匀堆叠时，角态转变为沿z轴的铰链态（hinge states）得到三维二阶相，无间隙边界态转变为侧表面态（side-surface states）得到三维一阶相。二聚化堆叠时，这些态分别被进一步限制在z轴两端形成三维三阶相，或局域在铰链处形成三维二阶相。

Conclusion: 建立了多能带体-边界对应（multiband bulk-boundary correspondence），并将堆叠工程（stacking engineering）识别为在非线性系统中探索混合阶拓扑相（hybrid-order topological phases）的通用平台。

Abstract: The bulk-boundary correspondence (BBC), which relates topological invariants to boundary modes, is well understood for linear systems but remains an open question in the presence of nonlinearity, where multigap topologies make the BBC obscure and the topological description troublesome. We address this by developing an auxiliary-system formalism that enables topological classification of nonlinear-eigenvalue systems. In the two-dimension (2D) case, we show that two fixed eigenvalues can harbor first-order gapless boundary modes and second-order corner modes. Stacking this 2D system along the third dimension (3D) reveals distinct hybrid-order realizations. Under uniform stacking, the corner states in the $xy$ plane transform into hinge states along the $z$ axis, yielding a 3D second-order phase, while the gapless boundary states become side-surface states, yielding a 3D first-order phase. For dimerized stacking, these states are further confined to the two ends of the $z$ axis, yielding a 3D third-order phase, and localized at the hinges, yielding a 3D second-order phase. Our results establish a multiband bulk-boundary correspondence and identify stacking engineering as a versatile platform for exploring hybrid-order topological phases in nonlinear systems.

### [91] [Graph-Based Kirchhoff Modeling of Non-Ohmic Electron Transport in Self-Assembled Nanonecklace Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03698)
*Obed Issakah,Srivathsan Badrinarayanan,Ravi F. Saraf,Janghoon Ock*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本研究通过构建基于图（graph）的基尔霍夫框架（Kirchhoff framework），模拟自组装金纳米项链网络（gold nanonecklace networks）中的集体库仑阻塞输运（collective Coulomb-blockade transport），成功复现了实验中观测到的非线性电流-电压（I-V）响应，并系统揭示了激活电压统计分布、网络密度与结构拓扑对宏观输运行为的影响机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 金纳米项链网络因集体库仑阻塞输运产生的非线性I-V特性，在单电子开关、化学传感与生物门控器件中具有重要应用前景。然而，由于实验测量通常仅限于网络拓扑与全局I-V响应，其宏观行为的微观机制尚不明确。

Method: 提出一个基于图的基尔霍夫框架，将自组装纳米项链网络表示为图结构，其中节点对应项链段之间的结（junction），边对应导电段本身。求解器返回每个施加偏压下的激活节点、导电子图、节点电势与边电流，并允许独立变化激活电压统计分布、网络密度和结构拓扑。

Result: 模型复现了实验中观测到的非欧姆响应，即 $I \propto (V-V_T)^ζ$，表明该行为源于阈值结的集体交错激活与电压驱动的导电子图逾渗（percolation）。独立参数扫描显示：平均激活电压平移阈值 $V_T$ 但几乎不影响 $ζ$；增加网络密度使 $ζ$ 从约1.9升至3.1并增强电流；在固定密度与节点特性下，拓扑仍可调控响应。

Conclusion: 以上趋势与实验观测定性吻合，建立了该模型作为工程设计工具，用于调控自组装纳米项链器件中的集体输运行为。

Abstract: Gold nanonecklace networks are promising platforms for single-electron switching, chemical sensing, and biogating devices because of their nonlinear current--voltage ($I$--$V$) characteristics arising from collective Coulomb-blockade transport. However, the mechanisms governing this macroscopic behavior remain poorly understood because experimental measurements are generally limited to the network topology and global $I$--$V$ response. To address this, we developed a graph-based Kirchhoff framework that represents a self-assembled nanonecklace network as a graph, with nodes corresponding to junctions between necklace segments and edges to the conducting segments themselves. The solver returns the active nodes, conducting subgraph, nodal potentials, and edge currents at each applied bias, while allowing the activation-voltage statistics, network density, and structural topology to be varied independently. The model reproduces the experimentally observed non-Ohmic response, $I \propto (V-V_T)^ζ$, and shows that this behavior emerges from the collective, staggered activation of threshold junctions and voltage-driven percolation of the conducting subgraph. Independent parameter sweeps reveal that the mean activation voltage shifts the threshold $V_T$ while leaving $ζ$ nearly unchanged, increasing network density raises $ζ$ from approximately 1.9 to 3.1 and enhances current, and topology controls the response even at fixed density and node characteristics. These trends agree qualitatively with experimental observations and establish the model as a design tool for engineering collective transport in self-assembled nanonecklace devices.

Abstract: Antiferromagnets offer a promising route toward robust spintronic devices because of their compensated magnetic order and exchange-enhanced spin dynamics. Here, we demonstrate a spin-orbit torque (SOT)-driven antiferromagnetic oscillator based on a nanoconstriction patterned from a synthetic antiferromagnet (SAF). Spin-rectification spectroscopy reveals electrical excitation of both acoustic and optical SAF eigenmodes, whose field and frequency dependences are quantitatively described by an antiferromagnetic resonance model. In addition to these linear eigenmodes, we observe low-field spin-rectification peaks that emerge only above a threshold DC current near the spin-flop transition. Their current-polarity-dependent sign and locking to an injected RF frequency provide electrical spin-rectification signatures consistent with current-selected chiral self-oscillatory dynamics. Micromagnetic simulations reproduce the threshold excitation of SOT-driven self-oscillations and injection locking, while macrospin simulations predict stable and chaotic nonlinear dynamics within the same spin-flop region. We interpret the multi-peak, weakly RF-frequency-dependent responses as a qualitative signature of complex nonlinear dynamics. These results establish SAF nanoconstrictions as an experimentally accessible platform for studying current-driven antiferromagnetic-like oscillator dynamics and motivate future work on nonlinear spintronic devices for signal processing and reservoir-computing concepts.

### [93] [Nonlinear Hall effect in Floquet-driven monolayer 1T$'$-MoS$_2$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03717)
*Muhammad Faisal,Muzamil Shah,Imtiaz Khan,Reza Asgari*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过Floquet有效哈密顿量和非线性半经典输运理论，研究Floquet驱动下单层1T'-MoS₂中的非线性霍尔效应，展示了离共振圆偏振光可通过光致拓扑相变控制非线性霍尔响应的符号和幅度，并指出该响应符号是Floquet工程拓扑的普适输运特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索在低对称性量子自旋霍尔材料单层1T'-MoS₂中，无需应变或三角翘曲即可存在的本征贝里曲率偶极子（Berry-curvature dipole）所产生的非线性霍尔效应，并研究利用Floquet驱动光场对该效应进行拓扑调控的可能性。

Method: 采用Floquet有效哈密顿量（Floquet effective Hamiltonian）和非线性半经典输运理论（nonlinear semiclassical transport theory），分析离共振圆偏振光驱动下的贝里曲率（Berry curvature）及贝里曲率偶极子（Berry-curvature dipole）演化。

Result: 发现各向异性晶体对称性强制贝里曲率偶极子分量D_x≡0，而有限D_y源于本征能带倾斜（band tilt）。Floquet驱动逐次反转单个自旋-谷（spin-valley）扇区，导致贝里曲率在动量空间重构，且每次体带隙闭合时非线性霍尔电导与贝里曲率偶极子同步发生符号反转；而调节能带倾斜仅改变响应幅度，不改变符号。

Conclusion: 非线性霍尔响应的符号是Floquet拓扑相变（Floquet topological phase transition）的明确输运标识；单层1T'-MoS₂可作为全电学探测非平衡拓扑相（nonequilibrium topological phases）的可行平台，且驱动强度、垂直电场、费米能及温度均可作为调控手段。

Abstract: We study the nonlinear Hall effect in Floquet-driven monolayer \(1T'\)-MoS\(_2\), a low-symmetry quantum spin Hall material whose tilted Dirac bands sustain an intrinsic Berry-curvature dipole without the need for strain or trigonal warping. We show that off-resonant circularly polarized light offers a way to control both the sign and the magnitude of the nonlinear Hall response through optically induced topological phase transitions using a Floquet effective Hamiltonian and nonlinear semiclassical transport theory. We show that the anisotropic crystal symmetry enforces a selection rule in which the Berry-curvature dipole elements satisfy $D_x\equiv0$, while a finite $D_y$ originates from the intrinsic band tilt. The Berry curvature is recreated in momentum space as the Floquet drive successively inverts individual spin-valley sectors, resulting in an identical sign reversal of the nonlinear Hall conductivity and the Berry-curvature dipole at each bulk gap closing. In contrast, tuning the band tilt modifies only the magnitude of the response without changing its sign, establishing the observed sign reversal as an unambiguous transport signature of genuine Floquet topological phase transitions. We further show that the nonlinear Hall response can be controlled by the driving strength, perpendicular electric field, Fermi energy, and temperature, providing multiple experimental knobs for observation. Our findings establish the sign of the nonlinear Hall response as a universal transport fingerprint of Floquet-engineered topology and point to monolayer \(1T'\)-MoS\(_2\) as a viable platform for all-electrical detection of nonequilibrium topological phases.

### [95] [Phase-Factor-Controlled Interaction and Bonding between a Chiral Bobber and a Skyrmion String in the Conical Phase](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04266)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用三维微磁学模拟，计算局域松弛约束能量景观作为bobber-斯格明子弦间距R和表面相位因子φ₀的函数。

Result: 改变φ₀能定性重塑相互作用，产生排斥、吸引和键合类三种形态，这些形态无法简化为常规的仅与距离相关的势能。实空间分析表明，该行为源于相位依赖的非轴对称外层畸变壳（outer distortion shells）重构。该相位控制的相互作用在有限磁场范围内持续存在，并遵循锥形态抗磁织构预期的顶-底相位关系。

Conclusion: 锥形态中的传播方向——常在投影或厚度平均描述中被忽略——是斯格明子弦与有限长度手性织构（如手性bobber）之间相互作用中一个此前未被充分认识的自由度。

Abstract: Skyrmion interactions govern the formation of skyrmion lattices, clusters, and particle-like growth patterns. In contrast, the interaction between a chiral bobber and a skyrmion string remains largely unexplored, despite the role of bobbers as intermediate states in skyrmion-string formation and annihilation. Here we show that this interaction is intrinsically phase dependent in the conical phase. Using three-dimensional micromagnetic simulations, we compute the locally relaxed constrained energy landscape as a function of the bobber--skyrmion separation $R$ and the surface phase factor $φ_0$. We find that changing $φ_0$ qualitatively reshapes the interaction, producing repulsive, attractive, and bonding-like regimes that cannot be reduced to a conventional distance-dependent potential. Real-space analysis shows that this behavior originates from phase-dependent reconstruction of nonaxisymmetric outer distortion shells. The phase-controlled interaction persists over a finite field range and follows the expected top--bottom phase relation of surface-sensitive conical textures. These results identify the conical phase direction, often hidden in projected or thickness-averaged descriptions, as a previously underappreciated degree of freedom in the interaction between skyrmion strings and finite-length chiral textures, as demonstrated here for chiral bobbers.

### [96] [Quasi-two-dimensional Majorana zero modes from finite-size-coupled chiral hinge states](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04358)
*Wenhao Liang,Xun-Jiang Luo*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过理论模型研究，提出在准二维手性高阶拓扑绝缘体（HOTI）中，利用常规s波超导体的近邻效应实现空间分离的马约拉纳零模（MZMs），并证明其可形成具有马约拉纳角模的二阶拓扑超导体，且这些角模在弱到中等强度无序下保持鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 作者基于理论模型，将三维手性高阶拓扑绝缘体（higher-order topological insulator, HOTI）沿x方向约束、沿y方向展开、沿z方向有限，使z方向手性铰链态（chiral hinge states）杂化形成一维螺旋通道（helical channels）；随后引入常规s波超导体的近邻效应（superconducting proximity effect），在这些螺旋通道中诱导出有效p波配对，从而打开拓扑能隙。

Result: 在全开放边界条件下，系统在四个螺旋通道端点各产生一个局域化的马约拉纳零模，构成二阶拓扑超导体（second-order topological superconductor）的马约拉纳角模；在三维情形中，超导配对产生扩展的马约拉纳铰链态。无序计算表明，在激发能隙保持打开的条件下，这些马约拉纳角模对弱到中等强度无序具有鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 有限尺寸耦合的手性铰链态为通过常规超导近邻效应工程化多个马约拉纳零模提供了一条有前景的实现路径。

Abstract: Majorana zero modes (MZMs) in topological superconductors have attracted broad research interest for their potential applications in topological quantum computation. In this work, we propose a quasi-two-dimensional route to realize spatially separated MZMs in a chiral higher-order topological insulator (HOTI) proximitized by a conventional $s$-wave superconductor through a theoretical model study. In three dimensions, the chiral HOTI hosts gapless hinge states along the $z$ direction, arising from a mass term that anisotropically gaps the surface Dirac cones of a topological insulator. By confining the sample along the $x$ direction while keeping it extended along $y$ and finite along $z$, opposite $z$-directed chiral hinge states hybridize and effectively form one-dimensional helical channels. Incorporating the superconducting proximity effect into this quasi-two-dimensional system induces effective $p$-wave pairing in these helical channels, thereby opening a topological gap. A fully open-boundary sample then hosts four localized MZMs, one at each endpoint of the helical channels, realizing a second-order topological superconductor characterized by Majorana corner modes. In addition to MZMs, we also find that superconducting pairing in this model produces extended Majorana hinge modes in three dimensions. Furthermore, representative disorder calculations indicate that these Majorana corner modes are robust against weak-to-moderate disorder, provided the excitation gap remains open. These results establish finite-size-coupled chiral hinge states as a promising platform for engineering multiple MZMs via conventional superconducting proximity effect.

### [97] [Quantum Geometric Friedel Oscillations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04654)
*Xing-Lei MA,Jinchao Zhao,Bo-Qing Wu,K. T. Law*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出量子几何弗里德尔振荡（QGFOs），指出当布洛赫波函数具有非平庸量子几何时，传统弗里德尔振荡理论不再完整。在费米能级处存在（近）平带的金属中，量子度量（quantum metric）诱导出一种新型振荡，其周期由平带量子度量热点的动量空间间隔决定，衰减长度由量子度量长度设定，且可在远高于平带带宽的温度下持续存在，体现了量子度量保护效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统弗里德尔振荡理论假设杂质诱导的实空间电荷密度振荡周期仅由费米动量决定，但该理论在布洛赫波函数携带非平庸量子几何时是不完整的。本文旨在揭示量子几何对弗里德尔振荡的修正，并探索一种新的振荡模式。

Method: 论文通过理论分析，研究在费米能级处具有孤立（近）平带的金属体系，考虑布洛赫波函数的量子几何效应，推导出量子度量诱导的弗里德尔振荡，即量子几何弗里德尔振荡（QGFOs）。分析其周期、衰减长度与量子度量热点间距、量子度量长度等几何量的关系。

Result: QGFOs的周期由平带量子度量热点（quantum metric hot spots）的动量空间间距决定，而非费米动量。传统振荡与QGFOs在低温下共存；高温下传统振荡被热效应抹除，而QGFOs的衰减长度由量子度量长度（quantum metric length）设定，可在远高于平带带宽的温度下持续，且在宽温度范围内与温度无关。

Conclusion: 量子度量诱导出新型弗里德尔振荡，QGFOs的测量可作为探测量子度量长度和量子度量热点间距的有效手段，这些量分别与量子度量的积分及其在动量空间的分布相关。

Abstract: In conventional Friedel oscillations, the real-space charge density oscillations induced by an impurity are characterized by an oscillation period set by the Fermi momentum. In this work, we show that the conventional theory is incomplete when the Bloch wavefunctions carry nontrivial quantum geometry. We demonstrate that in metals with an isolated (nearly) flat band at the Fermi energy, quantum geometry induces a distinct type of oscillations, which we call the \emph{quantum geometric Friedel oscillations} (QGFOs). The period of the QGFOs is set by the momentum space separation of the quantum metric hot spots of the flat band. The conventional and quantum metric-induced oscillations coexist at low temperatures. At higher temperatures, the conventional Friedel oscillations away from the impurity site are set by the thermal length such that the oscillations can be easily washed out by temperature effects. Remarkably, the QGFOs decay length is set by the quantum metric length which is defined by the integration of the quantum metric of the flat band. As a result, the QGFOs can persist even at temperatures much larger than the bandwidth of the flat band. Moreover, the decay length is independent of temperature for a wide range of temperatures which is a manifestation of the quantum metric protection. In conclusion, we show that the quantum metric induces novel Friedel oscillations. Our work suggests that the measurement of the QGFOs is a powerful way to detect the quantum metric length (which is associated with the integral of the quantum metric) and the quantum metric hot spot separations (which are associated with the distribution of the quantum metric in the momentum space).

</details>


### [98] [Tunable Nonlinear Landscapes in Graphene Nanoelectromechanical Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04724)
*Ateesh K. Rathi,Rajan Singh,Javed A. Mondal,Arnab Sarkar,Ryan J. T. Nicholl,Kirill I. Bolotin,Saikat Ghosh*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在悬浮单层石墨烯鼓中施加栅极电压以打破膜的面外对称性（out-of-plane symmetry），将基频弯曲模（fundamental flexural mode）调谐至与二倍频高阶模形成1:2内共振（internal resonance），利用两模间的二次耦合产生整数高次谐波；进一步增大驱动后形成致密频率梳（frequency comb），并通过反向倍周期转变（reverse period-doubling transition）改变梳齿间距和线密度。

Result: 实验观测到相位锁定的整数高次谐波序列，增大驱动后发展为致密频率梳；进一步增加驱动出现反向倍周期转变，梳齿间距加倍、线密度减半、偶数阶梳齿能量回流。从测量光谱中提取了膜的二阶非线性系数ζ（quadratic coefficient）和三阶非线性系数β（cubic coefficient）。

Conclusion: 石墨烯的可调非线性景观（tunable nonlinear landscape）可按需支持不同的动力学区域，单个栅控器件可依次充当倍频器（frequency multiplier）、宽带梳源（broadband comb source）和混沌发生器（chaotic generator）。

Abstract: Nonlinear nanomechanical resonators give convenient solid-state access to classical analogs of extreme nonlinear optics and to phononic signal processing. Here we report integer high-harmonic generation and phononic frequency combs in a suspended monolayer graphene drum. A gate voltage breaks the out-of-plane symmetry of the membrane and tunes its fundamental flexural mode onto a 1:2 internal resonance with a higher mode at twice the frequency, where the quadratic coupling between the two modes becomes large. A single drive tone then generates phase-locked integer harmonics in sequence, and at larger drive these fill in to a dense frequency comb. Raising the drive further, we find a reverse period-doubling transition: the comb spacing doubles, the line density halves, and energy flows back into the even-order comb lines. The measured spectra yield the quadratic ($ζ$) and cubic ($β$) nonlinear coefficients of the membrane. These results show how the tunable nonlinear landscape of graphene supports distinct dynamical regimes on demand, allowing a single gated device to act in turn as a frequency multiplier, a broadband comb source, and a chaotic generator.

### [99] [Observation of Non-linear hall effect in Polycrystalline magnetic multilayes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04754)
*Preet Kamal,Chirag kalouni,Amiya Mondal,Awadesh Narayan,Debangsu Roy*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文报道在重/铁磁体（heavy-metal/ferromagnet）多晶多层膜中观察到稳健的非线性霍尔效应（nonlinear Hall effect, NLHE），该效应从2K延伸至室温，且由本征贝里曲率偶极子（Berry curvature dipole）主导，从而将NLHE材料体系从范德华（van der Waals）系统拓展至可规模化、工业兼容的薄膜自旋电子学（thin-film spintronics）架构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用溅射沉积（sputter-deposited）的多晶磁性多层膜，测量二次谐波横向电压并排除频率、外加垂直磁场及三次谐波（third-harmonic）响应的影响；通过二次霍尔电导率与纵向电导率的标度分析（scaling analysis）区分内禀与外在贡献，并结合第一性原理密度泛函理论（DFT）计算进行理论验证。

Result: 观测到从2 K到室温均存在的稳健NLHE；二次谐波横向电压与激发频率和外加垂直磁场无关，且三次谐波响应极小，排除量子度量（quantum-metric）主导；标度分析识别出与电导率无关的项，证实其为内禀的Berry curvature dipole贡献；理论计算与实验结果一致。

Conclusion: 溅射沉积多晶薄膜是首个经工程化验证的、可驱动Berry curvature dipole非线性霍尔输运的磁性多层膜平台，将NLHE材料研究从范德华系统扩展至可规模化、工业兼容的薄膜自旋电子学体系，适用于高频整流和非线性传感器。

Abstract: The Nonlinear Hall effect(NLHE) driven principally by the Berry curvature dipole has been established in non-centrosymmetric vander Waals crystals, topological semimetals, and moiré superlattices, but its extension to technologically mature heavy-metal/ferromagnet multilayer platforms remains largely unexplored. Here, we report the observation of a robust NLHE in polycrystalline magnetic multilayers, persisting from 2 K to room temperature. The second-harmonic transverse voltage is independent of both excitation frequency and applied out-of-plane magnetic field, while the vanishingly small third-harmonic response confirms that the observed signal is not dominated by a quantum-metric contribution and instead reflects a genuine second-order electronic response. A scaling analysis of the second-order Hall conductivity against the longitudinal conductivity identifies a dominant, conductivity-independent term establishing the intrinsic berry curvature dipole. Our theoretical analysis, supported by first-principles DFT calculations, further satisfies and corroborates the experimental results. These results establish sputter-deposited polycrystalline thin film as the first engineered magnetic multilayer platform for BCD-driven nonlinear Hall transport, extending the NLHE material landscape beyond van der Waals systems into scalable, industry-compatible thin-film spintronic architectures suitable for high frequency rectifications and nonlinear sensors.

### [100] [On the $\mathrm{In_{x}Ga_{1-x}As}$ channel noise in InP HEMTs from 4 K to 300 K](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04757)
*Junjie Li,Justin H. Chen,Austin J. Minnich,Jan Grahn*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 针对沟道铟含量分别为53%、60%和70%的100纳米栅长InP HEMT，在4 K至300 K温度范围内，通过片上测量（40–300 K）和基于LNA的测量（4–40 K）提取等效漏极噪声温度T_d来量化沟道噪声。

Conclusion: InP HEMT中的过剩噪声不仅源于与温度无关的散粒噪声（shot noise），还包括碰撞电离（impact ionization）和实空间转移噪声（real-space transfer noise）。

Abstract: The InP high-electron-mobility transistor (HEMT) is indispensable for low-noise amplifiers (LNAs) in radio astronomy and quantum computing. The composition of the $\mathrm{In_{x}Ga_{1-x}As}$ channel in InP HEMT is known to influence the LNA noise performance. However, the various physical mechanisms responsible for noise generation are not fully characterized and understood. Here, we investigate the $\mathrm{In_{x}Ga_{1-x}As}$ channel noise from 4 K to 300 K for 100-nm gate-length InP HEMTs with channel indium content of 53\%, 60\% and 70\%. Channel noise was quantified by extracting the equivalent drain noise temperature $\mathit{T}_{d}$ using both on-wafer and LNA-based measurements, covering 40-300 K and 4-40 K, respectively. The 60\% indium channel InP HEMT exhibited the lowest channel noise across the full temperature range. The $\mathit{T}_{d}$ extracted from on-wafer characterization was found to obey a parabolic temperature dependence which predicted the $\mathit{T}_{d}$ at 4 K for all InP HEMTs in good agreement with LNA-based measurements. By expressing the channel noise as the sum of one thermal and one excess noise term, it was found that the former increased linearly with ambient temperature and dominated at 300 K. The channel noise at 4 K was determined by the excess noise term and exhibited a non-monotonic dependence on the channel indium content in the InP HEMT. The results suggest that the excess noise in the InP HEMT originates not only from temperature-independent shot noise but also from impact ionization and real-space transfer noise.

### [101] [Strain- and potential-controlled tunneling in monolayer MoS$_2$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04766)
*Hasna Chnafa,Rachid El Aitouni,Clarence Cortes,David Laroze,Ahmed Jellal*

TL;DR: 本文从理论上研究了单层MoS₂在机械应变（mechanical strain）和外标量势（external scalar potential）共同作用下自旋分辨（spin-resolved）和谷分辨（valley-resolved）的量子输运问题，发现应变与静电势的协同作用可实现谷极化（valley polarization）和自旋极化（spin polarization）的高效调控，并提出了一种双旋钮控制方案（dual-knob control scheme）以及静电自旋反转（electrostatic spin inversion）现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 机械应变与外标量势在单层MoS₂中的同时作用尚未被探索，因此本文旨在填补这一空白，研究两者协同对自旋和谷分辨量子输运的影响。

Method: 采用包含内禀自旋-轨道耦合（intrinsic spin–orbit coupling）的有效有质量狄拉克哈密顿量（effective massive Dirac Hamiltonian）进行理论分析，其中应变诱导谷依赖动量偏移（valley-dependent momentum shifts），标量势则调控隧穿谱（tunneling spectrum）。

Result: 应变打破K与K′谷的简并并改变输运特性；标量势引起共振透射、法布里-珀罗干涉（Fabry–Pérot interference）和电导的显著变化。识别出一种双旋钮控制方案：势垒宽度调控电导振荡频率，应变独立控制振荡相位与振幅。还预测了静电自旋反转现象——在有限应变下纯通过栅极调谐实现自旋极化符号反转。

Conclusion: 应变与势能工程为单层MoS₂中的电导及自旋、谷自由度提供了正交且可独立操作的调控机制，为自旋电子学（spintronics）和谷电子学（valleytronics）器件应用展现了前景。

Abstract: We present a theoretical study of spin- and valley-resolved quantum transport in monolayer MoS$_2$ under the combined influence of mechanical strain and an external scalar potential, a combination whose simultaneous unexplored. Within an effective massive Dirac Hamiltonian that incorporates intrinsic spin--orbit coupling, strain induces valley-dependent momentum shifts that lift the degeneracy between the $K$ and $K'$ valleys and strongly modify the transport characteristics. The scalar potential modifies the tunneling spectrum, leading to pronounced changes in resonant transmission, Fabry--Pérot interference, and conductance. We show that the interplay between strain and electrostatic potential enables efficient control of both valley and spin polarization of the transmitted current. In particular, we identify a dual-knob control scheme in which the barrier width governs the frequency of conductance oscillations while strain independently controls their phase and amplitude. Furthermore, we predict electrostatic spin inversion -- a sign reversal of spin polarization achievable purely by gate tuning at finite strain, requiring no geometric reconfiguration. Depending on the strain orientation, the transmission probability and conductance can be selectively suppressed or enhanced, resulting in highly tunable valley- and spin-polarized transport. These findings demonstrate that strain and potential engineering provide orthogonal and independently operable mechanisms for controlling conductance as well as spin and valley degrees of freedom in monolayer MoS$_2$, offering promising prospects for spintronic and valleytronic device applications.

### [102] [Local Defects and the Topology of the Haldane Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04771)
*Vishesh Makwana,Eric Akkermans*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本论文在十重分类（tenfold classification）框架下研究Haldane模型中局部缺陷与拓扑之间的相互作用。通过引入空位缺陷，发现了由$\mathbb{Z}_2$不变量分类的拓扑缺陷态，并识别了三种可实验观测的签名来区分拓扑缺陷态与普通缺陷态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究Haldane模型中局部缺陷（local defects）与拓扑（topology）之间的相互作用，尤其是在十重分类（tenfold classification）框架下，理解空位缺陷如何产生拓扑保护的零能模，并寻找区分拓扑缺陷态与普通缺陷态的实验可观测特征。

Method: 在十重分类框架下分析Haldane模型中的空位缺陷。通过定义$\mathbb{Z}_2$不变量 $\nu = C \cdot m \mod 2$ 来分类缺陷态，其中 $C$ 为陈数（Chern number），$m = N_A - N_B$ 为空位配置的净子晶格不平衡度（net sublattice imbalance）。识别波函数轮廓中的位错特征、分数电荷积累以及概率流方向三种实验签名进行验证。

Result: 空位缺陷可产生由$\mathbb{Z}_2$不变量分类的拓扑缺陷态：奇子晶格不平衡对应受保护的零能模（protected zero-energy mode），偶不平衡则没有。三种实验签名包括：(1) 波函数轮廓中的特征位错；(2) 空位处积累 $e/2$ 分数电荷而普通缺陷（adatom）没有；(3) 空位诱导态的概率流方向与手征边缘态（chiral edge states）相反，类比于$p$-波超导体中涡旋产生的电流反转。

Conclusion: 三种实验签名均与$\mathbb{Z}_2$不变量预测定量一致，为区分拓扑缺陷态与普通缺陷态提供了清晰可实验验证的方案。

Abstract: We investigate the interplay between local defects and topology in the Haldane model within the framework of the tenfold classification. The Haldane model realizes a Chern-insulating phase characterized by an integer topological invariant ($C=\pm 1$) and supports chiral edge states. Introducing vacancies gives rise to localized states at the defect sites, classified by a $\mathbb{Z}_2$ invariant $ν= C\cdot m,\mathrm{mod},2$, where $m=N_A-N_B$ is the net sublattice imbalance of the vacancy configuration: an odd imbalance hosts a protected zero-energy mode, whereas an even imbalance does not. We identify three independent experimental signatures that distinguish these topological defect states from trivial (adatom) defects. First, vacancy-induced states exhibit characteristic dislocations in their wavefunction profiles that track the phase winding associated with the defect. Second, a fractional charge of $e/2$ accumulates at vacancy sites, while no such charge appears at adatoms. Third, the probability current circulating around a vacancy-induced state flows in the opposite direction to that of chiral edge states, in direct analogy with the current reversal produced by a vortex in a $p$-wave superconductor. All three signatures are in quantitative agreement with the $\mathbb{Z}_2$ prediction.

Abstract: In advanced complementary metal-oxide-semiconductor (CMOS) quantum chips, compact gate stacks make it difficult to connect lithographic geometry, electrostatic confinement and many-electron spin filling in one transparent model. This connection is central to design-technology co-optimization (DTCO). Here we develop a reduced-order analytical framework for asymmetric multigate silicon quantum-dot devices. Its electrostatic core, the Poisson-kernel coupled-interface Green-function (PK-GF) model, agrees with an independent finite-volume solution at the millivolt scale for the matched two-dimensional problem, without fitting to that solution. We then pass the gate-derived confinement, rather than a harmonic or fitted potential, to a spin-valley many-body calculation for a jellybean quantum dot with N = 2-17 electrons at B = 5 T. The unrestricted Hartree-Fock (UHF) solution supports occupation-dependent, Wigner-molecule-like charge localization but likely overestimates spin polarization. Complete active-space configuration interaction (CASCI) supports a low-spin branch within the tested active spaces, which aligns with the experiments. The workflow therefore connects CMOS layout, device electrostatics, and potential-determined quantum observables, providing an auditable modelling layer for CMOS-based qubit design and DTCO.

### [104] [Lindblad theory of linear response susceptibility and dispersive readout in minimal Kitaev junctions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04968)

Method: 基于Lindblad主方程（Lindblad master equation）构建线性响应形式，同时捕捉器件的多能级结构、探针读取灵活性以及有限频率响应中的非幺正效应，包括由速率和跳变算符（jump operator）涨落引发的Sisyphus与Hermes动力学磁化率。

Abstract: The field of hybrid superconductor-semiconductor quantum dots is advancing toward the development of functional devices that leverage the advantages of both types of materials. However, the inherent complexity of these devices demands a comprehensive theoretical framework for a complete understanding of their responses to external probes, readout and the dissipation arising from environmental coupling. We present a Lindblad-based linear response formalism that captures the multi-level nature of these devices, their probe-readout flexibility, and the non-unitary effects of finite-frequency response, including the so-called Sisyphus and Hermes dynamical susceptibilities. These arise from fluctuations in the rates and jump operators, and are hence absent in standard Kubo linear response treatments. We exemplify the framework using quantum dot-based Kitaev chain setups which are promising candidates for topologically protected Majorana-based parity qubits. Our results shed light onto the validity of the standard curvature-based approximation for fermionic parity and qubit readout, show that Hermes terms compensate decoherence in dispersive readout and implement important corrections beyond thermalized states.

### [105] [Functionalization of $g$-wave altermagnets: spin-splitter effect enabled by surfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04970)
*Sopheak Sorn*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过紧束缚模型和Kubo形式主义，证明g波交变磁体（altermagnet）的表面可实现d波交变磁性，并产生显著的自旋劈裂效应（spin-splitter effect, SSE），其自旋劈裂角可达15度。该效应源于两表面d波交变磁性的同号叠加，并伴随弱铁磁性，为通过外磁场调控交磁畴及优化SSE功能提供了途径。研究结果支持薄膜工程作为非d波交变磁体功能化的可行策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索g波交变磁体（altermagnet, AM）表面能否实现d波交变磁性，并由此产生体态中不存在的自旋劈裂效应（spin-splitter effect, SSE），旨在为非d波交变磁体的功能化提供新的物理平台。

Method: 采用最小平板模型（minimal slab model），并应用Kubo形式主义（Kubo formalism）计算由纵向电场诱导的横向自旋电流对应的自旋电导率，从而评估自旋劈裂效应（SSE）。

Result: 在平板几何中，表面诱导的d波交变磁性产生了体态中不存在的有限自旋劈裂效应（SSE）；两个表面的d波交变磁性符号相同，导致SSE贡献相加，自旋劈裂角高达15度；该响应伴随表面诱导的弱铁磁性（weak ferromagnetism）。

Conclusion: 表面态与体交变磁序参量之间存在体-边对应关系（bulk-boundary correspondence），其中磁多极矩（magnetic multipolar character）起核心作用；薄膜工程（thin-film engineering）可作为非d波交变磁体功能化的可行策略。

Abstract: We investigate surfaces of a $g$-wave altermagnet(AM) and show that they provide a platform for realizing $d$-wave altermagnetism and the associated spin-splitter functionality. Using the Kubo formalism applied to a minimal slab model, we evaluate the spin-splitter effect(SSE) by computing the spin conductivity corresponding to a transverse spin current induced by a longitudinal electric field. We find a finite SSE, absent in the bulk, that emerges from surface-induced $d$-wave altermagnetism. Strikingly, the sign pattern of the $d$-wave altermagnetism on both surfaces of the slab geometry is identical to each other, leading to additive contributions to SSE from the two surfaces, with a spin-splitter angle reaching up to 15 degrees. In addition, this response is intrinsically linked to an accompanying surface-induced weak ferromagnetism, which potentially enables control of altermagnetic domains via an external magnetic field and provides a route to optimize the SSE functionality. These results can be understood in terms of a bulk-boundary correspondence between surface states and bulk altermagnetic order parameters, where the magnetic multipolar character of the latter plays a central role. Our findings strongly suggest thin-film engineering as a viable strategy to functionalize non-$d$-wave AMs.

### [106] [Coexisting Charge Density Wave and Superconducting Order in Quantizing Magnetic Fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05039)
*Ron Q. Nguyen,Peiyu Qin,Hai-Tian Wu,Sparsh Mishra,Tobias Wolf,Joseph Roll,Erin Morissette,Naiyuan J. Zhang,Sarah Alkidim,Kenji Watanabe,Takashi Taniguchi,Aaron W. Hui,Dima E. Feldman,Allan MacDonald,J. I. A. Li*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 对菱方六层石墨烯（R6G）施加大的位移场以产生可调平带边缘（flat band edges），同时施加强磁场产生近简并的朗道能级流形，通过输运测量观测CDW有序、热滞现象、整数量子霍尔效应及超导相。

Abstract: Charge density wave (CDW) and superconductivity are both common in strongly interacting electron systems. While CDW order is ubiquitous in both quantum Hall systems and unconventional superconductors, superconductivity is generally suppressed by the strong magnetic fields required for Landau quantization. Here we investigate the intertwined CDW and superconducting phases of rhombohedral hexalayer graphene (R6G) in a large displacement field, which generates tunable flat band edges, and a strong magnetic field, which generates a manifold of nearly degenerate Landau levels. CDW order is accompanied by pronounced thermal hysteresis as expected for first-order melting transitions. Surprisingly, we find a series of strong integer quantum Hall effects at magnetic fields above ~2T with Hall conductance quantum numbers that deviate strongly from nearby integer filling factors, an observation that can be explained only by CDW order that mixes many Landau levels. We also find a nearby superconducting phase that is stabilized by perpendicular magnetic fields and persists deep within the quantum Hall regime. The CDW and superconducting phases develop on comparable temperature scales and emerge from the same manifold of strongly mixed Landau levels. These observations provide new insight into the interplay between superconductivity and CDW order in R6G at zero magnetic field.

### [107] [Finite-frequency magnetic common baths in ferromagnetic planar cavities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05066)
*O. J. Kwon*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该论文理论构建了铁磁平面腔中两个自旋探针的有限频率磁共浴模型，通过计算集体衰变核和兰姆移位核，揭示了在GHz探针跃迁与毫开温度下，磁共振线宽分裂可达单自旋散射线宽的三分之二，并为静态TE耦合频移提供了有限频率对应物。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将两个自旋探针耦合至铁磁平面腔的推迟磁格林张量（retarded magnetic Green tensor），通过其虚部和实部分别确定集体衰变核\(γ_{12}\)和兰姆移位核\(Ω_{12}\)；利用横向对角珀尔德磁导率（transverse diagonal Polder permeability）\(μ_\perp(ω,B)\)作为磁输入，在有限厚度标量TE通道中计算上述核函数。

Result: 在\(ω\to0\)极限下，常数反射基准重现静态镜像序列参考解，有限厚度薄膜保留相应的静态TE反射振幅；对200 nm厚Ni类参数薄膜在微米级中隙腔中，GHz探针跃迁取样毫开温度下的体辅助磁储层正频率响应；共振时，在\(ρ=3\,\mathrm{μm}\)处非对角谱线分裂达到单自旋散射线宽的三分之二。

Abstract: We formulate the finite-frequency magnetic common bath of two spin probes in a ferromagnetic planar cavity. The probes couple to the retarded magnetic Green tensor of the cavity, whose imaginary and real parts determine the collective decay kernel \(γ_{12}\) and the Lamb-shift kernel \(Ω_{12}\). We evaluate these kernels for a finite-thickness scalar TE channel formed by a ferromagnetic film on a nonmagnetic conducting substrate, using the transverse diagonal Polder permeability \(μ_\perp(ω,B)\) as the magnetic input. The normalization is fixed by the free-space magnetic-dipole decay rate. In the \(ω\to0\) limit, the constant-reflection benchmark reproduces the static image-series reference, while the finite slab retains the corresponding static TE reflection amplitude. For a \(t=200\,\mathrm{nm}\) film described by a representative Ni-like parameter set in a micron-scale mid-gap cavity, the GHz probe transition samples the positive-frequency response of the body-assisted magnetic reservoir at millikelvin temperature. On resonance, the off-diagonal linewidth splitting reaches about two thirds of the single-spin scattering linewidth at \(ρ=3\,μ\mathrm m\). The resulting linewidth splitting and collective Lamb shift provide finite-frequency counterparts of the static TE coupling-frequency shift.

### [108] [Platinum is a Photocatalyst: Large Visible-Light Quantum Efficiency Revealed](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05172)

Method: 采用定量扫描光电化学显微镜（quantitative scanning photoelectrochemical microscopy），测量Au和Pt纳米岛阵列在TiO2上的波长分辨外量子效率（EQE），并将其反应活性与形貌和消光光谱（extinction spectra）进行关联分析。

Result: 离散的10 nm Pt纳米岛表现出稳健的宽带可见光光活性，在蓝-绿光激发下超过相似尺寸的Au纳米岛；连接状态的Pt纳米岛光活性显著被抑制。Pt在455 nm处的每个原子EQE约为Au的20倍，在595 nm处约为2倍。Pt的内量子效率（IQE）在可见光谱范围内约为1%，且几乎不依赖于波长。

Conclusion: 这些发现将具有强阻尼光学响应（strongly damped optical response）的催化金属重新定位为金属-半导体杂化体系中的光响应组分，挑战了它们在光催化系统中仅作为被动助催化剂（passive co-catalysts）的主流认知。

Abstract: Metal-semiconductor junctions in optoelectronic devices are commonly engineered to promote charge separation. In Pt/TiO2 Schottky junctions, Pt is typically regarded as a catalytic electron sink rather than a visible-light-active component. Here, we demonstrate that Pt nanoislands on TiO2 can generate photochemically active carriers under visible light excitation. Using quantitative scanning photoelectrochemical microscopy, we measure the wavelength-resolved external quantum efficiency (EQE) of Au and Pt nanoisland arrays on TiO2, and correlate their reactivity with their morphology and extinction spectra. Discrete 10 nm Pt nanoislands exhibit robust broadband visible light photoactivity - exceeding the photoactivity of similar-sized Au nanoislands under blue-green excitation - whereas Pt's photoactivity is strongly suppressed when the nanoislands are connected. Surprisingly, Pt exhibits an EQE-per-atom approx. 20 times higher than Au at 455 nm and approx. 2 times higher at 595 nm (at Au's optimum). We show an approximately wavelength-independent Pt internal quantum efficiency of approx. 1 percent across the visible spectral region. These findings reposition catalytic metals with strongly damped optical response in the visible as light-responsive components in metal-semiconductor hybrids, challenging the prevailing perception that they function solely as passive co-catalysts in photocatalytic systems.

</details>


### [109] [Spectral-topology-induced criticality in non-Hermitian fermionic metals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05190)
*Ayan Banerjee,Julius T. Gohsrich,Flore K. Kunst*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过莫尔斯理论（Morse theory）建立非厄米系统（non-Hermitian systems）中复能谱拓扑与多体可观测量之间的统一框架，揭示了非平衡量子临界性（non-equilibrium quantum criticality）的拓扑基础，并发现增益-损耗选择的非平衡稳态会动态生成虚费米面（imaginary Fermi surface），其上的费米点拥有具有对数纠缠标度和代数关联的无标度无能隙模式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非厄米系统本质上处于非平衡态，展现出复能谱、谱缠绕、例外拓扑（exceptional topology）和非幺正动力学等全新现象。核心挑战在于理解复单粒子能谱如何控制普适的多体行为。

Method: 引入一个直接从复能谱导出的对称性保护动力学拓扑指标；利用代拓扑学中的莫尔斯理论（Morse theory），将能谱中的临界点识别为拓扑缺陷，其曲率和稳定性在连续形变下受到保护。

Result: 建立了能谱几何与多体可观测量的联系，统一了非厄米能带拓扑、纠缠和输运。非相互作用系统中的非厄米量子临界性由增益-损耗选择的非平衡稳态控制，该稳态动态生成一个虚费米面，其费米点拥有具有对数纠缠标度（logarithmic entanglement scaling）和代数关联的无标度无能隙模式。

Conclusion: 本工作为非厄米量子物质建立了统一框架，将能谱拓扑与莫尔斯理论联系起来，揭示了非平衡量子临界性的拓扑基础。

Abstract: Quantum matter emerges from the interplay of fluctuations, topology, and entanglement, which - in equilibrium - governs quantized transport, universal criticality, and topological classification. Non-Hermitian systems, widely explored in platforms ranging from electric circuits to photonics, are intrinsically out-of-equilibrium, and display fundamentally new phenomena, including complex spectra, spectral winding, exceptional topology, and non-unitary dynamics. A central challenge is understanding how the complex single-particle spectrum governs universal many-body behavior. We introduce a symmetry-protected dynamical topological index derived directly from the complex spectrum. Through the lens of algebraic topology, more specifically Morse theory, we identify critical points in the spectrum with topological defects, whose curvature and stability are protected under continuous deformations. This links spectral geometry to many-body observables, unifying non-Hermitian band topology, entanglement, and transport. We demonstrate that non-Hermitian quantum criticality in non-interacting systems is controlled by gain-and-loss-selected non-equilibrium steady states, which dynamically generate an emergent imaginary Fermi surface whose Fermi points host scale-invariant gapless modes with logarithmic entanglement scaling and algebraic correlations. Our work establishes a unified framework for non-Hermitian quantum matter, connecting spectral topology to Morse theory, revealing a topological foundation of non-equilibrium quantum criticality.

### [110] [Dielectric function in WSe2](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05371)
*Tiberius O. Cheche,Yia-Chung Chang*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该文发展了一套零温下二维电子气中维格纳晶体（Wigner crystal）的哈特里-福克（Hartree-Fock）能带结构数值方法，计算了自旋守恒通道中的单粒子激发谱，并应用于计算单层WSe2中维格纳晶体态的静态介电函数，为研究低密度二维系统中的屏蔽效应、能带重构和相互作用提供了理论工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为低密度二维电子气中维格纳晶体态的能带结构和介电响应提供第一性原理级别的理论计算工具，填补现有方法在自洽处理相互作用和屏蔽效应方面的不足。

Method: 基于哈特里-福克（Hartree-Fock）近似的数值方法，假设基态为完全自旋极化（fully spin-polarized），在自旋守恒（spin-conserving）通道中计算单粒子激发谱；利用哈特里-福克能带结构和本征函数，通过静态林德哈德型极化率（static Lindhard-type polarizability）得到介电响应。

Result: 成功实现了对二维维格纳晶体能带结构的哈特里-福克数值求解，并以单层WSe2中的维格纳晶体态为例，计算了其静态介电函数 epsilon(q,0)。

Conclusion: 该方法为研究低密度二维系统中的屏蔽、能带重构和相互作用效应提供了理论工具，对未来的相关实验研究具有潜在参考价值。

Abstract: We develop a Hartree-Fock numerical method for computing the band structure of a two-dimensional Wigner crystal in an electron gas at zero temperature. The ground state is assumed to be fully spin-polarized. Single-particle excitation spectra are evaluated in spin-conserving channel. As an application, we use the developed code to compute the static dielectric function epsilon(q,0) of a Wigner-crystal state formed in a two-dimensional transition-metal dichalcogenide, specifically monolayer WSe2. The dielectric response is obtained from the Hartree-Fock band structure and eigenfunctions through a static Lindhard-type polarizability. The method provides a theoretical tool for investigating screening, band-structure reconstruction, and interaction effects in low-density two-dimensional systems, with possible relevance for future experimental studies.
