### [111] [Reentrant localization transition, quantum butterfly and robust edge modes in aperiodic zig-zag ladder](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03954)
*Sayan Bhattacharya,Rhiddha Acharjee,Atanu Nandy*

Main category: cond-mat.other

TL;DR: 该论文研究了准周期性无序的低维紧束缚晶格（tight-binding lattice）中的局域化转变（localization transition），发现通过引入最小长程非对角调制，电子态可重新发生去局域化（delocalization），形成第二次量子相变，并伴随单粒子迁移率边（mobility edge）和多分形（multifractal）能谱等特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 准周期无序的低维紧束缚晶格通常表现出从扩散（diffusive）到局域化（localized）的量子相变，但论文希望探索偏离这一典型情形后，是否能在更复杂的参数条件下重新获得去局域化（delocalization）行为，从而揭示新的量子相变机制。

Method: 通过在紧束缚晶格（tight-binding lattice）中引入最小长程非对角调制（long-range off-diagonal modulation），并在哈密顿量（Hamiltonian）的动力学参数空间中进行组合调节，分析电子态局域化性质的变化。采用逆参与率（inverse participation ratio, IPR）、本征能谱（eigenspectrum）和量子动力学（quantum dynamical）研究来表征局域化转变。

Result: 当长程非对角调制的动力学参数组合适当时，本征谱（eigenspectrum）再次出现电子态的去局域化（delocalization），形成第二次量子相变（quantum phase change）。局域化转变伴随单粒子迁移率边（single-particle mobility edge）的明显存在。多分形（multifractal）能景观（energy landscape）还显示出量子蝴蝶（quantum butterfly）图案，以及带隙内鲁棒的边缘态（in-gap robust edge modes）。

Conclusion: 即使存在强准周期无序，通过合适的长程非对角调制仍可再次诱导出电子态的去局域化（delocalization），表明局域化—去局域化转变（localization-delocalization transition）并非单一过程，而是可以出现二次相变，这为调控量子输运提供了新的可能性。

Abstract: Low dimensional tight-binding lattices in presence of quasiperiodic disorder generally exhibits localization transition. The system supports diffusive modes upto a limiting strength of disorder and all the eigenstates become localized beyond that critical strength thereby quenching the kinetic signature of the wavepacket. However, moving away from this situation, we demonstrate that with minimal long-range off-diagonal modulation, the eigenspectrum again may offer delocalization of electronic states for some subtle combination of kinetic parameters of the Hamiltonian leading to a second quantum phase change. The localization transitions are associated with the obvious presence of single-particle mobility edges. Multifractal energy landscape also shows quantum butterfly pattern with the in-gap robust edge modes. The re-emerging localization transition is manifested through the evaluation of inverse participation ratio, eigenspectrum and a pertinent quantum dynamical study.

</details>


### [112] [Katsura-Nagaosa-Balatsky magnetoelectricity in molecular magnets: Bipartite entanglement transfer by means of rotating electric field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03965)
*Zhirayr Adamyan,Ani Chobanyan,Vadim Ohanyan,Azadeh Ghannadan,Jozef Strecka,Saeed Haddadi,Hamid Arian Zad*

Main category: cond-mat.other

TL;DR: 本文基于Katsura-Nagaosa-Balatsky (KNB)机制，研究自旋-1/2 Heisenberg三聚体在外部磁场和电场中的量子纠缠（quantum entanglement），发现自旋-电场耦合可有效控制双体和三体纠缠，并实现双体纠缠在自旋对之间的可控转移，对称情况下转移近乎理想。该结果表明具有KNB耦合的分子纳米磁体是分子尺度上电控量子纠缠的有前景平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索在分子纳米磁体中通过电场实现量子纠缠（quantum entanglement）的主动控制与操纵的可能性，尤其是利用Katsura-Nagaosa-Balatsky (KNB)机制中自旋诱导电极化（spin-induced electric polarization）与电场的耦合来调控量子关联。

Method: 对自旋-1/2 Heisenberg三聚体（spin-1/2 Heisenberg trimer）施加外磁场和外电场，电场位于磁离子平面内且强度和方向可独立调节；采用Katsura-Nagaosa-Balatsky (KNB)机制描述自旋诱导电极化；分别使用双体负性（bipartite negativity）和多体纠缠度量分析双体与三体纠缠（tripartite entanglement）。

Result: 双体纠缠（bipartite entanglement）可通过电场参数显著增强或抑制；多体纠缠（multipartite entanglement）对微观自旋-电场耦合表现出丰富依赖性。恒定大小的旋转面内电场可诱导双体纠缠在不同自旋对之间可控转移；在均匀交换相互作用和均匀KNB耦合的对称情形下，一个自旋对的负性（negativity）接近理论最大值，其余自旋对的纠缠同时消失，转移近乎理想。

Conclusion: 具有KNB自旋-电场耦合的分子纳米磁体（molecular nanomagnets）为在分子尺度上以电场方式操纵、导引和局域化量子纠缠（quantum entanglement）提供了有前景的平台；转移效率可通过交换相互作用、键几何结构（bond geometry）和非均匀自旋-电场耦合进行调控。

Abstract: We investigate quantum entanglement in a spin-1/2 Heisenberg trimer with spin-induced electric polarization described by the Katsura-Nagaosa-Balatsky (KNB) mechanism in the presence of external magnetic and electric fields. The electric field is assumed to lie in the plane of the magnetic ions, allowing its strength and orientation to be tuned independently. We analyze both bipartite and tripartite entanglement and demonstrate that the spin-electric-field coupling provides an efficient mechanism for controlling quantum correlations within the molecular nanomagnet. Depending on the electric-field parameters, the bipartite entanglement can be significantly enhanced or suppressed, while the multipartite entanglement exhibits a rich dependence on the microscopic spin-electric coupling. Most notably, we demonstrate that a rotating in-plane electric field of constant magnitude induces a controllable transfer of bipartite entanglement between different spin pairs. In the symmetric case of homogeneous exchange interactions and uniform KNB coupling, this transfer is found to be nearly ideal, with the bipartite negativity approaching its theoretical maximum for one spin pair while simultaneously vanishing for the remaining pairs. We show that the efficiency of the transfer can be tailored through the exchange interactions, bond geometry, and nonuniform spin-electric coupling. These results establish molecular nanomagnets with KNB spin-electric coupling as a promising platform for the electrical manipulation, steering, and localization of quantum entanglement at the molecular scale.

</details>

### [113] [A resonance in phonons scattering off a kink in the absence of a Peierls-Nabarro potential](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01450)
*Danial Saadatmand,Arpine Piloyan,David Amundsen,Aliakbar Moradi Marjaneh*

Main category: nlin.PS

TL;DR: 本文研究了一个无Peierls-Nabarro势垒的特殊离散化φ⁴模型中，声子（phonon）与初始静态扭结（kink）的相互作用，发现散射特性强烈依赖于晶格间距（lattice spacing），且在强离散性（strong discreteness）下出现显著反射和负辐射压（negative radiation pressure）等新效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究在消除静态Peierls-Nabarro势垒（Peierls-Nabarro potential）后，离散化效应对φ⁴模型中声子-扭结散射（phonon-kink scattering）性质的影响，特别是晶格间距如何改变原本连续模型中无反射的散射行为。

Method: 采用局部谐波源（localized harmonic source）产生声子，从扭结一侧发射并计算整个声子能带（phonon band）上的透射系数（transmission coefficient）和反射系数（reflection coefficient），分析不同晶格间距h下的散射行为。

Result: 在弱离散性（h<1）下，扭结近乎透明，声子大部分频谱可透射；在强离散性（h>1）下，出现显著反射，尽管连续模型中φ⁴扭结是无反射的。此外，所有晶格间距下扭结均经历负辐射压（negative radiation pressure），朝入射声子方向加速，且强离散性下效应更强。扭结速度及能量转移的频率依赖性与多普勒频移（Doppler-shifted）声子频率和声子群速度极值处的共振有关。

Conclusion: 即使在静态Peierls-Nabarro势垒缺失的系统中，强晶格离散性也能定性改变声子-扭结相互作用，揭示离散效应本身足以引发新的动力学现象。

Abstract: We investigate the interaction of small-amplitude waves called phonons, with an initially static kink in an exceptional discretization of the $φ^4$ model that is free of the Peierls-Nabarro potential. Phonons are generated by a localized harmonic source and scattered from one side of the kink. By computing the transmission and reflection coefficients over the entire phonon band, we demonstrate that the scattering properties depend strongly on the lattice spacing. In the weak-discreteness regime ($h<1$), the kink is nearly transparent and phonons are transmitted through it over most of the phonon spectrum. In contrast, for strong discreteness ($h>1$), significant reflection emerges even though the corresponding continuum $φ^4$ kink is reflectionless. We further show that depending on the frequency of the incoming phonons, the kink experiences negative radiation pressure and is accelerated toward the incoming phonons for all lattice spacings considered, and this effect is much stronger for the strong discretness. The frequency dependence of the kink velocity and energy transfer is explained in terms of resonances associated with Doppler-shifted phonon frequencies and extrema of the phonon group velocity. Our results reveal that strong lattice discreteness can qualitatively modify phonon-kink interactions even in systems where the static Peierls-Nabarro potential is absent.

</details>


### [114] [Source-Induced Reflection in Balanced Shallow-Water Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02581)
*Binan Gu,Cameron Norton,Andre Nachbin*

Main category: nlin.PS

TL;DR: 本文指出在循环网络上，顶点处的宽度平衡条件（width-balance condition）并不等价于无反射传输（transparency），因为后者还需要路径传播时间（travel time）的同步。基于浅水波模型，文章推导了通道宽度加权的散射定律（scattering law），引入了与源相关的平衡定义，并分析了多路径岛状结构中的反射特性，揭示了宽带抵消、频率选择零点以及无公共可公度性（commensurability）下的混合反射消失机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统观点认为一维波网络（one-dimensional wave networks）中节点处的宽度平衡条件对应无反射传输（reflectionless transmission），但该结论仅在简单网络上成立。作者旨在揭示在循环网络（cyclic networks）中这一对应关系不完整，需要引入传播时间同步条件，并对多路径结构中的反射行为进行精确描述。

Method: 采用浅水波模型（shallow-water wave model），推导了任意度数顶点（vertex of arbitrary degree）的通道宽度加权散射定律；引入相对于源的定义（source-relative definition）来刻画平衡（balance），反映同一节点在不同入射方向下可能具有反射性或无反射性。基于此，在频率空间（frequency space）中分析了 N 路径岛状结构（N-path island）的反射系数。

Result: 平衡顶点仅在同步入射振幅方向（synchronized incoming-amplitude direction）上透明。第一代上游反射（first-generation upstream reflection）由路径延迟的宽度加权分布决定；宽带抵消（broadband cancellation）要求所有路径传播时间相等；否则，路径长度差的可公度性产生周期性的频率选择零点（frequency-selective zeros）梳，且与通道宽度无关。对于 \(N \ge 4\)，还发现一种混合 regime，反射因子可在路径长度无公共可公度性时消失。

Conclusion: 循环网络上宽度平衡与无反射传输并不等价，后者还需要路径传播时间同步。不同入射方向下同一节点可呈现反射性差异，且多路径结构中的反射行为依赖于路径延迟分布，存在宽带与频率选择性抵消以及无公度性下的混合反射消失等多种机制。

Abstract: Width-balance conditions at a junction are often associated with reflectionless transmission, or transparency, in some one-dimensional wave models on networks. We show that, on cyclic networks, this identification is incomplete: local balance is a vertex-level condition, while transparency also requires synchronization of the path travel times. To make this precise, we consider a shallow-water wave model and derive the channel-width-weighted scattering law for a vertex of arbitrary degree and introduce a source-relative definition of balance, reflecting the fact that the same junction may be reflective or reflectionless depending on which edges carry incoming waves. Under this definition, a balanced vertex is transparent only to the synchronized incoming-amplitude direction. For an \(N\)-path island, the resulting first-generation upstream reflection is governed in frequency space by the width-weighted distribution of path delays. Exact broadband cancellation requires all path travel times to agree; when they do not, commensurability of the path-length differences produces a periodic comb of frequency-selective zeros, independent of channel widths. At $N\ge 4$ we further exhibit a hybrid regime in which the reflection factor vanishes without commensurability among the path lengths.

</details>


### [115] [On the Nonlinear Sensitivity of Phononic Frequency Combs to Physical Perturbations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03837)
*Madhurendra Mishra,Zhen Qi,Adarsh Ganesan*

Main category: nlin.PS

TL;DR: 本文利用约化双模自参量共振模型，系统研究了声子频率梳（phononic frequency comb）对外部物理参数变化的非线性灵敏度响应，揭示了不同参数（主/次失谐、驱动幅度、相对阻尼）对灵敏度分布的非均匀调控机制，并指出其共同的物理根源在于自参量共振、非线性饱和与耦合诱导同步。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 声子频率梳为非线性传感提供了丰富的平台，但其可观测量如何响应物理参数变化尚不清晰，缺乏系统性理解。

Method: 采用约化双模自参量共振模型（reduced two-mode autoparametric resonance model），系统扫描主失谐（primary detuning）、次失谐（secondary detuning）、驱动幅度（drive amplitude）与相对阻尼（relative damping）四个参数，分析它们如何共同塑造非线性参数空间中的幅度灵敏度与频率灵敏度。

Result: 灵敏度分布高度非均匀：主失谐使频率梳响应平滑移动；次失谐在共振流形附近产生尖锐的局域化跃迁；驱动幅度将峰值灵敏度集中在激活阈值附近，而非梳态深处；相对阻尼在模式间连续重新分配能量，不引入间断。

Conclusion: 所有参数下的幅度与频率观测量的非线性灵敏度均指向自参量共振、非线性饱和与耦合诱导同步这同一物理起源，为设计具有有意识、参数感知灵敏度工程的非线性传感平台提供了统一的物理基础。

Abstract: Phononic frequency combs offer a rich platform for nonlinear sensing, yet how their observable properties respond to changes in physical parameters remains poorly understood. Using a reduced two-mode autoparametric resonance model, we investigate how primary and secondary detuning, drive amplitude, and relative damping jointly shape amplitude and frequency sensitivity across the nonlinear parameter space. We find that sensitivity is far from uniform: primary detuning shifts the comb response smoothly, secondary detuning produces sharply localized transitions near resonance manifolds, and drive amplitude concentrates peak sensitivity close to the activation threshold rather than deep within the comb state. The relative damping redistributes energy continuously between modes without introducing discontinuities. The nonlinear sensitivity of amplitude and frequency observables across all parameters points to a common physical origin in autoparametric resonance, nonlinear saturation, and coupling-induced synchronization, offering a coherent basis for designing nonlinear sensing platforms with deliberate, parameter-aware sensitivity engineering.

</details>

# physics.flu-dyn [[Back]](#toc)

### [116] [Stability of gas flow past viscoelastic compliant solid](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03016)
*Mandeep Deka*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 本文研究可压缩气体流经柔顺固体（Neo-Hookean连续体模型）的线性稳定性。高固-流密度比下主导不稳定模式为固体的弹性剪切波；流动可压缩性对弹性模态增长率呈现非单调影响（Ma≈2时峰值）；热耦合使基态对导热率和底面温度敏感；渐近分析在ρ_r Re ≫ 1极限下推导出前导增长率的闭式表达式，与数值解高度吻合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高速气流流经柔顺固体表面的稳定性受高固-流密度比和流动可压缩性两个关键因素影响，现有研究对二者耦合作用的机理认识不足。

Method: 将柔顺固体建模为连续体Neo-Hookean固体，求解剪切驱动可压缩气流-固体系统的特征值问题；在ρ_r Re ≫ 1渐近极限下解析推导前导阶增长率的闭式表达式。

Result: 高密度比下主导不稳定为固体弹性剪切波；压缩性对弹性模态增长率具有非单调效应（Ma≈2时最大）；增大导热系数比使系统失稳，升高底面温度则起稳定作用；渐近解与数值解高度一致。

Conclusion: 导出的闭式增长率表达式显式量化了界面流体应力的影响，该应力可表达为流动解的积分形式，从而隔离出驱动不稳定的不同物理机制。

Abstract: Stability of a high-speed gas flow past a compliant solid is impacted by two distinct features: high solid-to-fluid density ratio ($ρ_r$), and flow compressibility when flow speeds are comparable to acoustic speed. This study investigates the linear stability of a shear-driven compressible gas flow past a compliant substrate modelled as a continuum Neo-Hookean solid. Numerical solutions of the eigenvalue problem reveal that at high density ratios, the dominant instabilities are the elastic shear-waves of the solid. Our study shows that flow compressibility exerts a non-monotonic effect on the growth rate of the elastic modes; the growth rate increases with increase in Mach number up to $\mbox{Ma} \approx 2$ before subsequently decreasing. Furthermore, for compressible flows, strong thermal-coupling renders the base state highly sensitive to both the solid-to-fluid thermal conductivity ratio and the substrate's bottom-surface temperature. Numerical results demonstrate that increasing the conductivity ratio destabilizes the system, whereas increasing the bottom wall temperature is stabilizing. The stability equations, analyzed in the asymptotic limit of $ρ_r \mbox{Re} \gg 1$, reveals that the fluid-solid system de-couples at the leading order with the elastic modes emerging as a solution of the linear elasticity equations under free-shear condition at the interface. We derive a closed-form expression for the leading-order growth rate of the instability, which shows an excellent agreement with the numerical solution. This expression explicitly quantifies the influence of fluid stresses at the interface, which can in-turn be expressed as integrals of the flow solution isolating the distinct physical mechanisms driving the instability.

</details>


### [117] [Development and application of a multiphase Lagrangian structure function model in anisotropic turbulence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03455)
*Andrew P. Grace,David Richter*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 本研究通过耦合欧拉-拉格朗日直接数值模拟（coupled Eulerian-Lagrangian direct numerical simulations），在中等雷诺数下分析了湍流壁面边界流中惯性沉降粒子的尺度分辨粒子相能量学，重点探讨了流场各向异性（flow anisotropy）如何通过粒子惯性（particle inertia）和沉降效应（particle settling）传递到粒子相，并推导了任意尺度下粒子相能量学的精确（但未闭合）守恒律。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 惯性粒子（inertial particles）对湍流运动能量响应（energetic response）的理解对于多相流动力学（multi-phase dynamics）基础研究和实际应用（如粒子弥散过程（particle dispersion processes）的降阶模型及粒子对流动相的双向耦合效应（two-way coupled effects））均具有重要意义；但现有研究多关注均匀各向同性湍流（homogeneous isotropic turbulence）中的粒子系综能量学，未预先考虑流场各向异性（如边界条件或外部强迫引起的各向异性）的影响。

Method: 采用耦合欧拉-拉格朗日直接数值模拟（coupled Eulerian-Lagrangian direct numerical simulations），在中等雷诺数下对湍流壁面边界流（turbulent wall bounded flow）中沉降惯性拉格朗日粒子（settling inertial Lagrangian particles）的欧拉尺度分辨粒子相能量学（Eulerian scale-wise particle phase energetics）进行研究；推导了任意尺度下粒子相能量学的精确但未闭合的守恒律（exact conservation law），并借助渐近论证（asymptotic argument）辅助分析直接数值模拟（DNS）数据。

Result: 揭示了粒子相尺度分辨能量学对湍流强度（turbulence intensity）、粒子惯性和粒子沉降的复杂依赖关系；分析了底层湍流因壁面存在而产生的各向异性（developing anisotropy）如何传递给粒子相，以及粒子惯性和沉降如何将这种大尺度各向异性（large scale anisotropy）保留到形式上各向同性的尺度范围（formally isotropic scale range）；讨论了脉动粒子场的准流向（quasi-streamwise）与垂直分量（vertical components）的相对变化。

Conclusion: 讨论了各向异性非局域效应（anisotropic non-local effects）对更一般流动的启示，以及对惯性沉降拉格朗日粒子的连续统模型（continuum models）的意义。

Abstract: The energetic response of inertial particles to turbulent flow motions is important for both a fundamental understanding of the multi-phase dynamics at play, and for applications such as reduced-order models of particle dispersion processes, and their two-way coupled effects onto the flow phase. Numerous studies focus on the energetics of ensembles of particles in homogeneous isotropic turbulence, where the influence of flow anisotropy (such as that provided by boundary conditions, or other external forcing) is not considered a priori. In this work, we investigate the role of flow anisotropy on the Eulerian scale-wise particle phase energetics in a turbulent wall bounded flow for settling inertial Lagrangian particles. By using coupled Eulerian-Lagrangian direct numerical simulations at moderate Reynolds number, we aim to unravel the complex dependency of the scale-wise particle energetics on the turbulence intensity, particle inertia, and particle settling. In particular, we focus on how the developing anisotropy of the underlying turbulent flow (derived from the presence of the wall) is donated to the particle phase, and how particle inertia and settling preserve this large scale anisotropy into the formally isotropic scale range of the flow. We derive an exact (but unclosed) conservation law for the particle phase energetics at arbitrary scale, and use an asymptotic argument to help elucidate our DNS data. We discuss the relative changes to the quasi-streamwise and vertical components of the fluctuating particle field, and finish by discussing the implications of anisotropic non-local effects for more general flows, and the implications for continuum models of inertial settling Lagrangian particles.

</details>


### [118] [An SO(3) Gauge Theory of Turbulence with Spontaneous Symmetry Breaking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05135)
*Ahmed Farooq*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 本文通过将湍流中的角动量识别为非阿贝尔规范联络、径向速度识别为希格斯场，证明各向同性湍流中连续能级串与离散涡丝的二元性来源于SO(3)规范对称性的自发破缺；基于高分辨率DNS数据，实证验证了能量谱的严格1:2均分、涡丝周围的BPS磁单极子廓线以及威尔逊环的面积律，从而揭示湍流真空的禁闭性质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 充分发展的各向同性湍流展现出一种二元性：连续的、标度不变的能级串（energy cascade）与离散的、强烈的涡丝（vortex filaments）共存。该工作旨在揭示这一看似矛盾的二元性背后的深层对称性起源。

Method: 将比角动量$\mathbf{L}=\mathbf{r}\times\mathbf{u}$识别为非阿贝尔规范联络（non-Abelian gauge connection），径速度$u_r$识别为希格斯场（Higgs field），从而将湍流真空描述为SO(3) Georgi-Glashow模型：当径向应变凝聚时，对称性SO(3) → U(1)自发破缺，产生拓扑质量隙$M_W = gv$；利用高分辨率直接数值模拟数据（JHTDB，$Re_λ\approx433$）进行实证验证。

Result: 三项关键预测得到实证确认：(i) 能量谱在惯性区严格遵循1:2均分（equipartition），在$M_W \approx 40$处出现尖锐发散；(ii) 孤立涡核周围提取的径向希格斯场精确遵循BPS磁单极子廓线（BPS monopole profile）$H(r)=\coth(r/η)-η/r$，其中$η=0.0093$域单位，真空期望值$v=0.338$，将常见的“蠕虫”（worms）识别为宏观的't Hooft-Polyakov磁单极子（'t Hooft-Polyakov monopoles）；(iii) 由速度场计算的威尔逊环（Wilson loop）呈现清晰的面积律$\langle W_C \rangle \sim e^{-σA}$，弦张力$σ=0.303\pm0.009$，直接证实湍流真空的禁闭性质。

Conclusion: 各向同性湍流的二元性本质上是规范对称性自发破缺的宏观体现：质量隙将能量划分为无质量的U(1)扇区（支撑Kolmogorov能级串的螺线管背景）与有质量的SO(3)/U(1)扇区（被禁闭在涡丝中）。

Abstract: Fully developed isotropic turbulence exhibits a dual nature: a continuous, scale-invariant energy cascade coexists with discrete, intense vortex filaments. We show that this duality arises from a spontaneously broken SO(3) gauge symmetry. By identifying the specific angular momentum $\mathbf{L} = \mathbf{r}\times\mathbf{u}$ as a non-Abelian gauge connection and the radial velocity $u_r$ as a Higgs field, the turbulent vacuum is described by the SO(3) Georgi-Glashow model. When the radial strain condenses, the symmetry breaks SO(3) $\to$ U(1), generating a topological mass gap $M_W = gv$. This gap partitions the energy into a massless U(1) sector (the solenoidal background) that sustains the Kolmogorov cascade, and a massive SO(3)/U(1) sector that is confined to vortex filaments. Using high-resolution DNS data (JHTDB, $Re_λ\approx433$), we empirically verify three key predictions: (i) the energy spectra obey a strict 1:2 equipartition over the inertial range, with a sharp divergence at $M_W \approx 40$; (ii) the radial Higgs field extracted around isolated vortex cores follows the exact BPS monopole profile $H(r)=\coth(r/η)-η/r$ with $η= 0.0093$ domain units and the VEV $v = 0.338$, identifying the ubiquitous "worms" as macroscopic 't Hooft-Polyakov monopoles; (iii) the Wilson loop computed from the velocity field exhibits a clean area law $\langle W_C \rangle \sim e^{-σA}$ with string tension $σ= 0.303 \pm 0.009$, directly confirming the confining nature of the turbulent vacuum.

</details>


### [119] [Experimental and numerical study of the dynamics of sedimenting pairs of semi-flexible fibers close to attractive `aligned' relative configuration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03410)
*Harish N. Mirajkar,Chandra Shekhar,Yevgen Melikhov,Piotr Zdybel,Maria L. Ekiel-Jezewska*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 本文通过实验和数值模拟研究了粘性流体中两根短半柔性纤维在重力作用下的沉降动力学，重点关注纤维初始靠近时是否会趋近于水平对齐构型（aligned horizontal configuration），并证实该构型对近距离半柔性纤维具有吸引性，即使在初始远离的情况下，纤维也会在长时间后返回并围绕该构型做阻尼振荡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 此前数值研究（Bukowicki & Ekiel-Jezewska, 2019）发现，中等弹性细丝在对称初始条件下会趋向水平对齐构型。然而，该构型对半柔性纤维（semi-flexible fibers）的吸引性是否普遍成立，以及初始远离的纤维能否最终趋近该构型，尚缺乏实验和长时间数值证据。本文旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 实验上，采用两根半柔性球链（ball chains）在特高粘度硅油中沉降，初始为平行水平构型，通过两台同步相机记录运动与形变。数值上，将中等弹性细丝建模为由弹簧连接的同尺寸珠子链（chains of identical beads），并引入抗弯弹性（elastic resistance to bending）。动力学求解基于Stokes方程的多极展开（multipole expansion），使用Hydromultipole数值代码实现。

Result: 大多数实验中，球链保持在一起，并围绕对称对齐构型做阻尼振荡（damped oscillations）；少数初始条件下球链会水平或垂直移开。短时间尺度上，半柔性球链与中等弹性细丝表现出相似动力学。长时间数值模拟显示，初始靠近的弹性细丝可能先水平或垂直移开，但在长时间后返回，并做阻尼振荡，最终趋近几乎端点相触的对齐构型。

Conclusion: 证实了水平对齐构型对非常靠近的半柔性沉降纤维具有吸引性，且该吸引性在纤维初始远离时仍然有效——纤维最终会返回并趋近该构型。这为理解半柔性纤维在低雷诺数流体中的集体沉降行为提供了新的动力学证据。

Abstract: Dynamics of two short semi-flexible fibers settling under gravity in a viscous fluid are investigated at Reynolds numbers Re << 1. We focus on fibers initially relatively close to each other, and we check if later they approach an aligned horizontal configuration, previously identified numerically (Bukowicki and Ekiel-Jezewska, Soft Matter 46 (2019) 9379) as attractive for symmetric initial conditions of moderately elastic filaments. In our experiments, two semi-flexible ball chains sediment in a highly viscous silicone oil. They are initially straight and close to a parallel horizontal relative configuration. Their motion and shape deformation are recorded using two synchronized cameras. For most of the trials, ball chains stay together, with damped oscillations around the symmetric aligned configuration. For a few initial conditions, the ball chains move away horizontally or vertically. To study the behavior over a longer time, we perform numerical simulations, modeling moderately elastic filaments as chains of identical beads, with the centers of consecutive beads connected by springs and with the fibers' elastic resistance to bending. Different initial positions and orientations are considered. Their dynamics are determined by the multipole expansion of the Stokes equations, implemented in the precise Hydromultipole numerical code. For short times, we observe the similar dynamics of semi-flexible ball chains and moderately elastic filaments. We provide examples of long-time numerical simulations illustrating that elastic filaments close to each other can move away horizontally or vertically, but after a long time, come back and perform damped oscillations while approaching the aligned configuration with almost touching filament ends. We confirm the attractive nature of the aligned configuration of very close semi-flexible sedimenting fibers, even if they are far away from each other.

</details>

### [120] [Correlation-Induced Topological Reconstruction in a Periodically Driven Kagome Mott Insulator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02717)
*Rahul Ghosh,Subhajyoti Pal,Ganesh C Paul*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文研究Kagome晶格Hubbard模型在周期性圆偏振光驱动下的电子关联效应，发现驱动会重整化跃迁并产生手性项，导致重复拓扑相变和平带的连续调谐；相互作用与驱动协同可引发非单调的Mott相变及拓扑重构，产生纯驱动或纯相互作用无法实现的拓扑平带自旋子绝缘体。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究Kagome晶格（Kagome lattice）上Hubbard模型（Hubbard model）中电子关联（electronic correlations）与圆偏振周期性驱动（circularly polarized periodic driving）之间的相互作用机理。

Method: 采用Brillouin-Wigner微扰论（Brillouin-Wigner perturbation theory）推导出有效的Floquet哈密顿量（Floquet Hamiltonian），并用slave-rotor平均场理论（slave-rotor mean-field theory）处理关联效应。

Result: 驱动重整化（renormalize）裸跃迁并产生手性（chiral）最近邻和次近邻项，从而引发重复拓扑相变（repeated topological transitions）以及一个能在能谱中连续调谐的平带（flat band）。Mott相变（Mott transition）在驱动振幅下呈现强非单调性（non-monotonic），导致重复的金属-绝缘体转变。Mott相中的自旋子（spinon）激发具有与无相互作用Floquet能带不同的拓扑结构，形成涌现的平带自旋子绝缘体（emergent flat-band spinon insulators）。

Conclusion: 周期性驱动的Kagome系统可作为构建非平衡（out-of-equilibrium）关联拓扑平带物理的平台，该方案在超冷原子晶格（ultracold atomic lattices）中具有可实现的实验前景。

Abstract: We study the interplay between electronic correlations and circularly polarized periodic driving in the Hubbard model on a Kagome lattice. Using Brillouin-Wigner perturbation theory, we derive an effective Floquet Hamiltonian in which the drive renormalizes the bare hopping and generates chiral nearest- and next-nearest-neighbor terms, producing repeated topological transitions and a flat band whose position is continuously tunable across the spectrum. Within slave-rotor mean-field theory, we show that the resulting Mott transition is strongly non-monotonic in the drive amplitude, yielding repeated metal-insulator transitions, and that the spinon excitations inside the Mott phase acquire a band topology distinct from that of the non-interacting Floquet bands. This correlation-driven topological reconstruction produces emergent flat-band spinon insulators inaccessible to either driving or interactions alone. Our results establish periodically driven Kagome systems as a platform for engineering correlated topological flat-band physics out of equilibrium, with proposed realizations in ultracold atomic lattices.

</details>


### [121] [Quantum magnetism of the spin-1 kagome-lattice antiferromagnet](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03086)
*Katsuhiro Morita*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文利用大规模Lanczos对角化和有限温度Lanczos方法研究自旋-1 kagome晶格海森堡反铁磁体，发现零温磁化过程中在m=0、1/3、7/9和8/9处出现平台，分别对应三聚体价键晶体态和磁振子晶体态；有限温度下比热呈现双峰结构，磁化曲线中高场平台受热涨落快速抹平。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究自旋-1 kagome晶格海森堡反铁磁体的零温磁化过程、磁化平台（magnetization plateau）的量子态性质，以及有限温度下的热力学行为，为候选自旋-1 kagome材料的热力学和高场磁化测量提供基准数据（benchmark data）。

Method: 采用大规模Lanczos对角化（large-scale Lanczos diagonalization）和有限温度Lanczos方法（finite-temperature Lanczos method）进行数值计算；利用高斯核平滑方法（Gaussian-kernel smoothing method）构建零温磁化曲线。

Result: 零温磁化过程中观察到m=0、1/3、7/9和8/9四个平台；m=0平台对应三聚体价键晶体态（trimer valence-bond-crystal state），m=7/9和8/9平台对应磁振子晶体（magnon crystal），其中m=8/9平台为精确局域磁振子晶体态（localized-magnon crystal state）。零温磁化曲线在m=1/3平台低场边缘以及m=7/9和8/9平台高场边缘出现磁化跃变。有限温度下比热（specific heat）呈现双峰结构，峰值分别位于T/J≈0.1和T/J≈1.1，低温峰可能与三聚体价键晶体有序相关。m=1/3平台在低温下仍可见，而高场平台被热效应迅速抹平。

Conclusion: 本文系统揭示了自旋-1 kagome海森堡反铁磁体在零温和有限温度下丰富的磁化和热力学行为，为实验研究候选kagome材料提供了理论基准。

Abstract: We investigate the spin-1 kagome-lattice Heisenberg antiferromagnet using large-scale Lanczos diagonalization and the finite-temperature Lanczos method. The zero-temperature magnetization process exhibits plateaus at $m=0$, $1/3$, $7/9$, and $8/9$, where $m$ is the normalized magnetization. The $m=0$ plateau is identified as a trimer valence-bond-crystal state, while the high-field plateaus at $m=7/9$ and $8/9$ are identified as magnon crystals. In particular, the $m=8/9$ plateau corresponds to the exact localized-magnon crystal state. A smoothed zero-temperature magnetization curve constructed using the Gaussian-kernel smoothing method indicates magnetization jumps at the lower-field edge of the $m=1/3$ plateau and at the upper-field edges of the $m=7/9$ and $8/9$ plateaus. At finite temperatures, the specific heat exhibits a double-peak structure with peaks around $T/J\simeq0.1$ and $T/J\simeq1.1$, and the low-temperature peak may be related to trimer valence-bond-crystal ordering. The finite-temperature magnetization curves show that the $m=1/3$ plateau remains visible at low temperatures, whereas the high-field plateaus are rapidly smeared out by thermal effects. These results provide benchmark data for thermodynamic and high-field magnetization measurements in candidate spin-1 kagome-lattice materials.

</details>


### [122] [Winding charge density wave: intertwining of structural chirality and phase topology of electronic order](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03102)
*Shun Asano,Youichi Yanase*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文提出了一类新型手性电荷密度波（chiral charge density waves, CDWs），称为缠绕CDW（winding CDWs），其在单一有序波矢下仍能展现宏观手性。在螺旋对称手性晶体中，手性声子驱动Peierls失稳，通过电子-声子耦合的选择定则赋予CDW整数方位角相位缠绕。该框架还可推广至具有离散旋转对称性的非手性晶体，自发对称性破缺可稳定任意手性的缠绕CDW，实现非手性到手性的相变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索在单一有序波矢下仍能展现宏观手性的电荷密度波新类型，并揭示手性晶体几何结构（geometry）与电子有序相位拓扑（phase topology）之间的内在联系。

Method: 基于手性声子（chiral phonons）驱动的Peierls失稳（Peierls instability）机制，推导电子-声子耦合的选择定则（selection rule），赋予CDW整数方位角相位缠绕（azimuthal phase winding）。进一步将框架扩展至具有离散旋转对称性（discrete rotational symmetry）的非手性晶体，利用自发对称性破缺（spontaneous symmetry breaking）稳定缠绕CDW。

Result: 在螺旋对称手性晶体中，缠绕CDW通过手性声子-电子耦合的选择定则获得确定的晶体角动量通道（crystal angular momentum channel），产生整数相位缠绕。在非手性晶体中，自发对称性破缺可稳定任意手性的缠绕CDW，实现非手性到手性的相变（achiral-to-chiral phase transition）。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了手性结构几何与电子有序相位拓扑之间的基本联系（fundamental link），为理解手性电荷密度波的产生机制和相变行为提供了新的理论框架。

Abstract: We propose a class of chiral charge density waves (CDWs), dubbed winding CDWs, that exhibit macroscopic chirality despite a single ordering wavevector. In screw-symmetric chiral crystals, chiral phonons drive a Peierls instability that selects a definite crystal angular momentum channel, thereby endowing the CDW with an integer azimuthal phase winding dictated by the selection rule governing electron-phonon coupling. We further extend this framework to achiral crystals with discrete rotational symmetry and demonstrate that spontaneous symmetry breaking stabilizes a winding CDW with either handedness, realizing an achiral-to-chiral phase transition. Our results reveal a fundamental link between the geometry of chiral structures and the phase topology of electronic orders.

</details>


### [123] [What Makes Three-Dimensional Quantum Spin Liquids Possible?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03352)
*Yasir Iqbal,Ronny Thomale*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文论证三维量子自旋液体（three-dimensional quantum spin liquid）并非脆弱例外，而是可以通过局部约束（local constraints）、相干隧穿（coherent tunneling）和规范缺陷拓扑（topology of gauge defects）等机制在三维空间中稳定存在，甚至三维空间可以反转低维直觉——在低维中不稳定或需精细调节的相，在三维中可在有限参数区域内稳定存在。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子自旋液体通常通过低维直觉引入，但这一视角忽略了另一条通向量子无序（quantum disorder）的路径，且三维量子自旋液体常被视为稳定的脆弱例外。本文旨在回答为何这类物相能在三维空间（three spatial dimensions）中稳定存在，并建立三维量子自旋液体的普适性理论框架。

Method: 通过理论分析组织论述，围绕三个方面展开：约束驱动的库仑相（constraint-driven Coulomb phases）、弱谐和序-by-无序选择（weak harmonic order-by-disorder selection），以及自旋-轨道或多极相互作用（spin-orbit or multipolar interactions）在产生所需微观动力学中的作用。讨论基于紧致规范理论（compact gauge theories）在三维空间中的拓扑特性。

Result: 三维量子自旋液体的稳定性来自三个条件：局部约束抑制过早序选择、相干隧穿过程连接约束流形、规范缺陷的拓扑允许退禁闭（deconfined）区域。对于紧致规范理论，三维空间甚至可反转通常的维度直觉：低维中不稳定或需精细调节的区域，在三维中可在有限参数空间内稳定存在。

Conclusion: 三维量子自旋液体不必被视为三维磁性系统倾向于有序这一趋势下的脆弱例外，而是可以通过约束和拓扑机制自然实现的稳定物相。文中提出了实验诊断手段、候选材料以及待解决的理论问题。

Abstract: Quantum spin liquids are often introduced through a low-dimensional intuition: weak coordination and strong zero-point motion frustrate conventional magnetic order. This view has shaped much of the field, but it misses another route to quantum disorder. In many frustrated magnets, the more natural starting point is not a fluctuating version of an ordered state, but a locally constrained manifold of low-energy configurations. Within such a manifold, quantum dynamics can generate an emergent gauge theory, with fractionalized excitations and collective modes absent in ordinary magnets. Here we ask why such phases can be stable in three spatial dimensions. We argue that three-dimensional quantum spin liquids need not be regarded as fragile exceptions to the tendency of 3D magnets to order. They can arise when local constraints suppress premature order selection, coherent tunneling processes connect the constrained manifold, and the topology of gauge defects permits a deconfined regime. For compact gauge theories, three dimensions can even reverse the usual dimensional intuition: regimes that are unstable or fine-tuned in lower dimensions may become stable over finite regions of parameter space. We organize the discussion around constraint-driven Coulomb phases, weak harmonic order-by-disorder selection, and the role of spin-orbit or multipolar interactions in generating the required microscopic dynamics. We close with experimental diagnostics, candidate materials, and open theoretical questions for three-dimensional quantum spin liquids

Method: 采用X射线衍射（X-ray diffraction, XRD）实验，在不同温度和压力条件下对La₂SmNi₂O₇样品进行结构表征和精修。

Abstract: We investigated the structural properties of bilayer nickelate La$_2$SmNi$_2$O$_7$ as a function of pressure and temperature. At ambient conditions, we show that the material crystallizes as a monoclinic superstructure distinct from the one previously reported and close to the pseudo-orthorhombic structure of pristine La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$. No signatures of satellite reflections associated with charge density wave (CDW) ordering are detected at low temperature. Upon compression, a sequence of pressure-induced structural transitions from monoclinic to orthorhombic 15 GPa and then tetragonal 21 GPa symmetry is observed. Within the superconducting dome, the quality of the X-ray diffraction data enables structural refinements enabling theoretical models to understand the emergence of superconductivity.

### [125] [Quantum Destabilization of Skyrmions in Centrosymmetric Frustrated Magnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03378)
*Amit Kumar,Kalpataru Pradhan*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究自旋量子数 $s$ 如何影响中心对称量子海森堡模型中斯格明子的稳定性，特别关注从半经典（semiclassical）到极端量子（extreme quantum）区间的转变过程。

Method: 采用神经网络量子态（neural network quantum states）方法，对正方晶格上的 $J_1-J_2-J_3$ 中心对称量子海森堡模型（centrosymmetric quantum Heisenberg model）进行数值模拟分析。

Result: 斯格明子稳定性 $Q$ 从半经典区间到极端量子极限（$s=1/2$）严重退化直至消失；$Q$ 随 $1/s$ 呈幂律衰减（power-law decay），但 $s=1/2$ 偏离该标度行为；斯格明子稳定性与二阶Rényi熵（second Rényi entropy）及局域自旋幅度呈线性关系。

Abstract: We investigate the role of the spin quantum number $s$ on the stability of skyrmions in a $J_1-J_2-J_3$ centrosymmetric quantum Heisenberg model on a square lattice using the neural network quantum states method. Our results reveal that the skyrmion stability $Q$ is severely degraded when transitioning from the semiclassical regime to the extreme quantum limit ($s=1/2$), where it ultimately vanishes. We demonstrate that this destabilization is driven by quantum longitudinal fluctuations, with $Q$ exhibiting a power-law decay as a function of the reciprocal spin moment $1/s$. Notably, the extreme quantum limit ($s=1/2$) deviates drastically from this scaling behavior, exhibiting distinct physics compared to larger spin moments. Furthermore, we reveal the microscopic origin of this decay by establishing a quantitative correspondence between skyrmion stability, entanglement, and local spin magnitude: as the local second Rényi entropy (an indicator of entanglement) increases and the local spin magnitude is suppressed, the skyrmion stability vanishes linearly. This regime marks a quantum state where the skyrmion number $C$ remains as remanent geometric feature of the spin orientations, yet the skyrmion stability $Q$ vanishes due to the longitudinal suppression of the local spin magnitude. Our findings suggest that classically robust skyrmion phases in frustrated lattices are fundamentally restricted to high-spin materials, indicating that a spin moment must of at least $s = 3/2$ is required for the realization of stable, atomic-scale topological textures.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用边界（开弦）数据与共形边界条件，为一般紧致化半径下的二维紧致化玻色子理论构建固定点张量；随后利用张量复重整化算法（tensor complex renormalization algorithm）分析所得张量的重整化群（renormalization group, RG）流。

Result: 所构造的固定点张量能够高精度重现闭弦谱，并在张量复重整化算法下生成稳定的RG流。此外，在单个张量层面上识别了可控的边缘形变（exactly marginal deformation），使得流动可以沿 c=1 模空间连续移动。

Conclusion: 该框架为描述一大类二维无理共形场论建立了一条具体的格点层次路径，有望推广至更广泛的CFT类别。

Abstract: Fixed-point (FP) tensor networks provide a discrete spacetime representation of conformal field theories (CFTs), offering a new route toward understanding holographic duality, generalized symmetries, and even quantum gravity. In this work, we construct FP tensors for the 2D compactified boson theory at a generic compactification radius, an archetypal irrational CFT, using boundary (open-string) data with conformal boundary conditions. We show that the resulting tensors reproduce the closed-string spectrum with high accuracy and generate stable renormalization-group (RG) flows under the tensor complex renormalization algorithm. Moreover, we identify a controllable exactly marginal deformation at the level of a single tensor, enabling flows that move continuously along the $c=1$ moduli space. This framework establishes a concrete lattice-level route toward describing a broad class of 2D irrational CFTs.

### [127] [Beyond-adiabatic flat Chern bands from a double-helix skyrmion crystal](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03707)
*Bin Xi,Ken Chen,Qiang Luo,Jie Lu,Jia-Wei Mei,Hong-Gang Luo,Jize Zhao*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种双螺旋斯格明子晶格（DHSKX）结构，通过相位聚集机制在保持贝里曲率（Berry curvature）的同时抑制动能，实现了平坦的Chern能带，并在超越绝热窗口下给出了与ν=1/3 Laughlin型分数量子霍尔态（fractional Chern insulator）一致的有限尺寸证据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 平坦带工程（flat-band engineering）面临的核心挑战是如何在抑制动能的同时不牺牲贝里曲率（Berry curvature），本研究旨在寻找一种同时满足这两项条件的实空间组织方案。

Method: 基于受挫蜂窝自旋模型（frustrated honeycomb spin model）的经典基态，构建双螺旋斯格明子晶格（double-helix skyrmion crystal, DHSKX），利用π锁定螺旋度（π-locked helicities）和磁C₃对称性（magnetic C₃ symmetry）实现相位聚集（phase clustering），从而在实空间实现波函数相位绕转的局域化与分布式的相消干涉。

Result: DHSKX在较宽的耦合窗口内产生了孤立的平坦|C|=1 Chern能带，其中一条能带在中等耦合强度下在量子几何（quantum geometry）上超越了绝热参考（adiabatic reference）。在超越绝热窗口（beyond-adiabatic window）中，能带投影精确对角化给出了与ν=1/3 Laughlin型分数量子Chern绝缘体（fractional Chern insulator）一致的有限尺寸证据；同一结构还支持一个更高Chern数（C=-2）的平坦能带。

Conclusion: DHSKX结构仅依赖位点分辨的复数跳跃（site-resolved complex hoppings）即可实现，可直接在拓扑电路（topolectric）、声学（acoustic）和光子学（photonic）平台中进行编程实现，为平坦带工程提供了新的实空间设计路线。

Abstract: A central challenge in flat-band engineering is suppressing kinetic energy without sacrificing Berry curvature. We show that a double-helix skyrmion crystal (DHSKX)--two sublattice-resolved skyrmion textures locked at opposite helicities, obtained here as the classical ground state of a frustrated honeycomb spin model--provides such a route under double exchange. The key mechanism is a single real-space organization, phase clustering: the $π$-locked helicities expel the wave function's phase winding from the skyrmion cores, and the magnetic $C_3$ symmetry pins it into three phase-locked clusters whose distributed destructive interference cancels net transport while preserving the Berry curvature. Ordinary skyrmion crystals, even with the same symmetry, do not develop this organization. Phase clustering yields isolated flat $|C| = 1$ Chern bands over broad coupling windows, one of which surpasses the adiabatic reference in quantum geometry at intermediate coupling. In this beyond-adiabatic window, band-projected exact diagonalization gives finite-size evidence consistent with $ν= 1/3$ Laughlin-type fractional-Chern-insulator physics; the same texture also hosts a higher-Chern ($C = -2$) flat band. Built from site-resolved complex hoppings alone, the DHSKX architecture is directly programmable in topolectric, acoustic, and photonic platforms.

### [128] [Pauli Spectrum and Stabilizer Rényi Entropy in Gapless Symmetry-Protected Topological Phases](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03762)
*Ying-Lin Li,Po-Yao Chang*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过稳定子Rényi熵（stabilizer Rényi entropy）和泡利谱（Pauli spectrum）研究对称性保护拓扑（SPT）相中的量子魔法（quantum magic），发现稳定子Rényi熵在相变点附近存在极值但无法区分不同SPT相，而泡利谱在相变点呈现特征性的交叉结构，且该交叉可通过局域幺正对偶性或非可逆对偶变换理解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子纠缠已被广泛用于拓扑相的诊断，但另一种非经典相关性——非稳定子性（non-stabilizerness，即量子魔法）在SPT相中的表现尚待系统研究。本文旨在探究稳定子Rényi熵和泡利谱能否作为区分不同SPT相（包括有能隙SPT、非本征无能隙SPT和本征无能隙SPT）的诊断工具。

Method: 采用数值方法计算对称性保护拓扑（SPT）相在对称性保持微扰下的稳定子Rényi熵（stabilizer Rényi entropy），并分析其在不同SPT相（有能隙SPT、非本征无能隙SPT、本征无能隙SPT）相变点附近的行为。同时利用泡利谱（Pauli spectrum）研究相变点处的泡利-弦关联（Pauli-string correlations）结构，并引入局域幺正对偶性（local-unitary duality）与非可逆对偶变换（non-invertible duality transformation）解释观测到的交叉结构。

Result: 稳定子Rényi熵在相变点附近呈现极值，但单独无法区分不同SPT相；泡利谱在相变点处呈现特征性的交叉结构（crossing structure），该交叉反映了两种拓扑不同相的非局域弦序参量（non-local string order parameters）所主导的泡利-弦关联的交换。对于有能隙SPT和非本征无能隙SPT，泡利谱交叉可由局域幺正对偶性解释；对于本征无能隙SPT，需通过非可逆对偶变换生成泡利谱映射。

Conclusion: 稳定子Rényi熵仅能作为相变的粗粒度诊断（coarse diagnostic），而泡利谱蕴含关于弦序扇区（string order sectors）交换的更精细信息。量子魔法（quantum magic）为表征有能隙和无能隙SPT相提供了互补视角。

Abstract: Quantum entanglement is widely used as a diagnostic of topological phases of matter. Beyond entanglement, non-stabilizerness captures a distinct aspect of quantum many-body states by quantifying their distance from the manifold of stabilizer states. In this work, we study the stabilizer Rényi entropy in symmetry protected topological (SPT) phases, including both gapped SPT, non-intrinsically gapless SPT, and intrinsically gapless SPT phases. Under symmetry preserving perturbations, we find numerically that the stabilizer Rényi entropy exhibits an extremum near the phase transition. However, the stabilizer Rényi entropy alone cannot distinguish different SPT phases. In contrast, the Pauli spectrum reveals a characteristic crossing structure at the transition point. This crossing reflects the exchange of dominant Pauli-string correlations associated with the non-local string order parameters of the two topological distinct phases. For gapped SPT and non-intrinsically gapless SPT phases, the crossing structure can be understood from a local-unitary duality that maps the Pauli spectrum between the two phases. For intrinsically gapless SPT phases, such a local-unitary mapping is absent. Instead, we find that the Pauli spectrum mapping is generated by a non-invertible duality transformation. These results show that although the stabilizer Rényi entropy provides only a coarse diagnostic of phase transitions, the Pauli spectrum contains finer information about the exchange of string order sectors. Our findings demonstrate that quantum magic offers a complementary perspective for characterizing both gapped and gapless SPT phases.

Abstract: We employ the nonperturbative many-body spin GW method to compute the single-particle Green's function, and the covariance method to evaluate the correlation functions of two body, for the Hubbard model for superconductors. The key transition temperatures, namely the Neel temperature and the superconducting critical temperature Tc are found to be in quantitative agreement with experimental data. The evolution of the Fermi surface in different doping regimes is also presented, which clearly shows transitions from pseudogap to strange metal and to Fermi liquid phase. The method has been benchmarked at strong coupling and low temperature and is free from the fermion sign problem. ### [130] [Orbital-Selective Mott and Antiferromagnetic Phases in Diagonally Compressed Kagome Lattice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04621)
*Jiewei Ding,Ho-Kin Tang,Wing Chi Yu*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过量子蒙特卡洛模拟，研究了在对角压缩的kagome晶格上半填充Hubbard模型的几何压缩效应，发现了几何压缩引起的子格分化、选择性Mott相变以及丰富的U-θ相图，揭示了晶格几何、磁阻挫与强关联之间的复杂相互作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在阻挫二维系统中，晶格几何、磁阻挫与强关联电子行为之间的相互作用尚未被充分理解。本文旨在通过引入可变的晶格角度和对角压缩，系统研究几何变形如何影响kagome晶格上的关联电子相变。

Method: 采用行列式量子蒙特卡洛模拟（determinant quantum Monte Carlo simulations）方法，在引入指数衰减长程跳跃（exponential decay long-range hopping）$t(r) = t_0 \exp(-r / r_0)$ 的对角压缩kagome晶格上，对半填充Hubbard模型进行模拟。通过改变晶格角度θ和原位相互作用U，测量了双占据数、电荷压缩率以及整体和每个子格的自旋-自旋关联函数。

Result: 发现几何压缩会引起清晰的子格分化：当θ≳52°时，A子格建立长程跳跃，抑制B/C子格的金属行为，驱动选择性Mott相变（selective Mott transition）；当θ≲52°时，B-C链在有限尺寸模拟中发展出长程反铁磁关联，抑制A子格的金属行为。A位点的临界相互作用U^c_A在B-C反铁磁关联出现附近急剧下降，而U^c_{B/C}则增大。

Conclusion: 这些竞争性有序导致轨道选择性Mott相（orbital-selective Mott phase）以及包含顺磁金属（paramagnetic-metal）、顺磁Mott（paramagnetic-Mott）、反铁磁金属（antiferromagnetic-metal）和反铁磁Mott（antiferromagnetic-Mott）态的丰富U-θ相图。结果突出了阻挫二维系统中晶格几何、磁阻挫与强关联之间的复杂相互作用。

Abstract: We perform determinant quantum Monte Carlo simulations of the half-filled Hubbard model on a diagonally compressed kagome lattice, introducing exponential decay long-range hopping $t(r) = t_0 \exp\bigl(-r / r_0\bigr)$ to account for the evolving bond length. By varying the lattice angle $θ$ and the on-site interaction $U$, double occupancy, charge compressibility, and spin-spin correlation functions of the whole system and each sub-lattice are measured. We find that geometric compression induces a clear sublattice differentiation: for $θ\gtrsim52^\circ$, the A sublattice establishes long-range hoppings, which in turn suppresses the metallic behavior of the $B/C$ sublattice and drives a selective Mott transition; for $θ\lesssim52^\circ$, the $B$-$C$ chains develop long-range antiferromagnetic correlations within the finite-size simulations, which in turn suppresses the metallic behavior of the $A$ sublattice and drives a selective Mott transition. The critical interaction $U^c_A$ for the $A$ sites decreases sharply near the onset of $B$-$C$ antiferromagnetic correlations, while $U^c_{B/C}$ increases. These competing orders give rise to an orbital-selective Mott phase and a rich $U$-$θ$ phase diagram featuring paramagnetic-metal, paramagnetic-Mott, antiferromagnetic-metal, and antiferromagnetic-Mott states. Our results highlight the complex interplay between lattice geometry, magnetic frustration, and strong correlations in frustrated two-dimensional systems.

</details>


### [131] [Supercritical fluid of quantum electrons in three-dimensional superconducting fullerides](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04693)
*Xinying Li,Yuki Matsuda,Chongli Yang,Huaxue Zhou,Takuma Ogasawara,Qin Wang,Liguo Zhang,Hidekazu Shimotani,Hailiang Xia,Khuong K. Huynh,Panagiotis Kotetes,Satoshi Heguri,Katsumi Tanigaki*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本研究首次通过电导率和磁化率双探针实验，在三维超导富勒烯CsxRb3-xC60中识别出热力学平衡的超临界流体（SCF）相及其Mott端点，揭示了两种金属-绝缘体转变线汇聚于单一Mott端点的微观图像，并给出了量子临界区临界指数和超导Tc穹顶起源的新解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在Mott金属-绝缘体转变中，量子电子的超临界流体（supercritical fluid, SCF）相是强关联电子物理学中最难以捉摸的现象之一。先前对Cr掺杂V2O3和有机Mott体系的研究报告了不一致的临界指数（critical exponents），且标度分析（scaling analysis）仅依赖单一实验观测量，未能解决相共存、非均匀性和逾渗（percolation）的作用。

Method: 采用电导率（electrical conductivity）和磁化率（magnetic susceptibility）两个独立探针，对三维超导富勒烯（fullerides）CsxRb3-xC60进行实验测量；并采用无假设的两粒子分析（hypothesis-free two-particle analysis）处理磁化率数据。

Result: 发现两条不同的金属-绝缘体转变线汇聚于单一Mott端点（Mott endpoint）；磁化率的两粒子分析通过展示最大两相混合熵（maximum two-phase mixing entropy），识别出金属-绝缘体共存的SCF相，与热力学平衡的Widom线（Widom line）图像一致；电导率标度分析给出的临界指数落在量子临界（quantum critical）预测范围内。

Conclusion: 该双探针方法（dual-probe approach）提供了Mott SCF的统一微观图像，其特征长度尺度低于当前衍射分辨率，同时为超导Tc穹顶（superconducting Tc-dome）的起源提供了新的解释。

Abstract: The supercritical fluid (SCF) of quantum electrons at the Mott metal-insulator transition without symmetry breaking is one of the most elusive phenomena in strongly correlated electron physics. Prior studies of Cr-doped V2O3 and organic Mott systems reported discrepant critical exponents. A key limitation is that the scaling analysis relies on a single experimental observable, leaving the roles of phase coexistence, inhomogeneity, and percolation unaddressed. Here we report the first experimental identification of a thermodynamically equilibrated SCF phase and its associated Mott endpoint in the three-dimensional superconducting fullerides CsxRb3-xC60, using two independent probes of electrical conductivity and magnetic susceptibility, which reveal two distinct metal-insulator transition lines converging at a single Mott endpoint. A hypothesis-free two-particle analysis of magnetic susceptibilities yields a metal-insulator coexisting SCF by exhibiting the maximum two-phase mixing entropy, in agreement with a picture of a thermodynamically equilibrated Widom line. Simultaneously, conductivity scaling yields a critical exponent in the regime of quantum critical predictions. Our new dual-probe approach provides a unified microscopic picture of the Mott SCF with a characteristic length scale below current diffraction resolution, in addition to a new interpretation on the origin of superconducting Tc-dome.

</details>


### [132] [Nonlocal Kondo-exchange-driven intrinsic anomalous Hall effect in localized-$4f$ antiferromagnetic metals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04805)

Method: 建立理论框架（theoretical framework），描述局域反铁磁有序（localized antiferromagnetic order）对巡游电子（itinerant electrons）的影响，并将该框架应用于新近发现的4f反铁磁金属Ce₂CuGe₆进行具体分析。

Result: 发现该材料中内禀反常霍尔电导率（intrinsic anomalous Hall conductivity）和能带自旋劈裂（spin splitting of the energy bands）的起源是自旋依赖的跨位点跃迁（spin-dependent intersite hopping），由非局域近藤交换耦合（nonlocal Kondo exchange coupling）诱导产生；而非局域作用的塞曼型有效场（Zeeman-type effective field）。

Conclusion: 在f电子反铁磁金属中，局域磁矩与巡游电子的轨道分离使得反常霍尔效应和自旋劈裂的产生机制不同于传统d电子体系，非局域近藤交换耦合在其中的关键作用为理解此类材料中的输运与电子结构提供了新的物理图像。

Abstract: The anomalous Hall effect in antiferromagnetic metals has attracted considerable attention. Most known realizations involve itinerant $d$ electrons that simultaneously mediate charge transport and magnetic order. Here, we focus on $f$-electron materials, where localized magnetic moments and conduction electrons are hosted in different orbitals. We develop a theoretical framework to describe the impact of localized antiferromagnetic order on itinerant electrons. Applying this approach to the recently discovered $4f$ antiferromagnetic metal $\mathrm{Ce}_{2}\mathrm{Cu}\mathrm{Ge}_{6}$, we identify the origin of both the intrinsic anomalous Hall conductivity and the spin splitting of the energy bands as spin-dependent intersite hopping induced by nonlocal Kondo exchange coupling, rather than a Zeeman-type effective field acting locally on the conduction electrons.

### [133] [Chirped Floquet linear drives activate forbidden charge-to-spin conversions in Rashba two-dimensional electron gases](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04946)
*Mohsen Yarmohammadi*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文提出一种通过啁啾线性Floquet驱动（chirped Floquet linear drive）来解锁Rashba二维电子气（2DEG）中原本禁戒的Edelstein效应（Edelstein effect）电荷-自旋转换通道的新方法，为自旋轨道转矩（spin-orbit torque）开关和高效自旋电子学（spintronics）提供了一条可调谐且无需静态磁场的实验途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 作者提出采用啁啾线性Floquet驱动（chirped Floquet linear drive）来替代简单的线性驱动。该啁啾效应会产生面内Floquet-Zeeman场（Floquet-Zeeman fields）和奇宇称动量漂移（odd-parity momentum drift），从而同时破坏旋转对称性（rotational symmetry）和时间反演对称性（time-reversal symmetry），进而激活原本禁戒的Edelstein电荷-自旋转换。

Result: 理论分析表明，啁啾线性Floquet驱动能够实现Rashba二维电子气中原本禁戒的Edelstein电荷-自旋转换。该方法具有可调谐性，并且可以通过可编程空间光调制器（programmable spatial light modulators）或光学延迟线（optical delay lines）在实验中实现。

Conclusion: 这种可调谐的啁啾线性驱动为自旋轨道转矩开关和高效自旋电子学提供了一条具有广泛适用性的新途径，克服了传统方法依赖静态磁场或复杂界面工程带来的限制。

Abstract: In Rashba two-dimensional electron gases (2DEGs), charge-to-spin conversion via the Edelstein effect is conventionally limited to the transverse plane. Accessing longitudinal or out-of-plane pathways typically requires static magnetic fields or interface engineering, which cause stray fields and lack tunability. While dynamic circular or elliptical Floquet drives can also unlock these forbidden pathways, a simple Floquet linear drive cannot. Here, we propose an alternative approach: a \textit{chirped} Floquet linear drive. The chirp induces in-plane Floquet-Zeeman fields and an odd-parity momentum drift, which simultaneously break rotational and time-reversal symmetries. This mechanism activates the forbidden Edelstein charge-to-spin conversions in Rashba 2DEGs. Experimentally accessible via programmable spatial light modulators or optical delay lines, this tunable chirped linear drive offers a broadly applicable route to spin-orbit torque switching and high-efficiency spintronics.

### [134] [Optical switching of antiferromagnetic domains by nonreciprocal heat current](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04975)
*Takeshi Hayashida,Shunsuke Izumikawa,Kenta Kimura,Carl S. Davies,Andrei Kirilyuk*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索在同时破坏空间反演对称性（space-inversion symmetry）和时间反演对称性（time-reversal symmetry）的反铁磁体中，能否利用非互易光学响应（nonreciprocal optical response）超越仅识别反铁磁畴的局限，实现对其的确定性操控。

Method: 使用中红外光（mid-infrared light）从相反方向照射磁电反铁磁体LiFePO₄，通过测量非互易光学响应来验证不同光照方向对反铁磁畴态的稳定作用，并在宽波长范围内测试开关效应。

Result: 从相反方向照射可选择性稳定相反的反铁磁畴态；开关效应在宽波长范围内持续存在，而非局限于窄的跃迁特定光谱区域；该宽带开关源于材料固有的非互易性，通过光生热电流（optically generated heat currents）实现。

Conclusion: 非互易性可作为一种通用原理，用于以光实现对称性破缺相（symmetry-broken phases）的确定性控制，克服了基于共振的光学开关方案在光谱和材料上的局限性。

Abstract: What distinguishes front from back? In physics, such directionality emerges only when an underlying symmetry is broken. Antiferromagnets that inherently break both space-inversion and time-reversal symmetries provide a striking example, exhibiting nonreciprocal optical responses that depend on the direction of light propagation. Beyond distinguishing antiferromagnetic domains, we show that this nonreciprocity can deterministically create them. Using mid-infrared light, we demonstrate deterministic switching of antiferromagnetic domains in the magnetoelectric antiferromagnet LiFePO4, where illumination from opposite sides selectively stabilizes opposite domain states. Remarkably, the switching persists over a broad wavelength range rather than being confined to a narrow transition-specific spectral region, overcoming the spectral and material constraints of resonance-based optical switching schemes. The broadband switching originates from the material's intrinsic nonreciprocity through optically generated heat currents. Our results establish nonreciprocity as a general principle for deterministically controlling symmetry-broken phases with light.

### [135] [Near itinerancy and slow singlet formation in the triangular lattice NaRuO2](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05287)
*Charles C. Tam,Alon Hendler Avidor,Pritam Bhattacharyya,Yongseong Choi,Daniel Haskel,Sven Luther,Hlynur Gretarrson,Liviu Hozoi,Stephen D. Wilson*

TL;DR: 对三角晶格材料NaRuO₂的共振非弹性X射线散射（RIXS）、X射线吸收光谱（XAS）和高场磁化测量表明，该系统缺乏自旋-轨道激子特征，表现为近巡游体系，强磁性和电荷涨落破坏了长程磁有序，形成量子无序磁性基态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: NaRuO₂在极低温下未显示磁有序并存在持续自旋涨落，暗示其具有量子无序磁性基态；本研究旨在表征该无序态所源自的物理体系状态（physical regime），特别是局域电子结构与磁相互作用的性质。

Method: 使用Ru-L₂,₃边的共振非弹性X射线散射（resonant inelastic X-ray scattering, RIXS）和X射线吸收光谱（X-ray absorption spectroscopy, XAS），结合脉冲强磁场磁化测量，表征局域电子结构（local electronic structure）和磁相互作用（magnetic interactions）。

Result: XAS测量显示显著的自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling），但RIXS中未观测到自旋-轨道激子（spin-orbit exciton）——即自旋-轨道辅助Mott绝缘体的特征信号；取而代之的是金属特征的阻尼轨道内激发现象（damped intraorbital excitations）。高场磁化数据与随机单态模型（random singlet model）相符。

Conclusion: NaRuO₂应被理解为近巡游体系（nearly itinerant system），其中强磁性和电荷涨落（strong magnetic and charge fluctuations）破坏了长程磁有序，从而形成量子无序磁性基态。

Abstract: NaRuO$_2$ forms a delafossite-like structure that contains triangular sublattices of edge-sharing RuO$_6$ octahedra. It shows no evidence of magnetic order down to 100 mK and persistent spin fluctuations, suggestive of a quantum disordered magnetic ground state. In order to characterize the physical regime from which this disordered state arises, we use resonant inelastic X-ray scattering (RIXS) and X-ray absorption spectroscopy (XAS) at the Ru-$L_{2,3}$-edge, along with pulsed high-field magnetization to characterize both the local electronic structure and the magnetic interactions. Despite significant spin-orbit coupling inferred from XAS measurements, a spin-orbit exciton, characteristic of a spin-orbit assisted Mott insulator, was not observed with RIXS due to the presence of damped intraorbital excitations, which are characteristic of a metal. Corroborated by models of the high-field magnetization to a random singlet model, we propose a picture of a nearly itinerant system with strong magnetic and charge fluctuations that destabilize long-range magnetic order.

### [136] [Hybrid pattern recognition for charged particle tracking: Hough transform and convolutional neural efficiency networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04723)
*Carlo Varni,Krzysztof Ciesla,Marcin Wolter,Radoslaw Karol Mienkowski,Tomasz Bold*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用混合策略：将HT作为第一级数据准备步骤，将其参数空间图像直接输入神经网络（neural network），训练网络以抑制虚假径迹候选。两个步骤之间无需数据变换，算法因此更简洁且性能更优。

Result: 在ACTS框架下使用Open Data Detector进行模拟，并在真实的HL-LHC堆叠（pileup）条件下开展性能研究，结果表明该方法在效率和纯度两方面均取得良好表现。

Conclusion: 所提出的混合方法有效结合了HT的快速几何驱动特性与机器学习的判别能力，在不引入额外数据变换的前提下显著提升了径迹寻找的效率和纯度，适用于HL-LHC等高占用率环境。

Abstract: Reconstructing charged-particle tracks in silicon detectors is a central task in high-energy physics experiments and a key component of both offline reconstruction and online event selection. Within the reconstruction chain, the efficient and high-purity formation of track candidates plays a critical role in the overall performance. Among the many approaches developed over the years, the Hough transform (HT) has been widely studied as a fast geometry-driven method for track finding. However, in high-occupancy environments such as those expected at the High-Luminosity LHC (HL-LHC), the HT tends to produce a large number of spurious candidates, leading to increased computational overhead in subsequent reconstruction stages. In this work, we present a hybrid approach in which the HT serves as a first-stage data preparation step, providing its parameters space image as an input to a neural network trained to suppress false track candidates. The method combines the speed of the HT with the discriminative power of machine learning to achieve both efficiency and purity. In addition no data transformations are involved when combining these steps resulting in a simpler and more performant algorithm. Performance studies using the Open Data Detector simulated in the ACTS framework under realistic HL-LHC pileup conditions will be presented.

### [137] [Energetic Protection, Monotonicity and Switching Far from Equilibrium](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05303)
*Uğur Çetiner*

Main category: physics.bio-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过将马尔可夫过程表示为图并用生成树（spanning trees）上的分布（arboreal distribution）来描述稳态，发现即使在远离平衡态的条件下，某些稳态概率比值仍可精确锁定在平衡态值（称为“energetic protection”）。该现象源于生成树权重的代数等式，为系统在驱动力波动（如ATP浓度变化）下的鲁棒性提供了新机制，并揭示了远离平衡态时仍存在的非平凡约束与不变性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 平衡态下稳态概率比值由玻尔兹曼因子（Boltzmann factor）给出，是热力学与信息处理的自然读出量。然而，系统被驱动远离平衡态后该比值不再成立，本文旨在探究非平衡条件下稳态概率比值的演化规律及其约束。

Method: 将马尔可夫过程（Markov processes）表示为图，其稳态表示为生成树（spanning trees）上分布（arboreal distribution）的平均值。通过沿“能量边（energetic edges）”（即违背细致平衡（detailed balance）的边）驱动系统，追踪比值π_i/π_j相对于平衡值的变化。

Result: 发现当生成树权重满足代数等式时，概率比值可在任意远离平衡的条件下精确锁定在平衡值（“energetic protection”）。单边驱动时响应由两个arboreal系数决定且单调，非单调控制不可能。双能量边时保护与单调性结合形成“热力学开关（thermodynamic switch）”，可保持功能在平衡值并尖锐释放。

Conclusion: 细致平衡（detailed balance）约束了环上的速率，而energetic protection约束了树间的权重，为抵抗驱动力波动（如ATP浓度变化）提供了新鲁棒性机制。非平衡系统中存在新的约束（no-go原则与精确不变性），揭示了能量耗散定位如何支配非平衡系统（物理学与生物学中）的功能逻辑。

Abstract: At equilibrium, the ratio of two steady-state probabilities is a Boltzmann factor, set by a free-energy difference. Such ratios are the natural, normalization-independent readouts of both thermodynamics and information processing, and are often used as a measure of fidelity in biophysical systems. What becomes of these ratios once a system is driven from equilibrium, where the Boltzmann factor no longer holds? Representing Markov processes as graphs and their steady states as averages over a distribution on spanning trees, the \emph{arboreal distribution}, we track the ratio $π_i/π_j$ under driving along \emph{energetic edges}, where detailed balance is broken, relative to its equilibrium value. Our central finding is that a chosen ratio can stay exactly locked to its equilibrium value arbitrarily far from equilibrium, a phenomenon we call \emph{energetic protection}, whenever an algebraic equality between spanning-tree weights holds. Just as detailed balance constrains rates around cycles, energetic protection constrains weights across trees, providing a new mechanism for robustness against fluctuations in the driving force, such as variations in ATP concentration. Away from this equality, single-edge driving collapses the response onto two arboreal coefficients and forces it to be monotonic, so nonmonotonic single-edge control is impossible at any strength. With two energetic edges, protection and monotonicity combine into a \emph{thermodynamic switch} that holds a function at its equilibrium value for as long as desired and releases it sharply. Equilibrium is known for the limits it places on information processing. We show that new constraints, both no-go principles and exact invariances, survive far from equilibrium. These results reveal how the localization of energy expenditure governs the functional logic of nonequilibrium systems in physics and biology.

</details>


<div id='astro-ph.CO'></div>

# astro-ph.CO [[Back]](#toc)

### [138] [Evading the CMB $μ$-distortion bound on Supermassive Primordial Black Hole seeds with Non-Gaussian tails](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03138)
*Sanket Dave,Sheng-Feng Yan,Amara Ilyas,Yi-Fu Cai*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文探讨了在$z\gtrsim6$类星体驱动的超大质量黑洞（SMBH）难以从恒星质量残骸生长的问题，提出利用原始黑洞（PBH）作为种子，但受CMB $\mu$-畸变（COBE/FIRAS）约束。对于高斯扰动，概率分布函数（PDF）的尾部与方差耦合，导致PBH丰度可忽略（高斯壁垒）。作者利用非微扰$\delta N$形式主义，通过解耦方差与尾部概率来规避该壁垒，分析了四种高斯核族的尾部形状，发现标准指数型尾部仍不足以打开种子窗口，而代数型和重对数正态型尾部能在满足畸变约束下提供种子相关丰度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高红移（$z\gtrsim6$）类星体所驱动的超大质量黑洞（SMBH）难以从恒星质量残骸通过常规吸积过程生长，因此需要引入质量在$10^5-10^7 M_{\odot}$范围的原始黑洞（PBH）作为种子。然而，COBE/FIRAS对宇宙微波背景（CMB）$\mu$-畸变的观测限制了小尺度曲率方差，使高斯扰动下PBH丰度过低，形成所谓的高斯壁垒（Gaussian barrier）。本文旨在寻找能够规避该壁垒、同时满足畸变约束的PBH产生机制。

Method: 采用非微扰$\delta N$形式主义（non-perturbative $\delta N$ formalism），将渐近概率分布函数（PDF）尾部与$\delta N$映射的全局形状关联起来。分析了四种高斯核（Gaussian-cored）族：广义正态（generalized-normal）、拉伸指数（stretched-exponential）、幂律（power-law）和对数正态（log-normal）尾部。在对每个族进行单位方差标准化后，施加FIRAS上限，在尾部形状参数空间（tail-shape parameter space）中计算畸变受限的PBH丰度。

Result: 标准单场非吸引子动力学（standard single-field non-attractor dynamics）产生的普通指数型尾部仍然太轻，无法打开种子窗口。分数势动力学（fractional-potential dynamics）产生的代数型尾部（algebraic tails），以及作为乘法动力学（multiplicative dynamics）现象学代理的足够重的对数正态尾部（log-normal tails），能够在满足畸变约束的同时提供与种子相关的PBH丰度。

Conclusion: 通过解耦CMB $\mu$-畸变所约束的小尺度方差与控制坍缩的PDF尾部概率，可以规避高斯壁垒。代数型和重对数正态型尾部形状能够在COBE/FIRAS约束下实现可观的PBH丰度，为高红移超大质量黑洞的种子来源提供可行的理论途径。

Abstract: Supermassive black holes (SMBHs) powering quasars at $z \gtrsim 6$ are difficult to grow from stellar mass remnants, motivating seeds from primordial black holes (PBHs) with masses $10^5-10^7 M_{\odot}$. This range is constrained by the COBE/FIRAS bound on the CMB $μ$-distortion, which limits the small-scale curvature variance to $σ_ζ^2 \lesssim 10^{-4}$. For Gaussian perturbations, the variance fixes the far tail of the one-point probability distribution function (PDF), making the PBH abundance negligible. We call this the Gaussian barrier. The barrier can be evaded only if the variance probed by the distortion is decoupled from the tail probability controlling collapse. We implement this idea in the non-perturbative $δN$ formalism and relate asymptotic PDF tails to the global shape of the $δN$ map. Four Gaussian-cored families are analyzed: generalized-normal, stretched-exponential, power-law, and log-normal tails. After standardizing each family to unit variance, we impose the FIRAS cap and compute the distortion-limited PBH abundance in the tail-shape parameter space. The ordinary exponential tail produced by standard single-field non-attractor dynamics is still too light to reopen the seed window. Algebraic tails from fractional-potential dynamics, and sufficiently heavy log-normal tails treated as a phenomenological proxy for multiplicative dynamics, can supply seed-relevant abundances while respecting the distortion bound.

</details>


### [139] [Neutrino mass constraints in the Schwarzschild-de Sitter black-hole dark energy model with ACT DR6 and DESI DR2 data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03183)
*Sheng-Han Zhou,Tian-Nuo Li,Guo-Hong Du,Yi-Min Zhang,Zhao-Yu Li,Jing-Fei Zhang,Xin Zhang*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本研究在Schwarzschild-de Sitter黑洞暗能量（SdSDE）框架下，结合CMB（Planck、ACT DR6）、重子声学振荡（DESI DR2）及Ia型超新星（DES-Dovekie、PantheonPlus）数据，考察中微子质量总和（∑m_ν）与有效中微子代数（N_eff）的宇宙学限制。结果表明，SdSDE场景偏好正的中微子质量（∑m_ν=0.207±0.047 eV），但这一偏好可能源于参数补偿而非全局拟合改进；ΛCDM扩展中微子参数的模型显著优于相应的SdSDE扩展。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期DESI观测对ΛCDM模型提出挑战，显示对动力学暗能量的偏好，并在ΛCDM框架下给出接近中微子振荡实验下限的中微子质量约束。因此，有必要在其他暗能量框架（如SdSDE）中重新检验中微子参数的限制。

Method: 采用Schwarzschild-de Sitter黑洞暗能量（SdSDE）宇宙学框架，联合分析Planck与ACT DR6的宇宙微波背景（CMB）数据、DESI DR2的重子声学振荡（BAO）数据，以及DES-Dovekie与PantheonPlus的Ia型超新星数据。通过贝叶斯推断获得∑m_ν和N_eff的后验约束，并比较不同模型下的最佳拟合χ²值。

Result: SdSDE场景在允许∑m_ν变化时偏好正的中微子质量；使用CMB+DESI+DES-Dovekie数据得∑m_ν=0.207±0.047 eV（SdSDE+∑m_ν），当N_eff也变化时降至0.162±0.056 eV。N_eff与∑m_ν呈正相关，且SdSDE系统性地偏好低于标准值的N_eff。最佳拟合χ²比较表明，ΛCDM扩展中微子参数的模型显著优于对应的SdSDE扩展。

Conclusion: SdSDE诱导的正中微子质量偏好可能反映参数补偿（parameter compensation）而非全局拟合的真正改善，这一可能性有待未来高精度观测数据进一步检验。

Abstract: Recent DESI observations have posed new challenges to $Λ$CDM, showing a preference for dynamical dark energy and yielding neutrino mass constraints within $Λ$CDM that approach the lower bound allowed by neutrino oscillation experiments. In this work, we investigate cosmological constraints on the key neutrino parameters, $\sum m_ν$ and $N_{\rm eff}$, within the Schwarzschild-de Sitter black-hole dark energy (SdSDE) framework. We use cosmic microwave background (CMB) data from Planck and ACT DR6, baryon acoustic oscillation data from DESI DR2, and type Ia supernova data from DES-Dovekie and PantheonPlus. We find that SdSDE scenarios prefer a positive neutrino mass whenever $\sum m_ν$ is allowed to vary. Using CMB+DESI+DES-Dovekie data, we obtain $\sum m_ν=0.207^{+0.047}_{-0.052}~{\rm eV}$ for SdSDE+$\sum m_ν$, reduced to $\sum m_ν=0.162^{+0.055}_{-0.056}~{\rm eV}$ when $N_{\rm eff}$ is also varied. This arises from the positive correlation between $N_{\rm eff}$ and $\sum m_ν$, together with the systematic preference of SdSDE for values of $N_{\rm eff}$ below the standard value. Furthermore, the best-fit $χ^2$ comparison shows that $Λ$CDM with extended neutrino parameters is strongly preferred over the corresponding SdSDE extension. Overall, the positive neutrino mass preference induced by SdSDE may reflect parameter compensation rather than an improved global fit, a possibility that should be further tested with future high-precision observational data.

</details>


### [140] [Strong-lensing effects in high-redshift massive black-hole binary population inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03345)
*Yan-Heng Jin,Wen-Biao Han*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本论文通过模拟四个种子形成通道（轻/重种子×延迟/非延迟并合），定量评估了星系尺度强引力透镜（galaxy-scale strong lensing）对LISA在红移10～20区间探测大质量黑洞并合（MBHB）事件的影响，发现在高透镜率情形下忽略透镜效应会显著偏误形成通道比例的推断，建议在高红移MBHB分析中纳入透镜效应与事件计数信息。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高红移大质量黑洞并合（massive black-hole binary, MBHB）是研究黑洞种子形成与早期星系组装的重要探针，但LISA所探测的种群可能受到星系尺度强引力透镜的修改。该研究旨在量化这种修改效应，并评估其对推断本征形成通道比例的影响。

Method: 论文采用四个形成通道（轻种子/重种子×延迟/非延迟并合），分别在有/无强透镜条件下计算LISA 4年可探测事件数。为覆盖不确定的透镜群，对比了保守的速散度函数（velocity-dispersion-function, VDF）方案与乐观的晕质量函数（halo-mass-function, HMF）方案，并设置参考混合及多种偏重特定通道的本征种群权重，联合推断形成比例与透镜贡献强度。

Result: 强透镜对不同通道的影响不均等，可同时改变检测通道混合比例与总检测数。该效应在保守VDF方案下较弱，但在高透镜率的HMF方案中显著，忽略强透镜会导致恢复的形成比例产生偏误。推断精度取决于潜在的本征通道组成，而透镜贡献在高透镜率情况下能更准确地恢复。

Conclusion: 使用高红移MBHB检测推断本征形成通道比例时，应将星系尺度强透镜效应与事件计数信息纳入分析，否则可能得到有偏的结论。

Abstract: High-redshift massive black-hole binary (MBHB) mergers provide a probe of black-hole seed formation and early galaxy assembly, but the population detected by LISA can be modified by galaxy-scale strong lensing. We quantify this effect for MBHB mergers at $10\leq z\leq20$ and assess its impact on the inference of intrinsic formation-channel fractions. We use four channels, corresponding to light- and heavy-seed scenarios with delayed and non-delayed mergers, and compute 4-year LISA-detectable event numbers with and without strong lensing. To bracket the uncertain lens population, we compare a conservative velocity-dispersion-function (VDF) prescription with an optimistic halo-mass-function (HMF)-based prescription. We consider a reference mixture with equal seed-channel weights and additional mixtures in which the intrinsic seed population is weighted toward selected formation channels, and jointly infer the formation fractions and the strength of the lensing contribution. Strong lensing does not affect all channels equally: it can change the detected channel mixture as well as the total number of detections. This effect is weak for the conservative VDF prescription, but becomes significant in the high-lensing-rate HMF case, where neglecting strong lensing can bias the recovered formation fractions. The inference precision depends on the underlying intrinsic channel composition, while the lensing contribution is more accurately recovered in the high-lensing-rate case. These results indicate that galaxy-scale strong-lensing effects and event-count information should be included when using high-redshift MBHB detections to infer intrinsic formation-channel fractions.

</details>


### [141] [Disentangling modified gravity and galaxy bias with field-level inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03514)
*Sophie Hoyland,Daniela Saadeh,Kazuya Koyama,Harry Desmond*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种利用星系分布全场信息（field-level information）检验引力理论的推断框架，通过直接在三维星系计数场（galaxy number counts field）上进行贝叶斯似然分析，联合约束修正引力（modified gravity, MG）和星系偏袒（galaxy bias）参数，成功打破了传统功率谱（power spectrum）分析中非高斯信息缺失导致的参数简并（degeneracy），并在f(R)引力理论和非线性偏袒模型的模拟数据中验证了该方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的大尺度结构（large-scale structure）分析仅依赖功率谱（power spectrum），丢弃了非高斯（non-Gaussian）和傅里叶相位（Fourier phase）信息，导致修正引力（modified gravity, MG）与星系偏袒（galaxy bias）参数之间存在严重的简并（degeneracy），限制了引力理论检验的精度。

Method: 该方法直接在三维星系计数场（galaxy number counts field）上执行贝叶斯似然分析（Bayesian likelihood analysis），同时利用振幅和相位信息联合约束修正引力（MG）与偏袒参数；非线性结构形成采用共动拉格朗日加速（COmoving Lagrangian Acceleration, COLA）方法进行模拟，并通过非线性偏袒模型映射为模拟星系目录。

Result: 在固定且已知初始相位的条件下，相较于仅依赖功率谱（power-spectrum-only）的分析，全场方法（field-level approach）对f(R)引力参数fR0和主要偏袒参数β的约束更紧，并有效打破了修正引力（MG）与星系偏袒（galaxy bias）之间的简并；通过宇宙网（cosmic web）分类发现，低密度区域（under-dense regions）是区分引力模型的主要贡献者。

Conclusion: 该全场推断（field-level inference）管道对初始条件变化、泊松噪声（Poisson noise）和星系场阈值化（galaxy field thresholding）具有鲁棒性，为下一代巡天项目（next-generation surveys）开展全场水平的引力理论检验提供了一条有前景的路径。

Abstract: We present a field-level inference framework for testing gravity with the large-scale structure that exploits the full information content of the galaxy distribution. Traditional analyses based on the power spectrum discard non-Gaussian and Fourier phase information, resulting in strong degeneracies between modified gravity (MG) and galaxy bias. Our approach overcomes this limitation by performing a Bayesian likelihood analysis directly on the three-dimensional galaxy number counts field, jointly constraining MG and bias parameters using both amplitudes and phases. As an illustrative application, we analyse mock data in the context of the $f(R)$ theory of gravity and a non-linear galaxy bias model. Non-linear structure formation is modelled using the COmoving Lagrangian Acceleration (COLA) method under different gravity strengths, parameterised by $f_{R0}$. The resulting dark matter fields are then mapped to mock galaxy catalogues via a non-linear bias prescription. We demonstrate that, with fixed and known initial phases, including non-Gaussian and phase information yields tighter constraints on both $f_{R0}$ and the primary bias parameter, $β$, relative to the power-spectrum-only analyses. Notably, the field-level approach breaks the degeneracies between MG and galaxy bias inherent to two-point statistics. Through a cosmic web classification into voids, walls, filaments and clusters, we find that under-dense regions are the primary drivers in distinguishing gravity models at the field level. Finally, we establish the robustness of our pipeline against variations in initial conditions, Poisson noise, and galaxy field thresholding, providing a powerful path forward for field-level tests of gravity with next-generation surveys.

</details>


### [142] [First Search for Kaluza-Klein Gravitons and Radion Using Planck Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02651)
*Alexander P. Cassem,Soubhik Kumar*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文在弯曲五维（5D）模型中计算了由radion和Kaluza-Klein（KK）引力子介导的原初非高斯性（NG）双谱，并利用Planck 2018温度与偏振数据首次搜索这些信号。未发现显著的NG证据，最大显著性为1.8σ（对应m_KK≈1.6H），同时识别出一个可自然产生f_NL~1-50量级NG的五维框架，该信号处于未来巡天可探测范围内。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 额外维度中的重模（heavy moduli）和Kaluza-Klein（KK）引力子虽可能逃逸地面探测器，但在暴胀期间可通过与密度扰动的不可避免耦合产生原初非高斯性（primordial non-Gaussianity, NG），从而提供一种间接探测额外维度的途径。

Method: 采用弯曲五维（5D）模型，系统计算了radion和KK引力子作为中间粒子所介导的双谱（bispectra）；利用Planck 2018温度与偏振数据，首次对该类信号进行统计搜索。

Result: 未发现显著的原初非高斯性（NG）证据，最大显著性为1.8σ，对应KK引力子质量参数m_KK≈1.6H；在构建的五维框架中，可自然产生f_NL~1-50的NG幅度。

Conclusion: 当前数据（Planck 2018）对radion和KK引力子介导的非高斯性信号不敏感，但一个合适的五维（5D）模型可以产生处于未来巡天（如更大精度CMB实验）可探测范围内的NG信号（f_NL~1-50），说明额外维度检验仍有潜力。

Abstract: Heavy moduli and Kaluza-Klein (KK) gravitons from extra dimensions may evade terrestrial probes but can be produced during inflation, generating primordial non-Gaussianity (NG) through unavoidable couplings to density perturbations. In a warped five-dimensional (5D) model, we compute the full radion- and KK-graviton-mediated bispectra and perform the first search for these signals using Planck 2018 temperature and polarization data. We find no significant evidence for NG, with the maximum significance being $1.8σ$ for $m_{\rm KK}\approx 1.6H$. We also identify a 5D setup which naturally generates NG with $f_{\rm NL}\sim 1-50$, within the reach of future surveys.

</details>


### [143] [Hubble constant measurement with 13 bright standard sirens from binary black hole mergers inside active galactic nuclei](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03672)
*Dhruv Kumar,Alejandro Torres-Orjuela*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本研究利用13例与活动星系核（active galactic nucleus, AGN）宿主相关联的引力波双黑洞并合事件，独立测量了哈勃常数（Hubble constant）H₀，获得了约4.4%的精度，其结果与Planck 2018和SH0ES 2024的测量均无显著偏差。进一步结合GW170817等样本后精度提升至3.5%。若引入特定宇宙学先验，则可实现对相反锚定值>4σ的排除。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 哈勃常数（Hubble constant）的宇宙学测量（如Planck）与局域距离阶梯测量（如SH0ES）之间存在持续张力，亟需一个独立于这两种传统方法的观测渠道进行交叉验证。引力波标准汽笛（standard siren）提供了一种独立于电磁距离阶梯的几何测距手段，但其精度受限于宿主星系的红移获取。本研究旨在通过活动星系核（active galactic nucleus, AGN）作为引力波事件宿主的方法，提高标准汽笛的样本量和红移信息完备性，从而对H₀进行高精度独立测量并检验当前宇宙学张力。

Method: 选取13例与活动星系核（AGN）宿主相关联的引力波二进制黑洞并合事件作为暗汽笛（dark siren）样本，利用宿主星系的电磁对应体红移信息构建光度距离-红移关系，通过贝叶斯推断（Bayesian inference）估计哈勃常数H₀。在分析中分别纳入统计不确定度（stat）和校准不确定度（cal）。进一步将该样本与亮汽笛（bright siren）GW170817以及一个独立的暗-亮混合汽笛样本进行联合分析，以优化约束精度。此外，还检验了在给定光度距离先验（分别锚定于Planck和SH0ES宇宙学）条件下的H₀恢复结果及其对对立锚定的排斥显著性。

Result: 单独使用13例AGN宿主引力波事件得到H₀=70.50⁺³·³⁷₋₂·₈₉ (stat) ± 1.56 (cal) km s⁻¹ Mpc⁻¹，精度约4.4%，与Planck 2018相差0.98σ、与SH0ES 2024相差0.76σ。联合GW170817后得H₀=70.31⁺³·⁰⁰₋₂·₈₅ (stat) ± 1.55 (cal) km s⁻¹ Mpc⁻¹（4.2%精度）；再联合独立暗-亮汽笛样本得H₀=69.71⁺²·⁵⁵₋₂·₄₀ (stat) ± 1.54 (cal) km s⁻¹ Mpc⁻¹（3.5%精度）。在引入光度距离先验时，Planck锚定恢复H₀=67.62±0.72 km s⁻¹ Mpc⁻¹，SH0ES锚定恢复H₀=72.91±0.72 km s⁻¹ Mpc⁻¹，且对对立锚定产生≥4σ的排斥。

Conclusion: 基于AGN宿主引力波事件的H₀测量在精度上已达到可与传统方法比较的水平，其结果同时兼容Planck和SH0ES两种先验测量，未对当前哈勃常数张力（Hubble tension）给出偏向性裁决。但该方法在引入先验假设时可实现对对立宇宙学锚定的>4σ排除，表明其具备区分不同宇宙学模型的统计潜力。未来随着引力波事件样本的增加，该方法有望成为解决哈勃张力问题的独立关键手段。

Abstract: We measure the Hubble constant $H_0$ using 13 gravitational-wave binary black hole mergers associated with active galactic nucleus hosts. We find $H_0=70.50^{+3.37}_{-2.89}\,({\rm stat})\pm1.56\,({\rm cal})$\,km\,s$^{-1}$\,Mpc$^{-1}$ ($4.4\%$ precision), consistent with both Planck\,2018 ($0.98σ$) and SH0ES\,2024 ($0.76σ$), with no significant preference between the two. Combining with the bright siren GW170817 sharpens the constraint to $H_0=70.31^{+3.00}_{-2.85}\,({\rm stat})\pm1.55\,({\rm cal})$\,km\,s$^{-1}$\,Mpc$^{-1}$ ($4.2\%$ precision), and further combining with an independent dark-and-bright-siren sample tightens it to $H_0=69.71^{+2.55}_{-2.40}\,({\rm stat})\pm1.54\,({\rm cal})$\,km\,s$^{-1}$\,Mpc$^{-1}$ ($3.5\%$ precision). Assuming a luminosity-distance prior centered around the value related to a fixed cosmology in turn, recovers $H_0=67.62\pm0.72$ (Planck-anchored) and $H_0=72.91\pm0.72$\,km\,s$^{-1}$\,Mpc$^{-1}$ (SH0ES-anchored). We show that under such an assumption, a rejection of $\gtrsim4σ$ to the opposing anchor is obtained.

</details>


### [144] [Strong gravitational lensing constraints on interacting dark energy models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04460)
*F. Villalobos,T. Verdugo,P. Troncoso-Iribarren,N. Piña,J. Magaña*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本研究利用强引力透镜（strong gravitational lensing）观测数据，检验了暗物质（dark matter）与暗能量（dark energy）之间的一种相互作用模型，该模型中的相互作用项Q正比于暗物质密度并依赖于减速因子q。结果显示宇宙正在加速膨胀，且支持暗区相互作用有助于缓解哈勃张力（Hubble tension）和巧合性难题（coincidence problem）的观点，同时表明强引力透镜可作为独立的宇宙学探针。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 暗物质与暗能量之间的可能相互作用被视为缓解巧合性难题和哈勃张力的潜在机制，但目前该方向缺乏充分的观测约束，需要利用独立探针进行检验。

Method: 采用强引力透镜观测数据，对一个相互作用模型Q进行宇宙学参数估计，该模型中的相互作用项Q正比于暗物质密度且依赖于减速因子q。

Result: 估计结果与加速膨胀宇宙的图像一致，并支持暗区相互作用有助于缓解宇宙膨胀历史中现有张力的观点。

Conclusion: 本研究的结果与先前研究一致，表明暗区相互作用可能缓解宇宙学中的现有张力，并凸显了强引力透镜作为独立宇宙学探针的潜力。

Abstract: The possible interaction between dark matter and dark energy has been proposed as a mechanism to alleviate the coincidence problem and the Hubble tension. Strong gravitational lensing observations provide valuable constraints to test the properties of the dark components of the Universe. We present estimates of cosmological parameters employing strong lensing data for an interaction model Q, proportional to the dark matter density and dependent on the deceleration parameter q. The obtained results are consistent with an accelerating Universe. Furthermore, these results agree with previous studies suggesting that an interaction in the dark sector may help alleviate existing tensions in the expansion history of the Universe and highlight the potential of strong gravitational lensing as an independent cosmological probe.
