### [145] [Inverse-k Primordial Oscillations from a Symbolic Regression Search](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04925)
*Ze-Yu Peng,Qing-Yu Lan,Yun-Song Piao*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文利用符号回归（symbolic regression）对原初功率谱中的振荡特征进行无模板搜索，发现逆k振荡（cos(B/k)）在Planck及Planck+ACT+SPT-3G数据中均为最优的低复杂度特征，相比传统线性与对数振荡模板拟合效果最好，但振幅非零的证据较弱。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 原初功率谱（primordial power spectrum）中的振荡特征可能是早期宇宙新物理的信号，但以往研究多依赖固定模板（fixed templates）进行搜索，存在模型依赖性问题。本文旨在发展一种无需预设模板的方法，以更无偏的方式探索数据中可能存在的振荡特征。

Method: 采用符号回归（symbolic regression）这种机器学习技术，对原初功率谱进行无模板（template-free）的特征搜索。分别使用Planck单独数据集以及Planck+ACT+SPT-3G联合数据集进行分析，并将符号回归发现的逆k振荡模板与传统的线性振荡和对数振荡（logarithmic oscillating）模板进行对比。

Result: 两个数据集独立选出了逆k振荡形式 cos(B/k)（其中B≈4 Mpc⁻¹）作为最优的低复杂度特征。该逆k模板对数据的拟合优于标准线性与对数振荡模板，但振幅非零的统计偏好较弱。

Conclusion: 符号回归作为一种强大的机器学习方法，能够为宇宙学发现提供可解释的、模型无关（model-independent）的分析路径，有助于在原初功率谱搜索中发现潜在的新物理信号。

Abstract: Oscillatory features in the primordial power spectrum, potential signatures of new physics in the early universe, are usually searched for using fixed templates. In this work, we perform a template-free search for primordial features using symbolic regression. We find that both Planck and the combined Planck+ACT+SPT-3G datasets independently select an inverse-$k$ oscillation, $\cos(B/k)$ with $B\simeq4\,\mathrm{Mpc}^{-1}$, as the leading low-complexity feature. Comparing this inverse-$k$ template with standard linear and logarithmic oscillating templates, we find that it fits the data best, showing a weak preference for a non-zero amplitude. Our results show that symbolic regression as a powerful machine learning technique can provide an interpretable, model-independent approach to cosmological discovery.

</details>


### [146] [Modeling Uncertainties in Modified Gravity Predictions for the Stochastic Gravitational-Wave Background](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05331)
*Rodrigo Fraga,Rafael C. Nunes*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文研究了修正引力对由未解析双黑洞并合产生的随机引力波背景（SGWB）的影响，分别考虑了波形产生修正（ppE框架）和宇宙学传播效应（修正引力波光度距离）两类超出广义相对论（GR）的效应，并通过注入-恢复分析表明，第三代探测器（尤其是Cosmic Explorer）能够有效约束频率依赖的ppE修正，而传播效应则与天体物理不确定性存在更强的简并。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有对广义相对论（General Relativity, GR）的检验主要依赖于单一可分辨的致密天体并合事件，而随机引力波背景（stochastic gravitational-wave background, SGWB）作为大量未解析天体事件的总和，可能提供互补的检验途径。本文旨在系统评估修正引力效应对SGWB的影响，并探究未来引力波探测器能否通过SGWB区分这些超出GR的信号。

Method: 采用参数化后爱因斯坦（parametrized post-Einsteinian, ppE）框架描述波形产生修正，并引入修正的引力波光度距离（luminosity distance）刻画宇宙学传播效应。天体物理不确定性通过幂律加峰值（Power-Law plus Peak）质量模型与Madau-Dickinson并合率演化模型一致纳入。针对Advanced LIGO、爱因斯坦望远镜（Einstein Telescope, ET）和宇宙探测器（Cosmic Explorer, CE），开展注入-恢复分析（injection-recovery analyses），联合变化修正引力参数与天体物理种群参数。

Result: 频率依赖的ppE修正会在SGWB谱形中产生特征性畸变，第三代探测器（尤其是CE）能够对此进行有意义的约束。相比之下，修正传播效应主要引起平滑的振幅重新标度，与天体物理不确定性之间存在更强的简并（degeneracy）。

Conclusion: 未来的SGWB观测将提供贯穿宇宙历史的引力物理补充探针，可能开辟超越单个可分辨致密天体事件来检验广义相对论偏差的新途径。

Abstract: We investigate the impact of modified gravity on the stochastic gravitational-wave background (SGWB) generated by a cosmological population of unresolved binary black hole mergers. We consider two complementary classes of beyond-General Relativity (GR) effects: waveform-generation modifications described within the parametrized post-Einsteinian (ppE) framework and cosmological propagation effects associated with a modified gravitational-wave luminosity distance. Astrophysical uncertainties in the binary black hole population are consistently incorporated using a Power-Law plus Peak mass model combined with a Madau--Dickinson merger-rate evolution. Using SGWB forecasts for Advanced LIGO, the Einstein Telescope (ET), and Cosmic Explorer (CE), we perform injection-recovery analyses jointly varying modified-gravity and astrophysical population parameters. We show that frequency-dependent ppE corrections produce characteristic distortions in the SGWB spectral shape and can be meaningfully constrained by third-generation detectors, particularly CE. In contrast, modified propagation effects mainly induce smooth amplitude rescalings and exhibit stronger degeneracies with astrophysical uncertainties. Our results demonstrate that future SGWB observations will provide a complementary probe of gravitational physics across cosmic history and may open new avenues for testing deviations from GR beyond individually resolved compact-binary events.

### [147] [Investigating a Possible Variation of the Gravitational Constant Through Gas Mass Fraction Measurements and Type Ia Supernovae Observations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05367)
*L. R. Colaço,R. F. L. Holanda,Marcelo Ferreira*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验引力常数（gravitational constant, G）是否随时间变化是验证广义相对论（general relativity）及替代引力理论（如标量-张量理论、屏蔽修正引力框架）的关键途径之一。

Method: 采用非参数（non-parametric）方法，利用X射线观测的星系团气体质量分数（gas mass fraction）作为宇宙学探针，同时考虑G变化通过钱德拉塞卡质量-光度关系（Chandrasekhar mass-luminosity relation）对Ia型超新星（SNe Ia）本征光度的影响；结合气体质量分数测量与Pantheon+样本的亮度距离，通过高斯过程（Gaussian Processes）重建G的演化。

Result: 恒定引力耦合（constant gravitational coupling）与观测数据总体一致，但允许低红移（low-redshift）区域存在轻微偏离。

Conclusion: 当前数据不支持引力常数存在显著时间变化，但为进一步检验修正引力理论提供了观测约束。

Abstract: In this paper, we investigate a possible time variation of the gravitational constant (G) using a non-parametric approach. Our main cosmological probe is the gas mass fraction of galaxy clusters measured from X-ray observations. We also account for the effect of a varying $G$ on the intrinsic luminosity of type Ia supernovae (SNe Ia) through the Chandrasekhar mass-luminosity relation. We consider a specific phenomenological scenario, motivated by some scalar-tensor and screened modified-gravity frameworks, in which the standardized luminosity of SNe Ia decreases with increasing Chandrasekhar mass. Using gas mass fraction measurements jointly with luminosity distances from the Pantheon+ compilation, we reconstruct the evolution of G through Gaussian Processes. Our results indicate that a constant gravitational coupling remains broadly consistent with the data, although mild low-redshift departures are allowed.

### [148] [Effects of Solar Wind Plasma Noise on Stochastic Gravitational Wave Background Searches with the LISA-Taiji Network](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05368)
*Mengfei Sun,Borui Wang,Jie Wu,Jin Li,Shengyi Ye*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本研究分析了LISA-Taiji双探测器网络中太阳风等离子体噪声对引力波背景（SGWB）交叉相关测量的影响，发现探测器间相关的等离子体噪声可导致参数估计偏差，其影响无法仅从单探测器残差噪声水平评估。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LISA-Taiji双探测器网络通过交叉相关（cross correlation）测量可提高毫赫兹频段随机引力波背景（SGWB）的灵敏度，但太阳风等离子体可能产生探测器间相关的噪声，进而偏置SGWB交叉相关估计。现有研究尚未充分评估这种互联噪声对参数估计的具体影响。

Method: 利用Wind/SWE的高时间分辨率电子密度数据，采用Lomb-Scargle方法估计太阳风电子密度涨落谱；将等离子体噪声传播至LISA-Taiji网络的TDI A/E通道；考虑有限臂传播、泰勒冻结流空间相关性（Taylor frozen flow spatial correlations）以及网络重叠缩减响应（network overlap reduction response），计算探测器间等离子体噪声引起的SGWB参数偏差。

Result: 单探测器等离子体残差低于参考噪声，但探测器间相关成分可直接进入SGWB交叉相关估计器。对于幂律SGWB，等离子体引起的参数偏差可达相应Fisher参数不确定度的12.73%；对于M2/M3宇宙弦谱，ln Gmu的偏差可达相应Fisher参数不确定度的19.26%。

Conclusion: 太阳风等离子体噪声对SGWB参数估计的影响无法仅从单探测器残差噪声水平评估；在LISA-Taiji的SGWB搜索中，探测器间相关的等离子体噪声分量会直接影响参数估计。

Abstract: The LISA-Taiji dual detector network improves millihertz SGWB sensitivity through cross correlation measurements. Solar wind plasma, however, can generate plasma noise correlated between detectors and bias SGWB cross correlation estimates. We use high time resolution electron density data from Wind/SWE, estimate the solar wind electron density fluctuation spectrum with the Lomb-Scargle method, and propagate the resulting plasma noise to the TDI A/E channels of the LISA-Taiji network. By including finite arm propagation, Taylor frozen flow spatial correlations, and the network overlap reduction response, we compute the SGWB parameter bias induced by interdetector plasma noise. Although the single detector plasma residual is below the reference noise, the component correlated between detectors can enter the SGWB cross correlation estimator directly. Under dual detector scale coverage, the plasma induced parameter bias for a power law SGWB can reach 12.73% of the corresponding Fisher parameter uncertainty. For M2/M3 cosmic string spectra, the bias in ln Gmu can reach 19.26% of the corresponding Fisher parameter uncertainty for the network configurations, observing times, and frequency bands considered here. These results show that the impact of solar wind plasma noise cannot be assessed from the single detector residual noise level alone. In LISA-Taiji SGWB searches, the interdetector correlated component of this noise can directly affect parameter estimation.

</details>

### [149] [Integral representations of $f$-divergences for general von Neumann algebras](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05195)
*Ricardo Correa da Silva,Markus B. Fröb,Gandalf Lechner,Leonardo Sangaletti*

Main category: math.OA

TL;DR: 本文在一般冯·诺依曼代数上定义并分析了曲棍球散度（hockeystick divergences）和 $f$-散度（$f$-divergences），将其推广并统一了经典概率论和有限维冯·诺依曼代数中的已有工作。通过自伴正规范函子的约当分解导出这些态可区分度量的主要性质（单调性、凸性、半连续性、边界、态区分、数据处理不等式），并通过积分表示将 $f$-散度与曲棍球散度联系起来，同时指出 $f_0$-散度（由信息函数 $f_0(t)=t\ln t$ 给出）与 Araki 相对熵等价，从而将 Frenkel 的结果推广到一般冯·诺依曼代数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将经典概率和有限维冯·诺依曼代数中已有的 $f$-散度与曲棍球散度理论推广到一般冯·诺依曼代数（general von Neumann algebras）上，实现更广泛的统一框架。

Method: 利用自伴正规范函子的约当分解（Jordan decomposition）导出态可区分度量的所有主要性质；通过将 $f$-散度表示为曲棍球散度的积分来建立二者的联系。

Result: 成功定义并分析了在一般冯·诺依曼代数上正规正泛函的曲棍球散度和 $f$-散度，证明了 $f_0$-散度（信息函数 $f_0(t)=t\ln t$）与 Araki 相对熵（Araki's relative entropy）等价，将 Frenkel 的结果推广到一般情形。

Conclusion: 该工作统一并推广了散度理论的已有结果，为量子假设检验（quantum hypothesis testing）等应用提供了更一般的数学基础。

Abstract: We define and analyze hockeystick divergences and $f$-divergences for normal positive functionals on general von Neumann algebras, generalizing and unifying previous work in classical probability and finite-dimensional von Neumann algebras. All the main properties of these state distinguishability measures (including in particular monotonicity, convexity, semicontinuity, bounds, state discrimination, data processing inequality) are derived from properties of the Jordan decomposition of selfadjoint normal functionals. This is done by representing the $f$-divergences as integrals over hockeystick divergences, and their significance in quantum hypothesis testing is reviewed. The $f_0$-divergence given by the information function $f_0(t) = t \ln t$ is shown to coincide with Araki's relative entropy, extending results of Frenkel to general von Neumann algebras.

</details>

### [150] [The SKAO Pulsar Timing Array](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03059)
*Ryan M. Shannon,N. D. Ramesh Bhat,Aurélien Chalumeau,Siyuan Chen,H. Thankful Cromartie,A. Gopakumar,Kathrin Grunthal,Jeffrey S. Hazboun,Francesco Iraci,Bhal Chandra Joshi,Ryo Kato,Michael J. Keith,Kejia Lee,Kuo Liu,Hannah Middleton,Matthew T. Miles,Chiara M. F. Mingarelli,Aditya Parthasarathy,Daniel J. Reardon,Golam M. Shaifullah,Keitaro Takahashi,Caterina Tiburzi,Riccardo J. Truant,Xiao Xue,Andrew Zic*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: 本文论证了利用平方千米阵列天文台（SKAO）构建脉冲星计时阵列（PTA）以在纳赫兹频段探测引力波背景（gravitational-wave background）的科学必要性、技术方案与预期影响，并阐述了与其他2030年代大型设施的互补性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有脉冲星计时阵列（PTA）实验已发现引力波背景（gravitational-wave background）存在的有力证据，但需要更多毫秒脉冲星（millisecond pulsar）及更高计时精度才能实现确定性探测并研究引力波辐射源。SKAO望远镜凭借比任何其他南半球设施高出3–4倍的灵敏度，有望填补这一关键空白。

Method: 本文为综述性章节，通过分析PTA观测中存在的引力波类别及可产生这些信号的源，讨论如何利用SKAO PTA进行探测与研究；同时描述了必须抑制的天体物理噪声源、SKAO PTA实验的现实实现方案及其与2030年代其他PTA实验的关联，并论证甚长基线干涉测量（very long baseline interferometry）如何提升SKAO PTA的灵敏度。

Result: SKAO PTA能够以更高灵敏度探测和研究纳赫兹引力波（nanohertz gravitational waves），通过对更多毫秒脉冲星进行更高精度计时来加速确认引力波背景信号。SKAO PTA将提供与2030年代其他大型设施互补的宇宙图景。

Conclusion: SKAO PTA是实现纳赫兹引力波天文学确定性突破的关键实验平台，其在2030年代将与其他PTA实验及大型设施协同，共同推动引力波天文学与基础物理检验的发展。

Abstract: Pulsar timing arrays (PTAs) are ensembles of millisecond pulsars observed for years to decades. The primary goal of PTAs is to study gravitational-wave astronomy at nanohertz frequencies, with secondary goals of undertaking other fundamental tests of physics and astronomy. Recently, compelling evidence has emerged in established PTA experiments for the presence of a gravitational-wave background. To accelerate a confident detection of such a signal and then study gravitational-wave emitting sources, it is necessary to observe a larger number of millisecond pulsars to greater timing precision. The SKAO telescopes, which will be a factor of three to four greater in sensitivity compared to any other southern hemisphere facility, are poised to make such an impact. In this chapter, we motivate an SKAO pulsar timing array (SKAO PTA) experiment. We discuss the classes of gravitational waves present in PTA observations and how an SKAO PTA can detect and study them. We then describe the sources that can produce these signals. We discuss the astrophysical noise sources that must be mitigated to undertake the most sensitive searches. We then describe a realistic PTA experiment implemented with the SKA and place it in context alongside other PTA experiments likely ongoing in the 2030s. We describe the techniques necessary to search for gravitational waves in the SKAO PTA and motivate how very long baseline interferometry can improve the sensitivity of an SKAO PTA. The SKAO PTA will provide a view of the Universe complementary to those of the other large facilities of the 2030s.

</details>


### [151] [Trigger system for the Payload for Ultrahigh Energy Observations (PUEO) balloon-borne neutrino detector](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05285)
*Q. Abarr,J. Alfaro,P. Allison,J. Alvarez-Muñiz,T. Anderson,H. Barnett,A. Basharina-Freshville,J. J. Beatty,L. Beaufore,D. Z. Besson,M. Betts,R. Bose,D. Braun,B. Chamanbahar,P. Chen,Y. Chen,J. M. TL;DR: PUEO（超高能观测载荷）是一款NASA气球载仪器，基于24块Xilinx RFSoC数字采样芯片构建全数字超采样率波束形成触发系统，用于探测能量超过10^17.5 eV的超高能中微子，在功耗5-7W下实现了最低信噪比约1.5的触发性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探测能量超过10^17.5 eV的超高能（ultra-high energy, UHE）中微子，通过Askaryan效应或向上大气簇射（upward-going air shower）的地磁辐射两种机制实现。

Method: 基于24块Xilinx射频片上系统（Radio Frequency System-on-a-Chip, RFSoC）数字化仪构建全数字超采样率波束形成器（supersample rate beamformer），以3 GSa/s采样率处理192个通道，系统时钟频率375 MHz。触发系统实现频带调节、动态射频干扰（RFI）抑制和匹配滤波（matched filtering），并构建48个合成天线波束（每个最多8根天线），覆盖天顶角约25°、方位角约60°的范围。

Result: 发射前测试（preflight testing）表明，使用模拟信号时触发系统实现了最低信噪比（signal-to-noise ratio, SNR）约1.5的性能，触发逻辑功耗介于5-7 W之间。

Conclusion: 该触发系统在保持探测灵敏度的前提下，通过优化显著降低了功耗和资源占用，验证了基于RFSoC的超高能中微子探测方案的可行性。

Abstract: The Payload for Ultrahigh Energy Observations (PUEO) is a NASA balloon-borne instrument for the detection of ultra-high energy (UHE) neutrinos with energies above $10^{17.5}~\textrm{eV}$ via either the Askaryan effect or geomagnetic emissions from an upward-going air shower. The main instrument trigger system for PUEO is a fully digital supersample rate beamformer based on 24 Xilinx Radio Frequency System-on-a-Chip (RFSoC) digitizers sampling 192 channels operating at $3~\textrm{GSa/s}$ and a system clock frequency of $375~\textrm{MHz}$. The trigger implements frequency band conditioning, dynamic radio-frequency interference (RFI) rejection, and matched filtering, with significant emphasis on optimization to reduce both the power and resource usage while maintaining sensitivity. The system implements 48 total synthetic antenna beams with up to 8 antennas each, covering a $\sim25^\circ$ range in zenith and $\sim60^\circ$ range in azimuth. Preflight testing demonstrated a trigger performance of a minimum signal-to-noise ratio (SNR) of $\sim1.5$ using simulated signals while consuming between $5-7~\textrm{W}$ in the trigger logic.

### [152] [SGN: A python framework for stream-processing pipelines](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03575)
*Yun-Jing Huang,Olivia Godwin,Chad Hanna,James Kennington,Jameson Rollins,Max Melching,Nathanael E Sovitzky,Aaron Viets,Madeline Wade,Zach Yarbrough,Yu-Kuang Chu,William Wyatt Phillips,Surabhi Sachdev,Rhiannon Udall*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: 本文介绍Stream Graph Navigator (SGN)，一个用于构建流式数据处理应用的轻量级Python框架。SGN通过将有向无环图（directed acyclic graph）中的计算组件连接起来构建流处理流水线，其时间序列扩展SGN-TS提供了信号处理方法。SGN和SGN-TS共同支撑了匹配滤波引力波搜索流水线SGNL，并被多个引力波数据分析项目采纳作为可扩展且可维护的框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 引力波（gravitational wave）数据分析的低延迟（low-latency）处理需求日益增长，现有系统在可扩展性和可维护性方面面临挑战。需要一种轻量级、灵活且易于扩展的流式数据处理框架来支撑未来的引力波观测任务。

Method: SGN采用基于事件循环（event loop）的架构，将计算组件连接成有向无环图（directed acyclic graph）来构建流处理流水线。通过时间序列扩展SGN-TS引入信号处理方法（signal processing methods），专门用于处理时间序列数据。

Result: 基于SGN和SGN-TS构建了匹配滤波（matched-filtering）引力波搜索流水线SGNL。该框架已被多个低延迟引力波数据分析基础设施项目采纳，作为可扩展且可维护的框架。

Conclusion: SGN作为轻量级Python框架，为流式数据处理提供了一种有效的解决方案，尤其适用于引力波数据分析领域。其组件化的有向无环图架构和事件循环机制使得系统具有良好的可扩展性和可维护性。

Abstract: We present the Stream Graph Navigator (SGN), a lightweight Python framework for building streaming data applications. In SGN, stream-processing pipelines are built by connecting computational components into directed acyclic graphs that run within an event loop. The time-series extension of the SGN library, SGN-TS, introduces signal processing methods to handle time series data. Together, SGN and SGN-TS provide the foundation for SGNL, a matched-filtering gravitational-wave search pipeline, and are being adopted by multiple projects across the low-latency gravitational-wave data analysis infrastructure as an extensible and maintainable framework for future gravitational-wave observations.

### [153] [Runaway electron induced explosions of graphite; modeling versus controlled DIII-D experiments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03914)
*T. Rizzi,A. Kavroulakis,S. Ratynskaia,P. Tolias,M. Tatarakis,E. Kaselouris,V. Dimitriou,E. Hollmann,F. Brochard,A. Kulachenko,M. Beidler,C. Lasnier,R. A. Pitts*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有石墨在失控电子（runaway electron, RE）冲击下的热力学响应建模仅基于单向耦合的线性热弹性（linear thermoelasticity）与Rankine强度失效准则（strength-based failure criterion），且局限于材料失效的初始阶段，无法描述失效后的非线性损伤行为。

Method: 通过引入Johnson-Holmquist本构模型（Johnson-Holmquist constitutive model）引入塑性，采用基于有效塑性应变（effective plastic strain）的失效准则，并将有限元分析（finite element analysis）与光滑粒子流体动力学（smoothed-particle hydrodynamics）耦合。

Result: 扩展后的热力学模型成功标定（benchmarked）了近期在DIII-D托卡马克上实施的两项受控RE损伤实验结果。

Conclusion: 该工作向最终目标——定量描述钨（tungsten）在失控电子冲击下的热力学响应——迈出了重要一步。

Abstract: The state-of-the-art concerning the modeling of the thermomechanical response of graphite to runaway electron (RE) impact is based on one-way coupled linear thermoelasticity combined with Rankine's strength-based failure criterion and limited to the onset of material failure. Here, the predictive capabilities are extended to the nonlinear damage phase characterized by material fragmentation and debris expulsion. This is achieved by introducing plasticity via the Johnson-Holmquist constitutive model, adopting an effective plastic strain-based failure criterion and coupling finite element analysis with smoothed-particle hydrodynamics. The extended thermomechanical model is successfully benchmarked against the results of two controlled RE-induced damage experiments recently carried out in DIII-D. This constitutes an important step towards the final objective of quantitatively describing the thermomechanical response of tungsten to REs.

### [154] [What if active and passive gravitational masses were not equal?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02614)
*Domenico Giulini*

Main category: physics.class-ph

TL;DR: 本文重新审视了牛顿引力中主动引力质量与被动引力质量之间必须相等的教科书论证，指出该所谓理论证明并不令人信服，揭示了牛顿力学中微妙的结构性假设。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 牛顿力学中，惯性质量与引力质量的等同是众所周知的，但主动引力质量与被动引力质量之间的区别常被忽视。教科书普遍认为二者必须相等，否则将违反牛顿第三定律。作者试图批判性地重新检验这一推理，指出其并非逻辑上无可辩驳。

Method: 作者对标准的教科书论证进行了回顾与批判性分析，审视了其中隐含的假设（subtle structural assumptions within Newtonian mechanics），并重新检验了主动与被动引力质量相等这一结论的逻辑必然性。

Result: 分析表明，常见的理论证明并不具有强制力（not compelling）。牛顿力学内部存在微妙的结构性假设，使得主动与被动引力质量必须相等的结论并非纯粹从牛顿定律中逻辑推导而来。

Conclusion: 该研究为物理教师和研究人员提供了重新审视牛顿力学基础问题的契机，这些问题在观测天文学（observational astronomy）中可能具有潜在的有趣应用。附录还提供了关于伽利略群（Galilean group）及其作为动力学对称群作用的数学背景材料。

Abstract: At first glance, combining Newton's laws of motion with his law of gravitation seems straightforward. Students learn to distinguish inertial from gravitational mass and that their empirical equality is a remarkable fact about nature that will later serve as the conceptual gateway to general relativity. However, a closer look reveals a further and often neglected distinction within Newtonian gravity: that between active and passive gravitational mass. A common textbook argument maintains that these must be equal, for otherwise Newton's third law would be violated. We review and critically re-examine this familiar reasoning and show that the supposed theoretical proof is not compelling. Our analysis highlights subtle structural assumptions within Newtonian mechanics and offers physics teachers and researchers a fresh opportunity to explore foundational questions with potentially interesting applications in observational astronomy. In addition, an extended appendix, which is not part of the published AJP paper, offers some mathematical background material on the Galilean group and its action as group of dynamical symmetries for the type of dynamical equations considered here.

</details>

### [155] [Programmable Hybrid Exceptional Points in Passive Scattering Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03040)
*Kaiyuan Wang,Niall Byrnes,Matthew R. Foreman*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于多端口散射网络（multi-port scattering networks）的全被动、相位调控方法，通过端口投影诱导的非酉性（non-unitarity）实现散射奇异点（exceptional points, EPs），并对其各向异性扰动响应进行定制设计。实验展示了各向异性EP与Dirac型EP的构建，并实现了全局热漂移抑制与局域信号平方根灵敏度保留，为抗噪声增强传感提供了全相位可重构路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 奇异点（exceptional points, EPs）长期被寄望于增强物理信号传感，但其实际应用受到噪声同步增强的限制。如何在对准EP的非解析响应（non-analytic response）以增强目标扰动的同时，有效抑制噪声，仍是一个尚未解决的挑战。

Method: 利用全被动、相位调控的多端口散射网络，通过测量系统端口的子集并通过投影诱导非酉性（projection-induced non-unitarity）实现有效非厄米行为（effective non-Hermitian behavior）。EP设计被表述为投影散射子块（projected scattering sub-block）的判别式（discriminant）及其方向导数（directional derivatives）的形式，并给出了将可编程链路相位数与可实现的黎曼曲面拓扑（Riemann surface topologies）相关联的控制计数规则（control-counting rules）。

Result: 在四端口光子网络中成功构建了各向异性EP和沿两个参数方向具有线性分裂的Dirac型EP。网络基传感器的全局热漂移响应被抑制至3/2幂律标度（3/2 power-law scaling），同时保留了对局域信号的平方根灵敏度（square-root sensitivity）。

Conclusion: 由于有效非厄米性完全源于端口投影，该方法可迁移至集成光子网格（integrated photonic meshes）、微波网格（microwave meshes）、声学电路（acoustic circuits）及投影超表面（projected metasurfaces），为可重构非厄米响应和抗噪声EP传感提供了一条纯相位调控路径。

Abstract: Exceptional points (EPs) have long promised enhanced sensing of physical signals, but have practically been limited by simultaneous enhancement of noise. Aligning an EP's non-analytic response with target perturbations while suppressing noise has, however, remained challenging. Here we show that fully passive, phase-tuned multi-port scattering networks enable scattering EPs with tailored anisotropic response to perturbations. We leverage projection-induced non-unitarity to realize effective non-Hermitian behavior when measuring only a subset of system ports. By formulating EP design in terms of the discriminant of the projected scattering sub-block and its directional derivatives, we give control-counting rules relating the number of programmable link phases to achievable Riemann surface topologies. We demonstrate our framework in a four-port photonic network by designing both an anisotropic EP and a Dirac-type EP with linear splitting along two parametric directions. We further suppress the global thermal drift response of a network-based sensor to a 3/2 power-law scaling while retaining square-root sensitivity to localized signals. Since the effective non-Hermiticity arises purely from port projection, our approach transfers to integrated photonic and microwave meshes, acoustic circuits, and projected metasurfaces, offering a phase-only route to reconfigurable non-Hermitian response and noise-robust EP sensing.

</details>


### [156] [Robust optical design and closed-form tolerancing through autodiff-based Hessian spectral analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03067)
*Bastien Laville,Benjamin Aymard*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文提出基于海森矩阵（Hessian matrix）本征模分解的光学公差分析方法，揭示经典雅可比（Jacobian）灵敏度分析无法捕捉的性能退化耦合机制，并证明完全补偿系统的一阶灵敏度与未补偿系统相同，仅通过海森矩阵的舒尔补（Schur complement）在二阶起作用。提出公差缩放海森矩阵的迹作为单一鲁棒性标量度量，并在离轴三反射镜无焦系统与23参数表面面形模型中验证，可生成确定性公差预算替代昂贵的蒙特卡洛（Monte Carlo）采样。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 鲁棒光学设计需要定量了解制造和装调公差如何降低系统性能。传统的基于雅可比矩阵（Jacobian matrix）的经典灵敏度矩阵分析无法揭示性能退化背后的耦合机制，因此需要更深入的分析方法。

Method: 分析海森矩阵（Hessian matrix）的扰动本征模（perturbation eigenmodes）以获得性能退化机制的定性洞察；利用包络定理（envelope theorem）证明完全补偿系统与未补偿系统的一阶灵敏度等价性；提出公差缩放海森矩阵的迹作为单一鲁棒性标量度量。

Result: 在离轴三反射镜无焦系统（off-axis three-mirror anastigmat）和23参数表面面形模型中，本征模分解揭示了主导灵敏度方向，并生成了确定性公差预算，可替代高成本的蒙特卡洛采样（Monte Carlo sampling）。

Conclusion: 海森矩阵本征模分析方法能够提供传统方法不可见的定性机制洞察，补偿效应仅在二阶层面通过海森矩阵的舒尔补（Schur complement）起作用，所提出的迹度量可直接作为系统鲁棒性的综合评价指标。

Abstract: Robust optical design demands quantitative knowledge of how manufacturing and alignment tolerances degrade system performance. We show that analysing the perturbation eigenmodes of the Hessian matrix gives qualitative insight about the mechanisms of performance degradation (such as couplings) that is invisible to classical sensitivity-matrix analysis based on the Jacobian alone. Via the envelope theorem, we prove that the first-order sensitivity of the fully compensated system is identical to that of the uncompensated one; refocusing only acts at second order through the Schur complement of the Hessian. We propose the trace of the tolerance-scaled Hessian %,$\Tr(\mathbf{S}\mathbf{H}\mathbf{S})$, as a single scalar robustness metric. Demonstrated on an off-axis three-mirror anastigmat and scaled to a twenty-three-parameter surface-figure model, eigenmode decomposition reveals the dominant sensitivity directions and yields deterministic tolerance budgets that replace costly Monte Carlo sampling.

</details>


### [157] [Where Does Surface $χ^{(2)}$ Come From? A Systematic Derivation of Nonlinear Surface Susceptibilities from Bulk Nonlocal Response](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04459)
*Zolla Frederic*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文将共伴论文[Zolla, arXiv:2605.15716]中发展的分布框架（distributional framework）推广至非线性情形，聚焦于二次谐波产生（SHG）中的二阶（χ^(2)）响应。通过将空间矩展开（spatial moment expansion）与分布薄层极限（distributional thin-layer limit）相结合，证明非线性界面响应的全部复杂性在领头阶（leading order）凝聚为两个标量——非线性表面磁化率（nonlinear surface susceptibilities）χ^(2),s_∥ 和 χ^(2),s_⊥。核心结构结果表明：通过单一场参数上的边际积分（marginal integration），非线性表面问题可递归地约化为一个有效的线性问题，其表面磁化率仅由体非线性核（bulk nonlinear kernel）决定。该形式化方法在平面和球面界面上推导出广义非线性麦克斯韦边界条件（Maxwell boundary conditions），并系统得到了曲率修正（curvature corrections）。该方法在Gaussian、Yukawa和张量Lorentz核上进行了示例说明。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的非线性光学界面理论在处理非局域、张量性的非线性本构关系时缺乏统一且简洁的数学框架，尤其是如何从高阶体非线性响应中提取有效的界面响应这一问题尚未得到系统解决。本文旨在建立一个分布形式的严格框架，将非线性界面响应的完整复杂性约化为少量可计算的标量参数，并推导出适用于任意界面几何的广义边界条件。

Method: 采用分布理论（distribution theory）框架，从最一般的张量性非局域二阶本构关系出发，结合空间矩展开（spatial moment expansion）与分布薄层极限（distributional thin-layer limit），将非线性界面响应在领头阶凝聚为两个标量表面磁化率。通过边际积分（marginal integration）实现非线性问题向有效线性问题的递归约化，并在平面和球形界面上系统推导广义非线性麦克斯韦边界条件及曲率修正。

Result: 证明了非线性界面响应在领头阶完全由两个标量参数描述：切向表面磁化率 χ^(2),s_∥ 和法向表面磁化率 χ^(2),s_⊥。建立了关键结构结果，即非线性表面问题可递归约化为有效线性问题。在平面和球形界面上得到了广义非线性麦克斯韦边界条件及曲率修正项。该形式化方法在Gaussian、Yukawa和张量Lorentz核三类典型非局域核上得到了成功验证。

Conclusion: 本文构建了一个统一且可计算的分布形式化方法，将非线性界面光学响应从复杂的张量非局域本构关系约化为极简的标量描述。该方法不仅适用于平面和球面几何，还可系统性纳入曲率效应，为实验和非线性界面光学的第一性原理计算提供了理论支撑。

Abstract: We extend the distributional framework developed in the companion paper [Zolla, arXiv:2605.15716] to the nonlinear case, focusing on the second-order ($χ^{(2)}$) response responsible for second-harmonic generation (SHG). Starting from the most general tensorial nonlocal second-order constitutive relation and combining a spatial moment expansion with a distributional thin-layer limit, we show that the full complexity of the nonlinear interfacial response condenses, at leading order, into two scalars, the nonlinear surface susceptibilities $χ^{(2),s}_\parallel$ and $χ^{(2),s}_\perp$, associated with the tangential and normal components of the electric field, respectively. A key structural result is established: via a marginal integration over one field argument, the nonlinear surface problem reduces recursively to an effective linear one, whose surface susceptibility is determined by the bulk nonlinear kernel alone. Generalized nonlinear Maxwell boundary conditions are derived explicitly for planar and spherical interfaces, and curvature corrections are obtained systematically. The formalism is illustrated on Gaussian, Yukawa, and tensorial Lorentz kernels.

</details>


### [158] [Ultrafast Third-Harmonic Spectral Modulation and Self-Action in Resonant Nonlocal Metasurfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02690)
*Alfonso Nardi,Sonia Freddi,Michael Scalora,Agostino Di Francescantonio,Johann Osmond,Sofia Martins,Attilio Zilli,Marco Finazzi,Michele Celebrano,Monica Bollani,Maria Antonietta Vincenti*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文研究了非局域超表面（nonlocal metasurface）中准连续态束缚态（quasi-bound states in the continuum）增强的非线性自作用效应，揭示了脉冲宽度和共振耦合对不同激发条件下三次谐波（third-harmonic, TH）产生中功率定标和光谱动力学的影响，并区分了纳秒与飞秒两种激发机制。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用两种互补的建模范式：连续波建模（continuous-wave modeling）模拟纳秒激发下的功率定标与高次谐波相互作用；时域模拟（time-domain simulations）解析飞秒激发下的瞬态动力学过程。实验上则分别使用窄带纳秒脉冲和宽带飞秒脉冲激发非局域超表面（nonlocal metasurface），测量共振增强的三次谐波（TH）信号。

Result: 在窄带纳秒激发下，共振增强的TH信号在强光强下偏离三次方定标（cubic scaling）；在宽带飞秒激发下，共振被瞬态驱动，非线性响应编码为TH信号的频谱重塑（spectral reshaping）与展宽。两种机制在对应模拟中均得到复现。

Conclusion: 本研究厘清了具有准连续态束缚态的超表面中非线性自作用的物理图像，将强场束缚与转换效率、定标行为及不同激发条件下的频谱动力学联系起来，为高Q值非局域介电超表面在超快与非线性纳米光子学中的应用提供了指导。

Abstract: Quasi-bound states in the continuum enable exceptional field confinement, strongly reducing the pump intensity threshold for nonlinear light-matter interaction in dielectric metasurfaces. As a result, nonlinear self-action effects, often elusive in bulk nonlinear media, emerge at moderate excitation intensities. Here, we show how pulse duration and resonant coupling govern the nonlinear self-action mechanism in resonantly enhanced third-harmonic (TH) generation from a nonlocal metasurface. We identify two excitation regimes that interact differently with the resonant mode, revealing complementary intensity-dependent responses. Under spectrally narrow picosecond excitation, resonance-enhanced TH generation shows pronounced deviations from cubic scaling at high intensities. In contrast, broadband femtosecond excitation transiently drives the resonance, encoding the nonlinear response in the spectral reshaping and broadening of the TH signal. Simulations reproduce both regimes: continuous-wave modeling captures picosecond power scaling and higher-harmonic interactions, while time-domain simulations resolve femtosecond dynamics. These results clarify nonlinear self-action in metasurfaces featuring quasi-bound states in the continuum, linking strong field confinement to conversion efficiency, scaling behavior, and distinct spectral dynamics under different excitation conditions. This work sheds light on the interplay between pulse duration, bandwidth, and resonant coupling in high-Q nonlocal dielectric metasurfaces, advancing their use in ultrafast and nonlinear nanophotonics.

These results establish electron-beam direct writing as a practical route to site-selective, spectrally uniform green quantum emitters in hBN, offering a promising basis for integrated room-temperature quantum photonic architectures.

### [160] [Griffiths Anomalous Absorption in Sparse-Loss Photonic Lattices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03205)

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文研究具有稀疏损耗位点的光子晶格，发现其光吸收行为类似于格里菲斯物理学（Griffiths physics）：在均匀激发下，透射功率呈现拉伸指数衰减（stretched-exponential decay）并对损耗强度呈现非单调依赖，存在最佳损耗率使吸收最大化。该现象源于稀有的长无损耗片段充当弱耦合长寿命光子通道，而非源于奇异点（exceptional point）物理或干涉效应。通过一个带二元淬火耗散（binary quenched dissipation）的最小紧束缚模型，研究证明稀有区域产生一种普适的格里菲斯型亚指数衰减，稀疏损耗光子晶格为观测无序诱导的反常吸收和稀有区域格里菲斯物理提供了可及平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索光子晶格中稀疏分布损耗位点导致的光吸收行为是否表现出类似格里菲斯物理学的特征，并揭示其背后的物理机制。

Method: 采用一个带二元淬火耗散的最小紧束缚模型（minimal tight-binding model with binary quenched dissipation）进行理论分析。

Result: 在均匀激发下，透射功率呈现拉伸指数衰减和对损耗强度的非单调依赖，存在一个最大化吸收的最佳损耗率。该行为源于稀有的长无损耗片段充当弱耦合长寿命光子通道，而非来自奇异点物理或干涉效应。稀有区域产生一种普适的格里菲斯型亚指数衰减。

Conclusion: 稀疏损耗光子晶格为观测无序诱导的反常吸收和稀有区域格里菲斯物理提供了一个可及的平台。

Abstract: Light absorption in photonic lattices with sparsely distributed loss sites exhibits behavior analogous to Griffiths physics. Under uniform excitation, the transmitted power shows a stretched-exponential decay and a non-monotonic dependence on the loss strength, with an optimal loss rate that maximizes absorption. This behavior arises from rare, long loss-free segments that act as weakly coupled, long-lived photonic channels, rather than from exceptional point physics or interference effects. Using a minimal tight-binding model with binary quenched dissipation, we show that rare regions produce a universal Griffiths-type subexponential decay. Sparse-loss photonic lattices thus provide an accessible platform to observe disorder-induced anomalous absorption and rare-region Griffiths physics.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: We demonstrate controlled transitions between competing radiative and nonradiative decay channels in the up-conversion luminescence of NaYF4:Er3+/Yb3+ nanocrystals placed in proximity to metallic nanowires. The nanocrystal-nanowire separation is used as a key control parameter governing the optical response. An essential aspect of our approach is the removal of inhomogeneous residual polymer layers from the nanowires, eliminating any compromise on distance control and reproducibility in emitter-metal hybrid nanostructures. Replacing them with a well-defined polymer spacer yields controlled access to three qualitatively distinct interaction regimes: luminescence quenching, plasmonic enhancement, and effective decoupling. Transitions between these regimes are shown to reflect changes in the dominant energy relaxation pathways: from nonradiative losses in direct contact with the metal, through modification of the local photonic density of states and coupling to plasmon-mediated modes, to behavior characteristic of quasi-isolated emitters. The plasmonic origin of the emission enhancement in the intermediate regime is evidenced by an increase in luminescence intensity accompanied by shortened decay times, as revealed by fluorescence lifetime imaging microscopy of up-conversion nanocrystals. All experiments were performed on single nanostructures, thereby excluding artefacts arising from aggregation effects and strengthening the interpretation of the observed phenomena. The presented approach provides controlled access to plasmon-modified decay channels and offers a basis for the rational design of functional nanophotonic and sensing structures with tailored optical properties.

*Edilberto O. Silva*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文论证了具有几何挠率（geometric torsion）的介质——即螺位错阵列的连续极限——可通过其材料联络的扭曲场（contortion）实现自旋到轨道角动量的转换，其选择定则为Δℓ=q，与潘查拉特南-贝里（Pancharatnam-Berry）机制（Δℓ=2q）不同；该过程守恒螺旋荷ṽJ_z，且通过偏振分辨光子晶格鉴别器可区分两种机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统Pancharatnam-Berry介质和线性双折射介质通过各向异性指向矢（一个二阶无头场）实现自旋到轨道角动量（OAM）的转换，其选择定则为单位织构荷（texture charge）q对应的Δℓ=2q。本文旨在探索能否通过几何挠率这一不同物理机制实现自旋-OAM转换，并揭示其背后的选择定则与守恒律。

Method: 作者建立了几何挠率介质作为螺位错阵列连续极限的理论框架，将材料联络的扭曲场引入有效近轴动力学，作为秩一矢量场（rank-one vector field）处理。通过傍轴模拟验证了理论预测，并提出了一个偏振分辨的光子晶格鉴别器方案来区分扭转机制与双折射机制。

Result: 几何挠率介质的选择定则为Δℓ=q，而非Pancharatnam-Berry机制的Δℓ=2q。该过程的绕数（winding）由几何和对称性决定，而非Pancharatnam-Berry指向矢；系统守恒螺旋转动荷ṽJ_z=L_z+(q/2)σ_z，同时每个转换光子与缺陷晶格交换(2-q)ℏ的角动量。傍轴模拟显示，圆高斯入射光在反转螺旋度中形成稳定的拓扑量子化涡旋ℓ=+q，在三个瑞利范围（Rayleigh range）内达到83%的转换效率，无需精细调谐。

Conclusion: 几何挠率提供了一种与Pancharatnam-Berry机制正交的自旋-OAM转换路径，其选择定则可通过测量OAM随独立写入的织构电荷的斜率加以区分——扭转机制斜率为1，双折射机制斜率为2。这一发现为光子角动量操控提供了新的几何自由度。

Abstract: Standard Pancharatnam-Berry and linear-birefringent media convert optical spin into orbital angular momentum (OAM) through an anisotropy \emph{director}, a rank-two, headless field, and therefore obey the selection rule $Δ\ell=2q$ per unit texture charge $q$. We show that a medium with geometric \emph{torsion}, the continuum limit of a screw-dislocation array, can convert spin to OAM through the \emph{contortion} of its material connection, which enters the effective paraxial dynamics as a rank-one vector field. The resulting selection rule is $Δ\ell=q$. Its winding is fixed by geometry and symmetry, not by a Pancharatnam--Berry director, and the process conserves the screw charge $\tilde J_z=L_z+(q/2)σ_z$ while exchanging $(2-q)\hbar$ of angular momentum per converted photon with the defect lattice. Paraxial simulations confirm the rule: a circular Gaussian input develops a stable, topologically quantized $\ell=+q$ vortex in the reversed helicity, with $83\%$ conversion over three Rayleigh ranges and no fine-tuning. We propose a polarization-resolved photonic-lattice discriminator in which the slope of the measured OAM versus the independently written texture charge, one for torsion, two for birefringence, separates the two mechanisms.

</details>


### [165] [Calibration of systematic distortions in quantum emitter localization microscopy for deterministic nanophotonic fabrication](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05370)
*Chenxi Ma,Maximilian Heller,Timon Handrup,Yiteng Zhang,Tobias M. Krieger,Thomas Oberleitner,Zenghui Jiang,Xian Zheng,Eddy P. Rugeramigabo,Folke Dencker,Armando Rastelli,Fei Ding,Michael Zopf*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 提出一种基于金纳米盘阵列和Zernike矢量场模型的原位校准协议，可将低温光学系统中的系统偏差降至5.3 nm，并将量子点确定性加工后的发射偏振方差降低49%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子光子技术需要高亮度、不可区分性和可靠偏振特性的量子光源，其最佳性能依赖于发射体在光子结构中的精确定位。然而，现有基于标记的光致发光成像技术受限于定制低温光学装置中未校正的系统畸变，导致集成良率受限。

Method: 使用光刻定义的金纳米盘阵列（gold nanodisk arrays）作为参考，结合Zernike矢量场模型（Zernike vector-field model）对光学畸变进行原位校准。

Result: 在校准数据集之外的验证图案上，残留系统偏差降至5.3 nm，整个视场内二维散点分布为24.6 nm。将该校正应用于半导体量子点（quantum dots）周围圆形台面结构的确定性加工后，发射偏振方差降低了49%。

Conclusion: 该校准策略为实现量子发射体向可扩展量子光子电路中的高良率确定性集成提供了一条实用路径。

Abstract: Quantum photonic technologies greatly benefit from quantum light emitters with high brightness, indistinguishability, and reliable polarization characteristics. Achieving optimal performance relies on the accurate localization of emitters and their deterministic integration into tailored photonic structures with nanometer-scale accuracy. Although marker-based photoluminescence imaging techniques can achieve statistical fitting uncertainties below 10 nm, the ultimate integration yield is often limited by uncorrected systematic distortions in custom cryo-optical setups that compromise metrological accuracy. Here, we present an in situ calibration protocol that uses lithographically defined gold nanodisk arrays as references to calibrate optical distortions with a Zernike vector-field model. On held-out validation patterns beyond the calibration dataset, this correction reduces the residual systematic bias to 5.3 nm with a 2D scatter of 24.6 nm across the analyzed field of view. Furthermore, we demonstrate that applying this correction to the deterministic fabrication of circular mesa structures around semiconductor quantum dots reduces the variance in emission polarization by 49%, indicating improved registration accuracy. This calibration strategy offers a practical route to high-yield deterministic integration of quantum emitters into scalable quantum photonic circuits.

### [166] [Shear and crystallization in deformable granular packings: why don't auxetics order?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02762)
*Joel T. Clemmer,Nicholas W. Hackney,Gary S. Grest*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本研究通过键合粒子（bonded particle）方法模拟三维高压缩颗粒堆积体的剪切过程，发现泊松比（Poisson's ratio）$ν$ 对流变学、堆积结构和颗粒形态产生显著影响：常规材料（$ν>0$）易于结晶，而拉胀材料（$ν<0$）则抵抗有序化，揭示了弹性、几何与结晶之间意想不到的相互作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究在高压缩颗粒堆积体（granular packings）剪切过程中，泊松比（Poisson's ratio）$ν$ 如何影响材料的流变学（rheology）、堆积结构（packing structure）和颗粒形态（grain morphology），并揭示常规材料与拉胀材料（auxetics）在结晶行为上的显著差异。

Method: 采用键合粒子（bonded particle）方法进行三维模拟，明确解析弹性变形（elastic deformation），并通过改变泊松比 $ν$ 来系统考察其对体系行为的影响。

Result: 常规体系（$ν>0$）在流动中容易发生结晶（crystallize），而拉胀体系（$ν<0$）则抵抗有序化（resist ordering）；常规颗粒会形成多面体状刻面（polyhedral-like facets）但保持体积守恒，拉胀颗粒则表现相反。

Conclusion: 颗粒堆积体的剪切行为与泊松比密切相关，弹性、几何和结晶之间存在一种此前未被预见的相互作用机制。

Abstract: Shear of three-dimensional, highly compressed granular packings is simulated using a bonded particle approach that explicitly resolves elastic deformation. Varying Poisson's ratio $ν$ produces significant changes in rheology, packing structure, and grain morphology. During flow, conventional systems ($ν> 0$) readily crystallize while auxetics ($ν< 0$) resist ordering. This duality reflects the fact that conventional grains develop polyhedral-like facets but conserve volume while auxetics behave oppositely, demonstrating an unexpected interaction between elasticity, geometry, and crystallization.

</details>


### [167] [Entropy density functional universality: Correlation, response, and entropic Ornstein-Zernike structure](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03032)
*Matthias Schmidt*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文系统阐述了针对经典多体系统平衡统计力学的熵密度泛函理论（entropy density functional theory），该理论在形式上是精确的，基于一体密度（one-body density）和全局对距离分布（global pair distance distribution）的联合巨势最小化原理，通过唯-的过剩熵泛函（excess entropy functional）描述关联效应，并给出了该理论存在性与唯一性的两种替代证明。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为经典多体系统的平衡统计力学（equilibrium statistical mechanics）提供一个形式上精确且计算高效的熵密度泛函理论框架，弥补标准密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）中通过过剩自由能泛函处理关联效应的局限，并建立熵泛函形式与响应函数、涨落关联函数之间的直接联系。

Method: 提出基于一体密度和全局对距离分布（依赖标量距离，保留低计算复杂度）的联合巨势最小化原理；通过泛函微分导出熵直接关联泛函（entropic direct correlation functionals），并借助耦合的 Ornstein-Zernike 方程生成熵响应和涨落关联函数。采用两种替代证明——Levy 约束搜索法（Levy's constrained search method）的推广和 Mermin-Evans 反证法（Mermin-Evans proof by contradiction）——证明元密度泛函映射（metadensity functional map）的存在唯一性。

Result: 标准平均场（mean-field）和第二维里（second-virial）过剩自由能密度泛函可作为简单过剩熵近似得到；描述了精确的熵泛函线积分（entropic functional line integrals），并与近期的一体涨落剖面（one-body fluctuation profiles）建立了联系；该熵方法还可推广到超越对相互作用势（pairwise interparticle potentials）的体系。

Conclusion: 熵密度泛函理论为经典多体系统提供了一个形式精确、普适且计算高效的平衡统计力学描述，其核心过剩熵泛函在具有对相互作用的系统中具有普适性，并能自然地扩展到更复杂的相互作用类型。

Abstract: We give a comprehensive account of the recent entropy density functional theory for the equilibrium statistical mechanics of classical many-body systems (arXiv:2606.28240). The approach is formally exact and based on a joint grand potential minimization principle for the one-body density and the global pair distance distribution. These variational fields depend respectively on position and on scalar distance, which retains the low computational complexity of standard density functional theory. Correlations effects are contained in a unique excess entropy functional, which is universal across all systems with pairwise interparticle potentials. Functional differentiation yields entropic direct correlation functionals that generate entropic response and fluctuation correlation functions via coupled Ornstein-Zernike equations. Two alternative proofs are given for the existence and uniqueness of the underlying metadensity functional map, based on generalizations of either Levy's constrained search method or Mermin-Evans proof by contradiction. Simple excess entropy approximations yield the standard mean-field and second-virial excess free energy density functionals. We describe exact entropic functional line integrals, make connections to the recent one-body fluctuation profiles, and generalize the entropy approach beyond pairwise interparticle potentials.

</details>


### [168] [Stability and equilibria of a compressible elastic membrane in Stokes flow](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03357)
*Sho Kawakami,Han Zhou,Po-Chun Kuo,Yoichiro Mori,Yuan-Nan Young*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该论文构建了一个可压缩脂质双层膜（compressible lipid-bilayer membrane）的连续介质模型，将脂质密度守恒替代局部面积不可伸缩性。膜自由能结合了Helfrich弯曲能、自发曲率与有限面积压缩惩罚项，使膜张力成为脂质密度变化的本构响应，而非约束局部面积守恒的拉格朗日乘子。由此产生的界面应力包含法向弹性力与脂质重分布引起的切向Marangoni应力；这些应力源于膜的可压缩性，并在局部脂质密度超过偏好值时产生有效负张力。研究进一步推导了二维圆形膜与三维球形膜在完整Stokes流体动力学耦合下的线性稳定性。两种情形下，弯曲稳定基态形状，而过量脂质密度通过增大膜面积而破坏稳定性。最低阶非平凡形状模式首先失稳：二维为m=2模式，三维为j=2模式。失稳附近的能量展开表明，二维不稳定性为叉形分岔（pitchfork bifurcation），而三维不稳定性一般为跨临界分岔（transcritical bifurcation），因为长球与扁球扰动在几何上不等价。这些结果为经典囊泡力学提供了一个可控的可压缩推广，并直接连接了脂质密度变化、膜张力、流体动力学耦合与形状不稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统囊泡模型通常假设膜局部面积不可伸缩，从而将膜张力作为拉格朗日乘子引入。该研究旨在建立一个可压缩膜的连续介质模型，将膜张力直接与脂质密度变化相关联，以更真实地描述生物膜的物理行为。

Method: 建立了可压缩脂质双分子层膜的连续介质模型，自由能由Helfrich弯曲能、自发曲率和有限面积压缩惩罚项构成。在Stokes流（Stokes flow）中推导了界面应力表达式，并对二维圆形膜和三维球形膜进行了线性稳定性分析以及失稳附近的能量展开。

Result: 弯曲项稳定基态形状，而过量脂质密度通过增加膜面积产生失稳。失稳首先出现在最低阶非平凡形状模式（二维m=2，三维j=2）。二维失稳为叉形分岔，三维失稳为跨临界分岔。

Conclusion: 该模型为经典囊泡力学提供了可控的可压缩扩展，建立了脂质密度变化、膜张力、流体动力学耦合与形状不稳定性之间的直接联系。

Abstract: We formulate a continuum model for a compressible lipid-bilayer membrane immersed in Stokes flow, replacing exact local area inextensibility by conservation of an areal phospholipid density. The membrane free energy combines Helfrich bending, spontaneous curvature, and a finite area-compression penalty, so that membrane tension becomes a constitutive response to lipid-density variation rather than a Lagrange multiplier enforcing local area conservation. The resulting interfacial stress includes normal elastic forces and tangential Marangoni stresses generated by lipid redistribution; these stresses arise from membrane compressibility and can produce an effective negative tension when the local lipid density exceeds its preferred value. We further derive the linear stability of circular membranes in two dimensions and spherical membranes in three dimensions under full Stokes hydrodynamic coupling. In both cases, bending stabilizes the base shape, while excess lipid density destabilizes it by favoring increased membrane area. The first instability occurs in the lowest nontrivial shape mode, m = 2 in two dimensions and j = 2 in three dimensions. Energy expansions near onset show that the two-dimensional instability is a pitchfork bifurcation, whereas the three-dimensional instability is generically transcritical because prolate and oblate perturbations are geometrically distinct. These results provide a controlled compressible extension of classical vesicle mechanics and directly connect lipid-density variation, membrane tension, hydrodynamic coupling, and shape instability.

</details>


### [169] [Intermittency Signatures in the Deformation of a Passive Droplet in Active Turbulence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03737)
*Sudeep Halder,Abhishek Chaudhuri*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过全分辨向列流体动力学（nematohydrodynamic）模拟，研究了无源向列液滴在二维伸展型活性向列湍流（active-nematic turbulence）中的变形统计特性。发现液滴纵横比可作为活性浴的标量探针，其增量呈现重尾分布、无标度爆发统计和多标度结构函数，表明时间间歇性（temporal intermittency）。与平移及应力涨落相比，液滴形状的间歇性最弱，体现了界面恢复力的滤波作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解活性湍流中嵌入的软性内含物（soft inclusions）如何响应外界活性驱动，特别是通过无源液滴的变形统计来揭示活性浴（active bath）的动力学特征。

Method: 采用全分辨向列流体动力学（nematohydrodynamic）模拟方法，对二维伸展型活性向列湍流中无源向列液滴的变形进行数值研究，分析其纵横比增量、结构函数、功率谱等统计量。

Result: 液滴纵横比增量呈现重尾分布，具有时间滞后的依赖性、无标度爆发统计和多标度结构函数，证实时间间歇性；平均变形随活性增加而增大，但归一化间歇性在低活性时最强；形状的间歇性弱于平移和活性应力涨落；最大法向界面速度的功率谱呈现近$1/\omega$行为，而界面活性应力谱为约$1/\omega^{2}$。

Conclusion: 界面恢复力将活性驱动转化为爆发式、多尺度的变形动力学，软性内含物（soft inclusions）可作为一种有效的探针，揭示活性浴的间歇性特征及其与界面响应之间的层次关系。

Abstract: We use fully resolved nematohydrodynamic simulations to study deformation statistics of a passive nematic droplet in two-dimensional extensile active-nematic turbulence. We find that the droplet aspect ratio serves as a scalar probe of the active bath. Its increments show heavy-tailed distributions with dependence on the time lag, scale-free burst statistics and multiscaling structure functions which establish temporal intermittency. While the mean deformation increases with activity, normalized intermittency is strongest at lower activity. This suggests slower and more coherent bath forcing. When compared with translational and forcing-side fluctuations, it reveals a hierarchy of intermittency: shape is more weakly intermittent than translation and active-stress fluctuations, consistent with filtering by interfacial restoring forces. Power spectra show an extended near-$1/ω$ regime for the maximal normal interface velocity, distinct from the steeper, approximately $1/ω^{2}$ spectrum of the interfacial active stress. Soft inclusions thus reveal how interfacial restoring forces convert active forcing into bursty, scale-rich deformation dynamics.

</details>


### [170] [Mass weighting algorithm optimizes Fourier-based physics-informed neural network in adhesive contact mechanics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04288)
*Yunong Zhou,Kaifeng Huang,Chaofan Du,Yang Xu,Hengxu Song*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 针对物理信息神经网络（physics-informed neural networks, PINNs）在弹性接触力学中因谱刚度不平衡导致的收敛停滞问题，提出一种傅里叶空间谱预处理（spectral preconditioning）策略，通过质量加权（mass weighting, MW）函数放大低频分量并内置低通滤波器抑制亚网格噪声，使质量加权PINN在400次Adam迭代内达到机器零残差损失，位移与接触应力场定量吻合格林函数分子动力学（Green's function molecular dynamics, GFMD）解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: PINNs在弹性接触力学中存在谱刚度不平衡（spectral stiffness imbalance）——弹性核随波数线性增长，导致短波长模式主导梯度更新，宏观变形收敛停滞。

Method: 在傅里叶空间反向传播前对位移梯度进行谱重加权（spectral reweighting）：通过质量加权（MW）函数放大低波数分量，同时利用内置低通滤波器抑制亚网格噪声。该方法直接在均匀实空间网格上操作，无需显式格林函数积分或求积规则，仅以标量能量函数最小化形式表述。

Result: 在粘着线接触基准问题中，质量加权PINN在400次Adam迭代内达到机器零残差损失，而参考基准损失高出三个数量级且停滞。收敛后的位移和接触应力场在平滑赫兹接触（涵盖从拉伸到压缩的压力范围）及粗糙表面（粗糙度跨越多个波长量级）下均与GFMD解定量一致。

Conclusion: 该方法可扩展至二维粗糙表面问题，因为傅里叶弹性能量和谱预处理算子均仅依赖于波数大小。

Abstract: Physics-informed neural networks (PINNs) for elastic contact mechanics suffer from a spectral stiffness imbalance,that is, the elastic kernel grows linearly with wave number, causing short-wavelength modes to dominate gradient updates and stall convergence of the macroscopic deformation. We introduce a spectral preconditioning strategy that reweights displacement gradients in Fourier space before back-propagation, amplifying low wavenumber components through a mass weighting (MW) function while suppressing sub-grid noise via a built-in low-pass filter. Applied to adhesive line contact problems, the mass weighted PINN reaches machine-zero residual loss within 400 Adam iterations for specified benchmark, whereas the reference benchmark stalls at three orders of magnitude higher loss. The converged displacement and contact stress fields agree quantitatively with Green's function molecular dynamics (GFMD) solutions for both smooth Hertz contact at pressures spanning tension to compression and rough surfaces with roughness covering several decades of wavelength. The method operates directly on a uniform real-space grid, requires no explicit Green's function integration or quadrature rules, and is formulated entirely in terms of minimising a scalar energy function. Extension to two-dimensional rough surfaces is direct, as both the Fourier elastic energy and the spectral preconditioner depend only on the wave-number magnitude.

</details>


### [171] [Synchro-nematic and -antinematic ordering of spheroidal circle swimmers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04589)
*Anson G. Thambi,Alexander N. Dodge,William E. Uspal*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过动理学理论（kinetic theory）和晶格玻尔兹曼模拟（Lattice Boltzmann simulations），研究了手性微型游动物体（chiral microswimmer）之间由于流体动力学相互作用（hydrodynamic interactions）而产生的集体有序态，揭示了由内在旋转、应力张量流（stresslet flows）和类杰弗里重定向（Jeffery-like reorientation）共同导致的相位锁定（phase-locking）机制，并预测了同步向列相（synchro-nematic order）和同步反向列相（synchro-antinematic order）等涌现集体相。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 手性（chirality）为微型游动物体提供了一个直线运动所不具备的变量——相位（phase），该变量既调制又受制于游动体间的流体动力学相互作用。本文旨在探索当多个手性游动体自由运动时，会涌现出何种集体有序态（collective order），以及单个游动体的形状与驱动各向异性（actuation anisotropy）如何决定这一结果。

Method: 基于流体动力学相互作用的圆形游动体（circle swimmers）的动理学理论；通过非轴对称应力张量（non-axisymmetric stresslet tensor）编码驱动各向异性；构建粗粒化场论（coarse-grained field theory）预测流体动力学不稳定性（hydrodynamic instability）导致的向列序（nematic order）；采用晶格玻尔兹曼方法（Lattice Boltzmann method）对手性扁球状游动体（chiral oblate squirmers）进行数值模拟，解析有限尺寸效应和近场流（near-field flows）。

Result: 在成对层面，推力型游动体（pusher swimmers）根据粒子的形状和驱动不对称性，选择两种同步态之一：同相/反相锁定（in-phase/anti-phase locking）或四分之一相移锁定（quarter-shifted locking）。在多体系统中，这些成对同步机制驱动涌现集体相：当流体动力学耦合倾向于平行或反平行相位锁定时，形成全局同步向列序；当四分之一相移锁定占优时，形成局部同步反向列序。此外，集体态表现出由周期平均流体动力学相互作用导致的晶体状或无序超均匀（disordered hyperuniform）结构。晶格玻尔兹曼模拟恢复出同步向列序。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，游动体的几何各向异性（geometric anisotropy）和驱动各向异性可被用于编程手性活性物质（chiral active matter）中的同步化（synchronization）和时空有序态（spatiotemporal order）。

Abstract: Chirality gives a microswimmer something a straight-line swimmer lacks: a phase. This variable both modulates, and is affected by, the hydrodynamic interactions between microswimmers. Here we ask what collective order emerges when many such chiral swimmers are free to move, and how the shape and actuation anisotropies of an individual swimmer dictate the outcome. Using a kinetic theory for hydrodynamically interacting circle swimmers, we show that the interplay between intrinsic rotation, stresslet flows, and Jeffery-like reorientation generates effective phase-locking interactions. Asymmetries in the actuation are encoded through a non-axisymmetric stresslet tensor. At the pair level, pusher swimmers select one of two synchronized states depending on particle shape and actuation asymmetry: in-phase/anti-phase locking, or quarter-shifted locking. Extending the analysis to many-body systems, we find that these pair-level synchronization mechanisms drive emergent collective phases. The swimmers develop global \textit{synchro-nematic} order when the hydrodynamic coupling favors parallel or anti-parallel phase locking, and \textit{synchro-antinematic} local order where quarter-shifted locking prevails. A coarse-grained field theory predicts the onset of nematic order through a hydrodynamic instability criterion. In addition, we find that the collective states exhibit crystalline or disordered hyperuniform structure arising from period-averaged hydrodynamic interactions that are effectively repulsive between swimmers. Lattice Boltzmann simulations of chiral oblate squirmers, resolving finite-size and near-field flows, recover the synchro-nematic ordering. Together, these results show how a swimmer's geometric and actuation anisotropies can be leveraged to program synchronization and spatiotemporal order in chiral active matter.

</details>


### [172] [Statistics of rupture in phantom chain network simulations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04639)
*Yuichi Masubuchi,Takato Ishida,Takashi Uneyama*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本研究通过大规模幻影高斯网络（phantom Gaussian network）模拟，验证了星形聚合物网络断裂主曲线（master curves）的普适性，并系统分析了断裂性质（break stretch、break stress、break energy）与循环秩（cycle rank）的统计涨落及分布特征，指出其与随机熔断模型（random fuse model）的极值统计行为相反。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 此前基于较小样本的幻影链模拟（phantom chain simulation）发现星形聚合物网络的平均断裂性质可崩塌至关于循环秩密度（cycle rank density）的主曲线上。本研究旨在通过大幅扩大样本量，检验该普适性结论的稳健性，并进一步探讨断裂性质的统计涨落特征。

Method: 通过端链接星形预聚物（end-linking star prepolymers）构建幻影高斯网络，设置官能度（functionality）$f=3$–$8$、转化率（conversion）$p=0.60$–$0.95$共30种条件，每种条件收集1000个实现（realization），共计30000个网络。记录每个实现的断裂拉伸比（breaking stretch）$λ_b$、断裂应力（breaking stress）$σ_b$、断裂能（breaking energy）$W_b$及循环秩（cycle rank）$ξ$。

Result: 主曲线在更大样本下保持不变，证实了此前基于较小样本平均值的结论。但个体实现存在内在随机性：在固定$f,p$下，$ξ$的涨落很小（变异小于0.01），而$λ_b$、$σ_b$、$W_b$的散布范围为0.05–0.3；$ξ$的涨落与断裂性质的涨落几乎不相关。散布具有确定结构：其幅度随平均循环秩密度$ξ$增大而减小，$λ_b$–$σ_b$相关性随$ξ$增大而增强，且分布偏离高斯分布（Gaussian distribution）。$λ_b$在小$ξ$时呈右偏分布，$σ_b$在大$ξ$时呈左偏分布。

Conclusion: 基于极值统计（extreme-value statistics）框架的分析表明，观察到的趋势与随机熔断模型相反——后者强度随尺寸减小而降低且弱无序时出现最弱链统计（weakest-link statistics）。这一差异可能反映了涨落的来源不同，即当前网络中的交联（cross-linking）过程。

Abstract: Phantom chain simulations have shown that the mean rupture properties of star polymer networks collapse onto master curves against the cycle rank density $ξ$. This study revisits this universality with a much larger ensemble than in earlier studies to discuss the statistics. Phantom Gaussian networks were made by end-linking star prepolymers, and 1,000 realizations were collected for each of 30 conditions with functionality $f=3$--$8$ and conversion $p=0.60$--$0.95$, giving 30,000 networks in total. For each realization, the breaking stretch $λ_b$, the breaking stress $σ_b$, the breaking energy $W_b$, and the cycle rank $ξ$ were recorded. The master curves are unchanged by the larger sample, demonstrating that the earlier conclusions reported for the averages of smaller ensembles hold. However, the individual realizations are inherently random, and their statistical properties, rather than the individual values, are examined. At fixed $f,p$, the fluctuation of $ξ$ is small, varying by less than 0.01, whereas $λ_b$, $σ_b$, and $W_b$ scatter by 0.05--0.3. The fluctuation of $ξ$ is almost uncorrelated with that of the breaking properties. In addition, the scatter has a definite structure; its magnitude decreases with the mean cycle rank density $ξ$, the $λ_b$--$σ_b$ correlation grows with $ξ$, and the distributions deviate from Gaussian. The $λ_b$ distribution is skewed to the right at small $ξ$, whereas $σ_b$ is skewed to the left at large $ξ$. These rupture statistics were discussed in the framework of extreme-value statistics to demonstrate that the observed trends are opposite to those of the random fuse model, in which strength decreases with size and weakest-link statistics appear for weak disorder. The difference may reflect the source of fluctuation, i.e., the cross-linking in the present networks.

</details>


### [173] [Uniform distributions in nonuniform systems: Wall potentials generating constant density profiles in classical density functional theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04863)
*Jiří Janek,Alexandr Malijevský*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文研究了经典密度泛函理论（classical density functional theory）中对非均匀流体的反问题：寻找能够产生恒定平衡密度分布（即平坦密度分布）的壁面势。在Rosenfeld基本度量理论（fundamental measure theory）框架下，针对硬球流体和含截断Lennard-Jones吸引项的流体，在平面、球面和柱面几何中求解了该问题，获得了显式解析或数值解，并验证了其准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在解决经典密度泛函理论中的反问题——对于非均匀流体，找出能够生成完美平坦密度分布的壁面势。这一问题与界面理论中润湿（wetting）和干燥（drying）现象中的特殊匹配条件下的平坦轮廓条件有关，具有重要的理论意义。

Method: 在Rosenfeld基本度量理论（fundamental measure theory）框架下，对单组分流体在平面、球面和柱面三种几何结构中进行了分析。平面壁情形得到了显式解析表达式；球面壁虽形式较复杂但也获得了解析处理；柱面情形则采用数值方法求解。同时考虑了硬球流体和添加了平均场（mean-field）水平截断Lennard-Jones吸引项的流体。

Result: 获得了三种几何结构下的结构消除壁面势（structure-cancelling wall fields）的显式微观实现。同时推导了加权密度（weighted densities）和单体直接关联函数（one-body direct correlation functions）的紧凑公式集。独立密度泛函计算验证了所得到的解析壁面势能够在数值精度内恢复预设的平坦密度分布。

Conclusion: 本文为经典密度泛函理论中的反问题提供了解析和数值解决方案，获得了可消除结构效应的壁面势，并在平面、球面和柱面几何中得到了验证，为密度泛函实现提供了有用的参考表达式。

Abstract: We study the inverse problem of classical density functional theory for inhomogeneous fluids: finding the wall potential that produces a constant equilibrium density profile, i.e., a perfectly flat density distribution in the accessible region adjacent to a substrate. Within Rosenfeld's fundamental measure theory, we solve this problem for a one-component fluid in planar, spherical, and cylindrical geometries, considering both a hard-sphere fluid and a fluid with an additional truncated Lennard-Jones attraction treated at the mean-field level. Explicit analytical expressions are obtained for planar walls, while spherical walls also admit an analytical treatment in a more cumbersome form. The cylindrical case is treated numerically. The construction provides an explicit microscopic realization of structure-cancelling wall fields, related to flat-profile conditions that occur under special matching conditions in interfacial theories of wetting and drying. The theory also yields a compact collection of formulae for weighted densities and one-body direct correlation functions in the three fundamental geometries, providing useful reference expressions for density-functional implementations. The resulting analytic wall potentials are validated in independent density functional calculations, which confirm that the prescribed flat profiles are recovered within numerical accuracy.

### [174] [Unveiling Structural Bottlenecks of Dynamic Disorder in a Density-Tunable Glass Former: From Strong to Fragile Regimes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04870)
*Shubham Kumar,Shinji Saito*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过可调密度的软排斥二元混合物体系，研究了玻璃态液体脆弱性（fragility）如何影响微观跳跃动力学，发现脆弱性的增大伴随着笼寿命分布展宽、生存概率非指数化，以及控制跳跃速率的慢变量从局域邻居距离波动（强性体系）向扩展邻居重排（中等及脆弱体系）转变，脆弱体系还需引入Voronoi自由体积来描述额外的笼体积涨落。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 玻璃态液体在过冷过程中表现出的强性（strong）与脆弱性（fragile）行为是否源于相同的微观弛豫机制尚不清楚，本文旨在回答这一核心问题。

Method: 采用密度可调的软排斥二元混合物模拟不同脆弱性体系，利用动态无序（dynamic disorder）框架分析粒子跳跃动力学；通过Kullback-Leibler散度和Pearson相关分析识别与跳跃运动最相关的邻居层级；引入结构慢度参数（structural slowness parameter）结合邻居距离涨落构建慢涨落生存概率；比较Voronoi自由体积等结构描述子的适用性。

Result: 脆弱性增大导致笼寿命分布更宽、生存概率更非指数化；强性体系中局域邻居距离涨落控制跳跃速率，中等和脆弱体系中扩展邻居重排变得重要，慢变量空间有效维度增加；脆弱体系在最低温度下距离描述子不足，需引入Voronoi自由体积；点对点关联（point-to-set correlation）随脆弱性增大，但慢变量的空间尺度超过点对点长度。

Conclusion: 脆弱性改变了微观速率涨落的结构瓶颈，将动态无序与多维慢变量联系起来，表明强性与脆弱性行为并非源于同一弛豫机制，而是在慢变量的局域性与维度上存在本质差异。

Abstract: Fragility characterizes how rapidly a glass-forming liquid slows down upon supercooling, but whether strong and fragile behaviors arise from the same microscopic relaxation mechanism remains unclear. Here, we address this question using a density-tunable soft-repulsive binary mixture spanning distinct fragility regimes and analyze particle jump dynamics within the framework of dynamic disorder. Across these regimes, we show that increasing fragility leads to progressively broader cage-lifetime distributions and increasingly non-exponential survival probabilities, revealing non-Poisson cage-to-jump statistics governed by fluctuating jump rates and slowly evolving structural variables. To characterize their structural origin, we first identify the neighbor ranks most strongly coupled to jump motion using Kullback-Leibler divergence and Pearson correlation analyses. We then introduce a structural slowness parameter that combines these neighbor-distance fluctuations into a reduced slow coordinate for constructing the slow-fluctuation survival probability. A comparison with the actual survival probability shows that localized neighbor-distance fluctuations control the jump rate in the strong regime, whereas extended neighbor rearrangements become relevant in the intermediate and fragile regimes, increasing the effective dimensionality of the slow-variable space. In the fragile regime, distance-based descriptors alone become insufficient at the lowest temperature, where the Voronoi free volume captures additional cage-volume fluctuations in the rate-controlling slow variable. Point-to-set correlations grow with fragility, but the spatial extent of the slow variables exceeds the point-to-set length. These results show that fragility changes the structural bottleneck for microscopic rate fluctuations, linking dynamic disorder and multidimensional slow variables.

*Xianggui Zhou,Nengjie Cao,Xiang-Meng Jia,Jinyuan Mao,Jiajia Zhou*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过粗粒化分子动力学（coarse-grained molecular dynamics）模拟，系统研究了抗衡离子（counterion）与共离子（co-ion）的尺寸如何影响聚电解质（polyelectrolyte, PE）刷在不同盐浓度下的结构演化和标度行为（scaling behavior），揭示了离子尺寸对局部电荷补偿及非经典标度行为的微观调控机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 聚电解质刷对盐浓度和离子特异性效应高度敏感，但实际模拟中常偏离经典标度律（例如从渗透刷区间的 $H \propto c_\mathrm{s}^{0}$ 到盐刷区间的 $H \propto c_\mathrm{s}^{-1/3}$）。本文旨在系统探究抗衡离子和共离子的尺寸如何影响PE刷的结构与标度行为，以理解非经典行为的微观起源。

Method: 采用粗粒化分子动力学（coarse-grained molecular dynamics）模拟，在较宽的盐浓度范围内系统改变抗衡离子与共离子的尺寸，分析其对聚电解质刷的离子渗透、电荷补偿及刷高演化的影响。

Result: 抗衡离子尺寸起主导作用：低盐时小抗衡离子更易渗透，增强局部电荷补偿并导致更强的刷塌缩；高盐时刷高对抗衡离子尺寸不敏感，但出现经典标度关系的偏差。共离子尺寸间接影响系统：小共离子削弱局部电荷补偿并抑制刷塌缩，该效应在高盐下更显著。同时减小两种离子尺寸时系统表现出耦合响应。

Conclusion: 本工作提供了离子尺寸与盐浓度如何共同调控聚电解质刷结构响应及非经典标度行为的微观理解，为真实溶液环境中PE刷行为的预测提供了理论基础。

Abstract: The conformation of polyelectrolyte (PE) brushes is highly sensitive to external conditions, particularly salt concentration and ion-specific effects. As salt concentration increases, PE brushes transition from an osmotic brush regime at low salt ($H \propto c_\mathrm{s}^{0}$) to a salted brush regime at high salt ($H \propto c_\mathrm{s}^{-1/3}$). However, deviations from this ideal scaling behavior are frequently observed in molecular simulations. In this work, we employ coarse-grained molecular dynamics simulations to systematically investigate how the sizes of counterions and co-ions affect the structural evolution and scaling behavior of PE brushes over a broad range of salt concentrations. Our results show that counterion size plays a dominant role in regulating ion penetration and coordination with PE monomers. At low salt concentration, smaller counterions penetrate more easily into the brush, leading to enhanced local charge compensation and stronger brush collapse. At high salt concentration, however, the brush height becomes largely insensitive to counterion size, while deviations from the classical scaling relation emerge. On the other hand, co-ion size mainly affects the system indirectly by modifying ion distributions and the local electrostatic environment. Smaller co-ions weaken local charge compensation and suppress brush collapse, with this effect becoming more pronounced at high salt concentration. When the sizes of counterions and co-ions are reduced simultaneously, the system exhibits a coupled response. Collectively, this work provides a microscopic understanding of how ion size and salt concentration jointly govern the structural response of PE brushes and the emergence of non-classical scaling behavior in realistic solution environments.

### [176] [Inhomogeneous thinning of dielectric membranes under uniaxial tension and electric fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04997)
*Xiang Yu,Yibin Fu*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过变分渐近方法推导了介电弹性体膜和板的一致简化模型，利用线性分岔分析和弱非线性分析建立了Hessian稳定性判据与零波数分岔条件的等价关系，揭示了该失稳对应局部颈缩现象，并证明膜模型能准确捕捉失稳起始与局部化行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 从三维非线性电弹性（electroelastic）公式出发，采用变分渐近方法（variational--asymptotic method）推导了膜模型和板模型这两个渐近一致简化模型；随后进行线性分岔分析（linear bifurcation analysis）建立与Hessian判据的等价性，再通过弱非线性分析（weakly nonlinear analysis）研究失稳后行为。

Result: Hessian稳定性判据等价于零波数分岔（zero-wavenumber bifurcation）条件；该分岔导致局部颈缩（localized necking），表现为膜的非均匀变薄；在平面应力（plane-stress）构型下，膜模型能同时准确描述失稳起始和局部化行为，而弯曲效应可忽略。

Conclusion: 本文为Hessian失稳提供了物理解释，建立了能量稳定性分析与分岔理论之间的直接联系，并为介电弹性体膜的失稳分析提供了一个理论框架。

Abstract: Dielectric elastomers exhibit rich electromechanical instabilities arising from the coupling between mechanical deformations and electric fields. A widely used approach for analyzing instabilities in dielectric elastomers is the Hessian stability criterion proposed by Zhao and Suo (2007), which identifies the onset of instability of a homogeneous deformation but does not determine how the deformation develops beyond the instability threshold. To address this problem, we investigate dielectric membranes subjected to uniaxial tension and an electric field. Starting from a three-dimensional nonlinear electroelastic formulation, we derive asymptotically consistent reduced models, including a membrane model and a plate model, using the variational--asymptotic method. A linear bifurcation analysis first shows that the Hessian stability criterion is equivalent to a zero-wavenumber bifurcation condition, thereby establishing a direct connection between energy-based stability analysis and bifurcation theory. A subsequent weakly nonlinear analysis demonstrates that the zero-wavenumber bifurcation gives rise to localized necking, manifested as inhomogeneous thinning of the membrane. Furthermore, for the plane-stress configuration considered here, the membrane model accurately captures both the onset of instability and the associated localization behavior, while bending effects remain small. These results provide a physical interpretation of the Hessian instability and offer a framework for analyzing instabilities in dielectric membranes.

### [177] [Structural crossovers of quasi-one-dimensional patchy hard superellipses](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05081)
*Sakineh Mizani,Martin Oettel,Péter Gurin,Szabolcs Varga*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过转移算子方法（Transfer Operator Method）研究了一种准一维的、带有定向Kern-Frenkel势的硬超椭圆贴片流体的结构与相行为，发现贴片选择性结合与硬核排斥竞争驱动了从水平键合链到垂直非键结构的结构转变，并推广了Wertheim的一阶热力学微扰理论，结合Parsons-Lee硬体理论定量描述了该体系的结构特性与相行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在理解准一维贴片流体（associating fluid）中定向吸引作用与硬核排斥作用之间的竞争如何驱动结构转变，并建立能够定量描述该体系热力学与结构性质的理论框架。

Method: 采用转移算子方法（Transfer Operator Method）进行精确理论分析；推广了Wertheim的一阶热力学微扰理论（first-order thermodynamic perturbation theory），引入与取向相关的未成键位点分数（orientation-dependent fraction of sites not in a bond），并结合Parsons-Lee硬体理论（Parsons-Lee hard-body theory）描述硬核作用贡献。

Result: 在低至中等密度下，选择性贴片-贴片结合促进水平排列和链形成；在高密度下，硬核相互作用有利于无键的垂直排列。压缩过程中，体系从水平键合的链状结构转变为完全无键的垂直排列结构，表现为状态方程（equation of state）中出现平台。贴片椭圆体发生倾斜到垂直的重定向，而贴片矩形类超椭圆体则呈现水平到垂直的转变。

Conclusion: 推广的Wertheim理论与Parsons-Lee理论相结合，能够定量可靠地预测该准一维贴片流体的结构性质与相行为，且该方法可推广至更高维体系。

Abstract: We study a quasi-one-dimensional associating fluid composed of hard superellipses carrying two patches interacting through a directional Kern--Frenkel potential. Using the Transfer Operator Method, we show that the selective patch--patch association promotes horizontal alignment and chain formation at low-to-intermediate densities, whereas hard-core interaction favours vertical alignment without bonds at high densities. The competition between these two mechanisms drives a structural crossover upon compression from a horizontally aligned bonded chain structure to a completely unbonded, vertically aligned structure. While patchy ellipses undergo a tilted-to-vertical realignment, patchy rectangle-like superellipses exhibit a horizontal-to-vertical change. These structural changes manifest as a plateau in the equation of state. To capture these properties, we generalise Wertheim's first-order thermodynamic perturbation theory by introducing an orientation-dependent fraction of sites not in a bond. When combined with the Parsons--Lee hard-body theory, the orientationally resolved perturbation theory provides quantitatively reliable results for the structural properties and phase behaviour. Therefore, the generalised Wertheim theory together with Parsons-Lee theory can be suitable in higher dimensions, too.

</details>


### [178] [Swimming-limited aggregation of bacteria in liquid crystals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05239)
*Guillaume Sintès,Martyna Goral,Teresa López-León,Anke Lindner,Maria Tătulea-Codrean*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文研究了各向异性环境中运动细菌（E. coli）在向列相液晶一维受限空间内的聚集与破碎过程，发现细菌链长度与游泳速度呈正相关，并通过最近邻聚集模型和基于智能体的模拟揭示了这一“游泳限制型聚集”的物理机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 聚集与破碎过程在工程和自然界中广泛存在，但现有理论（如力平衡模型）预测游泳速度与链长无关，与实验观察到的长链游得更快相矛盾，因此需要揭示这一看似矛盾的主动聚集机制背后的物理原理。

Method: 结合实验观察、最近邻聚集（nearest-neighbour aggregation）的简约模型以及基于智能体（agent-based）的一维主动粒子聚集模拟，分析细菌链长与速度的相关性及其时间演化。

Result: 实验和模拟均发现主动粒子链长与速度存在正相关，该相关性与个体速度分布的方差有关，并随时间减弱；细菌链并非随机形成，而是由个体间的相对速度自组织而成。

Conclusion: 提出一种“游泳限制型聚集”（swimming-limited aggregation）机制，其演化受主动粒子固有速度分布约束，为细菌自组织（bacterial self-organization）提供了新的理解视角。

Abstract: Aggregation and fragmentation processes are widespread in engineering and the natural world. Here, we investigate a distinct colloidal aggregation mechanism in an active system of motile bacteria in highly anisotropic environments. Specifically, we examine \textit{Escherichia coli} bacteria swimming in one-dimensional confinement within nematic liquid crystals and observe long-lived chains of bacteria swimming along the nematic director. Crucially, we find that longer chains swim faster, in apparent contradiction to fundamental force-balance models that predict the swimming speed to be independent of chain length, as chains should swim at the average speed of their individual components. The seeming discrepancy is resolved by recognizing that chains do not form randomly but self-organize due to the relative velocities between bacteria. To elucidate the physical mechanism behind this active aggregation process, we combine our experimental findings with a minimal model of nearest-neighbour aggregation and agent-based simulations of active particles aggregating in one dimension. Consistent with experimental observations, our agent-based simulations reveal a positive correlation between the length and speed of dynamically self-assembled chains of active particles, with the correlation depending on the variance of the individual speed distribution and diminishing over time. Together, our experiments and theoretical models indicate a distinct regime of swimming-limited aggregation whose evolution is constrained by the intrinsic speed distribution of active agents, providing new insight into bacterial self-organization.

</details>

### [179] [First measurement of flux of the neutron background induced by accelerated neutrinos at the J-PARC facility](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02783)
*Hiroshi Ito,Ryo Shibayama,Chisako Ise,Akihiro Minamino,Yusuke Koshio,Masaki Ishitsuka*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 本文报道了在日本J-PARC设施中由中微子束意外诱发的中子本底通量的测量结果。利用BGO和液体闪烁探测器，基于2.972×10^{20}个质子数（POT）的数据，观测到88个中子诱导的反冲质子事件，测定的中子通量为[1.45^{+0.22}_{-0.24}(统计)±0.55(系统)]×10^{-7} cm^{-2} s^{-1} POT^{-1}。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 中微子-原子核中性流准弹性散射（NCQE）事件可能被大量中子-原子核散射事件的本底所掩盖，因此需要准确测量J-PARC中微子设施中的意外中子本底通量，以评估其对中微子实验的影响。

Method: 使用BGO探测器和液体闪烁探测器测量意外中子事件，并采用塑料闪烁探测器作为主动反符合（active veto）计数器；通过脉冲形状甄别（pulse-shape discrimination）技术从液体闪烁探测器中筛选出中子诱导的反冲质子事件。

Result: 基于2.972×10^{20} POT的中微子模式数据，在电子等效反冲能量（electron-equivalent recoil energy）0.98–11.60 MeV_{ee}范围内观测到88个中子诱导的反冲质子事件；考虑探测效率和分辨率后，通过与模拟对比，假定指数型中子能谱，测定中子通量为[1.45^{+0.22}_{-0.24}（统计）±0.55（系统）]×10^{-7} cm^{-2} s^{-1} POT^{-1}。

Conclusion: 该测量结果将为评估J-PARC设施中中微子实验的中子本底提供关键参考依据。

Abstract: This article reports the measurement of the neutron background flux accidentally induced by the neutrino beam at the J-PARC facility in Japan. In particular, neutrino-nucleus neutral-current quasi-elastic (NCQE) scattering events, $ν~(\barν)+\rm{N}\toν~(\barν)+\rm{N'}$, can be obscured by a massive background of neutron-nucleus scattering events. The neutrons are produced within the materials (such as sand and concrete) located between the beam dump and the experimental area where the detectors are placed. We measured the accidental neutron events at the J-PARC neutrino facility using BGO and liquid scintillation detectors, with a plastic scintillation detector serving as an active veto counter. Based on a neutrino-mode data set of $2.972 \times 10^{20}$ POT, we observed 88 neutron-induced recoil proton events within an electron-equivalent recoil energy range of 0.98-11.60 $\rm MeV_{ee}$, selected via pulse-shape discrimination in the liquid scintillation detector. Accounting for the detection efficiency and resolution, and through comparison with simulations, the neutron flux was determined to be$[1.45^{+0.22}_{-0.24}~\rm{(stat.)} \pm 0.55~\rm{(sys.)}] \times 10^{-7}~\rm{cm}^{-2} \rm{s}^{-1}\rm{POT}^{-1}$,assuming an exponential neutron energy spectrum. This result will contribute to the evaluation of neutron backgrounds for neutrino experiments at the J-PARC facility.

### [180] [Detection of scintillation light in noble gases with wavelength-shifting optical fibers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04944)
*S. R. Soleti,S. Torelli,G. Martínez-Lema,H. Almazán,A. Beck,A. Castillo,M. del Barrio-Torregrosa,P. Dietz,C. Echeverria,L. Gurriana,Y. Ifergan,I. Israelashvili,F. Lopez,F. Monrabal,E. Oblak,J. Pelegrin,J. G. M. Saraiva,M. Seemann,L. Arazi,J. J. Gómez-Cadenas,V. Álvarez,I. J. Arnquist,F. Auria-Luna,S. Ayet,Y. Ayyad,C. D. R. Azevedo,F. Ballester,J. E. Barcelon,J. M. Benlloch-Rodríguez,F. I. Larizgoitia,A. Larumbe,P. Lebrun,N. López-March,R. Madigan,R. D. P. Mano,A. Marauri,A. P. Marques,J. Martín-Albo,A. Martínez,M. Martínez-Vara,R. L. Miller,K. Mistry,J. Molina-Canteras,C. M. B. Monteiro,F. J. Mora,K. E. Navarro,P. Novella,D. R. Nygren,I. Osborne,J. Palacio,B. Palmeiro,A. Para,A. Pazos,M. Pérez Maneiro,M. Querol,J. Renner,I. Rivilla,C. Rogero,L. Rogers,B. Romeo,C. Romo-Luque,E. Ruiz-Chóliz,P. Saharia,F. P. Santos,J. M. F. dos Santos,I. Shomroni,A. L. M. Silva,P. A. O. C. Silva,A. Simón,M. Sorel,J. Soto-Oton,J. M. R. Teixeira,S. Teruel-Pardo,J. F. Toledo,C. Tonnelé,J. Torrent,A. Trettin,P. R. G. Valle,M. Vanga,P. Vázquez Cabaleiro,J. F. C. A. Veloso,J. D. Villamil,J. Waiton,A. Yubero-Navarro*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 本文研究了基于四苯基丁二烯（TPB）涂层波长位移（WLS）光纤的闪烁光探测系统，在高压气态氙和氩中的性能，测量了光收集效率（LCE）和闪烁波形，验证了该系统在NEXT计划未来高压氙时间投影室（TPC）中的应用可行性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: NEXT计划需要开发适用于高压气态氙时间投影室（time-projection chamber, TPC）的闪烁光探测技术。由于惰性气体的闪烁光主要发射在真空紫外（vacuum-ultraviolet）波段，需要波长位移（wavelength-shifting, WLS）技术将其转换为可探测的可见光。

Method: 研究采用两种探测器配置：一种为配备四块PTFE面板、WLS光纤和温控SiPM（硅光电倍增管）的高压长腔体，另一种为在1 bar氙气下运行、WLS光纤由PMT（光电倍增管）读出的紧凑盒式探测器。两种配置均采用连续气体纯化，利用宇宙线μ子和$^{241}$Am源的α粒子表征探测器响应。

Result: SiPM配置下，氙和氩的光收集效率（light collection efficiency, LCE）分别为${1.18 \pm 0.01~\mathrm{(sta.)}~^{+0.07}_{-0.09}~\mathrm{(sys.)}~\%}$和${1.07 \pm 0.01~\mathrm{(sta.)}~^{+0.06}_{-0.08}~\mathrm{(sys.)}~\%}$；PMT配置下氙的LCE为${0.45 \pm 0.01~\mathrm{(sta.)} \pm 0.05~\mathrm{(sys.)}~\%}$，与SiPM结果在考虑光子探测效率后一致。1.5 bar下宇宙线μ子测量给出产生一个闪烁光子所需的平均能量为$45\pm7~\mathrm{(sta.)}~^{+4}_{-5}~\mathrm{(sys.)}~\mathrm{eV}$。

Conclusion: TPB涂层的WLS光纤系统能够可靠探测高压气态惰性探测器中的闪烁光，其测量的光收集效率可作为实际大规模TPC中预期性能的上限——实际系统中材料吸收和光纤衰减会引入额外的光子损失。

Abstract: Wavelength-shifting (WLS) techniques enable particle detectors based on noble gases, whose scintillation light is predominantly emitted in the vacuum-ultraviolet. We investigate WLS fibers coated with tetraphenyl butadiene (TPB) for scintillation light detection in gaseous xenon and argon at pressures up to 8.5 bar, motivated by future high-pressure xenon time-projection chambers of the NEXT program. Two detector configurations are studied: an elongated high-pressure vessel with four PTFE panels equipped with WLS fibers read by temperature-stabilized SiPMs, and a compact box-shaped detector operated at 1 bar Xe with WLS fibers read out by PMTs. Both operate with continuous gas purification. The detector response is characterized using cosmic muons and alpha particles from a $^{241}$Am source. With the SiPM setup, we measure a light collection efficiency (LCE) of ${1.18 \pm 0.01~\mathrm{(sta.)}~^{+0.07}_{-0.09}~\mathrm{(sys.)}~\%}$ for xenon and ${1.07 \pm 0.01~\mathrm{(sta.)}~^{+0.06}_{-0.08}~\mathrm{(sys.)}~\%}$ for argon. With PMT readout, we measure a LCE of ${0.45 \pm 0.01~\mathrm{(sta.)} \pm 0.05~\mathrm{(sys.)}~\%}$ in xenon, in agreement with the SiPM result once photon detection efficiency is accounted for. Average scintillation waveforms in xenon and argon are studied to assess the time structure of the emitted light. Cosmic-muon measurements yield a mean energy required to produce a scintillation photon $45\pm7~\mathrm{(sta.)}~^{+4}_{-5}~\mathrm{(sys.)}~\mathrm{eV}$ at 1.5 bar, in agreement with the literature. The results demonstrate that TPB-coated WLS fiber systems can reliably detect scintillation light in high-pressure gaseous noble detectors, with a LCE representing an upper limit for realistic large-scale TPCs, where additional photon losses from materials and fiber attenuation are expected.
