### [181] [A high-sensitivity resistance bridge for nanoscale thermal microscopy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03495)
*Wilfrid Poirier,Victor Guillemot,Mohammed Mghalfi,Valentina Valentina Krachmalnicoff,Yannick De Wilde*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 本文介绍了一种基于惠斯通电桥（Wheatstone bridge）和三开尔文臂（Kelvin arms）的测量仪器，可在直流和交流模式下实现高精度电阻测量（精度达10⁻⁴，相对标准偏差低至10⁻⁸）。通过与扫描热显微镜（SThM）结合，该仪器能够测量亚毫开尔文（sub-mK）温度变化，并以数纳瓦（nanowatts）级不确定度测定由表面声子-极化激元（surface phonon-polaritons）耦合引起的近场辐射热通量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在真空或空气中测量微观物体间的热通量因物体尺寸小、介质热导率低而极具挑战。现有方法虽可采用配备温度依赖性电阻温度计的扫描热显微镜（SThM），但该方案需要仪器同时具备精确注入焦耳加热功率和进行高灵敏度电阻测量的能力，现有仪器难以满足此双重需求。

Method: 设计了一种基于惠斯通电桥（Wheatstone bridge）并配备三个开尔文臂（Kelvin arms）的测量仪器。该仪器可在100 Ω至1000 Ω范围内进行直流（direct current）和交流（alternating current）电阻测量，交流频率可达数十千赫兹。结合电热模型（electro-thermal model），分析了扫描热显微镜（SThM）温度计的热时间常数对信号频率响应的影响，从而优化了温度和热通量的测量协议。

Result: 电阻标准测量精度达到10⁻⁴量级，一秒测量的相对实验标准偏差可低至10⁻⁸。在扫描热显微镜测试中，仪器能够测量亚毫开尔文（sub-mK）温度变化，并以数纳瓦（nanowatts）级不确定度测定了加热玻璃微球与玻璃基底之间的近场辐射热通量（near-field radiative heat flux）。

Conclusion: 所提出的仪器方案实现了高精度电阻测量与高灵敏度温度及热通量测量的结合，能够有效解析由表面声子-极化激元（surface phonon-polaritons）耦合驱动的近场辐射传热，为微尺度热测量提供了可行的技术路径。

Abstract: Measurements of heat flux between micro-objects, in vacuum or in air, are challenging because of their small size and the low thermal conductance of the medium between them. One way to address this issue consists in using a scanning thermal microscope (SThM) equipped with a temperature dependent resistance thermometer. However, this requires an instrument able to both injecting a defined heating Joule power and performing highly-sensitive resistance measurements. Here, we present such an instrument based on a Wheatstone bridge equipped with three Kelvin arms. It can perform resistance measurements in the range from 100 $Ω$ to 1000 $Ω$ not only in direct current but also in alternating current regimes at frequencies up to a few tenths of kHz. We first show that measurements of resistance standards are accurate to within one part in $10^4$ with a relative experimental standard deviation which can be as low as one part in $10^8$ for one second measurement. The instrument is then tested with a SThM thermometer. With the support of an electro-thermal model considering thermal time constants of the thermometer, we explain the frequency dependence of detected signals and optimize the measurement protocols of temperature and heat flux. By measuring sub-mK temperature variations, this instrument is then used to determine with a few nanowatts uncertainty the near-field radiative heat flux between a heated glass microsphere and a glass substrate, which is caused by the coupling of surface phonon-polaritons.

# math-ph [[Back]](#toc)

### [182] [Van Vleck spectra of high-order Heun operators:\ finite-band universality and exterior asymptotics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02700)
*Boris Shapiro*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究高阶Fuchs指数为1的Heun算子（Heun operator）的多项式谱问题，建立了有限带行列式表示与普适性定理（universality theorem），证明谱多项式（spectral polynomial）零点归一化后的固定幂和极限仅依赖于算子的最高阶系数，并证明了在外区域上的局部一致收敛性、确定性准则及零根计数测度的弱收敛结果，同时推导了外Cauchy变换的全纯性与WKB周期的Picard–Fuchs方程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典Heun算子是数学物理中的重要对象，其高阶推广的谱性质尚未被充分理解。本文旨在建立这类高阶Heun算子的谱多项式与Van Vleck多项式（Van Vleck polynomials）的渐近行为，揭示其普适性特征，并连接有限带矩方法（finite-band moment method）与势理论（potential theory）。

Method: 采用有限带行列式表示（finite-band determinant representation）构造谱多项式；通过归一化幂和（normalized power sums）的显式常数项公式（constant-term formula）分析零点渐近；结合Van Vleck根的局部化定理（localization theorem）研究Cauchy变换（Cauchy transform）与对数势（logarithmic potential）的局部一致收敛；利用确定性准则（determinacy criterion）刻画弱极限的唯一性；推导外Cauchy变换的全纯性（holonomicity）与WKB周期（WKB periods）的Picard–Fuchs方程（Picard–Fuchs equations）。

Result: 主要结果包括：(1) 谱多项式零点的归一化幂和极限由显式常数项公式给出，仅依赖于最高阶系数$Q_k$，低阶系数仅贡献修正项；(2) 归一化Cauchy变换和对数势在$Q_k$零点凸包（convex hull）的外部区域上局部一致收敛；(3) 若谱根渐近地限制在具有空内部和连通补集的紧集内，则有限带矩确定实际的弱极限；(4) 当$Q_k$的零点共线时，谱多项式的根计数测度弱收敛到该线段上的概率测度，且与低阶系数无关；(5) 在$k=3$的非经典情形下，推导出明确的三阶Picard–Fuchs方程。

Conclusion: 本文建立了高阶Heun算子谱理论的普适性框架：有限带矩的渐近行为仅由最高阶系数主导，低阶系数仅产生高阶修正。根计数测度的弱收敛独立于低阶系数。论文最后提出了一个关于真正复情形的母体猜想（mother-body conjecture），并明确将其与无条件成立的结果区分开来。

Abstract: We study high-order analogues of the classical Heun operator of Fuchs index one, \[
  \dq=\sum_{i=1}^k Q_i(z)\frac{d^i}{dz^i},
  \qquad °Q_i\le i+1,
  \qquad °Q_k=k+1. \] For a fixed degree $n$ we consider the linear Van Vleck polynomials $V$ for which $\dq+V$ has a polynomial solution of degree $n$, and we form the spectral polynomial $Sp_n$ whose zeros are the zeros of these Van Vleck polynomials. The main result is a finite-band determinant representation and the resulting universality theorem: after normalization, all fixed power sums of the zeros of $Sp_n$ have limits given by explicit constant-term formulae depending only on the leading coefficient $Q_k$. The lower coefficients of $\dq$ enter only lower order correction terms. Combining this with the localization theorem for Van Vleck roots, we strengthen the usual germ-at-infinity conclusion to locally uniform convergence of the normalized Cauchy transforms and logarithmic potentials on the whole exterior of the convex hull of the zeros of $Q_k$.
  We also prove a determinacy criterion: if the spectral roots are asymptotically confined to a compact set with empty interior and connected complement, then the finite-band moments determine the actual weak limit. In particular, when the zeros of $Q_k$ are collinear the root-counting measures of $Sp_n$ converge weakly to a probability measure supported on the corresponding segment; this limit is independent of all lower coefficients of $\dq$. Finally, we prove holonomicity of the exterior Cauchy transform and derive Picard--Fuchs equations for the WKB periods, with an explicit third-order equation in the first non-classical case $k=3$. The paper ends with a precise mother-body conjecture for the genuinely complex case, clearly separated from the unconditional results.

</details>


### [183] [Transition-Set Morphometry for Inter-Scale Contacts in Digital Sandstones](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02737)
*O. M. Kiselev*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种过渡集形态测量法（transition-set morphometry），用于量化数字砂岩中孔隙、喉道与裂缝等不同尺度几何子系统之间的接触结构，并通过渗透率预测验证了该描述子的信息承载能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 数字岩石物理中，不同尺度（如孔隙体、喉道、裂缝）之间的接触结构缺乏系统的定量描述方法，现有形态测量工具难以有效捕捉跨尺度（inter-scale）几何接触信息，进而限制了结构描述子对宏观物性（如渗透率）的预测能力。

Method: 将孔隙体积、介质孔喉子系统和裂缝孔隙度视为不同的几何子系统，定义它们之间的有限邻域接触为过渡集（transition sets），如T_VL、T_VF及T_LF（当残存骨架可解时）。测量这些过渡集的密度、有限尺度维数（finite-scale dimension）及带权接触测度（weighted contact measures）。

Result: 在21个数字砂岩样本上的矩阵模式测试表明，单一过渡维数d_VL的独立预测增益很小，而结合过渡集密度与局部孔隙半径的接触测度更具信息量。自适应测度\widehat C_{VL}^{(d+1)}将留一法R²从0.752提升至0.881（合并样本），在DRP-317子集中从0.287提升至0.807。裂缝数据集上的迁移测试进一步支持了过渡集的可重复性。

Conclusion: 过渡集可作为可重复的形态测量描述子（reproducible morphometric descriptors），有效表征跨尺度接触结构，并显著提升渗透率预测性能。

Abstract: This paper introduces a transition-set morphometry for quantifying inter-scale contacts in digital sandstones. Pore volume, a medial pore-throat subsystem, and fracture porosity are treated as distinct geometric subsystems. Their finite-neighborhood contacts are represented by transition sets such as $T_{VL}$, $T_{VF}$, and, when a residual skeleton is resolved, $T_{LF}$. The method measures the density, finite-scale dimension, and weighted contact measures of these sets. A matrix-mode test was performed on 21 digital sandstone samples from the Imperial College micro-CT collection and Digital Porous Media Portal dataset DRP-317. Permeability, expressed as $\log_{10}K$, served as an external response for assessing how much structural information the descriptors carry. The transition dimension $d_{VL}$ alone produced little independent predictive gain, whereas contact measures combining transition-set density with local pore radius were more informative. The adaptive measure $\widehat C_{VL}^{(d+1)}=μ_{VL}(\overline D_{VL}/D_*)^{d_{VL}+1}$ increased leave-one-out $R^2$ from 0.752 to 0.881 in the combined sample and from 0.287 to 0.807 within DRP-317. Fractured datasets DRP-5, DRP-31, and DRP-285 were then used to test the transfer of the same transition-set construction to fracture-related contacts. The results support transition sets as reproducible morphometric descriptors of inter-scale contact.

</details>


### [184] [A new PBW basis for the alternating central extension of the $q$-Onsager algebra](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02849)
*Haoran Zhu*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明了交错生成元（alternating generators）在另一种块序（block order）下也构成$\mathcal A_q$（$q$-Onsager代数的交错中心扩张）的PBW基，从而验证了Terwilliger的一个猜想。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过分析交错生成元在不同块序下的代数结构性质，证明乘法诱导出一个向量空间同构（vector-space isomorphism）$\mathcal W^-\otimes\mathcal G\otimes\widetilde{\mathcal G}\otimes\mathcal W^+ \longrightarrow \mathcal A_q$，从而建立新的PBW基。

Result: 成功建立了$\mathcal A_q$的一个新PBW基，该基对应于块序$\mathcal W^-<\mathcal G<\widetilde{\mathcal G}<\mathcal W^+$，并确认了Terwilliger的猜想。

Conclusion: 交错生成元可以在至少两种不同的块序下构成$\mathcal A_q$的PBW基，表明该代数具有丰富的PBW基结构。这为$q$-Onsager代数（$q$-Onsager algebra）及其交错中心扩张（alternating central extension）的进一步研究提供了新的代数基础。

Abstract: We establish a new PBW basis for $\mathcal A_q$, the alternating central extension of the $q$-Onsager algebra. We prove that they also form a PBW basis in the different block order $\mathcal W^-<\mathcal G<\widetilde{\mathcal G}<\mathcal W^+$. Consequently, multiplication induces a vector-space isomorphism \[ \mathcal W^-\otimes\mathcal G\otimes\widetilde{\mathcal G}\otimes\mathcal W^+ \longrightarrow \mathcal A_q, \] thereby confirming a conjecture of Terwilliger.

Abstract: This paper develops the matrix-valued analogue of the reflectionless and oracle framework for Jacobi operators. ### [186] [Anomalous rate of eigenstate thermalisation at singularities of the density of states](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03546)
*László Erdős,Joscha Henheik,Volodymyr Riabov*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明了一类具有一般关联结构的大N×N平均场随机矩阵的本征态热化假说（ETH），推翻了基于半经典理论的Feingold–Peres预测，并揭示了依赖多预解局部律（multi-resolvent local laws）的真实机制。分析发现，除尖点区域外，谱边界的本征向量涨落尺度与体区域一致，均为N^{-1}，与Haar酉矩阵相同。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子混沌领域中，Feingold和Peres基于半经典理论（semiclassical theory）提出了关于本征向量涨落的具体预测，但该预测的正确性在一般平均场随机矩阵模型中尚缺乏严格证明。本文旨在严格验证本征态热化假说（Eigenstate Thermalisation Hypothesis, ETH），并澄清Feingold–Peres预测的失效原因。

Method: 采用多预解局部律（multi-resolvent local laws）作为核心分析工具，对具有一般关联结构的大N×N平均场随机矩阵（mean-field random matrices）进行严格推导。通过求解底层矩阵Dyson方程（matrix Dyson equation）的精细抵消机制，建立微正则系综（microcanonical ensemble）并刻画本征向量重叠的涨落标度。

Result: 严格证明了ETH在该类随机矩阵中成立。在常规谱边缘（regular spectral edges），涨落尺度保持为N^{-1}，与体区域一致且与Haar酉矩阵相同；仅在尖点区域（cusp regime）涨落尺度退化为N^{-1/2}。这一结果推翻了Feingold–Peres基于半经典理论的预测。

Conclusion: 除尖点区域外，平均场随机矩阵的整个本征基（eigenbasis）的涨落尺度与Haar酉矩阵一致，表明该行为具有一般性。该反常现象源于矩阵Dyson方程解的精细抵消，构成了分析的核心。

Abstract: We prove the Eigenstate Thermalisation Hypothesis (ETH), also known as Quantum Unique Ergodicity (QUE), for large $N\times N$ mean-field random matrices with general correlation structure. We identify the microcanonical ensemble and establish the optimal fluctuation scale of eigenvector overlaps around it. Our results invalidate the prediction by Feingold and Peres [Phys. Rev. A 34, 591 (1986)] in the physics literature of quantum chaos, based upon popular semiclassical theory, and uncover the genuine mechanism which relies on multi-resolvent local laws. Although fluctuations are expected to increase as the density of states vanishes, and indeed scale as $N^{-1/2}$ in the special cusp regime, rather than $N^{-1}$ in the bulk, we find, unexpectedly, that the same $N^{-1}$ rate persists at regular spectral edges. Hence, generically, in the absence of cusps, the entire eigenbasis fluctuates on the same scale as a Haar unitary. This anomaly stems from delicate cancellations in the solution of the underlying matrix Dyson equation, which form the core of our analysis.

### [187] [The Dirichlet Laplacian with a point interaction on unbounded Lipschitz domains](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04349)
*Diego Noja,Francesco Raso Stoia*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了二维和三维无界区域（特别是外部区域和特殊Lipschitz区域）上Dirichlet Laplacian的单中心点相互作用，通过自伴延拓和显式Krein公式构造奇异扰动算子，完整刻画了负谱、临界耦合的单调性和渐近行为，并分析了阈值现象的多种类型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 此前关于点相互作用的研究多集中在有界区域或全空间，对于无界区域（尤其是外部区域和特殊Lipschitz区域）上Dirichlet Laplacian的奇异扰动缺乏系统性理论。本文旨在填补这一空白，建立此类算子的谱结构、临界耦合特性及阈值现象的完整刻画。

Method: 将点相互作用算子构造为Dirichlet Laplacian在相互作用中心处消失函数的自伴延拓（self-adjoint extension），利用显式Krein公式（Krein formula）给出预解式，其中包含单个延拓参数α。通过Weyl函数（Weyl function）的阈值极限定义临界耦合，并利用零能量Green函数（zero-energy Green function）分析阈值行为。在均匀C^{1,1}几何下推导近边界渐近估计，并在外部区域和特殊Lipschitz区域中证明极限吸收原理（limiting absorption principles）。

Result: 建立了Weyl函数、临界耦合以及（存在时的）唯一负特征值的区域单调性（domain monotonicity）；在均匀C^{1,1}几何下得到了临界耦合的尖锐近边界渐近估计，表明当相互作用中心趋近Dirichlet边界时非正谱消失。证明了外部区域和特殊Lipschitz区域中点相互作用的极限吸收原理和纯绝对连续正谱。揭示了临界耦合由零能量Green函数的远场行为控制：外部区域产生阈值共振（threshold resonance），三维半空间内区域产生阈值本征值（threshold eigenvalue），半平面产生p波共振，平面楔形展现出依赖于开口角的阈值态类型。最后在模型情形下计算了低能量预解展开并研究了阈值处本征值的存续或消失。

Conclusion: 本文是首个对该主题进行系统性研究的工作，为无界区域上Dirichlet Laplacian点相互作用的谱理论提供了完整框架，特别在临界耦合的单调性和渐近性以及阈值现象分类方面取得了重要进展。

Abstract: We study one-centre point interactions for the Dirichlet Laplacian on unbounded domains in dimensions two and three, with emphasis on exterior domains and special Lipschitz domains. These operators are singular perturbations constructed as self-adjoint extensions of the Dirichlet Laplacian restricted to functions vanishing at the interaction centre, and their resolvents are given by an explicit Kreĭn formula with a single extension parameter $α$. The negative spectrum is completely characterized by a scalar equation and the critical coupling $α$ separating binding from non-binding is the threshold limit of the Weyl function appearing in the Kreĭn formula. We establish domain monotonicity of the Weyl function, of the critical coupling, and of the unique negative eigenvalue when existing, and we derive sharp near-boundary asymptotics of the critical coupling in uniformly $C^{1,1}$ geometries. These estimates imply that, for every fixed coupling, nonpositive spectrum disappears when the interaction centre approaches the Dirichlet boundary. We also prove limiting absorption principles and purely absolutely continuous positive spectrum for a point-interaction in exterior domains case and in classes of special Lipschitz domains. We also analyze in depth several threshold phenomena. We show that the critical coupling is governed by the far-field behavior of the zero-energy Green function: exterior domains give threshold resonances, domains contained in a three-dimensional half-space give threshold eigenvalues, the half-plane gives a $p$-wave resonance, and planar wedges exhibit types of threshold states that are aperture-dependent. Finally, low-energy resolvent expansions are computed in the model cases and persistence or disappearance of eigenvalues at threshold are studied. The present paper seems to be the first systematic work on the subject.

</details>


### [188] [Hyperbolic Completion of Newton's Off-Center Orbit Problem: $SO(2,1)$ Symmetry, Inversion Duality, and Magnetic Classification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04521)
*Dipesh Bhandari*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过Jacobi度规和保对称性的Runge-Lenz型矩映射，将带奇异势V(r)=−α/(R²−r²)²的零能双曲离中心轨道问题完全分类，揭示其经典与量子力学中的对称性结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决奇异势V(r)=−α/(R²−r²)², α>0下的双曲离中心轨道（hyperbolic off-center-orbit problem）问题，该势在r=R处存在奇异圆环，经典与量子层面均需统一分析。

Method: 引入Jacobi度规（Jacobi metric），发现其内部区域为Poincaré盘度量的常数倍，外部区域通过圆反演（circular inversion）等距映射到带孔盘。利用显式Runge-Lenz型矩映射（Runge–Lenz-type moment map）构建到so(2,1)李代数的闭包，利用Casimir算符作为双曲测地线Hamilton量。量子层面区分Stäckel耦合变换（Stäckel coupling transform）与真酉等价，并引入径向磁场以保持对称性。

Result: 零能轨迹完全分类：非径向轨道为与r=R正交的欧几里得圆弧，径向轨迹沿过原点的直线，力心位于所有非径向支撑圆之外。奇异圆可在有限牛顿时间内到达，但Jacobi距离无穷远。量子层面，双曲连续谱底部映射到反平方边界模型的Hardy/振荡阈值。引入径向磁场后，移位的Casimir将轨迹分为闭合磁圆、horocycles（极限圆）或开放hypercycles（双曲圆），零场测地线为极限情形，且在Q²=8mαR²处发生相变。数值积分验证了轨道方程与守恒量。

Conclusion: 该奇异势问题在经典与量子层面均具有丰富的对称性结构，反演变换与径向磁场为理解双曲几何中的轨道分类提供了关键工具。

Abstract: We resolve the hyperbolic off-center-orbit problem for the singular potential \[ V(r)=-\fracα{(R^2-r^2)^2},\qquad α>0. \] At zero energy, the Jacobi metric has constant negative curvature on both components separated by $r=R$. The interior Jacobi metric is a constant multiple of the Poincaré disk metric, while circular inversion maps the exterior isometrically to the punctured disk. We classify all zero-energy trajectories: nonradial orbits are arcs of Euclidean circles orthogonal to $r=R$, radial trajectories lie on lines through the origin, and the force center lies outside every nonradial supporting circle. An explicit Runge--Lenz-type moment map closes into $\mathfrak{so}(2,1)$, whose Casimir is the hyperbolic geodesic Hamiltonian. The canonical cotangent lift of inversion preserves the symmetry generators and maps the zero-energy flow to itself up to positive time reparametrization.
  The singular circle is reached in finite Newtonian time but lies at infinite Jacobi distance. Quantum mechanically, we distinguish the Stäckel coupling transform from a genuine unitary equivalence, whose Euclidean representative is a divergence-form operator rather than the naive flat Schrödinger operator. The bottom of the hyperbolic continuum maps to the Hardy/oscillation threshold of the inverse-square boundary model. Finally, the symmetry-preserving radial magnetic field becomes a constant intrinsic field on the hyperbolic plane. Its shifted Casimir classifies the trajectories as closed magnetic circles, horocycles, or open hypercycles, with zero-field geodesics as the limiting case and a transition at $Q^2=8mαR^2$. Numerical integrations confirm the orbit equations and conserved quantities.

### [189] [Long-range interactions and Anderson localisation for one-dimensional high-contrast resonator chain](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04971)
*Habib Ammari,Silvo Barandun,Jiayu Qiu,Alexander Uhlmann*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 针对三维无限周期高对比度谐振子链，推导电容算子 C 的非对角元在 |n-m|→∞ 时的渐近衰减率，并利用该估计证明有限截断链对应电容算子的强收敛性，进而给出谱的收敛速率。

Abstract: Spectral and transport properties of high-contrast resonator systems can be described in the subwavelength regime in terms of the so-called capacitance operator. In this paper, we consider an infinitely periodic chain of high-contrast resonators in three dimensions. The first result is a precise estimate of the off-diagonal decay rate of the capacitance operator $C$. Importantly, we demonstrate that the decay rate is long-range and critical: as $|n-m|\to\infty$, \begin{equation*} C(n,m)\sim \frac{1}{|n-m|\log^2|n-m|}, \end{equation*} which is $\ell^1$ summable but slower than quadratic. This borderline decay of the off-diagonal entries makes the present proof of Anderson localisation with arbitrary disorder, which is observed numerically in this paper, out of reach; we hope that this physical example of classical wave systems with critical long-range interactions provides new insight in the field of Anderson localisation. As the second main result, based on the off-diagonal decay estimate, we prove a strong convergence of the finite capacitance operator, which corresponds to a truncated chain, to the capacitance operator as the size of the truncated chain grows to infinity. Using this strong convergence, we improve the results of [Ammari et al., SIAM J. Math. Anal., 2023 and Bull. London Math Soc., 2025] by presenting a rigorous estimate of the convergence rate of the spectrum.

### [190] [Collision geometry of relativistic spinning particles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05254)
*Simone Calogero*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该论文在狭义相对论框架下研究了相对论性自旋粒子（relativistic spinning particles）的二元弹性碰撞，通过引入反对称二阶张量（antisymmetric second order tensor）描述自旋，在完全洛伦兹协变的设定下将碰撞问题简化为圆上的二次方程求解，并给出了碰撞后状态的完整分类与显式重构公式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在相对论性体系中，粒子自旋对碰撞过程的影响尚未被充分几何化与代数化地理解。本文旨在建立一种完全洛伦兹协变（Lorentz covariant）的碰撞问题表述，并揭示其内在的几何结构。

Method: 本文以反对称二阶张量表示每个粒子的自旋，结合总四动量（total four momentum）守恒与总自旋张量（total spin tensor）守恒，并考虑质壳条件（mass shell）与自旋约束（spin constraints），在洛伦兹协变框架下建立碰撞方程组。通过将该系统几何化，将其简化为圆上的一个二次方程求解问题。

Result: 该几何化约化方法给出了碰撞后状态（postcollisional states）的完整分类，并得到了所有碰撞后变量关于守恒量的显式重构公式。一般情况下，碰撞后状态的数量是有限的，最大数量为八个。

Conclusion: 相对论性自旋粒子的弹性碰撞问题具有简洁的几何结构，可被完整解析地求解。该工作为相对论性自旋系统的碰撞动力学提供了清晰的分类与重构方案。

Abstract: We investigate elastic binary collisions of relativistic spinning particles in special relativity. The spin of each particle is represented by an antisymmetric second order tensor. Assuming the conservation of total four momentum and total spin tensor, together with the mass shell and spin constraints, we formulate the collision problem in a fully Lorentz covariant setting. We show that the relativistic collision problem admits a simple geometric formulation, reducing the original system of conservation laws to the solution of a quadratic equation on a circle. This reduction yields a complete classification of the postcollisional states together with explicit reconstruction formulas for all postcollisional variables from the conserved quantities. In particular, there are generically only finitely many postcollisional states, with the maximal number equal to eight.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索极化子模型中能量-动量关系、有效质量以及基态存在性之间的内在联系，为理解强耦合极化子系统的低能行为提供严格的数学基础。

Method: 利用总动量为零的哈密顿量（Hamiltonian）的真空重叠（vacuum overlap）和谱隙（spectral gap）来界定能量-动量关系（energy-momentum relation）的下界；通过对路径测度进行重缩放（rescaling），建立均方位移（mean square displacement）与有效质量倒数的收敛性；引入随机判据（probabilistic criterion）来判定大总动量下基态（ground state）的不存在性。

Result: 建立了能量-动量关系下界与真空重叠及谱隙的关系；证明了重缩放后路径测度的均方位移收敛于有效质量的倒数；得到了大总动量下基态不存在的概率性条件。

Conclusion: 该工作为极化子类模型提供了能量-动量关系、有效质量与基态存在性之间的严格数学关联，丰富了极化子理论的数学物理（mathematical physics）方法。

Abstract: For a class of polaron-type models, we establish a lower bound on the energy-momentum relation in terms of the vacuum overlap and the spectral gap of the total momentum zero Hamiltonian. We show convergence of the rescaled mean square displacement of the associated path measure to the inverse of the effective mass. We derive a probabilistic criterion for the absence of ground states at large total momentum.

</details>

### [192] [A population of LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA mergers happening inside active galactic nuclei](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03674)
*Dhruv Kumar,Alejandro Torres-Orjuela*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 通过分析LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA（LVK）O3–O4b运行阶段的18个引力波事件与28个活动星系核（active galactic nuclei, AGN）候选对应体，结合超大质量黑洞（supermassive black hole, SMBH）引起的环境红移修正与电磁巡天定位约束，发现21个正强成对关联，其中13个独特关联的累积贝叶斯因子$\ln\mathcal{B}_{\rm comb} \approx +81$，有力支持了AGN宿主并合假说。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 选取LVK O3–O4b运行期间的18个引力波事件，匹配28个候选AGN对应体，引入超大质量黑洞（SMBH）诱导的环境红移修正与电磁巡天定位约束，采用贝叶斯因子（Bayes factor）衡量成对关联强度。

Result: 28个候选对中21个呈现正强支持（最显著为GW190412_053044 ↔ J143041.67+355703.8，$\ln\mathcal{B} = +17.35$），3个不确定，4个负强不支持；从中识别出13个独特关联，累积贝叶斯因子$\ln\mathcal{B}_{\rm comb} \approx +81$，表明AGN宿主并合关联具有强集体证据。

Abstract: Multimessenger observations of compact binary mergers in active galactic nuclei (AGN) offer unique probes of black hole formation channels and cosmology. We analyse 18 gravitational-wave events from LVK observing runs O3--O4b paired with 28 candidate AGN counterparts, incorporating supermassive black hole (SMBH)-induced environmental redshift corrections and electromagnetic sky-localisation constraints. Of the 28 candidate pairs, 21 are positive-to-strong-favoured (the most compelling being GW190412\_053044 $\leftrightarrow$ J143041.67$+$355703.8 at $\ln\mathcal{B} = +17.35$), three are inconclusive, and four are negative-to-strong-disfavoured. From the 21 positive-to-strong-favoured binary black hole (BBH) AGN pairs, 13 unique associations can be identified as the preferred ones. The cumulative Bayes factor across all 13 BBH-AGN confirmed associations yields $\ln\mathcal{B}_{\rm comb} \approx +81$, establishing strong collective support for AGN-hosted merger associations. Sky localisation is the dominant driver of model selection; at current detector sensitivity, the environmental redshift corrections are neither decisively confirmed nor ruled out, motivating future high-precision multimessenger follow-up.

Abstract: We propose a new formulation of the multi-component short pulse (MCSP) equation that includes the coupled complex short pulse (CCSP) equation as a reduction. Using Hirota's bilinear method, we construct its $N$-soliton solutions in Pfaffian form. We then derive integrable semi-discrete and fully discrete analogues of the MCSP equation admitting Pfaffian $N$-soliton solutions. The resulting fully discrete system provides a practical self-adaptive moving mesh scheme for numerical simulations. For the parameter sets considered, numerical simulations demonstrate excellent agreement between the numerical and exact solutions, confirming the robustness and high accuracy of the proposed scheme.

### [195] [Improving Jet A-1 Thermal-Oxidative Stability through Selective Removal of Unwanted Trace Species via 3.7 Å Chabazite Filtration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03375)

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过密度泛函理论（DFT）和从头算分子动力学（AIMD）建立了一个吸附-传输-电子筛选统一框架，用于优化菱沸石（3.7 Å chabazite）的组成，在去除Jet A-1燃料沉积促进剂的同时保留抗氧化剂功能，发现双金属取代比单纯调节酸性更能实现选择性吸附。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）和从头算分子动力学（ab initio molecular dynamics, AIMD）进行评估，使用两种组成描述符：骨架酸性（Si/Al = 35–8）和固定Al含量下的双金属取代（Co、Mg、Zn）。

Result: 降低Si/Al比会增强包括BHT在内的所有物种的吸附，证实了仅调节酸性存在内在选择性代价；双金属取代可引入化学选择性行为，增强特定促进剂的吸附，同时根据掺杂剂种类抑制或增强抗氧化剂吸附。AIMD模拟（400 K）显示仅用吸附能不足以描述趋势，因为分子在菱沸石内部的迁移性会影响停留时间和有效捕获。态密度和波函数分析揭示了掺杂剂依赖的吸附偏移特征。

Conclusion: 建立了一个统一的吸附-传输-电子筛选框架，可用于选择既能去除沉积促进剂又能保留Jet A-1中抗氧化剂功能的菱沸石组成。

Abstract: The thermal stability of Jet A-1 fuel is strongly affected by trace heteroatomic species that promote thermal oxidative deposit formation, as well as antioxidant additives such as butylated hydroxytoluene, which preserve fuel stability. 3.7 Å chabazite is a tunable microporous adsorbent, but optimizing its composition requires balancing promoter removal against antioxidant loss. Here, we use density functional theory and \textit{ab initio} molecular dynamics (AIMD) to evaluate this trade-off using two compositional descriptors: framework acidity (Si/Al $= 35$--$8$) and bimetallic substitution (Co, Mg, Zn) at fixed Al content. Lowering Si/Al strengthens adsorption of all species, including BHT, confirming an intrinsic selectivity penalty for acidity-only tuning. In contrast, bimetallic substitution introduces chemically selective behavior, strengthening uptake of specific promoters while either suppressing or enhancing antioxidant adsorption depending on dopant identity. AIMD simulations at 400 K further show that adsorption energy alone is insufficient to describe calculated trends, because molecular mobility inside chabazite can influence residence time and effective capture during fuel treatment. Analysis of the density of states and the participating wavefunctions reveals signatures that are consistent with dopant-dependent adsorption shifts. These results establish a unified adsorption--transport--electronic screening framework for selecting chabazite compositions that remove deposit promoters while preserving antioxidant functionality in Jet A-1 treatment.

Conclusion: 生命过程的时间尺度受量子力学约束与人择限制的共同调节；简单的估算方法不足以准确描述这些速度极限，需要更严谨的理论框架。

### [198] [Reconfigurable Bitter-Type Electromagnet for Zeeman Slowing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02813)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 许多塞曼减速器（Zeeman slower）的磁体受真空腔体几何结构限制，一旦安装便无法在不破坏真空的条件下进行修改或维修，这给实验装置的维护和调整带来了极大不便。

Method: 采用Bitter型电磁铁线圈（Bitter-type electromagnet coil）设计，该线圈可拆卸、重构、修复和更换，而不影响真空系统（vacuum system）。线圈专为减速锂原子（lithium atoms）设计，使用单一直流电源（single DC power supply）。

Result: 该线圈电阻为5.7(9) mΩ，电感为8.8(2) μH，开关时间低至约100 μs，性能优于其他设计。采用强制风冷（forced-air cooling）时仅出现中等程度发热。线圈可反复拆卸、修改和重新组装而不损失性能。

Conclusion: 该线圈设计比传统电磁铁设计具有更高的灵活性，且可改装到现有的超高真空（UHV）腔体上。

Abstract: Many Zeeman slower magnets are geometrically captured by a vacuum chamber, preventing modification or repair without breaking vacuum. We describe a Bitter-type electromagnet coil design that can be easily disassembled, reconfigured, repaired, and replaced without disturbing the vacuum system. This coil, designed to slow lithium atoms, produces a near-ideal field profile with a single DC power supply. With a resistance of 5.7(9) m$Ω$, an inductance of 8.8(2) $μ$H, and switching times as low as $\sim100$ $μ$s, the coil compares favorably to other designs, and can be disassembled, modified, and reassembled repeatedly without loss of performance. With forced-air cooling, the coil experiences moderate heating. This coil design offers greater flexibility than traditional electromagnet designs, and it can retrofitted onto existing UHV chambers.

### [199] [From graphons to real-world networks: kinetic opinion dynamics under selective media influence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02821)
*Bertram Düring,Martina Fraia,Alessandro Licciardi*

Main category: physics.soc-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种在基于图论（graphon）和真实世界网络上的选择性媒体影响下的意见动力学（opinion dynamics）动力学模型。通过模型预测控制（model predictive control）策略引入媒体作用，推导了Boltzmann型描述、Fokker-Planck型方程及其稳态特征，并证明了Fourier度量下的指数收敛性。数值实验在Gaussian graphon生成网络和真实Twitter网络上验证了控制参数与媒体报道子集的影响，并通过对比图论方法与真实网络评价了图论方法的描述能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有意见动力学模型较少考虑媒体在选择性网络结构下的有控影响，且缺乏对图论（graphon）方法在真实社会网络中描述能力的定量评估。

Method: 基于Hallin的“领域理论（spheres theory）”设计模型预测控制（model predictive control）策略以引导意见；采用Boltzmann型描述分析矩演化，在拟不变相互作用极限（quasi-invariant interaction limit）下推导Fokker-Planck型方程并刻画稳态；在Gaussian graphon生成网络和真实Twitter单议题网络上进行数值实验。

Result: 推导了Fokker-Planck型方程的稳态特征；证明了Fourier度量下的指数收敛性；数值实验揭示了控制参数、交互参数以及受媒体影响的代理人子集对意见演化的作用；真实网络与拟合的Gaussian graphon网络之间的动力学对比评估了图论方法的描述能力。

Conclusion: 所提出的模型能够在图论和真实网络框架下有效捕捉选择性媒体影响下的意见动力学行为；图论方法在拟合真实网络结构后具有一定的描述能力，可作为简化真实复杂网络的可行工具。

Abstract: We propose a kinetic model of opinion dynamics under selective media influence on both graphon-based and real-world networks. The media action, inspired by Hallin's theory of spheres, is incorporated through a model predictive control strategy designed to steer agents' opinions toward a desired target opinion. For the resulting Boltzmann-type description, we analyse the evolution of the moments and, in the quasi-invariant interaction limit, derive a Fokker--Planck-type equation together with a characterisation of its stationary states. We also prove exponential convergence to equilibrium in the Fourier metric. Numerical experiments are performed on networks generated by a Gaussian graphon and on real-world, single-issue Twitter networks, allowing us to investigate the role of control and interaction parameters, as well as the impact of the subset of agents subject to media influence. Using real-world social networks data to initialise opinions and infer the interaction structure, we then compare the dynamics obtained on the original networks with those produced by Gaussian graphons fitted to their adjacency matrices, thereby assessing the descriptive power of the graphon approach for real-world opinion dynamics.

</details>


### [200] [Community structure of the pseudofractal web](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03010)
*Alexei Vazquez*

Main category: physics.soc-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过解析方法计算了确定性伪分形无标度网络（pseudofractal scale-free web）上的拉姆齐社群数（Ramsey community number, $r_κ$），表明在考虑度校正（degree correction）后，该网络的最佳描述并非两个社群，而是一个嵌套的层级社群结构（nested hierarchy of communities），其社群数量约为 $\sqrt{n}$ 个，每个社群大小约为 $\sqrt{n}$ 个节点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在无标度网络（scale-free graph）中进行社群检测时，块模型（block model）可能仅通过划分网络来吸收度分布（degree distribution），从而混淆真正的社群结构。作者旨在区分真实的社群结构与度异质性（degree heterogeneity）带来的虚假划分，并找到一个可解析求解的模型来阐明这一混淆问题。

Method: 作者以Dorogovtsev、Goltsev和Mendes提出的确定性伪分形无标度网络为研究对象，采用两种闭合形式的检测规则（closed-form detection rules）：一是朴素伯努利随机块模型（plain Bernoulli stochastic block model），二是度校正模型（degree-corrected model），并与配置模型零假设（configuration-model null）进行对比检验。通过解析计算拉姆齐社群数 $r_κ$ 及对数证据（log-evidence）的渐近增长，分析了不同划分方案的优劣。

Result: 在朴素伯努利块模型下，网络的自然递归二分（recursive bipartition）在较小规模时不被偏好，在 $r_κ=1095$ 个节点时被打破，对数证据增长率为 $(\ln 3 - \frac{2}{3}\ln 2)n$。在度校正模型下，相同划分在 $r_κ=42$ 时即被打破，对数证据增长率为 $(2\ln 3 - \frac{4}{3}\ln 2)n$，恰好为朴素模型斜率的两倍，且与先验（prior）无关。度校正反转了候选划分的排序，将中心-叶划分（hub-leaf split）降级，而提升了递归划分的地位。

Conclusion: 由于该网络具有自相似性（self-similar），最佳描述并非两个社群，而是一个嵌套层级结构：度校正证据在划分不断细化时持续上升，并在约 $\sqrt{n}$ 个社群（每个约 $\sqrt{n}$ 个节点）时达到最大。这表明一个纯粹的局部递归规则（local recursive rule）能够在产生无标度度序列的同时，构建出真实的层级社群结构。

Abstract: The Ramsey community number $r_κ$ is the smallest network size at which a graph is better described by a partition into communities than by no partition, under a prescribed detection rule. On a scale-free graph this question is confounded: a block model can split the network merely to absorb its degree distribution. I compute $r_κ$ analytically for the deterministic pseudofractal scale-free web of Dorogovtsev, Goltsev, and Mendes, separating genuine community structure from degree heterogeneity with two closed-form detection rules. Under a plain Bernoulli stochastic block model, the web's natural recursive bipartition is unpreferred while small and breaks at $r_κ=1095$ nodes, with a log-evidence growing as $(\ln 3-\tfrac{2}{3}\ln 2)n$. Under a degree-corrected model tested against the configuration-model null, the same partition survives, breaking far earlier at $r_κ=42$, with a log-evidence growing as $(2\ln 3-\tfrac{4}{3}\ln 2)n$ -- exactly twice the plain slope, and independent of the prior. Degree correction reverses the ordering of the candidate cuts, demoting the hub-leaf split and elevating the recursive one. Because the web is self-similar, the best description is not two communities but a nested hierarchy: the degree-corrected evidence keeps rising as the partition is refined, and is maximised at of order $\sqrt{n}$ communities of $\sim\sqrt{n}$ nodes. A purely local recursive rule thus builds true hierarchical community structure, over and above the scale-free degree sequence it also produces, in an exactly solvable setting.

</details>

### [201] [Transverse-spin dependent energy-energy correlators in proton-proton collisions within the dihadron fragmentation framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02441)
*Zhong-Bo Kang,Andreas Metz,Daniel Pitonyak,Congyue Zhang*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该论文计算了横极化质子-质子碰撞中喷注内两个强子的能量-能量关联，基于双强子碎裂和横度（transversity）部分子分布函数的全局QCD分析模型进行数值预言，结果与STAR实验测量高度吻合，并发现大横动量喷注数据倾向于支持与格点QCD核子张量荷计算一致的横度提取。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究横极化质子-质子碰撞中喷注内能量-能量关联，以检验非微扰机制并探索探测核子内横向自旋效应的可能性。

Method: 采用基于前期双强子碎裂和横度部分子分布函数（transversity parton distribution functions）全局QCD分析的简单模型，对横极化质子-质子碰撞中喷注内两强子能量-能量关联进行数值计算。

Result: 数值预言与STAR实验最新测量结果高度一致；大横动量喷注数据略微偏好与格点QCD（lattice QCD）核子张量荷（nucleon tensor charges）计算相一致的横度提取结果。

Conclusion: 该工作为近端能量-能量关联子（near-side energy-energy correlators）的非微扰机制提供了进一步证据，并突显了这些观测量在探测核子内横向自旋效应方面的潜力。

Abstract: We calculate energy-energy correlations for two hadrons produced inside a jet in transversely polarized proton-proton collisions. We make numerical predictions based on a simple model that utilizes a previous global QCD analysis of dihadron fragmentation and transversity parton distribution functions. The results show remarkable agreement with a very recent STAR measurement. We also find the data at large jet transverse momentum have a slight preference for extractions of transversity that are consistent with lattice QCD computations of the nucleon tensor charges. Overall, this work provides further evidence for the underlying non-perturbative mechanism of near-side energy-energy correlators as well as highlights the potential for these observables to probe transverse-spin effects inside the nucleon.

### [202] [Interpreting Parton Distributions with Shapley Values](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02647)
*Raphaël Bonnet-Guerrini,Stefano Carrazza,Stefano Forte,Eva Groenendijk,Vincenzo Piuri,Ramon Winterhalder*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文展示了沙普利值（Shapley value）可用于追溯单个部分子分布（PDF）如何塑造高能观测量理论预测，提供了一种评估数据对PDF影响以及PDF不确定性对观测量影响的分析工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有PDF确定方法（包括黑箱AI模型和固定参数化方法）缺乏对单个PDF如何影响理论预测以及数据如何约束PDF的定量可解释性，需要一种模型无关的方法来量化这种贡献。

Method: 将PDF从数据中的回归过程视为一个合作博弈（cooperative game），其中PDF为玩家，奖励为描述数据与预测之间一致性的似然（χ²），通过计算沙普利值来量化每个PDF对预测的边际贡献。

Result: 该方法能够定量地恢复全局拟合中关于哪些数据约束哪些PDF的已知预期；发现了胶子PDF在中等x区域存在意外的敏感性损失，这对BSM搜索和胶子聚变希格斯截面有潜在影响；同时展示了该方法可用于改进NNPDF合作组当前使用的超参数优化流程。

Conclusion: 沙普利值分析为PDF影响的量化和模型可解释性提供了一种通用、定量且模型无关的有效工具。

Abstract: We show that Shapley values can be used to trace how individual parton distributions (PDFs) shape the theory predictions for high-energy observables computed from them. This provides a tool for assessing the impact of data on PDFs when determining them, and the impact of PDF uncertainties when using the PDFs to compute collider observables.The Shapley value is computed by treating the regression of PDFs from data as a cooperative game. The PDFs are the players, and the reward is the likelihood ($χ^2$) that characterizes the agreement between data and the predictions obtained from a given PDF, with theory and methodology held fixed. The method is agnostic to the way PDFs have been determined in the first place: for PDFs determined with a black-box AI model it may be used in order to explain the behavior of the model, and for PDFs determined using a fixed parametrization it may be used in order to expose the features and potential limitations of the parametrization. We find that the method recovers known expectations about which data constrain which PDFs in a global fit, while placing them on a more quantitative footing. We demonstrate its effectiveness in two ways. We uncover an unexpected loss of sensitivity of the gluon PDF at intermediate $x$, with potential implications for BSM searches and the gluon fusion Higgs cross section. We also show that the method can be used to improve the hyperparameter optimization procedure currently used by the NNPDF collaboration.

</details>


### [203] [EFT Validity and Truncation Uncertainty from few Nuisance Parameters](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02649)
*Benoît Assi,Adam Martin,William Shepherd*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种在有效场论（EFT）中利用可计算的次领头阶项（dim-6²）来高效建模截断不确定性的方法。通过少量 nuisance parameter 估计全阶不确定性，并自动生成扫描算法，从而在 SMEFT 截断至 $\mathcal{O}(\Lambda^{-2})$ 的高能对撞机过程中显著降低 nuisance parameter 数量（通常比朴素估算降低一个量级）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 有效场论（Effective Field Theory, EFT）中的可观测量是对一组小参数的展开，截断后主导误差来自首项被丢弃的贡献。该被丢弃项本身包含可计算部分，但现有方法未能有效利用该部分来建模完整的 next-order 不确定性，导致 nuisance parameter 数量过多或 EFT 有效性判断缺失。

Method: 将可计算的 dim-6² 部分纳入信号，并用一组由 Wilson 系数（Wilson coefficient）扫描得到的少量 nuisance parameter 覆盖剩余的高维不确定性。通过算法自动确定相关 nuisance parameter 及其分布，适用于任意截断选择。方法在 SMEFT 截断至 $\mathcal{O}(\Lambda^{-2})$ 的高能对撞机过程中实现，其中 dim-6² 用于估计完整的 $\mathcal O(\Lambda^{-4})$ 依赖。

Result: 在多个高能对撞机过程实例中，该方法显著减少了 nuisance parameter 数量，通常比朴素估算降低一个量级。同时，该不确定性估计自然施加了 EFT 有效性约束，确保边界仅由截断不确定性远小于信号的运动学区域驱动。

Conclusion: 提出了一种自动化友好的算法，利用可计算的次领头阶部分高效建模 EFT 截断不确定性，只需少量 nuisance parameter 即可覆盖完整高阶不确定性，并在 SMEFT 示例中验证了 nuisance parameter 数量的大幅减少。

Abstract: An observable in an Effective Field Theory (EFT) is an expansion in a set of small parameters, no different than any other perturbation series. Truncating such a series expansion leaves the leading dropped term as the dominant source of error, and that term itself contains a calculable portion. We explore the partial calculation of this next-order error, available at dim-6$^2$ in SMEFT with no additional tools needed to simulate it, and explore how to efficiently use that partial calculation to model the next-order uncertainty in full using a minimal number of nuisance parameters. This estimate of the uncertainty of the EFT signal rate naturally imposes EFT validity by ensuring that bounds are driven by kinematic regions where truncation uncertainties are parametrically smaller than the signal. We incorporate the calculable dim-6$^2$ piece into the signal and cover the remaining higher-dimension uncertainty with a small set of nuisance parameters derived from a scan over Wilson-coefficient values. Our algorithm to determine the relevant nuisance parameters and distributions is automation-friendly and applies to arbitrary truncation choices. We then provide multiple examples of its implementation in high-energy collider processes focused on SMEFT truncated at $\mathcal{O}(Λ^{-2})$, where the dim-6$^2$ piece is used to estimate the full $\mathcal O(Λ^{-4})$ dependence. In the examples considered here the reduction of nuisance parameters is appreciable, generically reducing the nuisance parameter count by an order of magnitude compared to naïve estimates.

</details>


### [204] [Dark Matter in the General 2HDM with Extra Top Yukawa Couplings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02659)
*Leon M. G. de la Vega,Mohamed Krab*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文在广义双希格斯二重态模型（G2HDM）基础上引入一个实标量单态（G2HDM+S），提供一个可行的标量暗物质候选者，并分析了来自LHC希格斯信号强度测量、额外希格斯玻色子直接搜索以及宇宙学观测（暗物质遗迹密度、直接和间接探测）的约束，提出六个基准场景，其中味破缺的顶-粲耦合可产生独特的味破缺暗物质产生过程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在广义双希格斯二重态模型（general two Higgs doublet model, G2HDM）的基础上扩展一个实标量单态（real scalar singlet），以提供一个可行的标量暗物质候选者，并实现顶窗口暗物质（top-window dark matter）场景的紫外完备化（UV completion），其中暗物质主要通过顶夸克与标准模型（Standard Model）相互作用。

Method: 通过对可见希格斯扇区施加来自LHC的希格斯信号强度测量和额外希格斯玻色子直接搜索的约束，以及对暗扇区施加宇宙学观测（包括暗物质遗迹密度、自旋无关直接探测和间接探测）的约束，扫描并分析幸存参数空间。在该空间内识别由单态门户、扩展汤川扇区和重希格斯标量质量层级共同主导的LHC唯象学，并提出涵盖单态门户、玻色子级联、亲费米子和味破缺四个机制的六个基准场景。

Result: 幸存参数空间呈现出丰富的LHC对撞机唯象学。在味破缺基准场景中，非对角顶-粲耦合（top-charm coupling）$ρ_{tc}$诱导产生过程$cg \to tH$，使得顶夸克可作为不可见信号$H\to SS$（即暗物质粒子对）的触发子，这种味破缺的暗物质产生是G2HDM+S模型的独特特征。

Conclusion: G2HDM+S模型可为顶窗口暗物质提供紫外完备的标量暗物质候选者；味破缺的顶-粲耦合所导致的暗物质产生过程是该模型的显著特征，可帮助实验鉴别。

Abstract: We extend the general two Higgs doublet model (G2HDM), which introduces extra Yukawa couplings, by an additional real scalar singlet (G2HDM+S), providing a viable scalar dark matter (DM) candidate. This setup provide a viable UV completion of top-window dark matter scenarios, in which DM communicates with the standard model predominantly through the top quark. We analyze the constraints on the visible scalar sector from Higgs signal strength measurements and direct searches for additional Higgs bosons at the LHC, and those on the dark sector from cosmological observables, including the observed DM relic density and spin-independent direct-detection as well as indirect detection. Within the surviving parameter space, we identify a rich and diverse LHC phenomenology governed by the interplay between the singlet portal, the extended Yukawa sector, and the heavy scalar mass hierarchy. To facilitate experimental investigation, we propose six benchmark scenarios spanning the singlet-portal, bosonic-cascade, fermiophilic, and flavor-violating regimes. In the latter, the nondiagonal top-charm coupling $ρ_{tc}$ induces the production channel $cg \to tH$, allowing the top quark to serve as a trigger for an otherwise invisible $H\to SS$ signal. This flavor-violating DM production is a distinct feature of the G2HDM+S.

### [205] [Studying baryon number transport dynamics via hyperon-kaon correlations in $p + \mathrm{Au}$ collisions at $\sqrt{s_{_{\rm NN}}}=20$, $39$ and $62$ GeV](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02867)
*Siyuan Ping,Xiaozhou Yu,Long Ma*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本论文利用多相输运（AMPT）和超相对论量子分子动力学（UrQMD）模型模拟质子-金（p+Au）碰撞，研究超子-kaon关联作为相对快度（rapidity）的函数，并通过Wasserstein距离方法量化关联函数，为未来实验测量排除重子结（baryon junction）机制提供了基准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 重离子碰撞中观测到的正净超子重子数（positive net hyperon baryon numbers）表明，入射核子中的重子数可通过大快度间隙（rapidity gap）输运至超子，同时伴随奇异夸克对（strange quark pair）的产生。这种超子-kaon关联可敏感地探测重子数输运机制与奇异夸克对关联，并可用于检验胶子结（gluon-junction）相互作用机制。

Method: 使用多相输运（AMPT）模型和超相对论量子分子动力学（UrQMD）模型模拟质子-金（p+Au）碰撞，质心系能量（√s_NN）分别为20、39和62 GeV。超子-kaon对来源于碎裂机制（fragmentation scheme），并通过Wasserstein距离方法量化关联函数，系统研究关联对束流能量、超子发射方向及探测器接受度的依赖性。

Result: 模拟结果提供了在不存在重子结（baryon junction）机制情况下的基线（baseline）数据，量化了超子-kaon关联随相对快度的变化及其对束流能量、超子发射方向和探测器接受度的依赖。

Conclusion: 所获得的模拟基线将为未来实验测量提供参考，用于区分或验证重子结（baryon junction）机制在重子数输运中的作用。

Abstract: The observation of positive net hyperon baryon numbers at mid-rapidity in heavy-ion collisions indicates that baryon numbers from incident nucleons can be transported across a large rapidity gap to hyperons where strange quarks of $s-\bar{s}$ are pair-produced. Consequently, hyperons and kaons are expected to be correlated, providing a sensitive probe of both baryon number transport mechanism and strange quark pair correlation. Such correlation may be used to test the gluon-junction interaction mechanism where a $Y$-shaped gluonic field may carry the baryon number and be responsible for the baryon number transport to hyperons over a large rapidity gap. We present hyperon-kaon correlations as a function of their relative rapidity in $p + \mathrm{Au}$ collisions at $\sqrt{s_{NN}} = 20$, $39$, and $62$ GeV using a multiphase transport ($\texttt{AMPT}$) model and Ultra-relativistic Quantum Molecular Dynamics ($\texttt{UrQMD}$) models where hyperon-kaon pairs are originated from fragmentation scheme. We quantify the correlation function using the Wasserstein distance method and systematically investigate the correlation dependence on the beam energy, hyperon emission direction and detector acceptance. Our simulation results provide a baseline without the baryon junction mechanism for future experimental measurements.

</details>


### [206] [Revisiting $\bar B^0 \rightarrow Λ_c^+ \bar p$ decay with higher twist corrections](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02876)
*Zhou Rui,Zhi-Tian Zou,Ying Li*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文在微扰QCD（PQCD）框架下系统研究了单粲重子衰变 $\bar B^0 \to Λ_c^+ \bar p$ 和 $\bar B^0 \to \barΛ_c^- p$，发现高扭度（higher-twist）贡献不可忽略，$W$发射与$W$交换振幅之间的显著相消干涉有效降低了前者的分支比，使之与实验数据更好吻合；首次研究了双卡比博压低衰变 $\bar B^0 \to \barΛ_c^- p$，并首次给出了两个衰变道的衰变不对称参数理论预言。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 单粲重子B介子衰变同时涉及$W$发射（$W$-emission）和$W$交换（$W$-exchange）两种拓扑结构，其理论描述需要精确考虑高扭度修正，而现有研究对此尚不充分；同时，双卡比博压低道 $\bar B^0 \to \barΛ_c^- p$ 此前尚未被研究过。

Method: 采用微扰QCD（perturbative QCD, PQCD）框架，系统纳入与初态和末态强子的光锥分布振幅（light-cone distribution amplitudes, LCDAs）相关的高阶幂次修正（higher-power corrections）。

Result: 高扭度贡献在重子B衰变中起重要作用，不可忽略；$W$发射与$W$交换振幅之间存在显著相消干涉，大幅降低了 $\bar B^0 \to Λ_c^+ \bar p$ 的分支比，改善了与实验的吻合度；首次预言 $\bar B^0 \to \barΛ_c^- p$ 的分支比约为 $10^{-8}$ 量级；首次给出两个通道的衰变不对称参数理论预言。

Conclusion: 高扭度修正和振幅干涉效应是理解重子B衰变的关键；双卡比博压低道未来有望被高亮度实验检验；所预言的衰变不对称参数为检验衰变动力学提供了新观测量。

Abstract: We investigate the single-charmed baryonic decays $\bar B^0 \to Λ_c^+ \bar p$ and $\bar B^0 \to \barΛ_c^- p$, which receive contributions from both $W$-emission and $W$-exchange topologies, within the framework of perturbative QCD (PQCD). Higher-power corrections associated with the hadronic light-cone distribution amplitudes (LCDAs) of both the initial- and final-state hadrons are systematically taken into account. We find that these higher-twist contributions play an important role in baryonic $B$ decays and cannot be neglected. A sizable destructive interference between the $W$-emission and $W$-exchange amplitudes is observed, which significantly reduces the predicted branching fraction of $\bar B^0 \to Λ_c^+ \bar p$ and leads to improved agreement with experimental measurements. The doubly Cabibbo-suppressed decay $\bar B^0 \to \barΛ_c^- p$ is studied for the first time. Its branching fraction is predicted to be of order $10^{-8}$, placing it within the reach of future high-luminosity experiments. We further present the first theoretical predictions for the decay asymmetry parameters of both channels, which provide additional observables for testing the underlying decay dynamics and can be confronted with future experimental data.

</details>


### [207] [A Dispersive Look at Rare $B$-meson Semileptonic Decays](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03531)
*Marco Ciuchini,Marco Fedele,Ayan Paul,Josua Scholze,Luca Silvestrini,Silvano Simula,Mauro Valli,Ludovico Vittorio*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文利用色散矩阵方法（Dispersive Matrix method）对b→s ℓ⁺ℓ⁻稀有衰变中的强子不确定性进行全面分析，结果表明长距离强子效应比短距离新物理（C₉偏移）更受数据支持；同时给出了b→s νν̅过程的标准模型预言及新物理分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 稀有半轻子b→s味改变中性流（flavour-changing neutral current, FCNC）跃迁是检验标准模型（Standard Model）的严格探针，但其解释受限于强子不确定性，特别是B→K^(*)和B_s→φ形状因子（form factors, FFs）以及四夸克算符的矩阵元。

Method: 对b→s ℓ⁺ℓ⁻跃迁进行全局分析，通过色散矩阵方法（Dispersive Matrix method）确定形状因子（FFs）；比较了仅基于格点量子色动力学（lattice QCD, LQCD）输入与同时包含低q²光锥求和规则（light-cone sum-rule, LCSR）输入两种方案。

Result: 仅使用LQCD输入相比同时包含两种输入，在大反冲（large recoil）区域显著增大了FF不确定性。结合LHCb和CMS最新对角测量敏感于强相位的实验结果，全局拟合显示出对长距离强子效应（long-distance hadronic effects）的支持增强，而非C₉的短距离偏移（short-distance shift）。

Conclusion: 提出理论上干净的b→s νν̅过程的新标准模型预言（仅依赖局域FFs），并在弱有效理论（Weak Effective Theory）框架下对这些跃迁进行新物理分析，讨论了其对Belle~II最新测量结果及现有实验上限的影响。

Abstract: Rare semileptonic $b \to s$ flavour-changing neutral current transitions provide stringent tests of the Standard Model. Their interpretation is limited by hadronic uncertainties, notably the $B \to K^{(*)}$ and $B_s \to φ$ form factors (FFs) and the matrix elements of four-quark operators. We perform a global analysis of $b \to s \ell^+\ell^-$ transitions taking these uncertainties fully into account, determining the FFs through the Dispersive Matrix method and comparing a setup based solely on lattice QCD (LQCD) with one that also includes light-cone sum-rule (LCSR) inputs at low $q^2$. Compared to the case where both input are taken into account, using only LQCD substantially enlarges the FF uncertainties at large recoil. Combined with the latest LHCb and CMS angular measurements sensitive to strong phases, our global fit yields strengthened evidence in favour of long-distance hadronic effects rather than a short-distance shift in $C_9$. We further present new SM predictions for the theoretically clean $b \to s ν\barν$ modes, which depend only on local FFs, and a New Physics analysis of these transitions in the Weak Effective Theory, discussing their impact on the interpretation of the recent Belle~II measurement and on the available experimental upper bounds.

</details>

### [209] [Double strange hybrid baryon](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04237)
*B. Barsbay,K. Azizi,H. Sundu*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文利用QCD求和规则（QCD sum rule）对含有ssqg夸克成分的双奇异混杂重子（double strange hybrid baryon）的光谱性质进行了研究。通过包含高达十维真空凝聚（vacuum condensate）的算符乘积展开（OPE），从两种洛伦兹结构中提取了基态和第一激发态的质量与极点残值。基态质量为(1593.44±130.29) MeV，第一激发态质量为(1897.47±124.44) MeV，为未来实验搜寻和非微扰研究提供了理论预言。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 混杂重子（hybrid baryon）是包含显式胶子自由度的奇特强子态，其光谱性质对理解非微扰QCD（nonperturbative QCD）具有重要意义。双奇异混杂重子作为混杂重子家族中的重要成员，目前尚缺乏系统的理论研究，因此有必要利用QCD求和规则对其质量与极点残值（pole residue）进行定量预言。

Method: 在QCD求和规则框架下，采用包含显式胶子自由度的插值流（interpolating current）构建两点关联函数（two-point correlation function）。关联函数按两种独立的洛伦兹结构（\(\slashed{q}\) 和 \(I\)）进行分析；算符乘积展开包含高达十维的真空凝聚项，对两种结构分别导出求和规则，最终取两种结构结果的平均值以提取基态和第一激发态的物理参数。

Result: 基态双奇异混杂重子的质量为 \(\widetilde{M} = (1593.44 \pm 130.29)~\mathrm{MeV}\)，极点残值为 \(\widetilde{\lambda} = (2.57 \pm 0.40) \times 10^{-3} ~\mathrm{GeV}^5\)；第一激发态的质量为 \(M = (1897.47 \pm 124.44)~\mathrm{MeV}\)，极点残值为 \(\lambda = (2.88 \pm 0.62) \times 10^{-3} ~\mathrm{GeV}^5\)。

Conclusion: 本文提供了双奇异混杂重子光谱的理论预言，这些结果可用于指导未来实验搜寻，并为混杂强子（hybrid hadron）的进一步非微扰研究提供参考。

Abstract: We investigate the spectroscopic properties of the double strange hybrid baryon with quark content $ssqg$ within the framework of QCD sum rule. Using an interpolating current with explicit gluonic degrees of freedom, the two-point correlation function is analyzed in terms of two independent Lorentz structures, $\slashed{q}$ and $I$. The operator product expansion is carried out by including vacuum condensates up to dimension ten, and the corresponding sum rules are derived for both structures. By taking the average of the results obtained from the two Lorentz structures, we extract the masses and pole residues of the ground and first excited states. For the ground state, we obtain a mass of $\widetilde{M } = (1593.44\pm 130.29)~ \mathrm{MeV}$ and a residue of $\widetilde{λ} = (2.57\pm 0.40) \times10^{-3} ~\mathrm{GeV}^5$. For the first excited state, the corresponding values are $M = (1897.47\pm 124.44)~ \mathrm{MeV}$ and $λ= (2.88\pm 0.62) \times10^{-3} ~\mathrm{GeV}^5$. The obtained results provide theoretical predictions for the double strange hybrid baryon spectrum and may be useful for future experimental searches as well as further nonperturbative studies of hybrid hadrons.

### [210] [Updated analysis of minimal supersymmetric SO(10) with a universal soft spectrum](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04250)
*Cheng-Wei Chiang,Takeshi Fukuyama*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文更新了最小超对称SO(10)大统一理论（grand unified theory）的分析，在约束MSSM类（constrained-MSSM-like）软破缺谱下，通过对全局参数的扫描和约束-μ交叉检验，发现仅存一个狭窄的mini-split区域：标量粒子质量在数十TeV量级（m₀ ≥ 7.7 TeV，tanβ ≤ 9）。该存活区域将在十年内被Hyper-Kamiokande质子衰变实验和电弱微子（electroweakino）搜索直接检验。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 对最小超对称SO(10)大统一理论进行更新分析，在统一软破缺谱假设下考察参数空间的存活区域，并评估质子衰变、暗物质候选者等可观测后果的可检验性。

Method: 采用一对位于10 ⊕ 126-bar希格斯扇区（Higgs sector）的汤川矩阵（Yukawa matrices）来确定带电费米子质量、夸克混合、维数五质子衰变算符以及I型跷跷板（type-I seesaw）中的右手中微子马约拉纳质量（Majorana masses）。对软破缺参数进行全局扫描，辅以约束-μ（constrained-μ）交叉检验，通过辐射电弱对称性破缺（radiative electroweak symmetry breaking）从大统一标度（GUT-scale）边界条件确定电弱微子扇区（electroweakino sector）。施加的约束包括：规范耦合统一与真空稳定性、维数五质子衰变（同时计算了维数六规范模式且可忽略）、125-GeV希格斯质量、LEP电荷子（chargino）极限、μ→eγ、缪子g-2以及电偶极矩（electric dipole moments）。

Result: 存活区域为狭窄的mini-split区域：标量粒子质量在数十TeV量级，m₀ ≥ 7.7 TeV且tanβ ≤ 9。研究还考察了最轻超对称粒子（lightest supersymmetric particle, LSP）作为暗物质候选者（dark matter candidate）的命运，包括普适模型及其自由-μ非普适希格斯质量（free-μ non-universal-Higgs-mass）扩展两种情况。

Conclusion: 存活区域具有尖锐的边界，将在未来十年内被检验，最直接的检验途径包括Hyper-Kamiokande的质子衰变实验和电弱微子搜索，此外暗物质直接探测（dark matter direct detection）和电偶极矩实验也可提供补充检验。

Abstract: We update the analysis of minimal supersymmetric SO(10) grand unification with a universal, constrained-MSSM-like soft-breaking spectrum. A pair of Yukawa matrices in the ${\bf 10} \oplus \overline{\bf 126}$ Higgs sector fixes the charged fermion masses and quark mixing, the baryon number-violating dimension-five operators that mediate proton decay, and the right-handed neutrino Majorana masses of the type-I seesaw. The simultaneously imposed constraints include: (i) gauge coupling unification and vacuum stability; (ii) dimension-five proton decay (the dimension-six gauge mode also computed and negligible), the 125-GeV Higgs mass, and the LEP chargino limit; and (iii) $μ\to eγ$, the muon $g-2$, and electric dipole moments. We perform a global scan over the soft-breaking parameters, complemented by a constrained-$μ$ cross-check that fixes the electroweakino sector from the GUT-scale boundary conditions through radiative electroweak symmetry breaking. Subject to a single effective colored-Higgs scale $M_{H_C}$ for the proton decay normalization and to a constrained-$μ$ treatment, what survives is a narrow mini-split region: heavy, multi-tens-of-TeV scalars with $m_0 \gtrsim 7.7$~TeV and $\tanβ\lesssim 9$. We also examine the fate of the lightest supersymmetric particle as a dark matter candidate, in both the universal model and its free-$μ$ non-universal-Higgs-mass extension. The surviving region is sharply bounded and testable in the coming decade, most directly by Hyper-Kamiokande proton decay and electroweakino searches, with dark matter direct detection and electric dipole moment experiments.

### [211] [Anomalous triple gauge couplings in the light of dimension-8 operators in $W^+W^-$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04251)
*Daniel Gillies,Andrea Banfi,Adam Martin*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文对比了在大型强子对撞机（LHC）上，由夸克-反夸克（$q\bar q$）初始态和双光子（$γγ$）初始态产生的 $W^+W^-$ 过程中维度-8算符（dimension-8 operators）效应的大小。研究发现，$γγ$ 通道存在占主导的玻色子维度-8贡献，可用于理解有效场论（Effective Field Theory, EFT）的有效范围，并基于当前和未来数据给出了对高维算符的限制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于评估和比较来自不同初始态（$q\bar q$ 和 $γγ$）的维度-8算符对 $W^+W^-$ 产生的贡献，以确定利用有效场论（EFT）框架检验超出标准模型（BSM）物理时，哪个通道更能揭示EFT的适用范围和有效性边界。

Method: 方法上，将相关的维度-6和维度-8算符匹配到反常三规范玻色子耦合（anomalous triple gauge couplings），并通过MCFM-RE程序对 $q\bar q$ 通道中由喷注排斥（jet-veto）引起的大对数贡献进行重求和（resummation）。对于 $γγ$ 通道，则利用MadGraph程序，将因子化标度（factorisation scale）设置为喷注排斥标度（jet-veto scale）来实现重求和。

Result: 结果表明，在忽略费米子维度-8算符的情况下，$γγ$ 通道包含占主导地位的玻色子维度-8贡献。这一通道可用于理解有效场论（EFT）的有效范围。结合理论和实验不确定性，论文给出了对高维算符的约束。

Conclusion: 结论是 $γγ$ 通道在探测玻色子维度-8效应方面具有敏感性优势，可用于界定EFT的适用边界。基于当前与未来数据的分析，研究给出了对高维算符的约束条件。

Abstract: We compare the size of dimension-8 effects on $W^+W^-$ production at the LHC arising from the $q\bar q$ and $γγ$ initial states. In particular, we consider bosonic operators, which contribute to the anomalous triple and quadruple gauge couplings. The relevant dimension-6 and dimension-8 operators are matched to the anomalous triple gauge couplings that contribute to the $q\bar q$ channel, allowing for the resummation of large logarithmic contributions arising in the presence of a jet-veto through the program MCFM-RE. For the $γγ$ channel, which receives contributions from both triple and quadruple gauge couplings, such resummation can be performed through the program MadGraph, by simply setting the factorisation scale to the jet-veto scale. We find that, when neglecting fermionic dimension-8 operators, the $γγ$ channel has a dominant bosonic dimension-8 contribution and this channel can be used to understand the range of validity of the Effective Field Theory. With this in mind, and carefully considering theoretical and experimental uncertainties, we provide constraints on higher dimensional operators using current and future data.

### [212] [Quantum interference effects enhanced in $π^+p$ femtoscopic correlation functions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04351)
*Zhi-Wei Liu,Jun-Xu Lu,Duo-Lun Ge,Li-Sheng Geng*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 通过结合高斯源、Koonin-Pratt公式和数据驱动的πN分波振幅，该工作成功再现了ALICE合作组在√s=13 TeV高多重数pp碰撞中测量的π⁺p费米子对关联函数及其横质量依赖性，揭示了散射与Δ(1232)⁺⁺衰变两种贡献的竞争机制，并首次指出140 MeV/c处的关联峰源于入射波与散射波之间的量子干涉，从而解决了π⁺p关联中的峰位移动疑难。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: ALICE合作组在√s=13 TeV高多重数质子-质子（pp）碰撞中测量了π⁺p费米子对关联函数（femtoscopic correlation functions），但其中关联峰的峰位移动现象及其背后的物理机制尚未被阐明。本工作旨在通过理论建模揭示这一峰位移动的起源。

Method: 采用Koonin-Pratt公式，结合高斯型源函数（Gaussian source）和数据驱动的πN分波振幅（partial-wave amplitudes），分别计算π⁺p散射贡献与Δ(1232)⁺⁺衰变贡献，并将二者按横质量（transverse mass, m_T）依赖的相对权重进行加权求和，以拟合实验数据。

Result: 散射贡献在相对动量k≈140 MeV/c处产生一个峰，而Δ(1232)⁺⁺衰变贡献在k≈220 MeV/c附近产生另一个峰。观测到的关联峰是这两个贡献随m_T依赖权重叠加的结果。其中140 MeV/c处的峰源于入射波与散射波之间的量子干涉（quantum interference），这一机制在以往的费米子对关联（femtoscopic）研究中未被注意到。

Conclusion: 该发现解决了π⁺p关联中的峰位移动疑难，并为费米子对关联研究中的量子干涉效应提供了新的视角。

Abstract: We present a comprehensive analysis of the $π^+p$ femtoscopic correlation functions measured by the ALICE Collaboration in high-multiplicity $pp$ collisions at $\sqrt{s}=13$ TeV. Using the Koonin-Pratt formula with a Gaussian source and data-driven $πN$ partial-wave amplitudes, we account for the contributions from $π^+p$ scattering and $Δ(1232)^{++}$-decay, thereby successfully reproducing the measured data and their transverse-mass ($m_T$) dependence. The scattering contribution yields a peak near the relative momentum $k\approx140$ MeV/$c$, whereas the decay contribution peaks around $k\approx220$ MeV/$c$. The observed correlation peak results from a weighted sum of the two contributions, with $m_T$-dependent relative weights. We find that the 140 MeV/$c$ peak originates from quantum interference between the incident and scattered waves-a mechanism previously unnoticed in femtoscopic studies. This finding resolves the peak-shift puzzle in $π^+p$ correlations and provides a novel perspective for quantum interference effects in femtoscopy.

### [213] [Charting doubly strange hidden-charm pentaquarks: An electromagnetic mapping of spin-$\frac{1}{2}$ and $\frac{3}{2}$ states](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04355)
*Ulaş Özdem*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文利用QCD光锥求和规则（LCSR），首次系统计算了双奇异隐粲五夸克态（自旋宇称 J^P = 1/2^- 和 3/2^-）的磁偶极矩、电四极矩和磁八极矩，揭示了不同内部分子电流模型下电磁多极矩的显著差异，并发现粲夸克主导多数构型的磁矩，而奇异夸克仅在特定流结构中起决定性作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前对奇异数 S = -2 扇区的隐粲五夸克态（pentaquark states）的电磁多极结构（electromagnetic multipole structure）缺乏系统性研究，尤其是通过QCD光锥求和规则（QCD light-cone sum rules, LCSR）的理论计算尚属空白。本文旨在填补这一空缺，为未来的实验和格点QCD计算提供基准预测。

Method: 采用QCD光锥求和规则（LCSR），在夸克-双夸克-反夸克（diquark-diquark-antiquark）形式下构造独立的插入流（interpolating currents），以刻画不同的内部分色-自旋关联假设。对于自旋 3/2 态，额外计算电四极矩（electric quadrupole moment）和磁八极矩（magnetic octupole moment）。

Result: 磁偶极矩（magnetic dipole moment）随电流模型在较大范围内变动：自旋 1/2 态为 −2.15 μ_N 至 5.74 μ_N，自旋 3/2 态为 −4.25 μ_N 至 −0.43 μ_N。粲夸克（charm quark）在多数构型中主导磁矩，而奇异夸克（strange quark）仅在轴向矢量双夸克（axial-vector diquark）结构中起关键作用。电四极矩介于 −2.01×10⁻² fm² 至 5.55×10⁻² fm² 之间，磁八极矩通常小一个数量级。等旋敏感度（isospin sensitivity）源于轴向矢量双夸克结构导致的电荷不对称性 e_u/e_d = −2 的直接传播，比值 μ_u/μ_d = −2.00 精确验证了这一机制。

Conclusion: 磁偶极矩对电流选择的强依赖性定量刻画了理论不确定性，因此不同插入流模型可被实验和格点QCD区分。本文的计算结果为未来实验和格点QCD（lattice QCD）研究提供了基准预测，并有助于甄别不同的五夸克态结构模型。

Abstract: We calculate the magnetic dipole moments of doubly strange hidden-charm pentaquark states with spin-parity $J^P = 1/2^-$ and $3/2^-$ using QCD light-cone sum rules (LCSR), presenting the first systematic LCSR investigation of the electromagnetic multipole structure in the $S = -2$ sector. To assess the model dependence, we employ independent interpolating currents in diquark-diquark-antiquark form, which probe different assumptions about the internal color-spin correlations. For the spin-$3/2$ states, we also compute the electric quadrupole and magnetic octupole moments. The magnetic dipole moments exhibit a considerable spread across currents, ranging from $-2.15\,μ_N$ to $5.74\,μ_N$ for spin-$1/2$ pentaquarks and from $-4.25\,μ_N$ to $-0.43\,μ_N$ for spin-$3/2$ states, reflecting the sensitivity of magnetic moments to the internal wave function. A quark-level decomposition reveals that the charm quark dominates in most configurations, while strange quarks play a decisive role only in currents favoring axial-vector diquark structures. The electric quadrupole moments lie between $-2.01\times10^{-2}$ fm$^2$ and $5.55\times10^{-2}$ fm$^2$, and the magnetic octupole moments are typically an order of magnitude smaller. The current dependence of the magnetic dipole moments provides a quantitative measure of the theoretical uncertainty arising from the choice of interpolating operator. The pronounced isospin sensitivity of $J^3_μ(x)$ across all three multipole moments arises from its axial-vector diquark structure, which isolates the light quark from spin averaging and allows the charge asymmetry $e_u/e_d = -2$ to propagate directly into the electromagnetic moments; the ratio $μ_u/μ_d = -2.00$ confirms this mechanism exactly. Our predictions offer benchmarks for future experiments and lattice QCD calculations, and may help discriminate among competing structural models.

### [214] [Probing Neutrinophilic Long-Range Forces at DUNE](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04441)
*Sudip Jana,Pragyanprasu Swain*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了一种暗中微子门户（dark neutrino portal）模型，其中中微子质量产生与一个新的U(1)_D规范对称性下的轻暗扇区（light dark sector）耦合。该模型通过活性-暗中微子混合（active–dark neutrino mixing）使暗扇区与标准模型通信，并诱导超长程相互作用（ultra-long-range interactions），从而在地球、月球、太阳、银河系及宇宙学物质分布中产生显著的物质势（matter potentials）以改变中微子振荡。研究表明，即将开展的深地下中微子实验（DUNE）可探测此前未触及的参数空间，且同一耦合可同时产生可缓解哈勃张力（Hubble tension）的中微子自相互作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 中微子振荡为超越标准模型（Standard Model）的物理提供了有力证据，同时中微子的弱相互作用特征使其成为探测新相互作用和隐藏扇区（hidden sectors）的理想探针。本文旨在探索一个将中微子质量产生与暗扇区联系起来的理论场景，并评估其在下一代中微子实验中的可探测性。

Method: 作者构建了一个暗中微子门户模型，其中暗扇区带有一个新U(1)_D规范对称性，而标准模型粒子在该规范对称性下中性；暗扇区与标准模型仅通过活性-暗中微子混合进行通信。该模型引入的中微子亲和介质（neutrinophilic mediator）可诱导超长程相互作用，使得地球、月球、太阳、银河系及宇宙学物质分布中的电子和中子产生显著的等效物质势，进而修正中微子振荡行为。

Result: 研究表明，深地下中微子实验（DUNE）凭借其长基线（long baseline）和显著的物质效应（matter effects），特别适合探测此类超长程相互作用。DUNE能够访问此前未被实验覆盖的参数空间区域。此外，该模型中的同一耦合常数还可同时产生可观的中微子自相互作用（neutrino self-interactions），其强度覆盖有助于缓解哈勃张力（Hubble tension）的相关区域，同时与当前中微子振荡约束保持兼容。

Conclusion: 该暗中微子门户模型为中微子质量起源与暗扇区物理提供了统一框架，DUNE实验有望揭示此类新物理信号。该模型不仅能通过超长程物质效应改变中微子振荡，还能产生与宇宙学观测（如哈勃张力）相关的自相互作用，展现出丰富的物理可探测性。

Abstract: Neutrino oscillations provide compelling evidence for physics beyond the Standard Model, while the weakly interacting nature of neutrinos makes them powerful probes of new interactions and hidden sectors. In this work, we investigate a \textit{dark neutrino portal} scenario in which neutrino mass generation is linked to a light dark sector charged under a new $U(1)_D$ gauge symmetry. While Standard Model fields remain neutral under $U(1)_D$, the dark neutrino sector is charged and communicates with the Standard Model exclusively through active--dark neutrino mixing. The associated neutrinophilic mediator induces ultra-long-range interactions, whereby electrons and neutrons in the Earth, Moon, Sun, Milky Way, and the cosmological matter distribution generate sizable matter potentials that modify neutrino oscillations. We explore the sensitivity of the upcoming Deep Underground Neutrino Experiment (DUNE), whose long baseline and pronounced matter effects make it uniquely suited to probe such interactions. We show that DUNE can access previously unexplored regions of parameter space and demonstrate that the same underlying coupling can simultaneously give rise to sizable neutrino self-interactions, including regions relevant for alleviating the Hubble tension, while remaining consistent with current neutrino oscillation constraints.

</details>


### [215] [Implications of exclusive photon leptoproduction measurements for the proton charge-radius puzzle](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04481)

TL;DR: 本研究基于Bethe-Heitler过程主导的光生（EP）实验数据，拓展了质子电磁形状因子（FFs）的分析，发现CLAS 2018数据与其他数据集存在显著张力；排除该数据集后获得了稳定的拟合结果。提取的质子电荷半径小于Particle Data Group平均值和弹性电子-质子散射结果，但与PRad测量和μ子氢光谱一致；磁半径则与当前世界平均值相容。该工作表明BH主导的EP测量为质子电荷半径谜题的小半径解提供了独立支持。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 扩展了此前对质子电磁形状因子（FFs）的分析框架，纳入CLAS和Hall~A合作组所有当前可用的高精度光子轻子产生（EP）数据，在Bethe-Heitler（BH）过程占主导的运动学区域中，采用相同的唯象学框架进行多组拟合场景分析，并考察不同数据集之间的一致性。

Conclusion: BH主导的EP测量为确定质子的电磁结构提供了一种独立且互补的方法，为质子电荷半径谜题中的小半径解（small-radius solution）提供了额外支持。

Abstract: In the present study, we extend our previous analysis of the proton electromagnetic form factors (FFs) extracted from exclusive photon leptoproduction (EP) measurements in kinematic regions where the Bethe-Heitler (BH) process dominates the cross section by including all currently available high-precision EP data from the CLAS and Hall~A Collaborations. Using the same phenomenological framework, we investigate the consistency among the different data sets, determine the proton electromagnetic FFs within several fitting scenarios, and extract the corresponding charge and magnetic radii. A significant tension is observed between the CLAS 2018 measurements and the remaining EP data. We show that excluding this data set, or restricting its kinematic coverage by imposing suitable low-$|t|$ cuts, leads to stable fits with good quality and consistent FFs. For all analyses, the extracted proton charge radius is smaller than the Particle Data Group average and most determinations based on elastic electron-proton scattering. However, the results are consistent, within uncertainties, with the PRad measurement and muonic hydrogen spectroscopy. In contrast, the magnetic radius is found to be compatible with the current world average. These results demonstrate that BH-dominated EP measurements provide an independent and complementary approach to determine the electromagnetic structure of the proton and offer additional support for the small-radius solution of the proton charge-radius puzzle.

Abstract: We study exclusive electroproduction of dijets in the collinear factorization framework as a probe of generalized parton distributions (GPDs). ### [217] [The variable flavor number scheme to three-loop order](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05235)

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了三阶变味数方案（variable flavor number scheme, VFNS），通过单质量和双质量效应修正无质量部分子密度，并引入粲夸克（charm）和底夸克（bottom）的重味部分子分布函数（parton distribution functions, PDFs）。重整化群（renormalization group）分析表明该图像在大尺度Q²下有效，能完全描述非幂次抑制的重味修正，并提供了电荷流与中性流Wilson系数（Wilson coefficients）的数值实现。

Method: 采用三阶（three-loop order）的变味数方案，通过将单质量与双质量效应纳入无质量部分子密度的修正中，引入粲夸克和底夸克的重味部分子分布函数。利用重整化群（renormalization group）分析验证该方案在大尺度Q²下的有效性，并数值实现一系列带电流（charged current）与中性流（neutral current）的Wilson系数（Wilson coefficients）。

Result: 大尺度Q²下，该三阶变味数方案能够完全描述非幂次抑制的重味修正，表明其在高能区域的适用性。数值实现了带电及中性流Wilson系数，为后续物理分析提供了具体的计算工具。

Conclusion: 三阶变味数方案为重味夸克效应提供了系统且高阶的微扰论框架，在大动量传递下能够准确捕捉重味部分的完整修正。相关Wilson系数的数值实现有助于在精确检验标准模型（Standard Model）过程中应用该方案。

Abstract: We describe the variable flavor number scheme to three-loop order, which modifies the massless parton densities by single- and two-mass effects and introduces heavy-quark parton distribution functions for charm and bottom. A renormalization group analysis shows the validity of this picture at large scales $Q^2$, where it resembles the non-power-suppressed heavy-flavor corrections completely. We also provide numerical implementations of a series of charged and neutral current Wilson coefficients.

### [218] [Majoron Dark Energy via Freezing Induced by Quantum Coherence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03070)
*Keunsu Cheon,Sin Kyu Kang,Jungjai Lee*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解释马约拉子暗能量（Majoron dark energy）的动力学冻结起源，避免对精确静态宇宙学常数（cosmological constant）的依赖，为非平衡暗能量提供微观物理实现。

Method: 基于因果响应核（causal response kernel）在短记忆（short-memory）极限下的线性响应匹配，推导出包含交换结构q_exch φ̈/φ̇的有效标量场方程，并将滞后变量（lag variable）的微观起源归因于隐藏伪狄拉克系综的相位滞后离对角相干性（phase-lagged off-diagonal coherence）。

Result: 即使马约拉子本征质量大于当前哈勃尺度（Hubble scale），交换项仍可动态抑制其速度，维持响应主导的冻结分支（response-dominated freezing branch）。响应强度由响应加权隐藏密度控制，而非独立的引力组分。

Conclusion: 所得到的态为亚稳态非平衡冻结相，状态参数w_φ≈-1，与精确静态宇宙学常数不同，为非平衡暗能量模型提供了可检验的微观理论基础。

Abstract: We propose a nonequilibrium mechanism for Majoron dark energy in which the late-time freezing of a physical Majoron is induced by quantum coherence in a hidden pseudo-Dirac sterile fermion reservoir. The evolving Majoron background derivatively couples to the hidden pseudo-Dirac number current and drives a lagged reservoir response with a finite memory time. In the short-memory regime, the causal response kernel reduces to \(\dot X+Γ_{\rm PD}X=β\ddotφ\). The leading linear-response matching \(Q=αX\) then yields an effective scalar equation containing the exchange structure \(q_{\rm exch}\ddotφ/\dotφ\). We show that this term can dynamically suppress the Majoron velocity and sustain a response-dominated freezing branch even when the intrinsic Majoron mass is larger than the present Hubble scale. The microscopic origin of the lag variable is identified with the phase-lagged off-diagonal coherence of the hidden pseudo-Dirac ensemble, while the response strength is controlled by a response-weighted hidden density rather than by an independent gravitating component. The resulting state is a metastable nonequilibrium frozen phase with \(w_φ\simeq -1\), rather than an exactly static cosmological constant.

### [219] [Flipped rotating axion: Baryogenesis and Dark Matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03085)

Abstract: It is shown that the co-genesis of baryon asymmetry and dark matter can be achieved through the rotation of a spectator axion-like particle, because of a flip in the vacuum manifold's orientation at the end of inflation. This can occur if the axion has a periodic non-minimal coupling to gravity (while preserving the discrete shift symmetry) in non-oscillating inflation models, where the inflaton field is characterised by a runaway potential. Our rotating axion can generate the baryon asymmetry of the Universe through spontaneous baryogenesis, while at a later epoch it can oscillate as dark matter. We show that in order to avoid fragmentation of the axion condensate during the rotation, we require the non-minimal coupling $ξ\sim(f/m_P)^2$, where $f$ is the axion decay constant.

### [221] [Gravitational Wave Signatures of Cosmological Stasis: A Unified Spectral Template](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03537)
*Gabriela Barenboim,Anne-Katherine Burns*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个封闭形式的谱模板（closed-form spectral template），用于刻画早期宇宙中任何停滞时期（stasis epoch）留下的暴胀引力波印记。该模板仅由状态参数 $w_s$ 和停滞持续时间 $\Delta N_\mathrm{stasis}$ 两个物理输入控制，并导出一条可由实验检验的一致性曲线（consistency curve），使该理论模型具备可证伪性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Dienes 等人于 2022 年提出的停滞（stasis）是早期宇宙中的一个动力学不动点（fixed point），其状态方程（equation of state）$w_s$ 固定为常数。本文旨在证明任何停滞时期所留下的暴胀引力波（inflationary gravitational wave）印记均可由一个统一的封闭形式谱模板描述，并进而导出可供实验检验的可观测预言。

Method: 通过理论推导，构造了一个封闭形式的谱模板（closed-form spectral template），该模板对任何微观物理实现均普适适用，仅依赖于两个物理参数：状态参数 $w_s$ 和停滞持续时间 $\Delta N_\mathrm{stasis}$。进一步消去 $w_s$ 得到一条一参数一致性曲线 $C^2 = C^2(\alpha)$，作为判断宇宙是否经历常数 $w$ 时期的检验标准。

Result: 该模板给出了两个独立可测的观测量：停滞波段内的谱倾斜（spectral tilt）$\alpha(w_s)$ 以及停滞波段起点和终点处的振幅阶跃（amplitude step）$C^2(w_s)$。通过一致性曲线 $C^2 = C^2(\alpha)$，任何测得的 $(\alpha, C^2)$ 对若偏离该曲线即可排除常数 $w$ 时期模型。BBO 和 DECIGO 实验在张标比（tensor-to-scalar ratio）$r = 0.01$ 下，可分辨垂直于一致性曲线的偏移至 $\sigma_\perp \simeq 1.5\times10^{-5}$，比曲线在 $C^2$ 上的变化范围低四个数量级。

Conclusion: 该工作表明，无需预先知道 $w_s$ 的具体数值，即可通过一致性曲线对常数 $w$ 时期的引力波谱进行可证伪性检验。未来引力波探测实验（如 BBO 和 DECIGO）在较宽的 $r$ 值范围内均能有效探测到任何偏离一致性曲线的信号。

Abstract: Proposed in 2022 by Dienes et al., stasis is a dynamical fixed point in the early universe in which the equation of state, $w_s$, is fixed at a constant value. In this study we show that the inflationary gravitational wave imprint of any stasis epoch is captured by a closed-form spectral template controlled by two physical inputs, the equation of state $w_s$ and the stasis duration $ΔN_\mathrm{stasis}$, that applies uniformly across every microphysical realization. The template presented here yields two independently measurable observables, the spectral tilt of the spectra in the stasis band, $α(w_s)$ and the amplitude step $C^2(w_s)$ at the beginning and end of the stasis band. Eliminating $w_s$ gives a one-parameter consistency curve $C^2 = C^2(α)$ on which the data must lie if the underlying cosmology is any constant-$w$ era. This makes the spectrum falsifiable without knowing $w_s$ in advance: a measured $(α, C^2)$ pair either lands on the curve or rules out the constant-$w$ class. We show that BBO and DECIGO can resolve the perpendicular displacement from the consistency curve to $σ_\perp \simeq 1.5\times10^{-5}$ at a tensor-to-scalar ratio, $r = 0.01$, four orders of magnitude below the curve's range in $C^2$ meaning that any off-curve deviation is detectable across a broad range of allowed $r$ values.

</details>


### [222] [Probing a 146 GeV cLFV scalar using the LHC and low-energy experiments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03249)
*Christina Gao,Lingfeng Li,Z. J. Xiong*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文基于CMS实验在146 GeV处观测到的轻子味违反（lepton flavor violation, LFV）信号，采用贝叶斯MCMC方法，在有效场论框架下系统评估该信号与所有低能cLFV约束的兼容性，发现与现有μ→e转化极限已存在张力，未来十年内高能与低能实验将能验证或排除该标量解释。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: CMS合作组在13 TeV的质子-质子对撞中，于eμ末态搜索希格斯玻色子及额外希格斯玻色子的轻子味违反衰变时，观测到约146 GeV处的局域超出。若该信号得到确认，将成为带电轻子味违反（charged lepton flavor violation, cLFV）的重要证据。因此需检验该信号与现有低能cLFV实验限制的兼容性。

Method: 采用自下而上的有效描述（bottom-up effective description）：引入一个质量为146 GeV的实标量粒子，与胶子及所有带电轻子双线性（charged-lepton bilinears）耦合。模型共有7个自由参数，同时控制LHC产生截面、所有双轻子衰变道及所有低能cLFV可观测量。利用贝叶斯MCMC方法，针对μ→e转化、muonium-反muonium振荡、三轻子及辐射LFV衰变、半轻子τ LFV衰变以及LHC双轻子搜索等数据进行拟合分析。

Result: 贝叶斯MCMC分析给出偏好参数模式，其中耦合强度Y_{eμ}的峰值约为10^{-4.09}，该区域已被当前的μ→e转化极限所覆盖。此外，Mu2e、COMET、Mu3e、MACE、MEG II、Belle II、STCF及HL-LHC等实验的预期灵敏度将直接探测CMS超出所选中的耦合参数空间。

Conclusion: 高能与低能cLFV探测手段之间的互补性，将在未来十年内要么证实、要么决定性地排除该146 GeV异常信号的标量粒子解释。该信号与现有低能cLFV约束之间已存在张力，尤其是μ→e转化实验的限制已经切入所偏好的参数区域。

Abstract: The CMS Collaboration reported a local excess at $146~\mathrm{GeV}$ in the search for the lepton-flavor-violating decay of the Higgs boson and additional Higgs bosons in the $eμ$ final state at $\sqrt{s}= 13~\mathrm{TeV}$. If confirmed, this would constitute a major piece of evidence of charged lepton flavor violation (cLFV). We investigate the compatibility of the claimed signal with the full suite of existing low-energy cLFV constraints in a bottom-up effective description: a single real scalar of mass $146~\mathrm{GeV}$ coupled to gluons and to all charged-lepton bilinears, with seven free parameters that simultaneously control the LHC production cross section, every di-lepton decay channel, and every low-energy cLFV observable. A Bayesian MCMC analysis against $μ-e$ conversion, muonium-antimuonium oscillation, three-lepton and radiative LFV decays, semileptonic $τ$ LFV decays, and LHC di-lepton searches yields a preferred mode with peaked value $Y_{eμ} \sim 10^{-4.09}$, already cut into by the current $μ-e$ conversion limits. The projected sensitivities of Mu2e, COMET, Mu3e, MACE, MEG~II, Belle~II, STCF, and the HL-LHC directly probe the region of coupling space selected by the CMS excess, so the complementarity between high-energy and low-energy cLFV probes will either corroborate or decisively exclude the scalar interpretation of the anomaly within the next decade.

</details>


### [223] [First look at the evaluation of two-loop Feynman integrals for radiative return processes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03343)
*Mattia Pozzoli,William J. Torres Bobadilla*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文计算了低能电子-正电子对撞机中辐射返回过程所需的平面双圈四点费曼积分，这些积分用于构建次次领头阶（NNLO）QED预言，并成功实现了在整个物理区域的稳定数值评估。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 低能电子-正电子（electron-positron）对撞机中辐射返回（radiative return）过程的精密研究需要次次领头阶（next-to-next-to-leading order, NNLO）的量子电动力学（QED）预言，且必须保留对电子质量的完整依赖。现有的计算精度不足以满足这一需求。

Method: 计算了与初态辐射（initial-state radiation）贡献相关的平面双圈四点费曼积分（planar two-loop four-point Feynman integrals）；构建了关于维度正则化参数（dimensional regulator）的多项式形式的微分方程（differential equations），并采用数值积分方法求解。

Result: 成功实现了在整个低能实验相关物理区域内的稳定数值评估，尽管存在大尺度层次（large hierarchies of scales）的挑战。

Conclusion: 所得到的积分结果为辐射返回过程的NNLO QED预言提供了关键构建模块（essential building blocks）。

Abstract: Precision studies of radiative return processes at low-energy electron--positron colliders require next-to-next-to-leading order QED predictions retaining full dependence on the electron mass. We present the calculation of planar two-loop four-point Feynman integrals relevant for initial-state radiation contributions to these processes. The calculation presents considerable analytical complexity, due to the presence of a nested square root and of integrals associated with elliptic geometries. We construct differential equations for the Feynman integrals which are polynomial in the dimensional regulator, and are suitable for numerical integration. We demonstrate stable numerical evaluations throughout the physical region relevant for low-energy experiments, despite the presence of large hierarchies of scales. Our results provide essential building blocks for NNLO predictions for radiative return processes.

*Jian Wang,Xing Wang,Yefan Wang*
