Abstract: In working conditions, chalcogen vacancies spontaneously occur in two-dimensional transition metal dichalcogenides (TMDCs) monolayers, affecting their optoelectronic and photocatalytic properties. To study how chalcogen vacancies affect such properties, we use quantum mechanical calculations considering prototypical MX$_2$ (M = Mo, W, X = S and Se) TMDCs monolayers. Structural optimisations show that M-X bond lengths about a vacancy are different compared to the bond lengths in the pristine structure. Band structure calculations reveal that the introduction of vacancies produce electronic states about the Fermi level, hence resulting in the reduction of the band gap. Work function and electrostatic potential calculations show that the introduction of vacancies induce an asymmetry in the electrostatic potential facilitating the charge separation; such feature is absent in a pristine monolayer. All the considered defective structures are capable of performing hydrogen evolution reaction, while co-catalyst is required to perform oxygen evolution reaction when used for water splitting. WS$_2$ and WSe$_2$ defective monolayers can serve as an efficient photocatalytic material for reducing CO$_2$ into useful chemical products. The presented results show that vacancy-containing TMDCs monolayers own photocatalytic capabilities compared to the pristine counterparts, thus showing that defective TMD monolayers have prospective applications and should not be regarded as flawed products to be discarded. Finally, the results might constitute guidelines for the experimental synthesis of vacancy-engineered MX$_2$ monolayers for optoelectronic devices and photocatalytic applications.

### [262] [Twist-configured moire-moire reconstruction governs diverse commensurate double-moire phases in twisted bilayer graphene on h-BN](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02822)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 范德华异质结构（van der Waals heterostructures）中常存在多个莫尔晶格共存，但不同莫尔图案之间如何相互作用与重构，是一个尚未解决的基础问题。

Method: 采用导电原子力显微镜（conductive atomic force microscopy, c-AFM）结合连续模型模拟（continuum-model simulations），研究六方氮化硼（h-BN）上的扭曲双层石墨烯（twisted bilayer graphene, tBG），其中tBG与石墨烯/h-BN莫尔结构共存。

Conclusion: 莫尔-莫尔重构可作为多层莫尔材料中结构序与电子序（包括魔法角以下的拓扑平带）工程化的通用框架。

Abstract: The coexistence of multiple moire lattices in van der Waals heterostructures raises a fundamental question: how do distinct moire patterns interact and reconstruct? Here, we investigate twisted bilayer graphene (tBG) on hexagonal boron nitride (h-BN), where tBG and graphene/h-BN moire structures coexist, using conductive atomic force microscopy combined with continuum-model simulations. We show that reconstruction between these moire lattices-moire-moire reconstruction-manifests across multiple length scales, giving rise to diverse commensurate double-moire phases. Locally, the stacking registry between the two moire lattices is uniquely selected by the global twist configuration (helical or alternate), mediated by rotational relaxation of the shared graphene layer. This registry, together with twist angle and strain, governs commensurate domains from C3z-symmetric to strained symmetry-modified structures. These results establish moire-moire reconstruction as a general framework for engineering structural and electronic order -- including theoretically predicted topological flat bands below the magic angle -- in multilayer moire materials.

### [264] [Thermophysical and mechanical properties of UFe$_2$ fabricated by spark plasma sintering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02918)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Following the accident at the Fukushima Daiichi Nuclear Power Plant in 2011, core meltdown produced fuel debris whose safe retrieval and management require reliable thermophysical and mechanical property data. Among the metallic phases identified in the debris, the U-Fe system is particularly important because of the abundant iron originating from in-vessel stainless steel structures. However, within this system, the high-temperature thermophysical properties of UFe$_2$ have received relatively little attention, with most prior studies focusing on its magnetic and electronic properties. To fill this data gap in the literature, we fabricated dense, nearly single-phase polycrystalline UFe$_2$ by arc melting followed by spark plasma sintering, and characterized its thermal and mechanical properties from room temperature to 1073 K. Results show that the thermal conductivity of UFe$_2$ increased monotonically from 10 Wm$^{-1}$K$^{-1}$ at 306 K to 25 Wm$^{-1}$K$^{-1}$ at 1073 K, surpassing those of the iron intermetallics Fe$_2$Zr and Fe$_2$B at high temperatures. In addition, UFe$_2$ is mechanically more compliant, displaying a Young's modulus $E$ of 69 GPa, a shear modulus $G$ of 24 GPa, and a Vickers hardness $H_{\mathrm{V}}$ of 5.6 GPa, all well below those of both Fe intermetallics. Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

Conclusion: 该工作确立了原子手性（atomic chirality）作为设计压电材料的独特路径，可能拓展至其他非中心对称无机半导体，用于可持续能量收集和可穿戴传感。

Abstract: The growth of wearable electronics, soft robotics, and Internet-of-Things systems has intensified the demand for inorganic piezoelectric materials that harvest weak biomechanical energy. Advances through composition optimization, defect engineering, strain engineering, and orientation control have improved existing electromechanical responses, but have not introduced a new mechanism for enhancing piezoelectricity. Here we propose atomic chirality engineering as a design principle for inorganic piezoelectric nanomaterials. Unlike conventional strategies that modify composition or morphology, atomic chirality alters the handedness of the crystal lattice itself, adding a degree of freedom for controlling dipole alignment, electromechanical coupling, and potentially spin-dependent transport. Using atomically chiral trigonal selenium nanowires as a model system, we show that crystal handedness alone changes piezoelectric performance at identical chemical composition. Piezoresponse force microscopy resolved a consistent enantiomeric difference, with right-handed D-Se nanowires reaching a higher effective piezoelectric coefficient than their left-handed counterparts, and flexible nanogenerators and self-powered acoustic sensors built from the two enantiomers produced distinct outputs under identical deformation. This work establishes atomic chirality as a distinct route for designing piezoelectric materials, one that may extend across non-centrosymmetric inorganic semiconductors for sustainable energy harvesting and wearable sensing.

Abstract: Carbon-supported single-atom catalysts maximize metal utilization, but how metal nanoparticles transform into isolated atoms within carbon remains unclear. Using Pt-catalysed hydrocarbon oxidation as a model, we combine operando electron microscopy, near-ambient-pressure X-ray photoelectron spectroscopy and mass spectrometry to track coupled structural and chemical evolution. Graphitic carbon grows at step edges of Pt nanoparticle, continuously reconstructing Pt surface and generating undercoordinated sites for atom release. In-situ generated CO accumulates at the metal-carbon interface, weakening bonding and facilitating self-amplified atom release and migration. ### [267] [Martensitic Transformation in Crystal-Amorphous Superlattices of NiTi Shape Memory Alloy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03172)
*Bhavna Singh,Shivam Tripathi*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过大规模分子动力学模拟，系统研究了晶态-非晶态超晶格（crystal-amorphous superlattices, CAS）中部分非晶化对镍钛形状记忆合金（shape memory alloy, SMA）马氏体相变（martensitic transformation）及热-力学行为的影响，发现部分非晶化可改变相变路径、降低热滞（thermal hysteresis）并提升弹性模量与临界应力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 形状记忆合金通过可逆马氏体相变展现独特的热-力学性能，利用共格第二相（coherent second phases）调控这些性能虽然有效，但识别热力学相容的第二相十分困难。晶态-非晶态超晶格（CAS）作为一种替代方案，其第二相源自基体材料本身；然而，部分非晶化对马氏体相变及热-力学行为的影响尚未被充分探索。

Method: 采用大规模分子动力学（molecular dynamics, MD）模拟，研究不同晶相分数（crystalline phase fraction）的CAS-NiTi在温度诱导和应力诱导条件下的马氏体相变行为。

Result: 部分非晶化从根本上改变了相变路径，在传统一级马氏体相变之前引入了一个连续的（类似二级相变）转变。非晶态相增强了相变可逆性，将热滞从完全晶态NiTi的275 K降低至CAS-NiTi的95–110 K。同时，弹性模量和应力诱导马氏体相变的临界应力提升约60–90%，具体幅度取决于晶相分数。

Conclusion: 性能改善源于晶态-非晶态界面处的异质成核（heterogeneous nucleation）、促进逆马氏体相变的残余奥氏体（retained austenite）以及非晶态相施加的力学约束。研究结果表明，晶态-非晶态超晶格是一种调控形状记忆合金热-力学性能的有前景的微观结构设计策略。

Abstract: Shape memory alloys (SMAs) exhibit unique thermo-mechanical properties arising from reversible martensitic transformation. Tailoring these properties through coherent second phases is effective but is often limited by the difficulty of identifying thermodynamically compatible phases. Crystal-amorphous superlattices (CAS), in which the second phase is derived from the base material itself, provide an attractive alternative. However, the influence of partial amorphization on martensitic transformation and thermo-mechanical behavior remains largely unexplored. Here, large-scale molecular dynamics simulations are used to investigate temperature- and stress-induced martensitic transformations in CAS-NiTi with different crystalline phase fractions. Partial amorphization fundamentally modifies the transformation pathway, introducing an initial continuous (second-order-like) transformation before the conventional first-order martensitic transformation. The amorphous phase also enhances transformation reversibility, reducing the thermal hysteresis from 275 K in fully crystalline NiTi to 95-110 K in CAS-NiTi. Simultaneously, the elastic modulus and the critical stress for stress-induced martensitic transformation increase by approximately 60-90 percent, depending on the crystalline fraction. These improvements originate from heterogeneous nucleation at crystal-amorphous interfaces, retained austenite that promotes the reverse transformation, and mechanical constraint imposed by the amorphous phase. These findings establish crystal-amorphous superlattices as a promising microstructural design strategy for tailoring the thermo-mechanical performance of shape memory alloys.

</details>


### [268] [Data-driven multi-objective optimization for alloy recycling using factorization machines and quantum annealing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03208)
*Thomas Plehn,Katrin Bugelnig,Silvana Tumminello,Daniel Barragan-Yani,David Melching*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文系统评估了集成因子分解机与量子退火（FM+QA）的工作流程，用于金属再循环中合金设计的多目标帕累托优化，并采用数据驱动的切比雪夫标量化（DDTS）方案处理非凸帕累托前沿。结果表明，FM+QA将基于QUBO的优化扩展至数据驱动的多目标材料发现问题；通过规模行为分析以及与经典模拟退火的对比，文章对量子退火优化在近期可能实际获益的问题规模和编码策略提供了批判性视角。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子退火（quantum annealing）有望为复杂优化任务带来实际量子优势。本文旨在探索其在高技术相关应用——即金属再循环中通过合金设计实现的多目标帕累托优化（multi-objective Pareto optimization）——中的可行性和性能。

Method: 采用集成因子分解机与量子退火（FM+QA）的工作流程，并引入数据驱动的切比雪夫标量化（DDTS）方案处理帕累托前沿的非凸性。通过分析该方法在不同问题规模下的标度行为，并与经典模拟退火（simulated annealing）在常规二进制编码（binary encoding）和独热编码（one-hot encoding）两种策略下进行对比。

Result: FM+QA方法将QUBO（二次无约束二进制优化）框架的适用性从传统优化领域扩展到数据驱动的材料发现问题，且能够处理多个竞争性目标。文中给出了该方法的标度行为分析，并提供了与经典模拟退火的对比结果。

Conclusion: 对近期内基于量子退火的优化可能在何种问题规模和编码策略下获得实际收益进行了批判性展望。该工作为量子退火在真实材料科学优化场景中的潜在应用提供了评估基准和方向指引。

Abstract: Quantum annealing has the potential to provide practical quantum advantage for complex optimization tasks. Here, we present a systematic assessment of an integrated factorization-machine and quantum-annealing workflow (FM+QA) for a technologically relevant application: multi-objective Pareto optimization in metal up-cycling through alloy design. To address the non-convex nature of the Pareto front, we employ the recently proposed data-driven Tchebycheff scalarization (DDTS) scheme. Our results show that FM+QA extends the applicability of QUBO-based optimization to data-driven materials discovery problems with multiple competing objectives. In particular, we analyze the scaling behavior of the approach and compare quantum annealing with classical simulated annealing using both regular binary encoding and one-hot encoding. Finally, we provide a critical perspective on the problem sizes and encoding strategies for which quantum-annealing-based optimization may become practically beneficial in the near future.

### [269] [NanoBTE: Fast Iterative Solution of the Phonon Boltzmann Transport Equation for Nanoscale Heat Transport](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03226)
*Hongjiang Chen,Hai-Xuan Lin,Xiaole Tian,Hongyu Chen,Juan Zhang,Shengyao Yan,Hezhu Shao,Yu Wu,Junjie Liu,Hao Zhang*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出NanoBTE，一种基于确定论有限体积法的非灰体声子玻尔兹曼输运方程（non-gray phonon Boltzmann transport equation）求解器，支持复杂几何、多种边界条件和多尺度加速方案，适用于纳米尺度热耗散模拟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 纳米尺度热耗散已成为先进半导体器件的关键挑战，此时声子输运（phonon transport）因边界散射和弹道效应（ballistic effects）而强烈偏离经典傅里叶描述（Fourier description），亟需能够准确模拟此类非平衡输运的高效数值工具。

Method: 采用确定论有限体积法（finite-volume method）求解松弛时间近似（relaxation-time approximation）下的非灰体声子玻尔兹曼输运方程；支持二维与三维复杂几何、带分辨（band-resolved）声子性质、离散纵标角求积（discrete-ordinates angular quadrature）、体热生成以及热化、漫反射和镜面反射等多种边界条件；实现序贯和合成迭代（sequential and synthetic iterative）两种多尺度加速方案，其中合成迭代将微观声子输运方程与宏观扩散型温度方程耦合以加速近扩散区收敛；采用带-方向任务分解（band-direction task decomposition）策略，实现基于MPI的CPU并行化和GPU加速。

Result: 通过带-方向任务分解策略，NanoBTE实现了高效的MPI并行计算和GPU加速，显著提升了主导的稀疏输运操作的计算性能。

Conclusion: NanoBTE为纳米尺度声子输运模拟提供了一套兼具几何灵活性、物理精度和计算效率的确定论求解框架，尤其适用于多尺度热输运问题。

Abstract: Nanoscale heat dissipation has become a critical challenge in advanced semiconductor devices, where phonon transport can strongly deviate from the classical Fourier description owing to boundary scattering and ballistic effects. Here, we propose NanoBTE, a deterministic finite-volume solver for the non-gray phonon Boltzmann transport equation under the relaxation-time approximation. NanoBTE supports complex two- and three-dimensional geometries, band-resolved phonon properties, discrete-ordinates angular quadrature, volumetric heat generation, and multiple phonon boundary conditions, including thermalizing, diffuse, and specular reflections. To improve the efficiency of multiscale simulations, we implement both sequential and synthetic iterative schemes, with the latter coupling the microscopic phonon transport equation to a macroscopic diffusion-type temperature equation to accelerate convergence in near-diffusive regimes. Furthermore, NanoBTE adopts a band-direction task decomposition strategy, enabling efficient MPI-based CPU parallelization and GPU acceleration of the dominant sparse transport operations.

Conclusion: He辅助溅射通过形成更开放的传感层结构、增加活性表面积，有效提升了Cu掺杂TiO₂薄膜的氢气传感性能。基于模拟支撑的生长机制认为，高能反向散射He、减弱的锤击效应（hammering effect）以及冷却相关的吸附原子迁移率（adatom mobility）抑制共同促进了纳米结构化和多孔结构形成。He辅助溅射为气体传感应用中调控氧化物薄膜提供了一条有效的物理路线。

By combining normal-angle deposition (NAD) and glancing-angle deposition (GLAD) with post-deposition annealing, the effects of He on microstructure formation and sensor performance were examined. X-ray diffraction and electron microscopy revealed that He promotes nanostructuring, lattice expansion in as-deposited NAD films, increased porosity after annealing, and a stronger anatase character in the final oxide layers. These structural changes, which enhance the reactive surface area, lead to improved hydrogen sensing at 300\,$^\circ$C in 1~vol.\,\% H$_2$. The response of NAD films increased from 1.4 to 6.0 simply by replacing part of the argon with helium, whereas GLAD films showed only a modest increase. The observed nanostructuring is discussed in terms of a simulation-supported growth scenario involving energetic backscattered He, a reduced hammering effect, and cooling-related suppression of adatom mobility, which together favour the formation of a more open sensing layer. Helium-assisted sputtering represents a useful physical route for tailoring oxide thin films for gas-sensing applications.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: We report high-pressure single-crystal X-ray diffraction measurements on the quasi-one-dimensional (Q1D) antiferromagnetic metal KMn6Bi5 up to 12.5 GPa, revealing the detailed pressure evolution of its atomic coordination environment. We find that the lattice exhibits pronounced anisotropic compressibility-the relative changes in the a and b lattice parameters reach a/a0=0.91 and b/b0 = 0.94 at 12.5 GPa-and a distinct structural anomaly emerges near 11 GPa without any symmetry-breaking. Detailed structural analysis further uncovers an anomalous hardening of the Mn nanotubes between 5 and 11 GPa, followed by a configuration optimization of the Mn/Bi nanotubes around 11 GPa. These features correlate closely with the reported pressure-temperature phase diagram of KMn6Bi5 and compare favorably with the chemical pressure effects induced by substituting K with Na, Rb, or Cs. Our findings provide key microscopic insights into how coordination environment modulation governs the stability of electronic orders in low-dimensional systems.

### [272] [Color Centers in Cubic Boron Nitride](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03322)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Cubic boron nitride (c-BN) is a wide-bandgap semiconductor (WBGS) with potential applications in both power electronics and quantum technologies. Color centers in WBGS can be used as single photon emitters and quantum sensors. Several zero phonon lines have been measured in c-BN experiment but not yet identified. To systematically probe the combinatorially complex chemical space of defects, we generate a large-scale point defect data set for c-BN. We apply density functional theory calculation implemented in a high-throughput workflow Automatic Defect Analysis and Qualification (ADAQ) to broadly screen for point defect complexes containing s- or p-elements. More than 8000 defects have been calculated in different charge and spin states. The calculated properties are stored in defect database and are then filtered to find defects with properties similar to the NV-center in diamond. More accurate calculations using hybrid functionals are then performed on a selected set of promising defects to further assess their suitability for quantum technology. In particular, we reexamined the ONVB defect which likely explains the GC-2 line. The hybrid calculations also suggest other defect candidates with bright emission, such as two carbon defects and the NaB- defect.

### [273] [Computational Determination of Optimal Growth Protocols for Metastable Polymorphs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03371)
*Simon B. Hollweger,Anna Werkovits,Tadeas Lesovsky,Oliver T. Hofmann*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 有机-无机界面（organic-inorganic interfaces）中，目标结构的可靠生长是一项核心挑战，尤其是当目标结构在热力学上处于亚稳态（metastable）时，识别能够选择性产生该给定表面结构的生长条件非常困难。

Method: 将动力学蒙特卡洛模拟与参数化成核-生长模型相结合，并应用最优控制理论，以预测能够最大化目标结构产率的生长方案（growth recipes）。

Result: 在一个有机分子吸附于金属表面的原型模型中，优化的控制轨迹（control trajectory）在相同的总协议时长内，将所需亚稳态相（metastable phase）的产率从手动优化三步协议的73%提升至97%。

Conclusion: 该研究表明，通过优化时间依赖的温度和压力协议，可以有效引导系统穿越相空间（phase space），避开有利于热力学稳定结构（thermodynamically stable structure）形成的动力学生长区间，从而实现亚稳态表面多晶型的高产率制备。

Abstract: The reliable growth of a desired target structure remains a central challenge for organic-inorganic interfaces. Specific interface structures can exhibit properties that are superior compared to those of other possible interface structures, but identifying growth conditions that selectively produce a given surface structure is difficult, particularly when the target structure is thermodynamically metastable. Here, we demonstrate how time-dependent temperature and pressure protocols can be optimized to promote the high-yield formation of a metastable surface polymorph. To this end, we combine kinetic Monte Carlo simulations with a parameterized nucleation-and-growth model and apply optimal control theory to predict growth recipes that maximize the yield of the desired target structure. Applying this approach to a prototypical model of an organic molecules adsorbed on a metal surface, we identify experimentally plausible protocols that guide the system through phase space while avoiding kinetic growth regimes in which formation of the thermodynamically stable structure is favored. Compared to a manually optimized three-step protocol, the optimized control trajectory increases the yield of the desired metastable phase from 73 % to 97 % for the same total protocol duration.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基础机器学习原子间势（foundation MLIPs）正越来越多地被用作第一性原理计算的替代方案，但在有限热力学系综中，其对结构和动力学观测量的准确性尚未得到验证，缺乏基于真实基态（ground truth）数据的系统评测。

Method: 构建 Dyna-Mat-v1.0 基准数据集，包含凝聚相第一性原理分子动力学（first-principles molecular dynamics）轨迹；对 15 个 foundation MLIPs（跨越四个模型层级）进行评测，对比单点能量与力误差，以及基于 MLIP 轨迹生成的结构和动力学观测量。

Result: 总体上，单点力误差较低的模型在结构和动力学观测量上也表现出较低误差；但存在个别系统，尽管力误差很小，预测的结构却出现定性失效。压力（pressure）在大多数模型中描述较差，表明当前大规模训练数据集中密度泛函理论（DFT）应力标签存在局限性。通过构建精度-成本帕累托前沿（accuracy-cost Pareto frontier），发现最新的跨训练模型接近帕累托最优（Pareto-optimal）。

Conclusion: Dyna-Mat-v1.0 表明，端到端（end-to-end）有限温度验证对于量化 foundation MLIPs 的预测行为至关重要，并为在静态和谐波基准之外评估它们提供了一条简单且可扩展的路径，这对材料设计具有重要参考价值。

Abstract: Foundation machine learning interatomic potentials (MLIPs) are increasingly being used as drop-in replacements for first-principles calculations, enabling simulations of materials at length and time scales that were previously inaccessible. However, due to lack of ground truth data, their accuracy on structural and dynamical observables in finite thermodynamic ensembles is yet to be established. Here, we introduce Dyna-Mat-v1.0, a benchmark dataset of condensed-phase first-principles molecular dynamics trajectories designed to test foundation MLIPs at realistic finite-temperature conditions. Using this dataset, we evaluate 15 foundation MLIPs across four model tiers by comparing both single-point energy and force errors on first-principles configurations and observables generated from MLIP-driven trajectories. We find that "on average" models with lower single-point force errors also yield lower errors for structural and dynamical observables. However, there are individual systems for which low force errors lead to qualitative failures in the predicted structure. Pressure remains poorly described across most models, pointing to limitations in the density functional theory stress labels available in current large-scale training datasets. Finally, we construct an accuracy-cost Pareto frontier to identify the best trade-offs for molecular dynamics with foundation MLIPs, finding that the latest generation of cross-trained models is close to Pareto-optimal according to the accuracy metrics considered here. Overall, Dyna-Mat-v1.0 shows that end-to-end finite-temperature validation is essential for quantifying the predictive behaviour of foundation MLIPs, and provides a simple, scalable route for assessing them beyond static and harmonic benchmarks relevant to materials design.

</details>


### [275] [From Stacking Disorder to Cubic Order: Ice Crystallization from Deeply Supercooled Water](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03465)
*Yulin Lin,Weimin Guo,Suvo Banik,Tao Zhou,Thomas E. Gage,Lei Yu,Maksim A. Sultanov,Martin Holt,Subramanian Sankaranarayanan,Peng Zhang,Ilke Arslan,Jianguo Wen*

TL;DR: 本文通过原位低温冷冻电镜（cryogenic TEM）直接观测深过冷水分子尺度结晶过程，发现均相成核产生堆垛无序冰，其中立方冰初始仅以孤立单层存在，其逐渐增厚是结晶的关键动力学机制。增厚过程中，纳米级无缺陷立方冰晶种在无序晶格基面上成核，以晶面匹配方式诱导孪晶并逐级倍增生长分支，最终可重复地生成具有全局立方（八面体）对称性的八分支枝晶，尽管每个分支仍高度堆垛无序。后期潜热释放驱动热力学上更稳定的六方相转变，但预先建立的全局立方对称性得以保留。研究揭示了强动力学驱动力如何将微观无序转化为涌现的宏观对称性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 远离平衡态结晶（crystallization far from equilibrium）可产生违背经典晶体习性的形貌，但连接原子尺度无序与涌现宏观有序（emergent macroscopic order）的微观机制尚不明确。该工作旨在通过分子分辨率的直接观测来揭示这一机制。

Method: 采用原位低温冷冻透射电镜（in situ cryogenic transmission electron microscopy）结合膜封装微滴平台（membrane-encapsulated microdroplet platform），在分子分辨率下直接可视化深过冷水（deeply supercooled water）的冻结过程。

Result: 均相成核产生由六方序列和立方序列混合而成的堆垛无序冰（stacking-disordered ice）；立方冰初始仅以孤立单层存在，其逐渐增厚成为调控整个结晶路径的关键动力学机制；增厚过程中纳米级无缺陷立方冰晶种在无序晶格基面上成核并以晶面匹配方式诱导立方孪晶（cubic twinning）和生长分支的逐级倍增；该动力学途径可重复生成具有全局立方对称性的八分支枝晶；后期潜热释放驱动向六方相（hexagonal phase）转变，但预先建立的全局立方对称性得以保留。

Conclusion: 结果表明强动力学驱动力可将微观无序转化为涌现的宏观对称性，为理解和控制远离平衡态的快速结晶过程提供了一个通用框架。

Abstract: Crystallization far from equilibrium can generate morphologies that defy classical crystal habits, yet the microscopic mechanisms linking atomic-scale disorder to emergent macroscopic order remain elusive. Here we use in situ cryogenic transmission electron microscopy with a membrane-encapsulated microdroplet platform to directly visualize the freezing of deeply supercooled water at molecular resolution. We show that homogeneous nucleation produces stacking-disordered ice composed of mixed hexagonal and cubic sequences, in which cubic ice initially exists only as isolated monolayers. The gradual thickening of these cubic layers constitutes the key kinetic mechanism that governs the entire crystallization pathway. As thickening proceeds, nanoscale, defect-free cubic ice germs nucleate on the basal planes of the disordered lattice. These faceted cubic germs act as facet-registered kinetic seeds that enforce cubic twinning and sequentially multiply growth branches. This kinetic pathway reproducibly generates robust eight-branched dendrites with global cubic (octahedral) symmetry, even though each branch remains highly stacking-disordered. At later stages, latent heat release drives a crossover to the thermodynamically favored hexagonal phase; remarkably, the pre-established global cubic symmetry is retained. These results reveal how strong kinetic driving forces convert microscopic disorder into emergent macroscopic symmetry, providing a general framework for understanding and controlling rapid crystallization far from equilibrium.

Abstract: Metal-insulator-transition (MIT) materials are promising candidates for switchable electronics, neuromorphic hardware, and reconfigurable photonics, yet experimentally verified examples remain limited and the underlying mechanisms are often complex. We argue that generative AI for MIT discovery should move beyond the search for stable crystal structures alone and instead prioritize mechanism-informed phase-transition hypotheses. A modular physics-adapted framework, combined with staged verification of phase competition, electronic contrast, transition-pathway plausibility, and control accessibility, can guide credible discovery under severe label scarcity.

Abstract: The continued scaling of ferroelectric devices is critical for next-generation computing architectures, yet it is fundamentally challenged by a metrological bottleneck: at the deep sub-micrometer scale, intrinsic material properties are heavily masked by extrinsic parasitic impedances and geometric fringing fields. Here, we introduce a quantitative, in-situ nanoprobing framework capable of resolving the true electrical response of ferroelectric capacitors down to 165 nm in diameter without the need for lithographic bond pads. Using 20 nm thick AlScN as a model system, we establish a non-linear 'Screened Power Law' model to decouple attofarad-level device capacitances from massive near-field probe interactions. Furthermore, we demonstrate that the apparent degradation of dielectric loss at the nanoscale is a geometric dilution artifact, which we overcome through a conductance scaling analysis. Finally, we apply this framework to large-signal characterization, utilizing leakage-compensation and noise filtering protocols to extract pristine intrinsic hysteresis (C-V and J-E) loops in the discrete few-grain limit. These findings provide a universal analytical toolkit required to overcome the measurement limits of deep-submicron ferroelectrics.

### [278] [Correlated-Electron Theory of Triplet-Triplet Multiexciton States in Polypentacene](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03706)
*Rupali Jindal,Alok Shukla,Sumit Mazumdar*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文基于多体电子结构计算，研究了并五苯低聚物中光学自旋单重态和三重态-三重态多激子态，发现1(T1T1)本征态构成一个窄的、近乎简并的能量窗口，且每个三重态-三重态本征态是所有可能的三重态间距构型的量子叠加，而非局域化的单个三重态对构型。这一电子结构解释了并五苯低聚物、多聚并五苯和多聚并四苯溶液中观察不到分子内三重态扩散的原因，同时保留了对具有显著链间相互作用的薄膜中分子间单重态裂变的可能性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用Pariser-Parr-Pople哈密顿量（Pariser-Parr-Pople Hamiltonian）、多参考单双激发组态相互作用（multiple-reference singles and doubles configuration interaction）以及分子激子基（molecular exciton basis），在实空间中将Frenkel激子、电荷转移（charge-transfer）和三重态对（T1T1）构型分解开来，对三单元和四单元并五苯低聚物进行关联电子计算。

Result: 所有1(T1T1)本征态存在于一个靠近最低光学激子的窄而近乎简并的能量窗口内；没有任何本征态可被识别为单一的局域化三重态对构型；每个三重态对本征态是所有可达的三重态间距构型的量子叠加（quantum superposition）。

Conclusion: 该电子结构解释了并五苯低聚物、多聚并五苯和多聚并四苯溶液中分子内三重态扩散（intramolecular triplet diffusion）不可观测的原因，同时指出在具有显著链间相互作用的薄膜中，分子间单重态裂变仍有可能发生。

Abstract: We present correlated-electron calculations of optical spin-singlet and triplet-triplet multiexciton states in three- and four-unit pentacene oligomers as microscopic models for polypentacene. The calculations use the Pariser-Parr-Pople Hamiltonian, multiple-reference singles and doubles configuration interaction, and a molecular exciton basis that resolves Frenkel, charge-transfer, and triplet-pair (T1T1) configurations in real space. We find that the complete set of 1(T1T1) eigenstates lies in a narrow, nearly degenerate energy window near the lowest optical exciton and that no eigenstate can be identified with a single localized triplet-pair configuration. Instead, each triplet-pair eigenstate is a quantum superposition of configurations containing all accessible intertriplet separations. This electronic structure explains the perceived absence of intramolecular triplet diffusion in pentacene oligomers, polypentacene, and polytetracene solutions, while leaving open the possibility of intermolecular singlet fission in films with appreciable interchain interactions.

### [279] [Janus MgAlB_2 MBene: a dipole-engineered anode for ultrafast Li-ion transport and exceptional lithium storage](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03823)
*Pritam Samanta,Sashank Kumar Pandey,Amit Kumar Jana,Prakash Parida*

Abstract: In this work, we propose a group II/IIIA-based Janus MBene, MgAlB_2, and investigate its electrochemical properties using first-principles calculations. The substitution of one Mg layer in Mg_2B_2 MBene by an Al layer breaks the structural symmetry and generates a permanent out-of-plane polarization, giving rise to a distinct electronic environment compared with the parent Mg_2B_2 and Al_2B_2 monolayers. Electronic-structure analysis reveals enhanced orbital hybridization among B, Mg, and Al states near the Fermi level, resulting in improved electronic delocalization across the monolayer. The Janus MgAlB_2 monolayer is found to possess excellent dynamical, mechanical, and thermal stability. Owing to its polarization-modified energy landscape, Li ions migrate with an exceptionally low diffusion barrier of 17.1 meV, corresponding to a room-temperature diffusion coefficient of 3.43x10^-10 cm^2/s. Unlike the pristine Mg_2B_2 and Al_2B_2 monolayers, which support only a single stable adsorption layer, MgAlB_2 accommodates two complete Li layers. Detailed analysis shows that the residual polarization retained after first-layer lithiation continues to promote Li adsorption, whereas increasing Li-Li electrostatic interactions eventually limit further storage. As a result, the Janus monolayer delivers a high theoretical specific capacity of 1470.24 mAh/g together with a small volume expansion of only 3.7% during maximum lithiation. The present study demonstrates that intrinsic polarization can be utilized to regulate both the thermodynamics and kinetics of Li storage, providing a design strategy for high-rate and high-capacity two-dimensional electrode materials.

The optical response exhibits pronounced polarization dependence. Result: 模拟预测 BiAlO₃ 具有菱方铁电（rhombohedral ferroelectric, R3c）基态，由顺电立方相（cubic, Pm3̄m）经结构相变形成。室温自发极化（spontaneous polarization）为 81 μC/cm²（沿 [111] 方向），居里温度（Curie temperature）为 1160 K。铁电模式与反铁畸变（antiferrodistortive）模式在广泛的温度与电场范围内存在强耦合。静水压抑制自发极化和居里温度，而单轴和双轴应力均可诱导多级相变。

Conclusion: 该第一性原理原子模型能准确描述 BiAlO₃ 在实验相关条件下的关键性质，揭示了铁电与反铁畸变模式的耦合机制，以及不同应力条件对相变的调控作用，为无铅钙钛矿铁电体的设计与应用提供了理论依据。

Abstract: The lead-free perovskite ferroelectrics captivate researchers with their unique functional properties leading to important technological applications. In the search for a new lead-free perovskite of technological importance, we develop a first-principles based atomistic model to accurately predict the properties of BiAlO$_3$ in experimentally relevant conditions. Consistent with the experimental observations, our simulations predict a rhombohedral ferroelectric ($R3c$) ground state for BiAlO$_3$ facilitated by a structural phase transition from paraelectric (cubic, $Pm\Bar{3}m$) phase. The room-temperature spontaneous polarization and Curie temperature are obtained to be 81 $μ$C/cm$^2$ (along [111] direction) and 1160 K, respectively. Our simulations reveal strong coupling between ferroelectric and antiferrodistortive modes for a broad spectrum of temperature and electric field. We find that hydrostatic pressure suppresses both spontaneous polarization and Curie temperature, while both uniaxial and biaxial stresses induce multiple phase transitions in BiAlO$_3$.

### [282] [Morphology-Property Interplay in Chemo-Mechanics of Ion-Intercalation Active Particles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03893)
*Rongyue Lin,Royal C. Ihuaenyi,Juner Zhu,Ruobing Bai*

Method: 建立热力学一致的单粒子框架（thermodynamically consistent single-particle framework），结合解析解与多物理场模拟（multiphysics simulations），研究空心球形、圆柱形和椭球形颗粒在多种约束边界条件下的锂化与应力生成。采用通量分解分析（flux decomposition analysis）、相关性分析（correlation analysis）以及贝叶斯优化（Bayesian optimization）进行系统研究。

Abstract: Morphology, material property, and mechanical constraint jointly govern the chemo-mechanical behavior of ion-intercalation particles, yet their coupled effects remain insufficiently understood. Here we establish a thermodynamically consistent single-particle framework and combine analytical solutions with multiphysics simulations to determine how these factors regulate lithiation and stress generation. We study hollow spherical, cylindrical, and ellipsoidal particles with isotropic or transversely isotropic material properties under fully constrained, inner-free, or unconstrained boundary conditions. We show that the transient lithiation pathway and the associated stress and strain fields are governed not by morphology, property, or constraint alone, but by their coupled interaction: isotropic particles are sensitive to the mechanical constraint, whereas transversely isotropic particles exhibit persistent heterogeneous lithiation dominated by anisotropic diffusivity. Flux decomposition analysis reveals that the mechanical contribution to Li flux is negligible in spheres but dominant in ellipsoids. Correlation analysis further shows that Li concentration and volumetric strain exhibit strong anti-correlation in unconstrained particles but weak correlation under full constraints. Bayesian optimization of hollow ellipsoids identifies Pareto-optimal morphologies that balance lithiation capacity against peak tensile stress. These results provide a unified framework for the morphology-property interplay in intercalation particles and offer morphology design principles for chemo-mechanical stability.

### [283] [Surface Functionalization Enables Two-Dimensional Altermagnetism and Giant Tunnel Magnetoresistance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03908)
*Zhou Cui,Ziye Zhu,Bowen Hao,Xunkai Duan,Xuan Zhou,Yali Xie,Huali Yang,Baisheng Sa,Runwei Li,Tong Zhou*

TL;DR: 本文提出通过表面官能化（surface functionalization）作为一种对称性引导的非易失性化学开关，将已知的二维反铁磁体（AFM）转化为交错磁体（altermagnet, AM），并以单层FeSe为例，通过第一性原理计算和输运模拟验证了该策略的有效性，实现了高达1.87×10³%的隧穿磁电阻（TMR）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二维交错磁体（2D altermagnets）兼具补偿磁序、动量依赖的自旋分裂以及原子级薄材料的可扩展性与界面兼容性，在超快、无杂散场自旋电子学（spintronics）中极具潜力，但实际可用的二维AM材料仍然稀缺。因此，亟需一种不依赖搜索本征二维AM的新途径，通过对称性工程将已知的二维反铁磁体（AFM）转化为AM。

Method: 采用对称性引导的表面官能化（surface functionalization）方法，通过单侧官能化打破反演对称性（inversion symmetry）和面外镜面对称性（out-of-plane mirror symmetry），同时保持连接相反自旋子晶格的旋转对称性（rotation symmetry），从而实现反铁磁到交错磁的转变。以单层FeSe为平台，通过第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）研究氢化、氧化和氟化的效果，并在器件层面进行自旋输运模拟。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了一条从对称性到化学再到器件的策略（symmetry-to-chemistry-to-device strategy），用于工程化二维交错磁体并开发高性能交错磁自旋电子学器件。表面化学为调控交错磁输运提供了一种有效的控制手段。

Abstract: Two-dimensional (2D) altermagnets (AMs) are highly desirable for ultrafast, stray-field-free spintronics because they combine compensated magnetic order and momentum-dependent spin splitting with the scalability, tunability, and interface compatibility of atomically thin materials. However, practical 2D AMs remain scarce. Rather than relying solely on the search for intrinsic 2D AMs, an appealing route is to transform known 2D antiferromagnets (AFMs) into AMs through symmetry engineering. Here, we propose surface functionalization as a symmetry-guided, nonvolatile chemical switch for realizing this AFM-to-AM transformation. By breaking inversion and out-of-plane mirror symmetries while preserving the rotation symmetry connecting opposite-spin sublattices, single-sided functionalization lifts spin degeneracy and induces altermagnetic spin splitting. Using monolayer FeSe as a representative platform, first-principles calculations show that hydrogenation, oxidation, and fluorination convert spin-degenerate antiferromagnetic FeSe into a d-wave AM with pronounced momentum-dependent spin splitting. At the device level, our transport simulations reveal that the functionalized FeSe monolayer magnetic tunnel junctions exhibit giant tunnel magnetoresistance (TMR) up to $1.87\times10^3\%$, originating from momentum-selective spin filtering between parallel and antiparallel Néel-vector configurations. The strong dependence of TMR on functionalization geometry further demonstrates that surface chemistry provides an effective control knob for altermagnetic transport. Our work establishes a symmetry-to-chemistry-to-device strategy for engineering 2D AMs and developing high-performance altermagnetic spintronic devices.

Method: 通过理论分析狄拉克点附近激发的杂质修饰（dressing of impurities）过程，研究新型准粒子——狄拉克-费米极化子的形成机制及其光谱特征。

Conclusion: 极化子谱学（polaron spectroscopy）可作为探测远离费米面能级的狄拉克点的有力工具，为传统方法无法触及的能带结构效应提供直接观测途径。

Abstract: We investigate band-structure effects on the absorption spectra of quantum impurities in Dirac materials. These quasiparticles are remarkably robust, persisting for both attractive and repulsive interactions, and across the full range of electron and hole doping. We show that their spectroscopic signature is a generic feature of Dirac materials, accessible with established techniques in both solid-state and ultracold atomic platforms. Our results establish polaron spectroscopy as a powerful probe of Dirac points at energies far from the Fermi surface, providing direct access to band-structure effects beyond conventional approaches.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 结合同步辐射X射线衍射（synchrotron X-ray diffraction）、密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）和分子动力学（molecular dynamics, MD）计算，对AgSbTe₂在60 GPa以内的高压结构行为进行详细研究。

Result: 发现从环境相的R-3m结构经一个扩展的中间非晶态（intermediate amorphous state）转变为完全无序的立方Im3m相；焓计算表明R-3m与Im3m在宽压力范围内近乎简并，从而驱动非晶化；非晶化并非由先前推测的阳离子空位引起，而是由Te亚晶格的显著位移不稳定性（displacement instability）主导；减压路径的时间依赖性控制最终结构态，慢速减压得到非晶态，快速减压得到完全晶态，表现出反直觉的动力学效应。

Conclusion: AgSbTe₂的压力诱导非晶化源于Te亚晶格位移不稳定性及R-3m与Im3m相之间的近简并，且减压动力学而非热力学平衡决定最终结构，揭示了强反直觉动力学效应在结构调控中的关键作用。

Abstract: Pressure provides a powerful thermodynamic route to access hidden structural states in functional materials, yet the microscopic origin of pressure-induced amorphization remains elusive in many complex chalcogenides. Here we report a detailed high-pressure structural study of AgSbTe2,combining synchrotron X-ray diffraction with density functional theory and molecular dynamics calculations up to 60 GPa. We uncover a pressure-driven transformation from the ambient R-3m phase to a fully disordered cubic Im3m phase, through an extended intermediate amorphous state. Enthalpy calculations reveal a near-degeneracy between the R3m and Im3m structures over a broad pressure range, dictating amorphization. Contrary to previously speculated cation vacancies, the amorphization is governed by a pronounced displacement instability of the Te sublattice. Remarkably, the time dependent decompression pathway controls the final structural state, resulting in either amorphous (slow decompression) or fully crystalline (fast decompression) states, indicative of a strong counterintuitive kinetic effect.

### [287] [First-principles Floquet analysis from real-time propagation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04269)
*Ruipeng Li,Benshu Fan,Umberto De Giovannini,Hannes Hübener,Angel Rubio*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出一种实时Floquet分析方法，通过从传播波函数重构单周期演化算子来提取准能量和Floquet态，避免了显式构建扩展Floquet哈密顿量，并引入展开程序解决约化能带表征的模糊性。该方法在从二维单层到三维块体半导体的第一性原理含时模拟中得到验证，适用于非严格周期性的有限脉冲，可直接连接实时模拟与Floquet可观测量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统Floquet方法需要显式构建扩展Floquet哈密顿量（enlarged Floquet Hamiltonian），计算开销大；同时约化Floquet布里渊区（reduced Floquet Brillouin zone）中的能带表征存在模糊性，难以恢复平衡态的能带特征。本文旨在发展一种轻量级、普适的分析方法，直接从实时波函数演化中提取Floquet信息。

Method: 通过重叠积分（overlaps）重构时间演化状态间的单周期演化算子（one-period evolution operator），从而获得准能量（quasi-energies）和Floquet态（Floquet states），避免显式构建扩展Floquet哈密顿量。为消除约化能带表征的歧义，引入基于Floquet态谐波分解（harmonic decomposition）的展开程序（unfolding procedure），恢复平衡态能带特征。重构的波函数还可提供光诱导边带（light-induced sidebands）的对称性信息。

Result: 该方法在第一性原理含时模拟中成功应用于多种真实材料体系，包括二维单层材料和三维块体半导体。对于非严格周期性（non-strictly time-periodic）的有限脉冲（finite pulses）情况，该方法同样适用。

Conclusion: 该框架将实时模拟与Floquet可观测量直接连接，为分析材料中光驱动电子结构（light-driven electronic structure）提供了实用的分析工具。

Abstract: We present a real-time Floquet analysis method for extracting quasi-energies and Floquet states directly from propagated wavefunctions. By reconstructing the one-period evolution operator from overlaps between time-evolved states, the method avoids the explicit construction of the enlarged Floquet Hamiltonian and adds negligible computational overhead to time-dependent simulations. To resolve the ambiguity inherent in the reduced-zone representation, we introduce an unfolding procedure based on the harmonic decomposition of Floquet states, which recovers their underlying equilibrium band character beyond the reduced Floquet Brillouin zone. The reconstructed wavefunctions further provide access to the symmetry properties of individual light-induced sidebands. We demonstrate the applicability and generality of the method in first-principles time-dependent simulations of real materials, ranging from two-dimensional monolayers to a three-dimensional bulk semiconductor, and including finite pulses without strict time periodicity. This framework directly connects real-time simulations with Floquet observables, enabling practical analysis of light-driven electronic structure in materials.

### [288] [Data-Driven Prediction of NaCl-Type Entropy-Stabilized Oxide Compositions from First-Principles and Supervised Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04502)
*Sebastien Junier,Celine Barreteau,David Berardan,Yann-Andrev Kerneur,Jean-Claude Crivello*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文开发了一种高通量计算框架，结合密度泛函理论（DFT）、特殊准随机结构（SQS）、凸包热力学和机器学习，用于筛选等摩尔五元NaCl型熵稳定氧化物（ESO），仅需对约10%的五元体系进行显式DFT计算即可预测全部4368种候选组成的稳定性。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 该框架为数据驱动的多组分氧化物探索建立了一条高效途径，并为实验发现新的ESO提供了实用指导。

Abstract: Entropy-stabilized oxides (ESOs) open access to vast multicomponent compositional spaces, but identifying promising candidates remains challenging because of the large number of possible mixtures and the need to assess their stability against competing phases. In this work, we develop a high-throughput computational framework to screen equimolar quinary ESOs in the NaCl structure type by combining density functional theory (DFT), special quasirandom structures (SQS), convex-hull thermodynamics, and supervised machine learning. A consistent reference database of binary and ternary ordered oxides, including disordered phases such as all binary cation combinations in the NaCl-type oxide, is first constructed using GGA and meta-GGA calculations. Quinary disordered phases are then described by SQS supercells and used to train machine-learning models that predict the distance to the convex hull and the corresponding stabilization temperature over the full set of 4368 possible equimolar quinary compositions generated from 16 cation species. Among the tested models, an optimized multilayer perceptron provides the best predictive performance, with a test error of about 4 kJ/mol, while requiring explicit DFT calculations for only about 10% of the quinary systems. Comparison with experimental synthesis tests and computed decomposition paths further shows that the approach captures the main stability trends and the dominant competing phases, although absolute stabilization temperatures remain affected by systematic thermodynamic approximations. These results establish an efficient route for the data-driven exploration of multicomponent oxides and provide practical guidance for the experimental search for new ESOs.

### [289] [VASP Plugins: Linking the Vienna ab-initio Simulation Package with Python](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04622)
*Sudarshan Vijay,Martijn Marsman,Georg Kresse,Martin Schlipf*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将新特征和实验性算法集成到广泛使用的密度泛函理论（DFT）代码（如VASP）中，常受限于复杂的遗留架构（legacy architectures）和Fortran等编译语言的使用，导致软件开发与快速原型设计（rapid prototyping）面临巨大障碍。

Method: 采用C++中间层（intermediate layer）和pybind11库，通过共享内存缓冲区（shared memory buffers）将VASP内部数据以NumPy数组形式暴露给Python，避免数据重复拷贝；插件分为两类：在自洽场（SCF）收敛后修改量的插件（如structure、force_and_stress），以及在SCF循环中操作的插件（如local_potential、occupancies）。

Result: 通过三个应用案例验证了该基础设施的实用性：使用scipy库进行结构弛豫（structure relaxation）、实现隐式溶剂模型（implicit solvent model）、以及添加DFT-D4色散修正（dispersion corrections）。

Abstract: Implementing novel features and experimental algorithms into widely adopted density functional theory (DFT) codes is frequently hindered by complex legacy architectures and the use of compiled languages such as Fortran. These production codes, while optimised for high-performance computing clusters, present significant hurdles for software development and rapid prototyping, often requiring deep expertise in the code's internal structure to modify. To address this challenge, we present a Python plugin infrastructure for the Vienna ab-initio Simulation Package (VASP) that combines computational efficiency with the flexibility of high-level scripting. Our architecture uses a C++ intermediate layer and pybind11 to expose VASP data as NumPy arrays via shared memory buffers, ensuring high performance without data duplication. We implement two categories of plugins: those that modify quantities at the end of each converged self-consistent field (SCF) cycle, such as structure and force_and_stress, and those that operate during the SCF cycle, such as local_potential and occupancies. We demonstrate the utility of our implementation through three applications, structure relaxation using the scipy library, implementing an implicit solvent model, and adding the DFT-D4 dispersion corrections. This infrastructure effectively bridges the gap between high-performance electronic structure routines and the widespread scientific Python ecosystem.

Abstract: This study investigates the structural, electronic, mechanical, optical, thermodynamic, and superconducting properties of ZrRuAs and HfRuP. ### [291] [Chiral Phonons Coupled to Spin-Split Bands in Altermagnetic CrSb and MnTe](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04802)
*Armando Consiglio,Maximilian Ünzelmann,Giancarlo Panaccione,Domenico Di Sante*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过第一性原理计算，证明原型交错磁体（altermagnets）CrSb和MnTe中存在具有有限声子角动量（phonon angular momentum）的局域手性声子模（locally chiral phonon modes），其动量空间呈六瓣f波纹理。手性晶格运动与交错磁自旋分裂分别源于不同原子子晶格，并可通过等电子化学替代调控，同时揭示手性声子与动量依赖的自旋分裂电子带之间存在耦合，为手性声子学（chiral phononics）和自旋选择性晶格控制提供了新平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 交错磁体同时具有磁有序、电子结构和晶格动力学之间的交织，但手性晶格动力学与交错磁电子态之间的关联尚未明确，本文旨在揭示二者在微观层面的起源及相互作用。

Method: 采用第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations），针对原型交错磁体CrSb和MnTe，分析其声子模式的手性特征、声子角动量的动量空间分布，并通过等电子化学替代研究对称性降低对声子手性的影响。

Result: 发现CrSb和MnTe中存在局域手性声子模式，动量空间呈现六瓣f波纹理；手性晶格运动源自pnictogen/chalcogen子晶格，自旋分裂由磁性过渡金属原子贡献；原始化合物中各谷的声子角动量因反演对称性（inversion symmetry）相互抵消，而等电子替代可解除抵消并产生有限谷声子手性；手性声子与动量依赖的自旋分裂电子带通过动量依赖的电子-声子相互作用耦合，导致电子结构特征性修正。

Conclusion: 本文确立了交错磁体作为手性声子学和自旋选择性晶格控制的理想平台，为未来通过光发射实验探测手性声子-电子耦合效应提供了理论依据。

Abstract: Altermagnets exhibit momentum-dependent spin splitting without net magnetization, providing a unique platform where magnetic order, electronic structure and lattice dynamics intertwine. Here, using first-principles calculations, we demonstrate that the prototypical altermagnets CrSb and MnTe host locally chiral phonon modes carrying finite phonon angular momentum with a six-lobes $f$-wave texture in momentum space. Our results show that the chiral lattice motion originates from the pnictogen/chalcogen sublattice, while the altermagnetic spin splitting is generated by the magnetic transition-metal atoms, indicating that chiral lattice dynamics and altermagnetic electronic states originate from different atomic sublattices of the same crystal. In pristine compounds, at each valley, inversion symmetry suppresses the net phonon angular momentum despite local circular atomic motion. We further demonstrate that isoelectronic symmetry lowering induced by chemical substitution lifts this cancellation and generates finite valley phonon chirality, while keeping the altermagnetic nature of the compounds intact. Most importantly, we reveal that chiral phonons couple to momentum-dependent spin-split electronic bands through momentum-dependent electron-phonon interaction, producing characteristic modifications of the electronic structure, possibly accessible by photoemission experiments. Our results establish altermagnets as a promising platform for chiral phononics and spin-selective lattice control.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 受限空间中的水合物形成受毛细作用和组成主导，而非动力学历史；吉布斯-汤姆逊关系可定量关联微观晶粒尺寸与熔点偏移，为理解受限条件下水合物与冰晶的竞争提供了统一框架。

Abstract: Tetrahydrofuran (THF) is a benchmark guest for probing clathrate hydrate thermodynamics because a stoichiometric aqueous solution (THF.17H2O) forms structure-II (sII) hydrate at ambient pressure with a well-defined dissociation temperature. Here, we combine differential scanning calorimetry (DSC) and wide-angle X-ray scattering (WAXS) in bulk and confined media to resolve how composition, pore filling, and cooling rate govern hydrate formation in SBA-15 mesoporous silica. In confinement, the heating traces separate into a Gibbs-Thomson depressed ice melt (= -14.7 $\pm$ 0.2 {\textdegree}C), an in-pore hydrate dissociation (= -13.2 $\pm$ 0.2 {\textdegree}C). Confined hydrate appears only when two criteria are met: near-percolating filling ($φ$ = 1.0 -1.1 cm3/g) and sufficient THF ($\ge$ 1:16 mol:mol). Cooling-rate experiments (1.0 vs 0.5 {\textdegree}C/min) demonstrate that slower precooling increases the confined-hydrate fraction and reduces confined ice without shifting equilibrium temperatures: at $φ$ = 1.1, the hydrate enthalpy rises by ~60% at 1:11 and ~54% at 1:14, but by $\le$ 17% at 1:16. Temperature-cycling tests show invariant reheating peak positions, indicating that capillarity and composition, rather than kinetic history, fix the liquidus and dissociation temperatures. WAXS indicates that the phase formed in pores is crystallographically identical to bulk sII. Finally, the variation of melting points ($Δ$T___) plotted against inverse pore radius follows the Gibbs-Thomson law for both ice melting and hydrate dissociation, quantitatively linking the observed shifts to crystalline size and clarifying how confinement, cooling rate, and composition govern the competition between hydrate formation and water crystallization.

### [293] [Glassy Dynamics of LiCl.6H2O Solution in Nanoporous Media](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04817)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 限域在从玻璃态到液态的多个时间尺度上显著改变了LiCl·6H₂O的动力学，导致更慢、空间受限且更具异质性的运动，但并未破坏其玻璃形成性质。

Abstract: Understanding how nanoconfinement alters the dynamics of glass-forming aqueous electrolytes is essential for clarifying the interplay among ionic hydration, hydrogen-bond structure, and interfacial effects. Here, LiCl.6H2O was investigated in the bulk and under confinement in SBA-15 mesoporous silica with an average pore diameter of 8 nm. Differential scanning calorimetry, Raman spectroscopy, quasielastic neutron scattering, 1 H spin-lattice relaxation, and pulsed-fieldgradient NMR were combined to probe thermal behavior, hydrogen-bond structure, local mobility, and translational transport over complementary time and length scales. The calorimetric results show that LiCl.6H2O remains glass-forming under confinement, while its thermal signature of the glass transition becomes slightly broader and shifted upward relative to the bulk. Raman spectra in the O-H stretching region indicate that the concentrated LiCl solution possesses a weakened and less tetrahedrally connected hydrogen-bond network compared with bulk water. On the subnanosecond timescale, elastic fixed-window analysis reveals reduced mean-squared displacements under confinement, demonstrating suppressed motional amplitudes inside the pores. Inelastic fixed-window neutron scattering scans analyzed within a jump-diffusion framework yield lower effective translational diffusion coefficients and longer residence times for the confined liquid, indicating that confinement mainly hinders translational escape from transient local environments.  1 H relaxometry further shows that confinement broadens the distribution of local proton fluctuation times, while PFG-NMR confirms that the measured long-range water mobility in bulk LiCl.6H2O solution is reduced relative to bulk water. While the present data do not resolve distinct interfacial and pore-centered populations in confined LiCl.6H2O, its dynamics are markedly altered across timescales, from the glassy to the liquid state, resulting in slower, spatially constrained, and more heterogeneous motions.

### [294] [Disentangling Electronic and Lattice Contributions to Transient Absorption in Metal Halide Perovskites: A First-Principles Study of CH3NH3PbBr3](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04840)
*Lu Qiao,Ronaldo Rodrigues Pela,Claudia Draxl*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文发展了一种结合非平衡Bethe-Salpeter方程与第一性原理分子动力学的计算方法，系统分离了金属卤化物钙钛矿中瞬态吸收光谱的电子与热晶格贡献，揭示了飞秒至皮秒时间尺度上不同的主导机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 金属卤化物钙钛矿中软晶格与强电子-声子耦合导致电子与晶格自由度间存在复杂相互作用，从而增加了时间分辨激发光谱（如泵浦-探测光谱）的解释难度，亟需一种能定量解析其物理起源的理论方法。

Method: 提出一种第一性原理方法，将Bethe-Salpeter方程（Bethe-Salpeter equation, BSE）的非平衡拓展与第一性原理分子动力学（ab initio molecular dynamics）相结合，以实现飞秒至皮秒时间尺度上电子与热晶格贡献的定量分离。

Result: 以CH3NH3PbBr3为例发现：飞秒尺度下，X射线与光学瞬态吸收光谱主要由电子贡献主导——光致库仑屏蔽（Coulomb screening）削弱有效电子-空穴相互作用并使激子共振蓝移，而泡利阻塞（Pauli blocking）可忽略；皮秒尺度下，热晶格贡献成为关键，晶格振动主导X射线瞬态吸收谱的谱重分布，晶格膨胀则使光学瞬态吸收谱蓝移。

Conclusion: 该第一性原理方法能有效定量分离不同时间尺度下瞬态吸收光谱中的电子与晶格贡献，为理解金属卤化物钙钛矿中复杂的电子-晶格耦合动力学提供了理论工具。

Abstract: Soft lattices combined with strong electron-phonon coupling in metal halide perovskites result in a complex interplay between electronic and lattice degrees of freedom. This interplay complicates the interpretation of time-resolved excitation spectra like pump-probe spectra. Here, we develop a first-principles approach that combines a nonequilibrium extension of the Bethe-Salpeter equation with \textit{ab initio} molecular dynamics to resolve the origin of transient absorption. This approach can quantitatively disentangle electronic and thermal lattice contributions across femtosecond-to-picosecond timescales. Exemplified with \ce{CH3NH3PbBr3}, we find that on the femtosecond scale, both X-ray and optical transient absorption spectra are dominated by electronic contributions: Photoinduced Coulomb screening weakens the effective electron-hole interaction and blueshifts the excitonic resonances, whereas Pauli blocking is negligible. On the picosecond scale, thermal lattice contributions become essential, with distinct mechanisms dominating different spectral regions: Lattice vibrations lead to spectral redistribution in the X-ray transient absorption spectrum, whereas lattice expansion blueshifts the optical transient absorption spectrum.

Motivation: 探究不同离子半径的三价掺杂阳离子（Ga³⁺和In³⁺）对M型钡铁氧体（BaFe12O19）的磁学、介电及磁介电（magnetodielectric, MD）性质的影响机制，以理解结构与物性之间的关联。

Method: 采用固相反应法（solid-state reaction method）制备BaFe12-xMexO19（Me=Ga, In）陶瓷样品，并通过系统测量不同掺杂条件下的磁学、介电及MD性质进行分析。

Result: 小半径Ga³⁺优先取代FeO6八面体中的Fe³⁺，大半径In³⁺倾向于取代R块中FeO5双锥体中的Fe³⁺；Ga掺杂样品在10-300 K范围内保持亚铁磁性（ferrimagnetism），In掺杂样品呈现从非共线磁序（non-collinear magnetism）到共线亚铁磁性的转变；介电特性方面，纯样品的介电下降源于量子顺电态（quantum paraelectric state），Ga掺杂样品的介电峰归因于偶极玻璃态（dipole glass state），In掺杂样品的介电变化由低温电子跳跃（electron hopping）主导；高温介电性质均归因于Maxwell-Wagner效应（Maxwell-Wagner effect）引起的界面极化（interfacial polarization）；MD效应的低温起源因掺杂而异，包括自旋-声子耦合（spin-phonon coupling）、场致电子跳跃及场致非共线自旋有序等。

Conclusion: 不同离子半径的掺杂阳离子通过优先占据特定晶格位，显著改变了BaFe12O19陶瓷的磁序类型、介电弛豫行为及MD效应的微观机制，为调控多铁性（multiferroic）材料性能提供了结构设计依据。

Abstract: We systematically investigated the magnetic, dielectric, and MD properties of BaFe12-xMexO19 ceramics prepared by a solid-state reaction method. The Ga3+ cations with a smaller radius preferentially substitute the Fe3+ ions in FeO6 octahedra while the In3+ cations with a larger radius tend to replace the Fe3+ ions in FeO5 bipyramids of R blocks, inducing different physical characteristics. The pure BaFe12O19 and Ga-doped samples show ferrimagnetism in the temperature range from 10 K to 300 K. The In-doped samples exhibit a transition from non-collinear magnetism to collinear ferrimagnetism. The dielectric decrease of pure BaFe12O19 at around 10-175 K is attributed to the quantum paraelectric state, and the shoulder peaks of loss at about 140-200 K are from electron hopping. The dipole glass state is responsible for the dielectric peak of Ga-doped samples at around 20-40 K. The dielectric increase and plateau of In-doped samples are mainly ascribed to the electron hopping at low temperatures. Their dielectric properties at high temperatures are all attributed to the interfacial polarization caused by the Maxwell-Wagner effect. The MD effect also has different origins for the various samples at low temperatures. For the pure BaFe12O19, the negative MD effect at extremely low temperatures and the positive MD effect after warming are ascribed to spin-phonon coupling and field-dependent electron hopping, respectively. The positive MD effect in Ga-doped hexaferrites results from the field-dependent electric dipoles inside FeO5 bipyramids. For the In-doped samples, the negative MD effect and subsequent transformation to the positive MD effect originate from the field-dependent non-collinear spin ordering and electron hopping, respectively. The MD effect at high temperatures is attributed to the combination of magnetoresistance and Maxwell-Wagner effects.

</details>


### [296] [A Distributional Framework for Generative Modeling of Molecular Crystals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05266)
*Michael Kilgour,Alex Dong,Mark E. Tuckerman,Jutta Rogal*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出 MXtalGFlow 框架，通过规范参数化（canonical parameterization）和能量基生成流网络（energy-based generative flow networks, GFlowNets）对分子晶体的玻尔兹曼分布（Boltzmann distribution）进行近似采样，从而获得具有热力学意义的晶体结构分布，并识别出具有竞争概率的未报道堆积模式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 分子晶体具有高度多晶型性（polymorphic），同一分子常以多种堆积模式结晶，使得结构与性质预测极具挑战。现有晶体结构预测方法通常将候选结构独立处理，而非视为热力学分布中的样本；现代生成模型虽能自然采样分布，但缺乏对所采样分布的明确数学表述。

Method: 提出 MXtalGFlow 框架，包含两个核心组件：一是规范参数化（canonical parameterization），用于赋予生成分布以具体含义；二是损失函数（loss function），使生成样本与目标分布达成平衡。基于此，训练能量基生成流网络（energy-based GFlowNets）来近似目标分子和空间群下的晶体结构玻尔兹曼分布。

Result: 对两个分子分别在 Lennard-Jones 势和 Universal Model for Atoms 两种能量函数下进行采样与分析。表征了已知多晶型（polymorph）周围的局部结构盆地（local structural basins），并识别出多个尚未被报道、但与已知实验结构具有竞争概率的堆积模式。

Conclusion: MXtalGFlow 展示了如何定义并训练一个模型来采样具有热力学意义的分子晶体分布，并通过对该分布的分析提取有用信息。该框架超越了仅从低能结构中采样不连续集合的做法，为分子晶体建模提供了新的热力学分析工具。

Abstract: Molecular crystals are a highly polymorphic class of materials, with a single molecule commonly crystallizing via multiple packing patterns, making structure and property prediction very challenging. Crystal structure prediction typically comprises the production of sets of promising candidate structures, each considered in isolation rather than as samples in a thermodynamic distribution. Likewise, modern generative approaches to this problem, despite naturally sampling distributions of crystals, lack a concrete formulation of the distributions being sampled. Two components are required to impart meaning to the distributions of crystals generated under such models: a canonical parameterization, and a loss function which equilibrates the generated samples to some target distribution. We develop such a parameterization, and train energy-based generative flow networks (GFlowNets) to approximate the Boltzmann distribution over crystal structures for target molecules and space groups. Combined, these components comprise our MXtalGFlow framework for molecular crystal modeling. Going beyond sampling disconnected sets of low-energy structures, MXtalGFlow yields a thermodynamic distribution over crystal structures. We sample and analyze distributions of crystals for two molecules, each under two energy functions, a Lennard-Jones potential and the Universal Model for Atoms. We characterize the local structural basins about the known polymorphs, and identify additional as-yet un-reported packing modes with competitive probabilities to the known experimental structures. With MXtalGFlow, we illustrate how to define and train a model to sample a thermodynamically meaningful distribution of molecular crystals, and analyze such a distribution to glean useful information.

</details>


### [297] [Semiconductor nanofilms as thermal phonon polarizers: competing effects of scattering selection rules and boundary mode conversion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05296)
*Vasumathy Ravishankar,Navaneetha K. Ravichandran*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过第一性原理计算，揭示了声子散射选择规则与边界模式转换在纳米半导体薄膜中的竞争机制，该机制在低温下驱动模式极化热流（mode-polarized heat currents），并导致横向极化非平衡声子，为对称选择性工程提供了新途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已知声子散射选择规则（phonon scattering selection rules）在块体固体中调控热流，但其在纳米尺度薄膜中的作用机制尚不明确。本文旨在探索这些选择规则在纳米半导体薄膜中如何影响热传输。

Method: 采用第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations），分析纳米薄膜中声子散射选择规则与边界声子模式转换（phonon mode conversion）之间的竞争关系。

Result: 在低温（≤ 100 K）下，选择规则与边界模式转换的竞争驱动了模式极化热流。在磷化铟（indium phosphide）等材料中，基于声子支间速度差异的选择规则通过限制纵向声学（longitudinal acoustic, LA）声子的本征散射事件增强了其对热导率的贡献，而纳米薄膜中的边界模式转换则通过减少LA声子数量抑制了该贡献。

Conclusion: 纳米薄膜中产生的横向极化非平衡声子（transverse-polarized non-equilibrium phonons）使得对声子-电子、声子-应变及声子-缺陷耦合进行对称选择性工程（symmetry-selective engineering）成为可能，这在块体固体中难以实现。

Abstract: Phonon scattering selection rules are known to control heat flow through bulk solids. Here we show that these selection rules also modulate heat flow through nanoscale semiconductor films, although through a previously-unexplored mechanism. Using first-principles calculations, we expose a competition between these selection rules and phonon mode conversion at boundaries of nanoscale films, that drives mode-polarized heat currents at cryogenic temperatures ($\le$ 100 K). This polarizing effect is stronger in materials like indium phosphide, where selection rules based on large velocity differences between phonon branches amplifies the longitudinal acoustic (LA) phonon contribution to thermal conductivity by restricting their intrinsic scattering events, while boundary mode conversion in nanoscale films suppresses it by depopulating the LA phonons. The resulting transverse-polarized non-equilibrium phonons will enable symmetry-selective engineering of phonon coupling to electrons, strains and defects in nanoscale films, that is difficult to achieve in bulk solids.

</details>


### [298] [Phase-field modeling of elastically driven abnormal grain growth](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05298)
*Yazhuo Liu,Yin Zhang,Kunqing Ding,Yichen Yang,Alejandro Barrios,Xavier Maeder,Olivier Pierron,Xing Liu,Ting Zhu*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统认知中，异常晶粒生长（AGG）通常需要显著塑性变形或高温条件；然而近期实验发现，超细晶镍薄膜在室温循环加载且宏观处于弹性变形阶段时仍能发生AGG。这一现象缺乏物理机制层面的解释，亟需理论建模与模拟分析来阐明其驱动力与演化规律。

Method: 采用相场模拟（phase-field simulation）与微力学分析（micromechanical analysis）相结合的方法，对超细晶镍薄膜中取向选择性的AGG进行数值模拟，并进一步将框架推广至不同弹性各向异性（elastic anisotropy）体系以检验其普适性。

Result: 模拟表明，弹性各向异性导致的弹性能降低为取向选择性晶粒生长提供了热力学上合理的驱动力；相场模拟揭示了AGG的演化动力学，并确认局部晶粒几何与应力状态在决定生长路径中起关键作用。

Conclusion: 本研究建立了一个研究多晶材料中弹性驱动的异常晶粒生长（elastically driven AGG）的通用方法，为理解和预测晶粒粗化行为提供了理论工具。

Abstract: Grain-refined metals typically exhibit high strength, yet their engineering applications are often constrained by grain coarsening under thermo-mechanical loading. Recent experiments have revealed abnormal grain growth (AGG) in ultrafine-grained Ni thin films subjected to cyclic loading at room temperature. Unlike conventional AGG, which generally requires significant plastic deformation or high temperatures, this phenomenon occurs within the regime of macroscopic elastic deformation. This AGG is characterized by the preferential growth of grains with an in-plane <100> orientation aligned with the loading direction. Here, we investigate the underlying physical mechanisms by combining phase-field simulations with micromechanical analysis. The results indicate that elastic energy reduction provides a thermodynamically plausible driving force for this orientation-selective grain growth. Phase-field simulations reveal the evolution kinetics of AGG and confirm that local grain geometry and stress states play critical roles in determining the grain growth pathway. By applying this framework to systems with varying elastic anisotropy, we establish a general approach for investigating elastically driven AGG in polycrystalline materials.

We explore the role of critical device layers - including barrier and channel engineering, substrate selection, and passivation strategies - in mitigating high-temperature-induced effects, and evaluate the thermal stability of III-nitride HEMTs in logic, radiofrequency, and power electronics applications. We also highlight key remaining challenges in the design and optimization of III-nitride devices for high-temperature applications.

### [300] [Data-driven atomistic modelling of hybrid halide perovskite passivation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05321)
*Laura-Bianca Paşca,Henry J. Snaith,Volker L. Deringer*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种类似大语言模型连续微调的多步训练流程，结合一个大型开放数据集（hyP-26）和一个针对氨基硅烷分子钝化钙钛矿表面的专用小数据集，用于构建机器学习原子间势能（machine-learned interatomic potential），以模拟分子钝化钙钛矿表面的集体行为，并揭示了随分子覆盖度增加而演化的相互作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 表面缺陷的分子钝化（molecular passivation）对提升混合卤化物钙钛矿（hybrid halide perovskite）材料的光电性能至关重要，但其底层原子机制尚未被完全理解。同时，将机器学习原子间势能（machine-learned interatomic potentials）应用于分子配位钙钛矿表面等实验现实场景仍存在显著困难。

Method: 该方法包含一个多步训练流程，类似于大语言模型（large language model）中的连续微调。该流程由两部分组成：(i) 一个大型、精心筛选且开放的金属及混合卤化物钙钛矿结构数据集（hyP-26）；(ii) 一个针对氨基硅烷（amino-silane）分子钝化表面的专用小数据集，用于提供高特异性的微调信息。

Result: 将该方法应用于混合组分卤化物钙钛矿表面被不同覆盖度氨基硅烷分子钝化的场景，揭示了随着分子表面覆盖度（surface coverage）增加而演化的相互作用（collective behavior）。

Conclusion: 该多步微调训练协议能够有效支撑分子钝化钙钛矿表面这一实验现实场景的原子的建模与计算实验，有望加深对分子钝化底层原子机制的理解。

Abstract: Molecular passivation of surface defects is key to improving the optoelectronic performance of hybrid halide perovskite materials, but the underlying atomistic mechanisms are incompletely understood. While machine-learned interatomic potentials are now widely used to simulate complex molecular and crystalline systems, their application to experimentally-realistic scenarios - such as molecules coordinating to perovskite surfaces - is still far from trivial. Here, we describe a multistep training pipeline, resembling continuous fine-tuning used for large language models, to underpin atomistic modelling and computational experiments in this domain. Our protocol involves two components: (i) a large, curated, and open dataset of diverse metal and hybrid halide perovskite structures ('hyP-26'); and (ii) a small, specialised dataset for an amino-silane molecule passivating the surface, providing highly specific information for fine-tuning. We apply this approach to explore collective behaviour at a mixed-composition halide perovskite surface passivated with a varying coverage of amino-silane molecules, revealing an evolution of interactions with increasing molecular surface coverage.

### [301] [Magnetotransport and electronic band structure of EuNi$_2$As$_2$ antiferromagnet](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05337)
*Faheem Gul,Mane Sahakiyan,Orest Pavlosiuk,Piotr Wiśniewski*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了四方范德华化合物EuNi₂As₂单晶的磁输运性质，该化合物在14.6 K以下呈现非公度螺旋反铁磁序。通过磁化、磁电阻、霍尔效应测量及第一性原理计算，揭示了超磁转变、多带导电行为及磁有序对电子结构的显著影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究四方范德华化合物EuNi₂As₂在反铁磁有序态下的磁输运特性，特别是超磁转变与磁电阻之间的关联，以及磁有序对电子结构和霍尔效应的可能拓扑贡献。

Method: 采用单晶样品进行磁化率、磁电阻（magnetoresistance）和霍尔电阻率（Hall resistivity）测量；结合基于密度泛函理论的第一性原理（ab-initio）电子能带结构计算，并引入Hubbard修正（Hubbard corrections）分析Eu-4f轨道效应。

Result: 磁化测量在垂直于螺旋轴方向的外场下揭示了超磁转变（metamagnetic transitions），并清晰反映在磁电阻中。磁电阻整体较小，但在磁有序态下出现与超磁转变相关的显著异常；高于奈尔温度时，负磁电阻可由de Gennes-Friedel自旋无序散射（spin-disorder-scattering）机制很好描述。霍尔电阻率数据表明，反铁磁态下为空穴主导的多带导电，奈尔温度以上转为单带导电，载流子浓度约10²² cm⁻³。能带计算显示，磁有序后电子结构变化剧烈，但费米能级处态密度差异小于两倍，与霍尔实验结果一致。

Conclusion: EuNi₂As₂的金属性特征掩盖了霍尔电阻率中可能的拓扑贡献；Hubbard修正对态密度、磁矩及Eu-4f轨道屏蔽长度产生有意义的改变，需在理论描述中加以考虑。

Abstract: We investigated the magnetotransport properties of single-crystals of tetragonal van der Waals compound EuNi$_2$As$_2$, that orders antiferromagnetically below 14.6 K in an incommensurate helical structure. Metamagnetic transitions are revealed by the magnetization measured in the magnetic field applied transverse to the axis of the helix, and are clearly reflected in the magnetoresistance. Overall, the magnetoresistance is small, but shows complex changes with the temperature, the strength, and the angle of the applied magnetic field. In magnetically ordered state, magnetoresistance shows prominent anomalies related to the metamagnetic transitions. For temperatures above the Néel point the negative magnetoresistance can be modeled very well with de Gennes-Friedel mechanism of the spin-disorder-scattering reduction. Hall resistivity data indicate hole-dominated multi-band conductivity in antiferromagnetic state and single-band one above the Néel temperature, with carrier concentrations of the order of 10$^{22}$cm$^{-3}$. This metallic character of the compound seems to obscure the plausible topological contribution to the Hall resistivity. Our \textit{ab-initio} calculations of electronic band structure showed that the electronic structure changes very strongly upon magnetic ordering, but the density of states at the Fermi level differs by a factor smaller than two, in agreement with experimental Hall resistivity data. Meaningful changes in the density of states, magnetic moments, and screening length of Eu-4$f$ orbitals are discussed in terms of the effects of Hubbard corrections.

### [302] [Effective potentials for polar molecules under non-orthogonal dual microwave fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03179)
*Fulin Deng,Xinyuan Hu,Su Yi,Tao Shi*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文针对非正交双微波屏蔽中分子散射的时变问题，发展了一种Floquet理论框架，推导出解析有效势，实现了精确散射计算。研究发现非正交性虽轻微削弱屏蔽效果，但抑制了非弹性损失，并提供了额外的各向异性与强度可调性，可直接解释近期实验中的气-液滴转变与费米面形变现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 双微波屏蔽（dual-microwave shielding）实验中两个微波场通常不完全正交，导致偶极-偶极相互作用无法完全抵消，且单分子缀饰态（dressed state）具有内在时间依赖性，使得传统时间无关散射理论不再适用，亟需发展能够处理该非正交情形的新理论框架。

Method: 发展了一套Floquet理论，推导出解析有效势（analytic effective potential），实现了非正交双微波场中极性分子精确散射计算。

Result: 非正交性虽会适度削弱屏蔽效果，但在实验相关条件下非弹性损失（inelastic losses）仍被强烈抑制；同时，非正交性提供了额外的相互作用各向异性（anisotropy）和强度可调性，直接解释了气-液滴转变（gas-to-droplet transition）与费米面形变（Fermi-surface deformation）等实验观测。

Conclusion: 该Floquet理论框架不仅适用于双微波屏蔽，还可直接推广到任意多频率驱动（multi-frequency driving）场景，为复杂微波构型下超冷极性分子的操控提供了通用工具。

Abstract: Dual-microwave shielding has emerged as a powerful tool for stabilizing ultracold polar molecules while tuning their intermolecular interactions. However, the two microwave fields are generally not perfectly orthogonal in experiments. Such misalignment introduces an in-plane component of the linearly polarized microwave, whose frequency differs from that of the elliptically polarized field. This component prevents complete cancellation of the dipole-dipole interaction and, more critically, renders the single-molecule dressed state intrinsically time-dependent, so that the conventional time-independent scattering framework is no longer available. Here we develop a Floquet theory that yields an analytic effective potential and enables accurate scattering calculations for polar molecules in non-orthogonal dual microwave fields. We find that, though misalignment weakens the shielding moderately, inelastic losses remain strongly suppressed under experimentally relevant conditions. Meanwhile, misalignment provides additional tunability of the interaction anisotropy and strength, which has been directly applied to recent experimental observations on the gas-to-droplet transition~[Z. Shi \textit{et al}, arXiv:2508.20518 (2025)] and Fermi-surface deformation in microwave-shielded molecular gases~[S. Biswas \textit{et al}, arXiv:2602.22447]. The framework is not restricted to dual-microwave shielding and can be generalized straightforwardly to arbitrary multi-frequency driving, providing a versatile tool for manipulating ultracold polar molecules under complex microwave configurations.

</details>


### [303] [Experimental signatures of bosonic pairing in a two-component Bose gas](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03902)
*Omar Almonajed,M. Iskin,M. Ö. Oktel*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文在算符形式下重新表述了玻色配对理论（bosonic pairing theory），将其与Bogoliubov理论在均核二元玻色混合物（homonuclear binary Bose mixture）从弱相互作用气体到液滴区间的渡越中进行系统比较，发现玻色配对理论产生更低的巨势（grand potential）和定性不同的关联特征，为实验验证提供了可检验的信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在双组分玻色液滴（two-component bosonic droplets）的描述中，Bogoliubov理论虽常用但存在激发谱虚数分支（imaginary branch）的问题，该分支在计算超平均场（beyond-mean-field）能量时通常被忽略。玻色配对理论虽能提供全实数的激发谱，但其近似假设尚不够透明，需要建立更清晰的算符形式并进行系统比较。

Method: 在算符形式（operator formalism）下重新表述玻色配对理论，使其底层近似结构透明化；在固定粒子密度下自洽确定变分参数（variational parameters），聚焦于两种理论均具有实数激发谱的参数区间以进行直接比较。

Result: 玻色配对理论比Bogoliubov理论产生更低的巨势；预测了定性不同的关联特征，包括增强的长波长相间动量空间关联（long-wavelength interspecies momentum-space correlations）以及在实验可及的低动量区有限值的静态结构因子（static structure factor）；这些差异在广泛的相互作用强度下持续存在。

Conclusion: 这些差异表明，关联函数和结构因子测量可以为气体-液滴渡越（gas-to-droplet crossover）中的玻色配对提供直接的实验检验。

Abstract: Two-component bosonic droplets are commonly described within Bogoliubov theory, where beyond-mean-field quantum fluctuations stabilize the system against mean-field collapse. In the interaction regime where droplets form, however, the Bogoliubov excitation spectrum contains an imaginary branch associated with the underlying instability, which is typically omitted when evaluating the beyond-mean-field energy. Bosonic pairing theory provides an alternative description with a fully real excitation spectrum. In this work, we reformulate bosonic pairing theory within an operator formalism, making its underlying approximations transparent, and compare its predictions with those of Bogoliubov theory for a homonuclear binary Bose mixture across the crossover from a weakly interacting gas to the droplet regime. Working at fixed particle density, we determine the variational parameters of bosonic pairing theory self-consistently and focus on the regime in which both theories possess real excitation spectra, allowing a direct comparison. We find that bosonic pairing theory yields a lower grand potential than Bogoliubov theory and predicts qualitatively distinct correlation signatures, including enhanced long-wavelength interspecies momentum-space correlations and a finite density static structure factor at experimentally accessible low momenta. These differences persist over a broad range of interaction strengths and suggest that correlation and structure-factor measurements can provide direct experimental tests of bosonic pairing across the gas-to-droplet crossover.

</details>

*Michele Modugno,Marco Fattori,Giulio Pettini*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文提出并数值验证了一种在驱动双势阱（driven double-well）中利用非相互作用玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（non-interacting condensate）实现布洛赫球（Bloch sphere）赤道面任意轴旋转与快速z轴旋转的控制方案，并通过Floquet方法给出精确的两能级模型，该方案可直接应用于基于拍频超晶格（Beat-Note Superlattices）的实验平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用空间线性时间周期势（spatially linear time-periodic potential）驱动系统动力学，通过数值模拟进行分析；利用Floquet方法（Floquet-based approach）推导完整的含时演化算符，并建立一个精确的显式两能级模型来捕捉微观演化。

Result: 数值模拟表明，通过适当的控制协议，可以在驱动双势阱中实现布洛赫球赤道面内绕任意轴的受控旋转，以及与快速z轴旋转的组合操作；所构建的两能级模型能够准确描述驱动系统的微观动力学。

Conclusion: 该控制方案可直接应用于基于拍频超晶格的双势阱阵列实验平台，为量子信息处理和量子模拟中的操控提供可行的技术路径。

Abstract: We show that, by using suitable protocols for a non-interacting condensate in a driven double-well, one can achieve controlled rotations about arbitrary axes in the equatorial plane of the Bloch sphere, composed with fast rotations about the $z$-axis. Specifically, we investigate the dynamics induced by a spatially linear time-periodic potential, by means of numerical simulations. We also provide an explicit two-level model that accurately captures the microscopic evolution of the driven system, with the full time-dependent evolution operator obtained using a Floquet-based approach. The analysis is carried out using as a reference a recently realized experimental platform consisting of arrays of double-well potentials based on Beat-Note Superlattices, to which the proposed control scheme is directly applicable.

</details>


### [305] [Excitation spectra and rank tomography of linear matrix product tangent spaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05269)
*Otto T. P. Schmidt,Iacopo Carusotto*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文提出一种用于矩阵乘积态（MPS）代数簇的切空间方法，以研究具有开放边界条件的非均匀量子多体系统的激发谱，并通过秩断层扫描（rank tomography）刻画MPS切空间的表达能力；以Bose-Hubbard模型为例验证了该方法能准确再现低能激发并捕捉Mott绝缘体-超流体转变的有限尺寸前兆。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在处理非均匀量子多体系统（non-uniform quantum many-body systems）的激发谱时存在局限，尤其面对开放边界条件（open boundary conditions）下的代数几何结构缺乏系统的切空间框架。

Method: 提出一种针对矩阵乘积态（MPS）代数簇的切空间方法（tangent-space method）；引入MPS切空间的秩断层扫描（rank tomography），通过底层MPS簇的粒子扇区秩剖面（particle-sector rank profiles）来刻画切空间的表达力（expressivity）。

Conclusion: 所提出的MPS切空间方法为非均匀量子多体系统激发谱研究提供了新的代数几何工具，秩断层扫描为评估MPS变体的表达力提供了量化手段。

Abstract: We formulate a tangent-space method for algebraic varieties of matrix product states (MPS) to study excitation spectra of non-uniform quantum many-body systems with open boundary conditions. We further introduce a rank tomography of the MPS tangent space, which characterizes its expressivity in terms of particle-sector rank profiles of the underlying MPS variety. Using the Bose--Hubbard model as a benchmark, we illustrate that the method reproduces low-lying excitations and captures finite-size precursors of the Mott-insulator to superfluid transition.
