### [306] [Mass-imbalanced SU(N) Fermi gases](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05328)
*Jordi Pera,Joaquim Casulleras,Jordi Boronat*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文利用气体参数（gas parameter）x = kFa0的微扰理论，解析描述了具有任意质量不平衡的排斥性SU(N)费米气体（Fermi gas）中零温巡游铁磁性（itinerant ferromagnetism），给出了超越平均场（beyond-mean-field）修正的闭式解析表达式，并揭示了质量不平衡对极化相图的关键调控作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在质量平衡的多组分稀薄费米气体理论已经相对成熟，但实际超冷原子混合体系中各组分质量可以不同，而质量不平衡情形下的铁磁性行为尚缺乏完整的解析描述。本文旨在填补这一空白，建立任意质量比和自旋极化下的解析理论。

Method: 采用气体参数x = kFa0（kF为费米动量，a0为s波散射长度（s-wave scattering length））为展开参数的微扰理论（perturbation theory），推导了任意自旋极化（spin polarization）和任意质量比下系统的二阶能量修正，并得到闭合形式的超越平均场（beyond-mean-field）修正表达式。

Result: 质量不平衡在无相互作用极限下即破坏顺磁对称性（paramagnetic symmetry），并偏好较重组分占据，同时降低了达到完全极化态所需的相互作用强度。对于S = 1/2体系，系统从质量诱导的部分极化态连续演变为完全铁磁态；对于更大自旋，不同质量分布产生包括光滑和间断序列在内的不同极化路径。

Conclusion: 该解析结果将稀薄费米气体理论扩展到质量不平衡情形，提供了多组分混合物的紧致状态方程（equation of state），并揭示质量不平衡是超冷费米混合物中磁有序的强有力控制工具。

Abstract: We report a fully analytical description of zero-temperature itinerant ferromagnetism in repulsive SU(N) Fermi gases with arbitrary mass imbalance among components. Using perturbation theory in the gas parameter x = kFa0, with kF the Fermi momentum and a0 the s-wave scattering length, we derive the second-order energy for arbitrary spin polarization and arbitrary mass ratio. Our main result is a closed analytic expression for the beyond-mean-field correction in mixtures with unequal masses. This analytical result extends the theory of dilute Fermi gases beyond the mass-balanced case and provides a compact equation of state for multicomponent mixtures. We show that mass imbalance breaks the paramagnetic symmetry already in the non-interacting limit, favors the occu pation of heavier components, and lowers the interaction strength required to reach a fully polarized state. For S = 1/2, the system evolves continuously from a mass-induced partially polarized state to full ferromagnetism. For larger spins, distinct mass distributions generate qualitatively differ ent polarization paths, including smooth and discontinuous sequences. Our results identify mass imbalance as a powerful control tool for magnetic ordering in ultracold Fermi mixtures.

</details>

### [307] [Non-equilibrium coupling to a diffusing density breaks Ising universality](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02661)
*Mattia Scandolo,Johannes Pausch,Michael E. Cates,Luca Di Carlo*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该论文发现，当伊辛序参量（Ising order parameter）与非互易守恒扩散密度（nonreciprocal conserved diffusive density）耦合时，伊辛普适类（Ising universality class）的鲁棒性失效。在临界维度 $d_c=4$ 以下，重整化群（renormalization group）流向一个“快扩散不动点”（fast-diffusion fixed point），该不动点产生了一个全新的非平衡普适类，其特征是长程乘性噪声（long-range multiplicative noise）和涨落-耗散关系（fluctuation-dissipation relations）的大尺度破坏。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 伊辛普适类通常对非平衡扰动具有显著的鲁棒性，这些扰动在重整化下会流向零；本研究旨在检验当序参量与非互易守恒密度耦合时这一鲁棒性是否仍然成立。

Method: 采用重整化群方法，进行双圈（two-loop）计算以确定不动点的稳定性，并推导修正标度律（correction-to-scaling exponent）；同时提出全阶修正的哈里斯判据（modified Harris criterion）$ν>2/(d+z-2)$ 以确认不动点在 $d=3$ 下的主导地位。

Result: 在 $d_c=4$ 以下，系统流向一个快扩散不动点，产生新普适类；该不动点在 $d=3$ 下稳定，但修正标度指数 $ω≈0.020$ 极小，意味着强有限尺度修正（finite-size corrections）。同时，两点关联函数（two-point correlation function）和响应函数（response function）的标度指数发生分裂，表明涨落-耗散关系在大尺度上被破坏。

Conclusion: 该非平衡不动点（BIM fixed point）在 $d=3$ 下主导临界行为，伊辛普适类仅在 $d=2$ 时恢复。两圈计算和修正哈里斯判据共同确认了该不动点的稳定性，其大尺度破坏涨落-耗散关系是可测量的非平衡临界涨落（non-equilibrium critical fluctuations）标志。

Abstract: The Ising universality class is remarkably robust to non-equilibrium perturbations, which generically flow to zero under renormalization. We show that this robustness fails when an order parameter is coupled nonreciprocally to a conserved diffusive density. Below $d_c=4$, the renormalization group flows to a fast-diffusion fixed point at which the density acts as a long-range multiplicative noise, producing a novel universality class. The non-equilibrium nature of the fixed point is manifest in the large-scale violation of the fluctuation-dissipation relations, reflected in a splitting of the scaling exponents of the two-point correlation and response functions--a measurable hallmark of non-equilibrium critical fluctuations. A two-loop calculation establishes the stability of this fixed point but yields a small correction-to-scaling exponent $ω\approx0.020$ in $d=3$, implying strong finite-size corrections. An all-orders modified Harris criterion $ν>2/(d+z-2)$ confirms that the BIM fixed point governs criticality in $d=3$, with Ising universality recovered only at $d=2$.

</details>


### [308] [Non-equilibrium phase transition in the Brownian Ising Model: field theory, renormalization group, and exact results](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02667)
*Mattia Scandolo,Luca Di Carlo*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文对布朗伊辛模型（Brownian Ising Model, BIM）进行了完整的场论重整化群分析，发现密度与序参量的非平衡耦合在四维以下驱动系统进入一个全新的非平衡不动点，该不动点与伊辛普适类（Ising universality class）截然不同，其特征包括负反常维数、涨落-耗散定理（fluctuation-dissipation theorem）的显式破缺以及精确标度关系，并确立了BIM不动点是三维中唯一的红外吸引子。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在非平衡统计力学中，理解偏离细致平衡（detailed balance）的系统是否仍然属于平衡普适类，抑或形成全新的普适类，是核心问题之一。布朗伊辛模型通过将$\mathbb{Z}_2$序参量与守恒密度耦合打破了细致平衡，对其临界行为的完整重整化群分析尚未完成。

Method: 采用马丁-西格-罗斯（Martin-Siggia-Rose, MSR）形式论，结合$\varepsilon = 4 - d$展开方法，对布朗伊辛模型进行完整场论重整化群分析。临界指数在最低非平庸阶次计算，部分指数需要专门的双圈（two-loop）分析。进一步导出了重整化因子之间的精确关系，这些关系在全阶微扰论（all orders in perturbation theory）下成立。

Result: 密度-序参量耦合在四维以下是重整化群相关的（RG-relevant），驱动系统进入一个新的非平衡不动点。该不动点产生负反常维数$\eta$，且关联函数与响应函数具有不同的反常维数，即$\eta \neq 2 - \gamma / \nu$，直接表明涨落-耗散定理在大尺度上被破坏。还发现了较小的修正标度指数（correction-to-scaling exponent），预示数值和实验检验中需考虑大的预渐近修正。导出了精确标度关系$\nu = 2 / (d + z - 2)$，并证明了伊辛普适类以及淬火稀释伊辛普适类在$d=3$中是不稳定的。

Conclusion: BIM不动点被确立为任意非零扩散常数下唯一的红外吸引子（infrared attractor），代表了一类新的非平衡普适类。其在大尺度上的核心可观测特征是涨落-耗散定理的破缺以及关联与响应函数反常维数的差异。

Abstract: We present a complete field-theoretical renormalization-group (RG) analysis of the Brownian Ising Model (BIM), in which a $\mathbb{Z}_2$ order parameter is coupled to a passive conserved density, breaking detailed balance. Using the Martin-Siggia-Rose formalism and an $ε=4-d$ expansion, we show that this density-order parameter coupling is RG-relevant below four dimensions and drives the system to a new non-equilibrium fixed point, distinct from the Ising universality class. Critical exponents are computed at lowest nontrivial order, some of which require a dedicated two-loop analysis. At large scales, the density acts as an effective noise that is white in time but long-range in space, enhancing order-parameter fluctuations and producing a negative anomalous dimension $η$. A defining feature of the new class is that the correlation and response functions acquire different anomalous dimensions, $η\neq 2 - γ/ ν$ - a direct, observable signature of fluctuation-dissipation-theorem violation at large scales that cannot occur in equilibrium. We also find a small correction-to-scaling exponent, implying large preasymptotic corrections that must be accounted for in numerical and experimental tests. We further derive a set of relations among renormalization factors that hold to all orders in perturbation theory, following from the linearity of the density dynamics and an emergent shift symmetry. These yield an exact scaling relation $ν= 2/(d+z-2)$ at the BIM fixed point and establish that the Ising universality class, as well as that of quenched diluted-Ising, is unstable in $d=3$. This establishes the BIM fixed point as the unique infrared attractor for any nonzero diffusion constant.

</details>


### [309] [Finite-Time Thermodynamics of Battery Discharging: Power-Efficiency Trade-Off and Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03157)
*Rui-Han Liu,Yun-Qian Lin,Yu-Han Ma*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文揭示了电池放电中输出功率与能量转换效率之间的普适抛物线权衡关系 $P\propto\eta(1-\eta)$，最大功率处效率恰为1/2；并在此基础上，通过KKT条件解析求解，提出了多阶段恒流放电（MSCD）的最优调度策略 $I_{i}^{\star}=\max(I_{i}^{-},I_{0})$，为电池管理系统建立了严谨的热力学基准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 电池放电受限于输出功率与能量转换效率之间的根本性权衡（trade-off），该权衡源于内部耗散（internal dissipation）。现有文献虽在有限时间热力学（finite-time thermodynamics）中已知半卡诺极限（half-Carnot limit），但缺乏将这一理论界限转化为实际电池调度操作规则的系统性框架。

Method: 通过理论推导揭示功率-效率之间的抛物线包络关系；针对多阶段恒流放电（multistage constant-current discharging, MSCD）调度问题，考虑实时负载需求与全局放电截止时间（deadline）双重约束，利用Karush--Kuhn--Tucker (KKT) 条件进行解析求解，得到最优策略的闭式表达式。

Result: 最大功率处的效率精确等于1/2，与有限时间热力学中的半卡诺极限一致。最优电流政策为 $I_{i}^{\star}=\max(I_{i}^{-},I_{0})$：受外部需求限制的阶段以最小所需电流运行，其余阶段统一提升至由截止时间约束确定的基线电流 $I_{0}$。通过耗散-时间帕累托前沿（Pareto front）刻画了内阻（internal resistance）对运行边界的影响。

Conclusion: 该分析为电池管理系统（battery management system）的调度层（scheduling layer）建立了严谨的热力学基线（thermodynamic baseline），并可自然扩展至包含温度（temperature）和荷电状态（state of charge, SoC）依赖性的非线性模型中。

Abstract: Battery discharging is governed by a fundamental trade-off between output power and energy conversion efficiency due to internal dissipation. In this paper, we demonstrate that such a trade-off universally yields a parabolic envelope $P\proptoη(1-η)$. The efficiency at maximum power is exactly one half, mirroring the well-known half-Carnot limit in finite-time thermodynamics. To extend this bound into practical operational rules, we formulate a multistage constant-current discharging (MSCD) schedule subject to simultaneous real-time load demands and a global discharging deadline. Analytical resolution via the Karush--Kuhn--Tucker conditions reveals a remarkably compact optimal policy: $I_{i}^{\star}=\max(I_{i}^{-},I_{0})$. Under this rule, stages limited by external demand run exactly at their minimum required currents, while all remaining stages are elevated to a uniform baseline $I_{0}$ fixed by the deadline constraint. By tracing the dissipation--time Pareto front, we quantify how internal resistance shifts the operational boundaries and sharpens the trade-off corner. This analysis establishes a rigorous thermodynamic baseline for the scheduling layer of battery management systems, offering natural extensions to nonlinear models incorporating temperature and state-of-charge dependencies.

</details>


### [310] [Variance of the $SIS$ Epidemic on Networks: A Diffusion Approximation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03300)
*Lucija Nora Farkaš,Sebastian Morel Balbi,Hrvoje Štefančić,István Zoltán Kiss,Vinko Zlatić*

Result: 在对泊松（Poisson）网络、正则（regular）网络与幂律（power-law）网络的Gillespie随机模拟验证中，所提方差近似与模拟结果高度一致，仅在传染病阈值（epidemic threshold）附近以及强异质网络（strongly heterogeneous networks）中出现偏差。

Conclusion: 该工作为配置模型图上的SIS过程提供了一种可解析计算涨落的框架，弥补了对应FCLT缺失的空白，但在近阈值与高异质性情形下的精度仍需进一步改进。

Abstract: Functional laws of large numbers (FLLNs) describe the mean-field trajectory of epidemics on networks, but say nothing about the fluctuations around it. These fluctuations are governed by moments of the degree distribution not relevant at the level of the mean. A rigorous functional central limit theorem (FCLT) exists for the susceptible--infected ($SI$) process on configuration-model graphs, but no analogue exists for $SIS$, where recovery reintroduces vertices into the susceptible pool with partially known neighborhoods, breaking the clean neighborhood distribution the $SI$ derivation relies on. We develop a tractable variance approximation for Markovian $SIS$ on configuration-model graphs, combining Gleeson's approximate master equation (AME) framework with a van Kampen system-size expansion in the spirit of the $SI$ FCLT. We derive a closed drift and diffusion matrix for a reduced susceptible/$SI$-edge/$SS$-edge count vector and obtain the time-dependent covariance via the associated Langevin/Lyapunov equation. Validation against Gillespie simulation across Poisson, regular, and power-law networks shows close agreement, with deviations near the epidemic threshold and in strongly heterogeneous networks.

Method: 基于随机能量学（stochastic energetics），对从相同初始构型出发、向平衡态松弛的一组轨迹进行分析，将其投影到不同的候选坐标（putative coordinates）上，并直接计算每条轨迹上的熵产生。

Abstract: We show through theory and numerical experiments that a straightforward calculation of entropy production on short molecular dynamics trajectories allows estimating free-energy barriers and identifying optimal reaction coordinates of activated processes. To this aim, we perform an analysis based on stochastic energetics on a set of trajectories relaxing towards equilibrium from a same initial configuration, projected on different putative coordinates. After demonstrating the approach on simple benchmarks, we show that it is possible to estimate the free-energy barrier of a complex high-dimensional system (carbon nanoparticles in water) and to rank the quality of order parameters, in agreement with the committor probability. The results shed light on the entanglement between the second law, free-energy landscapes, reaction coordinates and kinetic rates.

Abstract: We study continuously monitored dynamics of a quasiperiodic free-fermion chain defined on a Fibonacci lattice. ### [313] [Quantum tunneling Mpemba effect](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03845)
*Hisao Hayakawa,Satoshi Takada*

TL;DR: 本文在连续一维对称双阱势中研究了量子隧穿Mpemba效应，通过非厄米谱分解证明首个非平凡偶宇称谱系数对初始温度的中间热峰是量子统计力学的普适拓扑性质，由Sturm-Liouville振荡定理决定且与系统尺寸无关，但异常交叉现象的观测需要严格的时间尺度分离条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索量子隧穿Mpemba效应在连续一维对称双阱势中的存在性与普适性机制，并弥合经典边界驱动耗散与开放量子动力学之间的理论鸿沟。

Method: 采用非厄米谱分解（non-Hermitian spectral decomposition）有效哈密顿量，在连续双阱势（$x=\pm L$处与环境耗散源耦合）中表征开放系统弛豫动力学，并运用Sturm-Liouville振荡定理（Sturm-Liouville oscillation theorem）分析谱系数的拓扑性质。

Result: 严格证明了第一个非平凡偶宇称谱系数$a_{2}(T_{i})$关于初始制备温度$T_i$的非单调行为是量子统计力学的普适拓扑性质；该中间热峰由Sturm-Liouville振荡定理控制，且完全不受系统全局尺寸$L$的影响，这与边界驱动的经典Mpemba效应形成鲜明对比。该普适峰源于高度局域化的未扰动态与扩展非厄米衰变通道之间的几何与节点对齐。异常交叉现象（总存活概率迹$S(t,T_i)$和迹距离$\mathcal{D}(t,T_i)$中）的观测需要严格的时间尺度分离：过垒逃逸率需远大于深阱隧穿双峰衰变率（$Γ_{2}\gg Γ_{0}$且$Γ_2\gg Γ_1$）。

Conclusion: 连续形式化成功桥接了实空间经典边界驱动耗散与开放量子动力学，为通过定制边界损耗工程非平衡态提供了新的见解。

Abstract: The quantum tunneling Mpemba effect is investigated within a continuous one-dimensional symmetric double-well potential open to external environmental sinks at the boundaries ($x=\pm L$). Using a non-Hermitian spectral decomposition of the effective Hamiltonian, we characterize the open-system relaxation dynamics without relying on abstract state-space quenches. We mathematically prove that the non-monotonic behavior of the first non-trivial even-parity spectral coefficient, $a_{2}(T_{i})$, with respect to the initial preparation temperature $T_{i}$ is a universal topological property born from quantum statistical mechanics. Crucially, we demonstrate that this intermediate thermal peak is governed by the Sturm-Liouville oscillation theorem and remains completely invariant with respect to the global system size $L$, contrasting sharply with the boundary-driven classical Mpemba effect. This universal peak arises from the geometric and nodal alignment between highly localized unperturbed states and extended non-Hermitian decay channels. Furthermore, we clarify that while this mechanism is robust, the actual observation of anomalous crossings in the total survival probability trace $S(t,T_{i})$ and the trace distance $\mathcal{D}(t,T_i)$ demand a strict separation of timescales, requiring the over-barrier escape rate to vastly exceed the decay rate of the deep-well tunneling doublet ($Γ_{2}\gg Γ_{0}$ and $Γ_2\gg Γ_1$). Our continuous formulation successfully bridges real-space classical boundary-driven dissipation with open quantum dynamics, providing novel insights for engineering non-equilibrium states via tailored boundary loss.

### [314] [The Reweighting Principle in Statistical Mechanics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03867)
*Salvatore Romano*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文通过概率测度的重加权（reweighting）统一描述了条件作用、指数倾斜（exponential tilting）以及统计力学中的系综变换，揭示了它们之间在信息论与热力学结构上的内在联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有统计力学框架中，条件作用、指数倾斜与系综变换常被分开处理，缺乏统一的数学基础。作者旨在通过概率测度的重加权视角，建立这些概念之间的内在联系，并揭示其共同的信息论与热力学结构。

Method: 采用最小相对熵（minimum-relative-entropy）更新框架，分别将软约束（soft constraints）与硬约束（hard constraints）对应到指数倾斜和条件作用。引入扩大的概率空间（enlarged probability space），将观测量（observables）作为显式变量处理，进而将微正则系综（microcanonical ensemble）和正则系综（canonical ensemble）视为同一结构性先验（structural prior）经指数重加权后的条件分布与边缘分布。在大偏差理论（large deviation theory）下分析热力学极限（thermodynamic limit），揭示从指数倾斜到条件作用的浓度现象。

Result: 指数倾斜产生正则系综的勒让德结构（Legendre structure），对均匀参考测度（uniform reference measure）退化为吉布斯熵（Gibbs entropy）；条件作用通过约束宏观态的惊讶性（surprisal）退化为玻尔兹曼熵（Boltzmann entropy）。系综等价性（ensemble equivalence）可归结为熵与偏差之间的竞争。该框架可自然延拓至路径空间（path space），统一描述平衡态热力学（equilibrium thermodynamics）与条件化随机动力学（conditioned stochastic dynamics）。

Conclusion: 概率测度的重加权为统计力学中的多种变换提供了统一的信息论基础，揭示了条件作用与指数倾斜之间通过熵-偏差竞争而建立的等价性，并为更广泛的随机动力学系统提供了统一的理论框架。

Abstract: Reweighting of probability measures provides a unifying perspective on conditioning, exponential tilting, and, more generally, ensemble transformations in statistical mechanics. We show that exponential tilting and conditioning arise as the minimum-relative-entropy updates associated with soft and hard constraints, respectively. Their relative entropies naturally inherit complementary thermodynamic structures: exponential tilting gives rise to the Legendre structure of the canonical ensemble and reduces to the Gibbs entropy for a uniform reference measure, while conditioning reduces to the Boltzmann entropy through the surprisal of the constrained macrostate. By introducing an enlarged probability space in which observables are treated as explicit variables, we further show that microcanonical and canonical ensembles arise as conditional and marginal distributions of a common structural prior after exponential reweighting. In the thermodynamic limit, described through large deviation theory, conditioning emerges from exponential tilting by concentration of measure, revealing ensemble equivalence as a consequence of entropy--bias competition. Finally, we outline how the same information-theoretic framework naturally extends to path space, suggesting a unified probabilistic description of equilibrium thermodynamics and conditioned stochastic dynamics.

### [315] [Universal fluctuations of first discoveries in competitive exploration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04252)
*Arthur Plaud,P. L. Krapivsky,S. Redner,Olivier Bénichou*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文通过引入“发现份额”（discovery share）$X_n$ 的概念，研究两个或多个竞争者在随机探索中首次到达资源的竞争动力学。研究发现，竞争平衡是否持久取决于谱维度（spectral dimension）$d_s$：当 $d_s<2$ 时表现为持续随机性，$2\le d_s<3$ 时为异常慢的非高斯集中，$d_s\ge3$ 时为高斯集中（$d_s=3$ 时含对数修正），揭示了首次到达不平等性的一般涨落理论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的随机探索研究通常关注新空间被发现的速率，但在竞争性探索（competitive exploration）中，首次到达（first arrival）直接决定了资源的独占权。因此，仅知道哪些位置被探明是不够的，还需要确定每个被发现位置由哪个搜索者率先到达。本文旨在回答竞争性探索中早期优势是否会被抹平这一核心问题。

Method: 引入发现份额 $X_n$（表示被标记搜索者在集体前 $n$ 次发现中所占比例），利用交换对称性（exchange symmetry）确定 $\langle X_n\rangle=1/2$，并通过谱维度 $d_s$（由单搜索者回到原点的概率 $p_0(t)\sim t^{-d_s/2}$ 定义）对竞争动力学进行分类。推导了 $d_s\ge2$ 时的渐近方差（asymptotic variance）及其前置因子（prefactor），并利用首次发现标签的两点关联（two-point correlation）识别不同相的记忆机制。

Result: 谱维度 $d_s$ 将竞争探索划分为三个相：$d_s<2$ 时，竞争结果持续随机（persistent randomness）；$2\le d_s<3$ 时，出现异常慢的非高斯集中（anomalously slow non-Gaussian concentration）；$d_s\ge3$ 时，为高斯集中（Gaussian concentration），其中 $d_s=3$ 处存在对数修正。该相结构在几何改变、竞争者异质性（competitor heterogeneity）、竞争者数量和记忆效应等因素下保持稳健。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了一般的首次到达不平等性（first-arrival inequalities）涨落理论，揭示了竞争性随机探索中早期优势是否被抹平的普适判据——谱维度 $d_s$，并证明该相结构具有广泛的稳健性。

Abstract: Random exploration is usually quantified by how fast new space is found, from
  the range of a single walker to the territory collectively covered by many
  walkers. In competitive exploration, first arrival secures an exclusive resource, as when foragers compete for food items or agents capture distributed targets. It is then no longer enough to know which sites have been discovered: one must determine, for each discovered site, which searcher reached it first. We introduce the discovery
  share $X_n$, the fraction of the first $n$ collective discoveries secured by
  a tagged searcher. For two identical competitors, exchange symmetry fixes
  $\langle X_n\rangle=1/2$, but the central question is whether this equal
  split emerges in each long exploration history or only on average, \emph{i.e.} whether early
  competitive advantages are erased or persist. Here we show that the answer is
  controlled by the spectral dimension $d_s$, defined by the large-time decay of the probability that a single searcher is at
  its starting point after $t$ steps, $p_0(t)\sim t^{-d_s/2}$.
  Across ordinary diffusion, long-range superdiffusion and subdiffusion induced
  by crowding or memory, $d_s$ separates persistent randomness in
  recurrent exploration $(d_s<2)$, anomalously slow non-Gaussian concentration
  for $2\le d_s<3$, and Gaussian concentration, logarithmically corrected at
  $d_s=3$, for $d_s\ge3$. For $d_s\ge2$, we derive exact asymptotic
  variances, including prefactors, and the discovery scale on which competitive
  imbalances are erased. Two-point correlations of first-discovery labels identify the memory mechanism behind these regimes.
  The same phase structure persists under changes in geometry, competitor
  heterogeneity, number of competitors and memory, revealing a general fluctuation
  theory of first-arrival inequalities.

</details>


### [316] [Geometric Characteristics of Subproblems in Ising-Machine-Assisted Large Neighborhood Search](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05014)
*Masashi Yamashita,Shu Tanaka*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文针对组合优化问题在伊辛机（Ising machines）上求解时规模受限的困难，对比了两种大规模邻域搜索（LNS）子问题构建策略（LNS-K基于当前解车辆路径、LNS-Q基于QUBO变量与约束关系），发现在控制子问题二进制变量数相同的条件下，LNS-K能获得更短的总距离，且空间分布指标（位置方差）在迭代中下降，表明子问题设计不仅要考虑规模，还需考虑从当前解继承的语义与几何结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大规模二次无约束二元优化（QUBO）形式的约束组合优化问题往往超出现有伊辛机（Ising machines）的输入规模限制，或随二进制变量数增加而导致求解质量下降。现有研究对区分子问题的结构性因素（超出二进制变量数量之外）仍不够充分，因此需要更深入地理解如何设计有效的子问题构建策略。

Method: 以车辆路径问题（vehicle routing problems）为研究对象，在控制子问题二进制变量数相同的条件下，比较两种大规模邻域搜索（LNS）子问题构建方式：LNS-K基于当前解的车辆路径进行构建，LNS-Q基于QUBO变量与约束关系进行构建。通过匹配子问题规模的实验对比两种策略的总距离与位置方差（position variance，衡量所选客户空间分散程度的指标）。

Result: 在控制子问题规模的条件下，LNS-K获得的总距离短于LNS-Q；LNS-K的位置方差（position variance）在迭代过程中逐步下降。

Conclusion: 面向伊辛机（Ising machines）的序列优化子问题设计，不仅应考虑子问题规模（subproblem size），还应考虑从当前解继承的语义结构（semantic structures）与几何结构（geometric structures）。

Abstract: Large-scale quadratic unconstrained binary optimization (QUBO) formulations of constrained combinatorial optimization problems often exceed the input-size limit of present Ising machines or suffer from degraded solution quality as the number of binary variables increases. Large neighborhood search (LNS) mitigates this difficulty by sequentially optimizing restricted subproblems, but the structural factors that distinguish subproblems beyond the number of binary variables remain insufficiently characterized. In this study, we examine vehicle routing problems and compare a construction based on the vehicle routes of the current solution, denoted by LNS-K, with a construction based on QUBO variables and constraint relations, denoted by LNS-Q, while controlling the number of binary variables in the subproblems. Under the tested conditions, LNS-K obtained shorter total distances than LNS-Q in the matched-size comparisons, and the position variance, a measure of the spatial spread of the selected customers, decreased during the iterations in LNS-K. These observations suggest that subproblem design for sequential optimization with Ising machines should consider not only subproblem size but also semantic and geometric structures inherited from the current solution.

*Ruohan Xu,Faezeh Khodabandehlou,Christian Maes*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文通过Floquet分析，完整描述了时间周期场驱动的宏观Curie-Weiss磁体在温度与驱动参数空间中的相图，发现低温度、大驱动振幅与频率下顺磁相与铁磁相共存，并首次详细分析了非平衡比热在临界点的发散行为，发现临界指数在β↓β_c时为α=1，在β↑β_c时为α≈0.86，且临界性具有动力学本质，这在热平衡系统中无法被观测到。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 此前对时间周期场驱动下Curie-Weiss磁体相图的认识尚不完整，尤其是偏离平衡时比热行为与临界指数的性质尚不清楚。本文旨在填补这一空白，揭示驱动频率与振幅对临界相变行为的调控作用。

Method: 论文采用宏观Curie-Weiss磁体模型，在时间周期外场下通过Floquet分析研究系统的临界动力学；通过数值与解析计算，在不同温度区间提取比热（specific heat）与磁化率（magnetic susceptibility）的发散行为，并标定临界指数α。

Result: 发现存在低温度、大驱动振幅与频率下顺磁相（paramagnetic phase）与铁磁相（ferromagnetic phase）共存的新相区；非平衡比热在临界逆温度β_c处发散，临界指数从高温侧（β↓β_c）为α=1，低温侧（β↑β_c）为α≈0.86，即使驱动幅度很小时该不对称性也依然存在；居里温度随驱动增强而下降。

Conclusion: 时间周期驱动引入了一类仅在动力学中呈现的临界性，其非对称临界指数与平衡系统截然不同，说明驱动可将系统推至不可逆的动力学临界行为，这对理解驱动开放系统的相变具有启示意义。

Abstract: We complete the phase diagram of the macroscopic Curie-Weiss magnet in a time-periodic external field, as a function of temperature and driving parameters. There is a regime (large enough driving amplitude and frequency, at low temperatures) where stable paramagnetic and ferromagnetic phases coexist. In particular, we present a new detailed analysis of the (nonequilibrium) specific heat, diverging at the same critical inverse temperature $β_c$ as the magnetic susceptibility. The new Curie temperature decreases with the driving, and we find critical exponent $α=1$ for $β\downarrow β_c$, and $α\simeq 0.86$ for $β\uparrow β_c$, even for small driving. A Floquet analysis shows the nature of the criticality, which is dynamical, with implications that remain unseen and are mostly impossible when the system is in thermal equilibrium.

</details>


### [318] [On data-driven parameterizations of multidimensional generalized Langevin dynamics in the presence of a quadratic potential](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05151)
*Maximilian Braun,Martin Hanke,Niklas Wolf*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 提出一种数值算法，利用平稳速度的自相关数据构建普罗尼级数（Prony series）近似，从而获得多维粗粒化（coarse-grained）物理系统在外势场中运动方程的马可夫模型（Markov model），避免了先求解记忆核（memory kernel）的逆问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在记忆效应显著的多维粗粒化物理系统中，传统的运动方程参数化需要先求解记忆核这一逆问题，过程复杂且计算代价高。该研究旨在提出一种直接利用速度自相关数据构建马可夫模型的替代方法。

Method: 利用平稳速度的自相关数据（autocorrelation data of stationary velocities），构建自相关函数的普罗尼级数近似，进而直接获得对应的马可夫模型参数，从而规避了先求解记忆核的逆问题步骤。

Result: 基于分子动力学（molecular dynamics）数据的数值实验表明，对于一维系统，使用五个辅助变量（auxiliary variables）的参数化模型即可取得良好匹配；对于二维系统，则需要十二个辅助变量。

Conclusion: 该算法为存在记忆效应的多维粗粒化系统提供了一种有效的运动方程参数化方案，通过自相关数据的普罗尼级数近似直接构建马可夫模型，避免了逆问题求解的复杂性。

Abstract: We propose a numerical algorithm to construct a Markov model with an extended list of variables to parameterize the equation of motion of a multidimensional coarse-grained physical system in an external potential, when memory effects are relevant. Our method uses autocorrelation data of the stationary velocities, but it avoids the inverse problem of finding the corresponding memory kernel from these data in a first step. Rather, the data are used to construct a Prony series approximation of the autocorrelation function, and the parameters of this Prony series provide the corresponding Markov model. Numerical results for molecular dynamics data show a good match for parameterized models with five auxiliary variables for a one-dimensional, and twelve auxiliary variables for a two-dimensional system.

</details>


### [319] [Ising-Machine-Assisted Large Neighborhood Search with Flexibly Tunable Subproblem Size](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05169)
*Koshiro Fujimoto,Masashi Yamashita,Shu Tanaka*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出 LNS-VT 方法，通过在伊辛机辅助的大邻域搜索（LNS）中引入每辆车连续重优化步数作为参数，实现对子问题规模的精细控制。实验表明，该方法在车辆路径问题（VRP）和多背包问题（QMKP）上均优于现有方法，子问题规模控制对求解质量至关重要。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 伊辛机（Ising machine）直接求解大规模带约束组合优化问题时解质量会下降；现有保持可行性的方法在求解车辆路径问题（vehicle routing problem, VRP）时只能整条路径重优化，无法精细调整子问题规模。因此需要一种能细粒度控制子问题规模同时保持可行性的方法。

Method: 提出 LNS-VT 方法，将每辆车连续重优化的步数（number of consecutive steps re-optimized per vehicle）作为参数，在保持可行性的前提下对子问题规模进行精细控制。该原理同样被应用于二次多重背包问题（quadratic multiple knapsack problem, QMKP）。

Result: 在一个 300 站点、5 辆车的 VRP 问题上，LNS-VT 在 100 次迭代后相比现有方法目标值降低约 10%；最佳子问题规模设定会随当前解质量而改变。在 QMKP 上的实验也证实存在合适的子问题规模。

Conclusion: 子问题规模控制（subproblem-size control）在伊辛机辅助的大邻域搜索中非常重要；LNS-VT 方法通过引入可调的步数参数实现了有效的细粒度控制，并能适应解质量的变化。

Abstract: Ising machines are heuristic solvers for combinatorial optimization, but their solution quality can degrade when large-scale constrained problems are solved directly. Ising-machine-assisted large neighborhood search (LNS) instead repeatedly updates a feasible current solution by solving smaller subproblems. An existing feasibility-preserving method for the vehicle routing problem (VRP) re-optimizes the entire routes of selected vehicles and thus cannot adjust the subproblem size finely. We propose LNS-VT, which introduces the number of consecutive steps re-optimized per vehicle as a parameter to control the subproblem size finely while preserving feasibility. For a 300-site, 5-vehicle VRP, its best setting reduced the objective value by approximately 10\% relative to the existing method after 100 iterations, and the appropriate setting changed with the current solution quality. Applying the same principle to the quadratic multiple knapsack problem, we confirmed that an appropriate subproblem size also exists, indicating that subproblem-size control is important in Ising-machine-assisted LNS.

</details>


### [320] [Semi-Markovian switching in a fluctuating harmonic trap: An age-structured formulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05173)
*Derek Frydel*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究了一个简谐势阱（harmonic trap）刚度在服从任意等待时间统计的两个值之间切换的布朗粒子（Brownian particle）系统，产生半马尔可夫动力学（semi-Markovian dynamics）。通过在年龄结构状态空间（age-structured state space）中恢复马尔可夫性（Markovianity），推导出稳态积分方程和精确表达式；随后分析了随机重置（stochastic-resetting）极限，将问题转化为方差空间中的切换过程并给出解析处理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实际物理系统中环境参数的切换往往具有非指数等待时间分布，导致非马尔可夫记忆效应（non-Markovian memory）。本文动机在于建立一套能够处理任意等待时间统计的刚度切换势阱中布朗运动的解析框架，以刻画此类半马尔可夫过程中的稳态统计量与能量学特征。

Method: 首先将原始问题嵌入放大年龄结构的状态空间，使非马尔可夫过程恢复局部福克-普朗克描述（local Fokker--Planck description），推导稳态积分方程；然后在随机重置极限下，将稳态空间分布表示为具有随机方差的高斯态（Gaussian states）叠加，转化为方差空间的切换过程，进一步简化分析。

Result: 精确求解了稳态空间分布和出生分布的积分方程，得到稳态矩（stationary moments）、注入功率（injected power）和势能（potential energy）的精确表达式；在随机重置极限下，方差分布的积分方程被显式给出，系统获得可直接解析处理的形式。

Conclusion: 所提的年龄结构状态空间方法和方差空间切换表示法为分析具有任意等待时间统计的刚度切换系统提供了有效解析工具，并揭示了半马尔可夫动力学与随机重置机制之间的深层联系。

Abstract: We study a Brownian particle in a harmonic trap whose stiffness switches between two values with arbitrary waiting-time statistics, generating semi-Markovian dynamics. To treat the resulting temporal memory, we formulate the problem in an enlarged age-structured state space, restoring Markovianity and yielding a local Fokker--Planck description. Within this framework, we derive exact steady-state integral equations for the spatial and birth distributions and obtain exact expressions for stationary moments, injected power, and potential energy. In the second part of the paper, we analyze the stochastic-resetting limit, corresponding to a particle alternately released and trapped. By representing the stationary spatial distribution as a superposition of Gaussian states with fluctuating variance, the problem can be reformulated as a switching process in variance space. This yields exact integral equations for the variance distributions and leads to a simplified description amenable to direct analytical treatment.

</details>


### [321] [Nucleation and time-reversal symmetry breaking in nonconserved scalar field theories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05194)
*Noah Ziethen,Michalis Chatzittofi,Michael E. Cates,Cesare Nardini*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出非平衡成核理论（NNT），将经典成核理论（CNT）推广至具有非守恒序参量的非平衡场理论，通过随机投影和Freidlin-Wentzell作用量最小化两种方法导出液滴半径动力学，并在活性物质、群体动力学等模型中验证了理论准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典成核理论（CNT）仅适用于平衡态系统，基于单个反应坐标（液滴半径）描述成核过程；该工作旨在将其推广至非平衡场理论体系，填补非平衡系统中成核理论系统性框架的缺失。

Method: 采用两种等价推导路径：(1) 随机路径（stochastic route），基于对随机场方程（stochastic field equation）向径向反应坐标的直接投影；(2) 作用量路径，基于Freidlin-Wentzell作用量（Freidlin-Wentzell action）最小化。利用大临界半径极限下出现的微扰结构（perturbative structure），并借助反应坐标的精确定义进行解析推导。

Result: NNT预测的准势垒（quasipotential barrier）不同于将瞬子（instanton）视为弛豫动力学时间反演所得到的势垒；界面密度分布（interfacial density profile）也与弛豫路径不同。在活性物质模型A（Active Model A）和群体动力学模型（population dynamics model）中，NNT的解析结果与基于作用量最小化的数值结果高度吻合。

Conclusion: NNT为一大类非平衡系统（包括活性物质、反应-扩散系统、群体动力学）提供了系统化的成核理论构建框架。

Abstract: Classical nucleation theory (CNT) describes the formation of a stable phase from a metastable one in terms of a single reaction coordinate that corresponds to the radius of a nucleating droplet. In this work, we provide a full account of nonequilibrium nucleation theory (NNT), which generalizes CNT to non-equilibrium field theories with non-conserved order parameter. We present two equivalent derivations of the dynamics of the droplet radius: a stochastic route, based on a direct projection of the stochastic field equation onto the radial reaction coordinate, and a route based on the minimization of the Freidlin-Wentzell action. Crucially, the quasipotential barrier predicted by NNT differs from the one found when assuming the instanton to be the time-reversal of the relaxation dynamics. Whereas the interfacial density profile differs from that on the relaxation path, an analytical derivation of NNT remains possible using a careful definition of the reaction coordinate. This leverages the perturbative structure that (in common with CNT) emerges in the limit of large critical radius. We further derive with similar techniques the dynamics of capillary waves, whose stability is required for the CNT/NNT precept of a near-spherical droplet to prevail. After deriving our theory for generic non-conserved field-theories, we address two explicit examples: a non-equilibrium generalization of Model A (Active Model A), and a population dynamics model (with two choices of noise that each break time-reversal symmetry). In both cases, we validate our analytical NNT against numerical results obtained by action minimization, with excellent agreement. NNT provide a systematic framework for constructing nucleation theories in a broad class of non-equilibrium systems from active matter, reaction-diffusion systems and population dynamics.

</details>


### [322] [A universal emulator for planar Ising lattices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05308)
*Riccardo Ben Alì Zinati,Alessandro Codello*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出一种“伊辛模拟器（Ising emulator）”概念，通过将二维伊辛模型（Ising models）的平面、单位边长的晶格表示为单一宿主晶格的位点或键稀释超胞，利用固定的Feynman–Vdovichenko/Kac–Ward解一次性求解。作者构造了显式的正方形和三角形模拟器，并用单个转移矩阵配合二进制掩码给出铁磁和反铁磁耦合下的全部热力学量。该框架应用于所有11种阿基米德晶格（Archimedean lattices）、20种二均匀晶格（2-uniform lattices）（首次获得热力学结果）以及若干五边形晶格，并可直接推广至分形和无序伊辛模型，无需修改底层机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二维伊辛模型的精确解通常依赖于特定晶格的几何结构，不同晶格需要分别推导；现有方法缺乏一种统一、可移植的求解框架。该研究旨在建立一种通用的模拟器机制，使得不同晶格（包括均匀、非均匀、分形和无序结构）的热力学性质均可从单一宿主晶格的已知解出发，通过简单的稀释掩码获得。

Method: 提出伊辛模拟器概念：将目标晶格表示为宿主晶格的位点稀释（site-diluted）或键稀释（bond-diluted）超胞。针对正方形和三角形宿主晶格，预先固定其Feynman–Vdovichenko/Kac–Ward解析解；再通过一个统一的转移矩阵（transition matrix）和对应晶格专用的二进制掩码（binary masks），计算铁磁和反铁磁耦合下的所有热力学量。该构造方法直接适用于分形和无序伊辛模型，无需改动底层计算结构。

Result: 成功构造了正方形和三角形两种宿主晶格的伊辛模拟器。将该框架应用于全部11种阿基米德晶格、全部20种二均匀晶格（首次获得其热力学结果），以及多种五边形晶格。验证了同一套模拟器机制在分形晶格和无序伊辛模型中的直接可扩展性。

Conclusion: 伊辛模拟器提供了一种统一、高效的方法来求解多种二维晶格伊辛模型的热力学量，显著降低了对不同晶格结构逐一推导的复杂度。该方法在均匀晶格、非均匀晶格乃至分形和无序系统中均有效，具有广泛的适用性和可扩展性。

Abstract: We introduce the notion of an Ising emulator for two-dimensional Ising models: flat, unit-edge-length lattices can be represented as site- or bond-diluted supercells of a single host lattice, for which the Feynman--Vdovichenko/Kac--Ward solution is fixed once and for all. We construct explicit square and triangular emulators and show that a single transition matrix, supplemented by lattice-specific binary masks, gives all the thermodynamic quantities of interest for both ferro- and antiferromagnetic couplings. We apply the framework to all eleven Archimedean lattices, to all twenty $2$-uniform lattices -- whose thermodynamics is obtained here for the first time -- and to several pentagonal lattices, and show that the same construction extends directly to fractal and disordered Ising models, with no modification to the underlying machinery.

</details>

### [323] [Pointwise Error Estimates for Numerical Physics-Informed Neural Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03431)
*Nivar Anwer,Marien Chenaud,José Alves,Frédéric Magoulès*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 本文针对基于网格的逐段线性数值物理信息神经网络（physics-informed neural networks, PINNs），提出了一种确定性的逐点误差区间估计方法。该方法通过有限元重构获得相容场，再利用有限维数值系统生成认证残差，从而在相容方形线性系统中获得带有精确伴随格林表示的逐点误差。此外，还发展了范数化、非精确、局部化和随机化变体，并将误差界推导推广至非线性残差系统。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 物理信息神经网络（physics-informed neural networks, PINNs）通常通过有限点上的残差损失进行评估，但这类评估无法认证偏微分方程（partial differential equation, PDE）解的逐点值，因此需要一种能够提供确定性逐点误差认证的方法。

Method: 提出基于网格的逐段线性数值物理信息神经网络的确定性逐点误差区间方法。首先，对网格上的可接受预测进行有限元重构（finite-element reconstruction），得到相容场（compatible field）；然后将该相容场作用于有限维数值系统，获得认证残差（certifying residual）。对于相容方形线性系统，逐点误差具有精确的伴随格林表示（adjoint Green representation）。当精确校正不可行时，发展了范数化、非精确、局部化和随机化变体。从离散目标到连续解的扩展由比较估计提供。对于一维强制反应-扩散类，利用基于残差的显式后验估计器（a posteriori estimator）使转移层完全可计算。对于非线性残差系统，通过显式泰勒余项（Taylor remainders）扩展了误差界推导。

Result: 数值实验通过制造算例、大规模公开三维弹性力学基准测试（three-dimensional elasticity benchmark）以及同一基准上的投影神经载荷族（projected neural load families），评估了方法的相容性和校准效果。

Conclusion: 所提出的方法能够为基于网格的逐段线性PINNs提供确定性的逐点误差认证，并适用于线性和非线性系统，具有良好的可计算性和可扩展性。

Abstract: Physics-informed neural networks are often evaluated by residual losses sampled at finitely many points, which do not by themselves certify pointwise values of a partial differential equation solution. In this work, deterministic pointwise error intervals are developed for mesh-based, piecewise-linear numerical physics-informed neural networks. The proposed error estimation is given for a compatible field, which is the finite-element reconstruction of an admissible prediction on a mesh. The certifying residual is then obtained by applying the finite-dimensional numerical system to this compatible field. For compatible square linear systems, the pointwise error relative to the discrete target has an exact adjoint Green representation, and the computed signed error recovers the finite element solution exactly. Norm-based, inexact, localized, and randomized variants provide computable intervals when the exact correction computation is impractical. The extension from the discrete target to the continuous solution is supplied by comparison estimates. For a one-dimensional coercive reaction-diffusion class, this transfer layer is made fully computable by an explicit residual-based a posteriori estimator with querywise constants. The error bound derivation is extended to nonlinear residual systems with explicit Taylor remainders. Numerical experiments assess compatibility and calibration on manufactured examples, on a large-scale public three-dimensional elasticity benchmark, and on projected neural load families on the same benchmark.

</details>

### [324] [Euclidean $\vee$-systems and real PK arrangements](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04859)
*Martin de Borbon,Dmitri Panov,Alexander P. Veselov*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文建立了欧几里得 $\vee$-系统（Euclidean $\vee$-system）与实多面体凯勒（PK）超平面排列（real polyhedral Kähler arrangement）之间的一一对应关系，证明每个不可约欧几里得 $\vee$-系统决定一个实PK排列，反之亦然。基于此，刻画了固定射影类中欧几里得 $\vee$-系统的模空间同胚于一个多面体的相对内部，并证明了其关联的超平面排列是单纯（simplicial）的。此外，在已知的单纯线排列中精确识别出由 $\vee$-系统产生的那些，进而证明了对于至多27个向量的不可约秩三欧几里得 $\vee$-系统，Schreiber–Veselov分类是完备的。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 揭示欧几里得 $\vee$-系统与实多面体凯勒（PK）超平面排列这两类几何结构之间的深层联系，并利用这一对应关系解决 $\vee$-系统的分类与模空间描述问题。

Method: 建立不可约欧几里得 $\vee$-系统与实PK排列之间的双射对应；通过分析$\vee$-系统的单纯性，结合已知单纯线排列分类进行匹配识别。

Result: 证明了固定射影类中欧几里得 $\vee$-系统的模空间与一个多面体的相对内部同胚；给出了欧几里得 $\vee$-系统关联超平面排列是单纯的直接证明；在已知单纯线排列中精确识别出由$\vee$-系统产生的那些；证明了对于至多27个向量的不可约秩三欧几里得 $\vee$-系统，Schreiber–Veselov分类的完备性。

Conclusion: 欧几里得 $\vee$-系统与实PK排列之间存在本质的等价关系，这一对应可用于系统性地刻画 $\vee$-系统的模空间结构和分类，并验证了低秩情形下已有分类的完备性。

Abstract: We establish a correspondence between two structures arising in the geometry of hyperplane arrangements: Euclidean $\vee$-systems and real polyhedral Kähler (PK) arrangements. We prove that every irreducible Euclidean $\vee$-system determines a real PK arrangement, and conversely that every real PK arrangement arises this way. As a result, we show that the moduli space of Euclidean $\vee$-systems in a fixed projective class is homeomorphic to the relative interior of a polytope. We also give a direct proof that the hyperplane arrangement associated with a Euclidean $\vee$-system is simplicial. Among the currently known simplicial line arrangements, we identify precisely those that arise from $\vee$-systems. As a consequence, we prove that the Schreiber--Veselov catalog is complete for irreducible rank-three Euclidean $\vee$-systems with at most $27$ vectors.

</details>


### [325] [A conformal reduction for the X-ADM mass](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03629)
*Stephen McCormick*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文证明了X-ADM质量的正性等价于标准ADM质量的正质量定理（positive mass theorem），通过共形约化（conformal reduction）论证在所有维度上确立了X-正质量定理，并推广到带边流形情形，同时推导出广义相对论中的质量—电荷不等式（mass–charge inequality）在所有维度上的成立。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用共形约化（conformal reduction）论证，通过将X-ADM质量的正性问题转化为标准ADM质量的正质量定理问题，建立两者之间的等价关系。

Conclusion: X-ADM质量的正性与标准ADM质量的正质量定理等价，因此X-正质量定理在所有维度上成立，并可以推广至带边流形和广义相对论的质量—电荷不等式。

Abstract: The X-ADM mass is a geometric invariant for asymptotically flat manifolds, recently introduced by Mantegazza and Oronzio [arXiv:2602.11372], generalising the weighted mass of Baldauf and Ozuch [arXiv:2201.04475] which itself is a generalisation of the well-known ADM mass.
  We show that the positivity of the X-ADM mass is in fact equivalent to the standard positive mass theorem for the ADM mass by way of a conformal reduction argument, which in particular proves the X-positive mass theorem in all dimensions, which previously was only established in dimension 3 under a topological condition. As a corollary, we obtain the Riemannian mass--charge inequality of general relativity in all dimensions. Finally, we prove a version of the X-positive mass theorem for a manifold with boundary.

### [326] [The Informational Cost of Structure: Representational Complexity in Networked Dynamical Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03608)
*Cyril Rommens,Pietro Traversa,Guilherme Ferraz de Arruda,Yamir Moreno*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文利用算法信息论（algorithmic information theory）提出“表征复杂度（Representational Complexity）”概念，证明结构加规则模型相对于最短动力学描述的冗余长度构成普适下界，并分析了图与超图等网络表征在信息代价和机制透明度上的差异条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 回答一个根本性问题：表示一个动力学系统（dynamical system）的交互结构（interaction structure）和演化规则（evolution rule）究竟需要多少信息？

Method: 采用算法信息论（algorithmic information theory）框架，定义“表征复杂度（Representational Complexity）”为结构加规则模型的描述长度与动力学最短可能描述之间的冗余。在图、超图及其他形式体系间进行比较分析，并在约束条件下推导信息等价条件及不同偏好区域的出现条件。

Result: 任意精确的结构表征均无法超越由动力学内在描述定义的普适下界；若允许任意规则，图、超图等形式体系可通过在结构与规则间转移信息达到该下界，因此表达力（expressiveness）本身无法区分它们。有意义差异仅在对结构与规则施加约束时出现，可产生图偏好（graph-preferred）、超图偏好（hypergraph-preferred）及混合（mixed）三种区域。

Conclusion: 网络表征的选择应被重构为信息代价（informational cost）与机制透明度（mechanistic transparency）之间的权衡问题，而非对普适表达力的追求。由于柯尔莫哥洛夫复杂度（Kolmogorov complexity）不可计算，文中还通过显式描述长度估计对形式结果进行了补充。

Abstract: How much information is required to represent a dynamical system in terms of an interaction structure and an evolution rule? We address this question using algorithmic information theory. We introduce Representational Complexity, the excess description length of a structure-plus-rule model relative to the shortest possible description of the dynamics itself. This intrinsic description defines a universal lower bound: no exact structural representation can be more concise. If arbitrary rules are allowed, graphs, hypergraphs, and other formalisms can all reach this bound by shifting information between structure and dynamics, so expressiveness alone cannot distinguish them. Meaningful differences arise only when scientific modeling restricts the admissible structures and rules. Within this setting, we identify conditions under which graph and hypergraph descriptions are informationally equivalent, and show how graph-preferred, hypergraph-preferred, and mixed regimes can emerge when those conditions are relaxed. Because Kolmogorov complexity is not computable, we complement the formal results with explicit description-length estimates. Our framework reframes the choice of network representation as a question of informational cost and mechanistic transparency rather than universal expressive power.

</details>

### [327] [Multivariate Bayesian P-spline estimation of spectral density matrices, with application to LISA TDI noise](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04833)
*Avi Vajpeyi,Renate Meyer,Patricio Maturana-Russell,Jianan Liu*

Main category: stat.ME

TL;DR: 提出一种贝叶斯P样条（Bayesian P-spline）方法，通过频变Cholesky分解参数化逆谱矩阵，结合粗粒度Whittle似然（coarse-grained Whittle likelihood）与安全贝叶斯η-退火（safe-Bayes η-tempering）推断平稳多元时间序列的互谱密度矩阵。在合成VAR(2)数据和LISA时延干涉测量（TDI）数据上验证了方法有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多元平稳时间序列的互谱密度矩阵估计面临两个关键挑战：谱矩阵在每个频率上必须满足Hermitian正定性（Hermitian positive definiteness），且需在平滑性与拟合精度之间取得平衡。现有方法在频率域正则化和贝叶斯推断方面存在局限。

Method: 将逆谱矩阵通过频率变化的Cholesky分解（frequency-varying Cholesky decomposition）进行参数化，确保Hermitian正定性。每个实对数对角元、实部和虚部非对角元均赋予独立的惩罚B样条先验（penalised B-spline prior）以控制平滑度。推断采用分块粗粒度Whittle似然（blocked, coarse-grained Whittle likelihood）并配合safe-Bayes η-退火稳定后验校准，通过No-U-Turn采样器（NUTS）从变分初始化（variational initialisation）进行采样。

Result: 在合成VAR(2)基准测试中，方法恢复了对角谱和互谱结构，达到接近名义值的可信区间覆盖率（credible-interval coverage），相对积分平方（Frobenius）误差（RISE）随样本量增加而减小。在LISA TDI数据中：理想对称噪声下，完整多元模型与假设对角AET噪声协方差的简化模型在RISE上差异约10⁻³；非对称真实噪声下，AET对角假设的RISE（~3.3×10⁻²）比完整模型（~10⁻³）差一个数量级以上。

Conclusion: 所提出的贝叶斯P样条方法能够有效估计多元谱矩阵，在合成数据和真实物理实验数据（LISA TDI）中均表现良好；在非对称噪声场景下，完整多元模型显著优于简化对角假设模型。

Abstract: We present a Bayesian P-spline method for estimating the frequency-dependent cross-spectral density matrix of stationary multivariate time series. The inverse spectral matrix is parametrised through its frequency-varying Cholesky decomposition, which guarantees Hermitian positive definiteness at every frequency. Each real log-diagonal entry and each real and imaginary off-diagonal entry is given an independent penalised B-spline prior that controls smoothness. Inference uses a blocked, coarse-grained Whittle likelihood with safe-Bayes $η$-tempering to stabilise posterior calibration, sampled by the No-U-Turn Sampler from a variational initialisation. On synthetic VAR(2) benchmarks with known ground truth, the method recovers both diagonal and cross-spectral structure, attains near-nominal credible-interval coverage, and achieves a relative integrated squared (Frobenius) error (RISE) that decreases with sample size. We then apply the method to publicly released simulated LISA time-delay interferometry (TDI) data in two noise configurations. In the idealised symmetric case, the full multivariate model and a reduced model that assumes a diagonal AET noise covariance agree to within $\sim10^{-3}$ in RISE. Under realistic noise that is asymmetric across the six Movable Optical Sub-Assemblies (MOSAs), the AET-diagonal assumption fails by more than an order of magnitude in RISE ($\sim\!3.3\!\times\!10^{-2}$ versus $\sim\!10^{-3}$), whereas the full multivariate model recovers the cross-spectral structure.

</details>

### [328] [Higher order Weyl coefficients for the operator curl](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03273)
*Giovanni Bracchi,Matteo Capoferri,Dmitri Vassiliev*

Main category: math.SP

TL;DR: 本文为定向闭黎曼3-流形上的旋度算子（curl operator）建立了精细的谱渐近（refined spectral asymptotics），分别处理正负特征值，得到前六个整体Weyl系数（global Weyl coefficients）的显式公式，并据此证明了旋度算子的eta函数（eta function）在复半平面 Re s > -2 上全纯，以及在测地流假设下改进了Bär的渐近公式，将余项优化至 o(λ²)。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旋度算子在三维流形上的谱理论是微分几何与数学物理交叉领域的重要课题。此前Bär已建立其Weyl渐近公式，但更高阶系数和余项估计尚未明确。本文旨在获得更精细的谱渐近展开，并探讨其与全局不变量（如eta函数）的关系。

Method: 采用谱渐近分析（spectral asymptotics）与伪微分算子技术，对正负特征值分别处理；通过局部Weyl系数（local Weyl coefficients）与整体Weyl系数的计算，推导出前六个系数的显式表达式，并利用eta函数的解析延拓性质分析其全纯区域。

Result: 获得了前六个整体Weyl系数的显式公式；对于局部Weyl系数，计算了前四个及第六个系数，第五个系数则确定至一个普适常数（universal constant）。证明了旋度算子的eta函数（局部与整体版本）在 Re s > -2 上全纯。在测地流（geodesic flow）的适当假设下，将正负计数函数的余项从原Bär结果的阶改进为 o(λ²)。

Conclusion: 本文建立的精细谱渐近结果揭示了旋度算子谱结构与流形几何之间的深层联系，eta函数的全纯性为理解该算子的谱不对称性（spectral asymmetry）提供了新信息，而余项改进则对进一步研究三维拓扑不变量和量子场论中的反常（anomaly）问题具有参考价值。

Abstract: We establish refined spectral asymptotics for the operator curl acting on a connected oriented closed Riemannian 3-manifold. We treat positive and negative eigenvalues separately and obtain explicit formulae for the first six global Weyl coefficients. With local Weyl coefficients we compute the first four coefficients as well as the sixth one, and we determine the fifth up to a universal constant. As a consequence, we prove that the eta function of curl (both in its local and global versions) is holomorphic in the complex half-plane $\operatorname{Re}s>-2$. Finally, under appropriate assumptions on the geodesic flow, we improve Bär's asymptotic formulae for the positive and negative counting functions, refining the remainder to $o(λ^2)$.

### [329] [Localization and unique continuation for the Anderson-Bernoulli model with long-range hopping on $\mathbb{Z}$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03472)
*Shihe Liu,Yunfeng Shi,Zhifei Zhang*

Main category: math.SP

TL;DR: 本文研究了具有长程跳跃（long-range hopping）的Anderson-Bernoulli模型在谱边附近的Anderson局域化（Anderson localization）现象。对于具有有理Laurent符号的跳跃，可证明唯一延拓原理（unique continuation principle）的定量版本并实现局域化；对于一般情形，给出了反例并证明了跳跃衰减快于指数率时的较弱结果。这是首次针对纯Bernoulli势的长程Anderson模型获得局域化结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长程跳跃下的Anderson局域化问题在数学物理中具有重要理论意义，但以往研究多集中于短程或独立势情形。本文旨在填补纯Bernoulli势（pure Bernoulli potentials）长程Anderson模型在谱边附近局域化证明的空白。

Method: 采用定量版唯一延拓原理（quantitative unique continuation principle）作为核心分析工具，该原理在跳跃具有有理Laurent符号（rational Laurent symbol）时成立；对于更一般的跳跃情形，则通过构造反例与分析指数级更快衰减的跳跃来推导较弱的局域化结论。

Result: 当跳跃具有有理Laurent符号时，证明了谱边附近Anderson局域化的存在；对于一般跳跃情形，给出了唯一延拓原理失效的反例，并证明了在跳跃衰减快于指数率（decays faster than exponential rate）时存在一个较弱的局域化结果。

Conclusion: 该工作首次为纯Bernoulli势的长程Anderson模型建立了局域化结果，揭示了跳跃符号的有理性与唯一延拓原理可证性之间的关键联系，并为后续研究更一般长程无序系统的局域化性质提供了分析框架。

Abstract: In this paper, we study Anderson localization near the spectral edge for the Anderson-Bernoulli model on $\mathbb{Z}$ with long-range hopping. When the hopping has a rational Laurent symbol, a quantitative version of the unique continuation principle can be proved, and localization occurs. For the unique continuation in the general case, we give some counterexamples and prove a weaker result for hopping that decays faster than exponential rate. To the best of our knowledge, this is the first localization result for the long-range Anderson model with pure Bernoulli potentials.

### [330] [Cellular Adaptation to Signal Fluctuations as Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03545)
*Tuan Minh Pham,David Saad*

Main category: q-bio.MN

TL;DR: 本文通过构建细胞内信号通路的多尺度模型，推导出描述其组分间协变关系的宏观理论，揭示了细胞通过自调节（self-regulation）而非简单噪声抑制来应对外界信号波动、实现稳健输出的机制，该机制对应于超越临界适应率（critical adaptation rate）时从随机集体模（random collective modes）向结构化集体模（structured collective modes）的转变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 细胞作为生命基本单位，能在不同细胞类型之间以及化学信号的时间波动等环境变化下维持稳健表现。为理解单个细胞如何利用基因调控网络（gene-regulatory network）与上游信号转导子（signal transducers）之间的反馈回路实现基因表达的自调节，需要建立能够刻画这一动态互关系的理论框架。

Method: 本研究首先构建了一个多尺度模型（multiscale model），其中负责信号解读的自适应变量遵循反馈诱导的学习过程（feedback-induced learning process）。在此基础上，推导出一个宏观理论，用于捕捉这些组分之间的协变关系，即所谓的集体模（collective modes）。

Result: 该理论表明，细胞并非通过简单的噪声抑制来抵抗信号波动，而是借助自调节实现稳健输出。这种稳健性对应于当适应率超过某个临界值时，系统从随机集体模向结构化集体模的转变。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了细胞内信号通路中自调节的集体动力学机制，为理解细胞在环境波动下的稳健性提供了理论依据：关键机制在于超越临界适应率后，集体模从无序走向结构化。

Abstract: Cells represent one of the most fundamental units of life. Underlying their robust performance against environmental variability, such as temporal fluctuations of chemical signals, between different cell types, is a dynamical interrelation between the two components of an intracellular pathway: a gene-regulatory network and its upstream signal transducers. To understand how a single cell utilizes this feedback to self-regulate its gene-expressions, we develop a multiscale model of the pathway's components, in which the adaptive variables responsible for signal interpretation follow a feedback-induced learning process. We then derive a macroscopic theory capturing the covariations between these components - so-called collective modes. Our theory shows how cells can achieve robust output against signal fluctuations via self-regulation rather than simple noise suppression. Such robustness corresponds to a transition from random- to structured collective modes beyond a critical adaptation rate.

### [331] [Time-Dependent Integrability from Gauge Theory, I](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02648)
*Shota Komatsu,Jun-ichi Sakamoto,Anders Wallberg,Masahito Yamazaki*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文证明四维Chern-Simons理论通过将全纯一次形式推广为时空依赖的一般一次形式，为构造可解含时系统提供了统一框架，并揭示了含时性与单圈重整化群流之间的普适关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 可解含时系统（solvable time-dependent systems）对非平衡物理研究和量子模拟基准测试至关重要，但精确解极为罕见。现有方法多针对特定模型，缺乏统一构造框架。

Method: 将四维Chern-Simons理论（four-dimensional Chern-Simons theory）中标准的全纯一次形式推广为更一般的时空依赖一次形式（spacetime-dependent one-form），系统性地生成含时可积场论（time-dependent integrable field theories）。

Result: 建立了一种普适关系：按此方法得到的每个理论中，允许的含时性恰好与单圈重整化群流（one-loop renormalization group flow）一致。这些理论尽管显式含时，仍保持Lax可积性（Lax integrability）并可通过逆散射方法（inverse scattering methods）求解。该构造同时适用于超局域（ultralocal）与非超局域（non-ultralocal）理论，并将此前已知的含时sigma模型推广到更广泛的可积系统类别。此外，该构造可改写为与物质场耦合的膨胀引力（dilaton gravity），从而产生一大类二维经典可积的膨胀引力理论。

Conclusion: 四维Chern-Simons理论为构造含时可积场论提供了统一框架，揭示了含时模型与重整化群流之间的深层联系，并连接了凝聚态物理中的含时可积系统以及降维爱因斯坦引力（Einstein gravity）导出的非自治可积系统（non-autonomous integrable systems）。

Abstract: Solvable time-dependent systems provide important settings for studying non-equilibrium physics, where exact results are rare. They are also useful for benchmarking quantum simulations, which can directly probe real-time dynamics beyond the reach of conventional numerical approaches. In this paper, we show that the four-dimensional Chern-Simons theory offers a natural and unifying framework for constructing such systems. Focusing on classically integrable field theories, we consider a generalization of the four-dimensional Chern-Simons theory in which the usual holomorphic one-form is replaced by a more general, spacetime-dependent one-form. This yields a systematic procedure for generating time-dependent integrable field theories and establishes a universal relation: for every theory obtained in this way, the allowed time dependence coincides with the one-loop renormalization group flow. Despite the explicit time dependence, these theories retain Lax integrability and remain solvable by inverse scattering methods. Our construction applies to both ultralocal and non-ultralocal theories and extends previously known time-dependent sigma models to a much broader class of integrable systems. It also admits rewriting as dilaton gravity coupled to matter, producing a large family of classically integrable dilaton gravity theories in two dimensions. We also comment on connections to time-dependent integrable models studied recently in condensed matter physics and non-autonomous integrable systems arising from dimensionally-reduced Einstein gravity.

</details>


### [332] [The giant graviton expansion in AdS$_5\times$SE$_5$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02658)
*Alfredo González Lezcano,Leopoldo A. Pando Zayas,Augniva Ray*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究AdS$_5\times$SE$_5$背景中的巨引力子（giant graviton）D3膜探针构型，重点分析五维Sasaki-Einstein流形SE$_5$的结构。通过横向Kähler势（transverse Kähler potential）将问题一般化，发现最大角动量构型可由横向Kähler势发散的位置描述。对特定激发进行量子化后，得到带有锥形亏缺（conical deficit）的Fock-Darwin问题，推广了$S^5$情形下的Landau问题。对AdS$_5\times T^{1,1}$情形，恢复了对偶标量超共形场论（quiver ${\cal N}=1$ superconformal field theory）在非阿贝尔量子化自由度所捕获扇区中的有限N受保护指标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究AdS/CFT对偶中巨引力子构型在更一般背景（SE$_5$而非仅$S^5$）下的行为，探索Sasaki-Einstein流形的几何信息如何编码在量子化描述中，并计算对超共形指标（superconformal index）的受保护贡献。

Method: 将巨引力子D3膜视为IIB型超引力背景AdS$_5\times$SE$_5$中的探针构型，利用横向Kähler势形式化描述；选取最大角动量构型，通过横向Kähler势发散的位置描述；对类似AdS$_5\times S^5$情形中的特定激发进行量子化，得到包含锥形亏缺的Fock-Darwin问题。

Result: SE$_5$的几何信息编码在外部势（external potential）和锥形亏缺的形式中；对AdS$_5\times T^{1,1}$情形，计算得到了对偶标量超共形场论中非阿贝尔量子化自由度扇区的有限N受保护指标。

Conclusion: 巨引力子构型在SE$_5$上的描述自然地推广了$S^5$情形，锥形亏缺和外部势构成了SE$_5$几何信息在量子化问题中的体现；该方法可用于计算更一般Sasaki-Einstein对偶中受保护超共形指标的部分贡献。

Abstract: We study giant graviton-like D3-branes as probe configurations in type IIB supergravity backgrounds AdS$_5\times$SE$_5$, with emphasis on the structure of the five-dimensional Sasaki-Einstein manifolds SE$_5$. These configurations wrap supersymmetric three-cycles in SE$_5$ and rotate at the speed of light along the Reeb direction. We formulate the general problem in terms of the transverse Kähler potential and show that configurations carrying maximal angular momentum can be described by loci where the transverse Kähler potential diverges in suitably chosen coordinates. We quantize a particular set of excitations, similar to those considered in the AdS$_5\times S^5$ case, and show that they are governed by a Fock-Darwin problem with a conical deficit, which generalizes the Landau problem obtained for $S^5$. Succinctly, the information about the geometry of SE$_5$ is encoded in the form of the external potential and the conical deficit. We compute a protected contribution to the superconformal index arising from quantized fluctuations of supersymmetric giant graviton configurations. For the explicit case of AdS$_5\times T^{1,1}$, we recover the finite-N protected index of the dual quiver ${\cal N}=1$ superconformal field theory in the sector captured by a non-Abelian generalization of the quantized degrees of freedom.

</details>


### [333] [Holographic Learning from Fermionic Spectra: Application to Strange Metal Phenomenology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02861)
*Hong-Zhi Xiao,Zhan-Zhi He,Zhuo-Yu Xian,Shao-Feng Wu*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出基于神经常微分方程（Neural ODEs）的数据驱动框架，利用边界费米子谱函数（fermionic spectral functions）学习静态平面对称黑洞的体度规（bulk metric）函数和U(1)规范势，并成功应用于铜氧化物超导体的奇异金属相分析，发现其可由近AdS₂×ℝ²黑洞有效描述。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 构建从边界量子系统（如奇异金属）的谱数据学习体几何（bulk geometry）的逆向数据驱动方法，以探索全息对偶（holographic duality）在凝聚态物理中的应用。

Method: 基于神经常微分方程（Neural ODEs）框架，从边界费米子谱函数反推体度规函数和U(1)规范势；在爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦（Einstein–Maxwell）和古布泽-罗查（Gubser–Rocha）模型上验证后，在半全息（semi-holographic）框架下应用于铜氧化物（Pb,Bi）₂Sr₂₋ₓLaₓCuO₆₊δ的奇异金属相，使用扩展幂律液体（extended power-law liquid, PLL）模型生成的谱数据。

Result: 在低温近最佳掺杂条件下，归一化扩展PLL模型可由近AdS₂×ℝ²黑洞的有效共形类代表良好描述，其规范势近乎为零（qA_t∼10⁻⁴ eV）；探测费米子是无质量的，因此对共形因子Ω(z)不敏感；框架适用性在低温下跨越不同掺杂，向过掺杂方向偏离边际费米液体点（marginal Fermi liquid point）时损失轻微增大，温度为主要限制因素。

Conclusion: 该数据驱动框架可从费米子谱数据有效学习黑洞体几何，但需独立输入（如电子比热）才能固定宏观热力学；其适用范围受温度主导，在低温掺杂区间表现稳健。

Abstract: We develop a data-driven framework based on Neural ODEs that learns the bulk metric functions and the $U(1)$ gauge potential of a static, planar-symmetric black hole from boundary fermionic spectral functions. After validating the framework on the Einstein--Maxwell and Gubser--Rocha models with high accuracy, we apply it to the strange metal phase of the cuprate $\mathrm{(Pb,Bi)_2Sr_{2-x}La_xCuO_{6+δ}}$ within a semi-holographic setting, taking as input the spectral data generated from the extended power-law liquid (PLL) model calibrated by angle-resolved photoemission measurements. At low temperatures and near-optimal doping, we show that the normalized extended PLL model can be well described by an effective representative of a conformal class near $\mathrm{AdS}_{2}\times\mathbb{R}^{2}$ black holes with a nearly vanishing gauge potential ($qA_t\sim10^{-4}\,\mathrm{eV}$). A key structural observation is that our probe fermion is massless and therefore insensitive to the conformal factor $Ω(z)$. This further implies that fixing the macroscopic thermodynamics such as the electronic specific heat would require independent input beyond the fermionic spectra. We also delineate the applicability boundaries of our framework: the learned effective model remains viable across doping at low temperatures, with the loss increasing mildly as the samples move away from the marginal Fermi liquid point toward the overdoped side; the principal limitation is temperature, where both the loss and $qA_t$ grow substantially.

Conclusion: 神经网络与场论之间存在一种自然的对偶关系：场论视角有助于理解神经网络，而神经网络的计算框架可以反过来实现并扩展场论的分析工具。这种双向交叉在基础物理（尤其是弦论）中具有广阔的应用前景。

Abstract: These notes are based on six lectures given over three days at the Pre-Strings 2026 school in Shanghai. Day 1 develops neural network essentials, organized around the expressivity, statistics, and dynamics of neural networks, presented with a field-theoretic lens. Day 2 develops a neural network approach to field theory (NN-FT), in which a field theory is defined by a network architecture and a density on its parameters, and surveys recent results. Examples include a universality theorem, a neural network realization of Liouville theory, famous string amplitudes, topological sectors and the Kosterlitz-Thouless transition, Ward identities and anomalies, and a new derivation of the critical dimension of the bosonic string. Day 3 turns the lens around and covers applied AI for string theory: agentic workflows that are changing how the other techniques are implemented, physics-informed neural networks and Calabi-Yau metrics, reinforcement learning and search in the string landscape and in knot theory, and interpretable supervised learning with an eye towards conjecture generation.

### [335] [Null-strings Gauged, Reloaded and Quantized, I: Canonical Quantization in the Light-Cone Gauge](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02970)
*Ida M. Rasulian,M. M. Sheikh-Jabbari,H. Yavartanoo*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了平直靶时空中零弦（null-string）的光锥量子化（light-cone quantization），通过引入卡洛尔-外尔规范对称性（Carroll-Weyl gauge symmetry）及其约束结构，将物理相空间约化至(D-3)个传播自由度（propagating degrees of freedom），并发现零弦具有离散谱且不存在临界维度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 零弦作为弦论中一种重要的极限情形，其量子化问题尚未被充分理解。已有研究多沿用标准弦的光锥规范，但未充分考虑零弦特有的规范对称性及其约束结构，导致对物理自由度（degrees of freedom, DoF）的刻画可能不完整。

Method: 在D维平直靶时空中，研究者将零弦的额外规范对称性（Carroll-Weyl规范对称性）和对应的约束结构纳入光锥规范，从而比标准光锥规范多解除一个自由度；量子化直接在薛定谔表象（Schrödinger representation）中实施，在约化后的位形空间上构造波函数所需的希尔伯特空间（Hilbert space），物理态空间建立于修正后的规范结构所对应的约化相空间之上。

Result: 零弦展现出离散谱（discrete spectrum），这是一个显著且出人意料的结果；此外，分析表明零弦不存在临界维度（critical dimension），维度D可以取任意值。

Conclusion: 被忽略的Carroll-Weyl规范对称性是零弦量子化的关键要素，它导致了离散谱的存在，并消除了对临界维度的要求，从而为任意维度的零弦量子化提供了自洽框架。

Abstract: We study the light-cone quantization of null-strings in $D$ dimensional flat target-space. Incorporating the essential new gauge symmetry and the associated constraint structure of the null-string, allows one to solve for one more degree of freedom (DoF) compared to the standard light-cone gauge, reducing the physical phase space to $(D-3)$ propagating DoF. Quantization is formulated directly in the Schrödinger representation, leading to a Hilbert space of wavefunctions on the reduced configuration space. The space of physical states is built on a reduced phase space associated with the corrected gauge structure. We discuss the ground-state wavefunction and a generic class of excited states. As a direct consequence of the overlooked Carroll-Weyl gauge symmetry of the null-strings, we find the remarkable and perhaps unexpected result that null-strings exhibit a discrete spectrum. Our analysis indicate that there is no critical dimension for null-strings, and $D$ can be arbitrary.

Abstract: We study a graph classification problem involving over 20 million graphs, arising from high-order perturbative computations of correlators in planar $\mathcal{N}=4$ super-Yang--Mills, a model closely related to the theory of the strong nuclear force. We benchmark graph neural networks, including graph transformers, achieving robust generalization to larger graphs with up to $99.996\%$ ROC AUC. Then, we analyze how the models can be used to gain a computational speedup compared to the traditional graphical bootstrap algorithm, through shrinking the redundant data by up to $85.5\%$ at the level of denominator graphs. ### [337] [Exact Schwarzian Metric Factor and Holographic Wilson-Loop Screening](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03120)
*Miguel Tierz*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文精确计算了极值Reissner-Nordström AdS$_5$黑膜的AdS$_2$喉区中Schwarzian平均生成的径向度量因子$h(ζ)$，得到了以Appell-Lerch级数表示的精确解，并证明了该几何不存在约束极小值——该极小值是由有限近边界截断产生的赝像。精确喉区几何给出的Wilson圈行为呈现代数屏蔽，标志着极端RN膜的半局域量子液体红外相。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在极端Reissner-Nordström AdS$_5$黑膜的AdS$_2$喉区中，Schwarzian平均被广泛用于构建有效几何，但以往仅通过有限近边界截断（near-boundary truncation）近似处理，导致非微扰效应（nonperturbative effects）缺失，并可能引入赝像（artifacts）。本文旨在精确求解该问题，检验截断近似的可靠性。

Method: 精确求解径向度量因子$h(ζ)$的Schwarzian平均，将其化为对$\coth(πy)$的高斯积分；利用Mordell恒等式（Mordell's identity）将其变换为精确的Appell-Lerch $q/q^\ast$级数表示；从积分表示出发证明$\mathcal{G}_0(ζ):=h(ζ)/ζ^2$的完全单调性（complete monotonicity）；计算Schwarzian核的相对方差（relative variance）以量化近似误差。

Result: 精确解包含非微扰尺度$e^{-π^2 C/ζ}$，该尺度被任何有限近边界截断所遗漏；求导过程中出现了经典Mordell恒等式不包含的拟模Eisenstein级数$E_2$（quasimodular Eisenstein series）。$\mathcal{G}_0(ζ)$完全单调，因而无内部极小值，故有限截断产生的约束极小值（confining minimum）为赝像。精确喉区的Wilson圈行为为$E(L)\sim -κ_{\rm IR}/L^2$，即代数屏蔽（algebraic screening），而非截断近似给出的常力（constant-force）行为。数值检验确认屏蔽鞍点为主要弦构型。

Conclusion: 有限近边界截断会遗漏非微扰贡献并引入赝像，精确解证实AdS$_2$喉区几何不产生约束极小值，对应极端RN膜的半局域量子液体（semi-local quantum liquid）红外相。这为AdS/CFT对偶中精确处理红外几何提供了严格基础，并指出需谨慎对待截断近似的结论。

Abstract: We evaluate exactly the radial metric factor $h(ζ)$ generated by Schwarzian averaging in the AdS$_2$ throat of an extremal Reissner--Nordström AdS$_5$ black brane. The result is a Gaussian integral against $\coth(πy)$, valid at all radial depths, which Mordell's identity turns into an exact Appell--Lerch $q/q^\ast$-series representation. The dual series identifies the nonperturbative scale $e^{-π^2 C/ζ}$ missed by any finite near-boundary truncation. The third parametric derivative required by the evaluation generates the quasimodular Eisenstein series $E_2$, absent from the classical Mordell identity. From the integral representation we prove that $\mathcal{G}_0(ζ):=h(ζ)/ζ^2$ is completely monotone and hence has no interior minimum, so any confining minimum produced by a finite near-boundary truncation is an artifact. We also compute the exact relative variance of the Schwarzian kernel, which makes the averaged-metric approximation error quantitative and shows that the absence of a confining minimum is robust across moment-based effective geometries. Applied to the temporal rectangular Wilson loop, the exact throat gives algebraic screening, $E(L)\sim -κ_{\rm IR}/L^2$, the Wilson-loop diagnostic of the semi-local quantum-liquid IR of the extremal RN brane. A numerical check in a simple matched geometry confirms that the screened saddle is the dominant string configuration, and an exact-versus-truncated force comparison shows that the apparent constant-force regime of the fourth-order truncation is not a feature of the exact geometry.

</details>


### [338] [Singularities, Entropy and the Arrow of Time, {\it or} Is CRT a Gauge Symmetry in Quantum Gravity?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03199)
*T. Banks*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究离散变换CRT是否构成“量子引力”（Quantum Gravity）中的规范对称性（gauge symmetry）。结论是通常为否：在渐近平直和AdS时空中，CRT是渐近规范对称性；在永恒dS时空中，若允许“Alice弦”构型，则可视为自发破缺的规范对称性，但受量子测量和半经典引力限制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探讨CRT（电荷共轭-空间反射-时间反演）离散变换是否可作为量子引力理论中的一种规范对称性，以澄清量子引力中对称性的基本结构。

Method: 首先界定提问的具体理论框架（渐近平直时空、反德西特（AdS）时空、永恒德西特（dS）时空），然后分别分析CRT在各框架下的对称性角色，并考虑热场双态（Thermofield double）希尔伯特空间中的“Alice弦”构型以及Chern-Simons重写方案。

Result: 在渐近平直和AdS空间中，CRT是渐近规范对称性（asymptotic gauge symmetry），与庞加莱/AdS等距群（isometry groups）的连续部分及标量内禀对称性（scalar internal symmetries）地位相同。在永恒dS空间中，若允许Alice弦构型，CRT可视为自发破缺的规范对称性（spontaneously broken gauge symmetry），但该解释仅当底层量子力学是时间无关（time independent）时才有意义。

Conclusion: CRT在量子引力中通常不是规范对称性，仅在某些特定框架下可被如此理解。此外，量子测量和半经典引力对测量设备施加先验限制，使得沿经典dS测地线测量固有时（proper time）的探测器（含时钟）实际上无法实现。

Abstract: We examine the question of whether the discrete transformation CRT is a gauge symmetry of ``Quantum Gravity". Since the phrase in quotes is not yet completely well defined, we first try to define specific frameworks in which one might ask the question. We find that the general answer is NO. In asymptotically flat and AdS spaces, CRT is an asymptotic gauge symmetry in the same sense that the continuous parts of the Poincare/AdS isometry groups and scalar internal symmetries are. In eternal dS space it can be considered a spontaneously broken gauge symmetry if a certain ``Alice String" configuration is allowed in the Thermofield double Hilbert space. This requires an extension of the conventional Chern-Simons rewriting of $2 + 1$ dimensional gravity. This interpretation only makes sense if we consider the underlying quantum mechanics to be time independent. General quantum measurement and semi-classical gravitational restrictions on measuring devices put {\it a priori} limits on the existence of detectors with clocks that can actually measure proper time along a classical dS geodesic.

</details>


### [339] [Falling through the horizon of a quantum black hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03344)
*Victor Franken,Thomas G. Mertens,Bruno de S. L. Torres*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在量子JT引力（quantum JT gravity）框架下，研究了一个穿过近极端黑洞（near-extremal black hole）视界的坠落探测器所受到的量子引力效应。通过引力修饰（gravitational dressing）来定义视界内外的局域可观测量，发现探测器能够局域地确定视界位置及其温度，从而违反等效原理（equivalence principle），但不会遇到火墙（firewall）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探讨量子引力效应对等效原理的修正，特别是研究坠入黑洞的探测器能否在视界附近区分局部惯性系与非惯性系，以及此类效应是否会导致火墙悖论（firewall paradox）的解决或加剧。

Method: 在量子JT引力框架下，利用引力修饰（gravitational dressing）方法定义微分同胚不变的坠落轨迹和局域可观测量；在外区将修饰与Schwarzian模（Schwarzian mode）相关联，并扩展至黑洞内区；在热场双态（thermofield double state）中构造两端同时修饰的局域可观测量。

Result: 引力修饰将近视界区域与Schwarzian理论的红外扇区（IR sector）耦合，导致探测器在靠近视界时能够局域测量视界位置和温度，从而违反等效原理；但该过程并未产生火墙。

Conclusion: 量子JT引力中的引力修饰效应会破坏等效原理，使坠落探测器能够感知视界，但这种违反并不伴随火墙的出现，暗示量子引力对黑洞视界的修正可能比火墙模型所设想的更为温和。

Abstract: We study quantum-gravitational effects on the response of an infalling detector as it crosses the horizon of a near-extremal black hole in the framework of quantum JT gravity. These effects are incorporated via the gravitational dressing needed to define both the infalling trajectory and the local observables probed by the detector in a diffeomorphism-invariant way. In the black hole exterior, a preferred choice of dressing to the Schwarzian mode of JT gravity can be motivated in connection to geometric modular flow. We show how to extend this dressing to the black hole interior, defining local observables that are gravitationally dressed to both boundaries in the thermofield double state. The gravitational dressing connects the near-horizon region to the IR sector of the Schwarzian theory, leading to measurable effects as the horizon is approached. We find that the infalling detector is able to locally determine the location of the horizon and its temperature, violating the equivalence principle, but without encountering a firewall.

### [340] [Berry Picking: Random Wave Chaos Hierarchy for BPS Microstate Geometries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03434)
*Vladan Djukić,Milica Stepanović,Mihailo Čubrović*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究不同超对称性和AdS喉长度变化的超引力背景中探针波与测地线的混沌强度，发现波混沌随超对称性降低和喉部增长而增强（趋近黑洞解），而测地线运动反而更规则；通过Berry随机波假设和庞加莱截面解释了这种二分性，并指出边界CFT的Rényi熵不具有普适趋势，表明BPS混沌层级在体理论与场论中表现不同，不能简单外推至黑洞。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究从高度超对称背景到黑洞解过渡过程中混沌强度的变化趋势，以及体理论（bulk）中的波混沌与测地线混沌、边界场论中的熵复杂性之间的关联与差异。

Method: 在LLM几何、超管（supertubes）和超纹层（superstrata）等不同超引力背景中，估算探针波和探针测地线的混沌强度；通过Berry随机波假设（Berry random wave hypothesis）检验波混沌，通过计算庞加莱截面（Poincare sections）检验测地线混沌；在弱耦合区计算对偶CFT态的Rényi熵（Renyi entropies）。

Result: 波混沌随超对称性降低和AdS喉长度增加而增强；测地线混沌呈现相反趋势，运动更规则。波与测地线行为的二分性源于长喉内部存在稳定周期轨道，同时KAM环面（KAM tori）整体测度减小。边界CFT的Rényi熵无普适趋势，其复杂度取决于态的具体特征而非仅超对称性和喉长度。

Conclusion: BPS混沌的层级结构在体理论和边界场论中表现不同，两种情况均不能简单外推至黑洞情形。

Abstract: We estimate the strength of chaos of probe waves and probe geodesics in different smooth supergravity backgrounds of decreasing supersymmetry and/or increasing length of the AdS throat in the interior (LLM geometry, supertubes, superstrata). We find that the wave chaos becomes stronger and stronger with less supersymetry and longer throats; in other words, chaos becomes stronger as we approach black hole solutions. Geodesic motion shows the opposite trend, becoming more and more regular. Testing the wave chaos by its compliance with the Berry random wave hypothesis and the geodesic chaos by computing Poincare sections, we explain the dichotomy between wave and geodesic motion by the existence of stable periodic orbits inside long throats while the overall measure of KAM tori decreases. Computing the Renyi entropies for the dual CFT states in the weak coupling regime, we show that they do not have such universal trends and the complexity depends on the specifics of the state rather than just the amount of supersymmetry and throat length. We conclude that the hierarchy of BPS chaos works differently in the bulk and in field theory, and in either case cannot be simply extrapolated to black holes.

### [341] [Finite path integral limits work in cases where the perturbative series is not Borel summable](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03439)
*Ariel Edery*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究在场论和量子力学中，当微扰级数（perturbative series）非波莱尔可求和（non-Borel summable）时，有限路径积分极限（finite path integral limits）方法是否仍能给出收敛级数。通过一个具有双阱势（double-well）的基本积分实例，分别在原点（局域极大值）和一个极小值附近展开微扰级数，两种展开在有限积分限下均绝对收敛，并在极限趋于无穷时精确还原原积分的解析表达式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子场论与量子力学中观测量的微扰展开通常得到渐近级数（asymptotic series），当系统具有非平庸真空结构（non-trivial vacuum structure）时，该级数非波莱尔可求和。近期研究表明，在有限路径积分极限下可得到收敛级数，但该工作仅针对波莱尔可求和（Borel summable）情形。本文旨在初步回答：有限积分极限方法是否适用于非波莱尔可求和情形。

Method: 以具有双阱形状、存在两个极小值的基本积分为模型系统，该积分存在精确解析表达式作为参照。设定有限积分限从 -L 到 L（L 为有限正实数），分别沿两种路径构建耦合常数幂次微扰级数：一是围绕原点（局部极大值）展开，二是围绕其中一个极小值展开。

Result: 两种微扰展开在有限积分限下均得到绝对收敛级数（absolutely convergent series），且当 L 趋于无穷时，级数求和结果精确还原原积分的解析表达式。特别地，围绕其中一个极小值的微扰展开同样恢复了精确解析表达式，表明该展开捕获了两个极小值的全部效应。

Conclusion: 在非波莱尔可求和情形下，有限积分极限方法仍能产生收敛级数并正确还原精确结果。围绕单个极小值的微扰展开能够完整反映双阱结构的整体贡献，这为将该方法推广至更复杂的量子场论系统（如具有非平庸真空结构的理论）提供了初步证据。

Abstract: The perturbative expansion in powers of the coupling of observables in quantum field theory and quantum mechanics is known to yield an asymptotic series. If the original physical system is well-behaved and a finite observable is expected, this can often be calculated via a Borel resummation of the asymptotic series. However, there are cases where a system is well-behaved and the series is not Borel summable. This typically occurs when the physical system has a non-trivial vacuum structure. It has recently been shown that if the perturbative series is carried out under finite path integral limits, one can obtain a convergent series that yields observables even at strong coupling. This was recently used to obtain the energy at strong coupling for the anharmonic oscillator. This is a Borel summable case so the question is whether finite path integral limits work when the series is not Borel summable. To begin answering this question we consider a simple non-Borel summable case: the series stemming from a basic integral where the function has a double-well shape and hence two minima. The integral has an exact analytical expression that the series can be compared to. Under finite integral limits that run from $-L$ to $L$, where $L$ is finite, positive and real, we develop two perturbative series in powers of the coupling: one by expanding the integral about the local maximum at the origin and the other by expanding it about one of the minima. In both cases, we obtain an absolutely convergent series and the series sums to the exact analytical expression of the original integral in the infinite $L$ limit. It is significant that a perturbative expansion about one of the minima reproduces the exact analytical expression because this implies that it captures the full effect of both minima.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 黑洞模拟体（black hole mimickers）作为无视界的超致密天体，其形成需要在施瓦西半径（Schwarzschild radius）量级的尺度上发生量子力学隧穿（quantum mechanical tunneling）。然而，这样的隧穿过程在上述尺度下概率极低，因此需要一种有效的放大机制来使其在物理上可行。本文旨在提出并论证一种基于量子混沌（quantum chaos）的催化机制，以大幅提升隧穿透射率，从而解释黑洞模拟体的形成。

Method: 提出了一种基于多通道增强（multichannel enhancement）并用量子混沌动力学（quantum chaotic dynamics）催化的机制，该机制能够显著放大跨隧穿势垒（tunneling barrier）的量子力学透射率。具体以弦论中的黑壳（black shell）成核（nucleation）过程为例，分析了该机制的增强效果。

Result: 该多通道增强机制可显著提升弦论黑壳的成核概率；作者预期类似结果也适用于其他类型的黑洞模拟体。

Conclusion: 量子混沌催化的多通道增强机制为黑洞模拟体的形成提供了可行的隧穿放大路径，有望在广义相对论（general relativity）的扩展理论及超出标准模型（Standard Model）的物质场景中为无视界超致密天体的存在提供理论支持。

Abstract: Black hole mimickers, ultracompact horizonless objects, have been proposed as alternatives to black holes in a variety of settings, including extensions of general relativity and scenarios involving matter sectors beyond the Standard Model. Their formation in gravitational collapse of matter requires quantum mechanical tunneling to occur on a length scale of the order of the Schwarzschild radius of the corresponding black hole. We propose a mechanism, based on multichannel enhancement catalyzed by quantum chaotic dynamics, that can dramatically amplify the quantum mechanical transmission across a tunneling barrier. We explore, in particular, how the nucleation of a string theoretic black shell is enhanced via this mechanism. We anticipate similar results to hold for other proposed black hole mimickers.

Method: 基于 Donnelly 等人（2020）和 Jiang 等人（2020）的工作，本文在拓扑弦论中构建体子系统。闭弦（closed strings）的子系统由结束于纠缠膜上的开弦构成，纠缠膜扮演动态纠缠面（dynamical entangling surface）的角色。局域全息通过纠缠膜的几何过渡实现。文中定义了子区域开弦代数（subregion open string algebra），并发展了适用于任意态和子区域的开弦模流（modular flow）图解法。

Abstract: How do we define a bulk subsystem in quantum gravity? In \cite{Wong:2025kpz}, we argued that such a subsystem must support local holographic degrees of freedom. These are gravitational edge modes, whose entanglement creates a backreaction that fuses together subregions of spacetime. In this work we give a realization of these ideas in topological string theory, building upon \cite{Donnelly:2020teo,Jiang:2020cqo}. In this theory, a subsystem for closed strings consists of open strings ending on entanglement branes, which play the role of a dynamical entangling surface. Local holography is implemented by the geometric transition of these branes. We check that the entanglement entropy of these open strings reproduces the gravitational entropy of the associated closed string background. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
