Method: 从具有因果序（causally ordered）事件的确定性前几何基底出发，对微观历史进行粗粒化（coarse-graining）处理；将基本确定性更新步识别为最小原时步（minimal proper-time step），粗粒化等价类（coarse-grained equivalence classes）的增长控制紫外耗散修正（ultraviolet dissipative correction）及有效量子化强度的尺度依赖性。

Result: 自下而上框架中的原时截断核（proper-time cutoff kernel）获得微观诠释，即未分辨确定性历史的逆增长；在红外极限（infrared limit）下耗散项消失，恢复标准幺正量子场论（unitary quantum field theory）；粗粒化结构自然导致涌现的相对论性时空几何，在宏观极限下与爱因斯坦引力相容。

Conclusion: 最小尺度结构（minimal-scale structure）、量子行为（quantum behavior）和相对论性时空（relativistic spacetime）可能共享同一个确定性起源。

Abstract: We develop a top-down counterpart of the minimal proper-time formulation of quantum field theory previously introduced as an effective bottom-up framework. Starting from a deterministic pre-geometric substrate of causally ordered events, we show how coarse-graining over microscopic histories leads, at low energies, to an effective Nambu-like quantum dynamics. The elementary deterministic update is identified with the minimal proper-time step, while the growth of coarse-grained equivalence classes controls both the ultraviolet dissipative correction and the scale dependence of the effective quantization strength, encoded in a running Planck constant. In this way, the proper-time cutoff kernel of the bottom-up formulation acquires a microscopic interpretation as the inverse growth of unresolved deterministic histories. In the infrared limit, the dissipative term vanishes and standard unitary quantum field theory is recovered. The same coarse-grained structure also provides a natural setting for an emergent relativistic spacetime geometry, compatible in the macroscopic limit with Einstein gravity. The resulting picture suggests a common deterministic origin for minimal-scale structure, quantum behavior, and relativistic spacetime.

Abstract: We derive new exact formulae for elliptic genera in two spacetime dimensions with $\mathcal{N}\ge 2$ supercharges, as well as their one- and zero-dimensional counterparts (for Witten indices and matrix-model partition functions). Our results are written as a discrete sum over geometric/combinatorial structures of crystals introduced previously by the authors. Our results provide vast generalisations of the celebrated Nekrasov partition function enumerated by the Young diagrams, and uncover new combinatorics underlying the crystal melting. We also analyse the thermodynamic limit of crystals arising from two-dimensional $\mathcal{N}=(0,2)$ theories associated with toric Calabi-Yau fourfolds, where a projection of the Calabi-Yau geometry emerges in the limit.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超对称旋转AdS$_5$黑洞具有等电荷分支（equal-charge branch），即$Q_1=Q_2=Q_3$，对应的$\mathcal{N}=4$超共形指标（superconformal index）微正则扇区需通过投影到等电荷来获得。理解该投影后大$N$极限下指标的结构，特别是高自旋尾部是否幸存，是本研究的主要动机。

Method: 通过提取两个电荷差化学势（fugacities）中的常数项，将超共形指标投影到等电荷扇区。对多引力子（multigraviton）扇区进行大$N$分析，证明投影指标可精确分解为包含分拆函数（partition function）$\mathsf{p}(n)$的开放形式；同时进行精确的$U(3)$计算以检验有限秩贡献。

Result: 大$N$等电荷投影指标$\mathcal{I}^{\rm eqQ}_\infty(x,p)$可分解为$\prod_{k\ge1}(1-p^kx^{3k})(1-p^{-k}x^{3k})\sum_{n\ge0}\mathsf{p}(n)^3x^{6n}$。该分解给出了每个自旋扇区（spin sector）的起始能量（onset energy），低于此能量大$N$系数为零。但在大$N$系数为零的能量处，有限秩系数仍可能出现，甚至超出经典$U(3)$黑洞界限。此外，确定了完整线$j=6J_R+6$，并报告了具体的系数数值。

Conclusion: 高自旋尾部（high-spin tail）在等电荷投影下得以幸存。需要指出，所有系数均来自$(-1)^F$-分级指标（graded index），而不是正数简并度（positive degeneracies）。

Abstract: The equal-charge branch of supersymmetric rotating AdS$_5$ black holes has $Q_1=Q_2=Q_3$. The corresponding microcanonical sector of the $\mathcal{N}=4$ superconformal index is obtained by projecting to equal charges, or equivalently by extracting the constant term in the two charge-difference fugacities. We prove that for the large-$N$ multigraviton sector the projected index factorizes exactly as \[
  \mathcal{I}^{\rm eqQ}_\infty(x,p)
  =\prod_{k\ge1}(1-p^kx^{3k})(1-p^{-k}x^{3k})
  \sum_{n\ge0}\mathsf{p}(n)^3x^{6n}, \] where $\mathsf{p}(n)$ is the partition function. This factorization gives, for every spin sector, an explicit onset energy below which the large-$N$ coefficient is zero. Exact $U(3)$ computations show that finite-rank coefficients can nevertheless appear at energies where the large-$N$ coefficient vanishes, including beyond the classical $U(3)$ black-hole bound. We also determine the full line $j=6J_R+6$. In particular, with $j^*(J_R)$ denoting this large-$N$ onset energy, \[
  d_3^{\rm eqQ}(87,\tfrac{27}{2})=1,
  \qquad
  j^*(\tfrac{27}{2})-87=1554, \] and the first giant-graviton sector already contributes one unit at this point. All coefficients are coefficients of the $(-1)^F$-graded index, not positive degeneracies. The main conclusion is that the high-spin tail survives the exact equal-charge projection.

</details>


### [348] [Holographic heat engines for Schwarzschild black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03749)
*Ripunjay Dwivedi,Manus R. Visser*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在渐近平坦时空中利用准局域引力热力学构造可逆黑洞热机，通过在有限球腔中封闭Schwarzschild黑洞并识别腔边界上的对偶热系统为工作物质，推导出五种热机循环的精确效率，其中再生式斯特林循环效率接近卡诺极限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将黑洞视为热机（heat engine）是探索黑洞热力学与引力理论之间深层联系的重要途径。已有研究多集中于反德西特（anti-de Sitter）时空中的黑洞热机，而渐近平坦（asymptotically flat）时空中的构造尚不明确。本文旨在拓展这一方向，利用准局域（quasi-local）引力热力学构建可逆热机模型，以检验黑洞的准局域状态方程。

Method: 采用准局域引力热力学框架，将Schwarzschild黑洞置于有限球形腔体内，将腔边界上的对偶热系统（dual thermal system）视为工作物质。在该对偶系统中，表面压力（surface pressure）与边界面积构成热力学压力-体积对，同时保持引力理论的所有耦合常数不变。在此基础上构造卡诺（Carnot）、奥托（Otto）、狄塞尔（Diesel）、布雷顿（Brayton）和斯特林（Stirling）五种可逆热机循环，并推导其精确效率。

Result: 推导出五种热机循环的精确效率表达式，并进行了数值比较。这些效率反映了黑洞的准局域状态方程。结果表明，再生式斯特林效率（regenerated Stirling efficiency）显著接近卡诺界（Carnot bound），并在高温极限下趋近于卡诺效率。

Conclusion: 准局域引力热力学为在渐近平坦时空中构造可逆黑洞热机提供了可行框架。再生式斯特林循环的高效性暗示黑洞准局域系统在高温下接近理想可逆热机的行为，为理解黑洞热力学与引力系统的热力学极限提供了新视角。

Abstract: We construct reversible black hole heat engines in asymptotically flat spacetime using quasi-local gravitational thermodynamics. We enclose a Schwarzschild black hole in a finite spherical cavity and identify the working substance with the dual thermal system on the cavity boundary. The surface pressure and boundary area define a thermodynamic pressure-volume pair in the dual system, while all coupling constants of the gravitational theory remain fixed. We derive exact efficiencies for the Carnot, Otto, Diesel, Brayton, and Stirling engines and compare them numerically. These efficiencies probe the quasi-local equations of state of the black hole. The regenerated Stirling efficiency remains remarkably close to the Carnot bound and approaches it in the high-temperature limit.

</details>


### [349] [ERG Kernels on Multiply Connected Configuration Spaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03750)
*Satoshi Ohya,Taichi Tanaka*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了欧几里得场论中精确重整化群（ERG）核在多重连通位形空间上的拓扑依赖性，揭示了ERG核由万有覆盖空间上的核加权求和构成，权重因子由基本群的一维表示决定，且不被ERG重整化；这些因子可解释为阿哈罗诺夫-玻姆相位，其归一化条件对应于通量量子化条件，等价于非线性西格玛模型中Wess-Zumino-Witten项的能级量子化条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在欧几里得场论的泛函积分表述中，精确重整化群（exact renormalization group, ERG）变换通过泛函积分核实现。与描述无穷小ERG变换的ERG流方程不同，ERG核显式依赖于位形空间的整体拓扑结构。本文旨在探索多重连通（multiply connected）位形空间上这种拓扑依赖性的具体形式及其物理含义。

Method: 通过将ERG核表达为万有覆盖空间（universal covering space）上核的加权和，权重因子由基本群（fundamental group）的一维表示（one-dimensional representation）决定。进一步将权重因子解释为背景磁通贯穿无限维位形空间时的阿哈罗诺夫-玻姆相位（Aharonov-Bohm phases），并建立了ERG变换的归一化条件与通量量子化条件（flux-quantization condition）的对应关系。此外，还提出了一个规范等价（gauge-equivalent）形式的ERG流方程，将拓扑信息局部纳入。

Result: 证明了ERG核一般可写为万有覆盖空间上核的加权和，权重由基本群的一维表示给出，且这些权重因子在ERG变换下不被重整化（never be renormalized）。权重因子可解释为阿哈罗诺夫-玻姆相位，归一化条件对应通量量子化条件，等价于非线性西格玛模型（nonlinear sigma models）中Wess-Zumino-Witten项（Wess-Zumino-Witten terms）的能级量子化（level-quantization）条件。

Conclusion: 多重连通位形空间的整体拓扑信息通过基本群的一维表示编码在ERG核中，且该拓扑权重在重整化过程中保持不变。ERG变换的归一化条件与通量量子化及WZW项的能级量子化条件等价，表明拓扑效应在重整化群框架中具有非平凡且稳定的角色。

Abstract: In the functional-integral formulation of Euclidean field theory, exact renormalization group (ERG) transformations are realized by functional-integral kernels. Unlike the ERG flow equations that describe infinitesimal ERG transformations, these ERG kernels explicitly depend on the global topology of the configuration space. This paper explores this topology dependence for multiply connected configuration spaces. We show that the ERG kernel is in general given by a weighted sum of kernels on its universal covering space, where the weight factors are determined by a one-dimensional representation of the fundamental group. These weight factors are shown never to be renormalized under the ERG. We also show that these factors can be interpreted as Aharonov-Bohm phases with respect to a background magnetic flux penetrating the infinite-dimensional configuration space. From this viewpoint, a normalization condition for ERG transformations corresponds to a flux-quantization condition, which is equivalent to the level-quantization condition for Wess-Zumino-Witten terms in nonlinear sigma models. Finally, we present an alternative gauge-equivalent form of the ERG flow equation that incorporates this topological information locally.

### [350] [A Smoothness Principle for Branch Selection Across Black-Hole Horizons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03800)
*Yoon-Seok Choun,Ki-Seok Kim*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出一个基于视界残差光滑性（horizon-residual smoothness）的分支选择原则，统一解释了黑洞波方程中的三个看似独立的结构：跨视界光滑延拓、边界推迟格林函数的极点跳跃（pole-skipping）以及SL(2,ℝ)表示的最低权重结构，并将其应用于全息超导体模型作为诊断工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 黑洞波方程在视界（horizon）处具有正则奇点，局部解分裂为不同分支，需从物理上区分出有意义的那个分支。以往这些现象被视为孤立的边界或视界性质，缺乏统一理解。

Method: 提出分支选择原则：去除主导的视界行为并对残差场（residual field）施加 C^∞ 光滑性条件。利用 JT/AdS_2 中的精确可解标量场模型，验证该原则能否统一解释三种结构。进一步将该框架应用于静态全息超导体模型（static holographic superconductor model）作为诊断工具。

Result: 单一原则成功组织并统一了跨视界光滑延拓、边界推迟格林函数的极点跳跃以及 SL(2,ℝ) 表示的最低权重结构。边界极点跳跃歧义是视界残差光滑性在全息对偶中的精确体现；群论分析表明该分支选择由时空对称性（spacetime symmetries）根本支配。在全息超导体模型中，真正的极点跳跃点需要同时满足残差光滑性和边界分支的严格线性无关性（strict linear independence），以避免虚假的分支塌缩伪迹（branch-collapse artifacts）。

Conclusion: 该分支选择原则将先前孤立的现象统一为连贯的体边界对应词典（bulk-to-boundary dictionary），证明极点跳跃是视界光滑性的全息表现，且受底层对称性支配。该原则可有效诊断全息超导体中的极点跳跃点真伪，具有广泛的推广应用价值。

Abstract: Many black-hole wave equations reduce to radial ordinary differential equations with regular singular points at horizons, where local solutions split into distinct branches. We propose a simple branch-selection principle to isolate the physically distinguished branch: removing the leading horizon behavior and imposing \(C^{\infty }\) smoothness on the residual field. Using an exactly solvable scalar field in \(JT/AdS_{2}\), we demonstrate that this single principle successfully organizes three seemingly distinct structures: smooth continuation across the black-hole horizon, the ambiguity of the boundary retarded Green function (pole-skipping), and the lowest-weight structure of an \(SL(2,\mathbb{R})\) representation. Rather than treating these phenomena as isolated boundary or horizon properties, our results unify them into a cohesive bulk-to-boundary dictionary, proving that the boundary pole-skipping ambiguity is the precise holographic manifestation of horizon-residual smoothness. Furthermore, the group-theoretic identification reveals that this physical branch selection is not a mere mathematical artifact, but is fundamentally governed by the underlying spacetime symmetries. Finally, we apply this framework as a diagnostic tool to a static holographic superconductor model, revealing that a genuine pole-skipping point requires both simultaneous residual smoothness and strict linear independence of the boundary branches to prevent deceptive branch-collapse artifacts.

### [351] [From OPE Associativity to Gravitational Wave Signatures: Critical Dimensions and AdS/dS Transition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.03969)
*Tetiana Obikhod*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本论文建立了一个理论框架，将共形场论中算子乘积展开（OPE）的代数一致性条件与随机引力波背景（SGWB）中的可观测特征联系起来。通过共形6j符号和AdS/CFT对偶，作者识别出一个临界反常维度γ_c，当越过该阈值时，对偶标度维度进入复数主级数，进而在四点关联函数中引发对数周期振荡，最终在引力波谱中表现为特定频率间隔的调幅结构，可通过LISA等探测器进行检验。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究的动机在于建立共形场论中算子乘积展开（OPE）代数一致性的抽象数学条件与宇宙学可观测现象之间的直接联系。作者希望通过AdS/CFT对应，将OPE关联性中的代数结构转化为引力波背景中的具体可探测信号，从而为量子引力和早期宇宙理论提供观测检验的窗口。

Method: 论文首先将共形6j符号（conformal 6j symbols）解释为穿越核（crossing kernels），并从穿越方程（crossing equation）的奇异性中提取双迹算子（double-trace operators）的反常维度（anomalous dimensions）γ_{n,J}。随后利用AdS/CFT对应，将这些代数偏移全息地重新解释为Anti-de Sitter（AdS）体中的有效质量偏移。通过解析延拓到de Sitter空间（L_{AdS} → iL_{dS}），分析临界反常维度γ_c及其对偶标度维度的复数化行为。

Result: 研究发现存在一个临界反常维度γ_c，当γ < γ_c时，有效质量违反Breitenlohner-Freedman界，对偶标度维度被迫进入复数主级数（complex principal series），Δ_{dS} = d/2 ± iμ。这一复数维度导致四点关联函数中出现特征性的对数周期振荡（logarithmic oscillations）。在宇宙学背景下，这些振荡表现为随机引力波背景（SGWB）中的对数周期调幅（log-periodic modulation），其频率间隔为Δln f = 2π/μ。

Conclusion: 该研究表明，利用LISA等下一代干涉仪探测引力波频谱中的对数周期结构，可直接测量参数μ，从而将抽象的OPE结合律（OPE associativity）与观测宇宙学联系起来。这为检验AdS/CFT对应及相关量子引力理论提供了一个潜在的观测途径。

Abstract: We present a framework connecting the algebraic consistency of the Operator Product Expansion (OPE) in Conformal Field Theories to observable signatures in the stochastic gravitational wave background (SGWB). By interpreting the conformal 6j symbols as crossing kernels, we extract the anomalous dimensions $γ_{n,J}$ of double-trace operators from the singularities of the crossing equation. Through the AdS/CFT correspondence, these algebraic shifts are holographically reinterpreted as effective mass shifts in the Anti-de Sitter bulk. We identify a critical anomalous dimension, $γ_c$, which marks the threshold where the effective mass violates the Breitenlohner-Freedman bound. Upon analytic continuation to de Sitter space ($L_{\text{AdS}} \to iL_{\text{dS}}$), we demonstrate that crossing this threshold ($γ< γ_c$) forces the dual scaling dimensions into the complex principal series, $Δ_{\text{dS}} = d/2 \pm iμ$. This complex dimensionality induces characteristic logarithmic oscillations in the four-point correlators. In the cosmological context, these oscillations manifest as a log-periodic modulation in the SGWB, characterized by a specific spacing $Δ\ln f = 2π/μ$. Detecting this log-periodic structure with next-generation interferometers such as LISA would directly measure the parameter $μ$, closing the loop between abstract OPE associativity and observational cosmology.

### [352] [The Normalised Wigner Negativity Rate as a Second-Moment Probe of Infall in AdS$_3$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04065)
*Ritam Basu*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出归一化Krylov-Wigner负性（normalized Krylov-Wigner negativity）的速率可作为边界态第二矩（second moment）的诊断量，捕捉算符沿Krylov链的波包展宽。通过解析推导宏观极限下的Bessel解析形式，发现负性按sinh^{4Δ}(πt/β)增长，仅当Δ=1（AdS_3中的Breitenlohner-Freedman饱和维数）时，负性速率与Krylov方差增长率等价，并对应于内落粒子潮汐拉伸的径向位置与动量乘积。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在展布复杂性（spread complexity）框架中，Krylov链上算符的平均位置可恢复AdS中内落粒子的径向动量，但仅反映第一矩，无法刻画波包偏离经典轨迹的展布。需要引入第二矩的诊断量来捕捉这一展布效应。

Method: 从种子归一化Krylov-Wigner分布（seed-normalized Krylov-Wigner distribution）出发——即对后代云（descendant cloud）做Wigner变换并除去衰减返回振幅——在宏观极限下得到解析的Bessel函数形式，并显式计算其总负性。利用Krylov链的精确负二项统计（negative binomial statistics）以及Caputa等人的动量字典，推导负性速率的渐近行为。

Result: 负性按sinh^{4Δ}(πt/β)增长；原始种子归一化态负性则受O(√D)约束而饱和。仅当Δ=1时，负性速率等于Krylov方差在晚时间渐近的增长率，且该速率等于径向位置与动量的乘积R ∝ C P_ρ，即近地测地线落入视界时的潮汐拉伸速率。

Conclusion: AdS_3中Breitenlohner-Freedman饱和维数（Δ=1）具有特殊性——此时负性速率与Krylov方差增长率精确对应，并揭示其全息对偶为内落粒子的潮汐拉伸速率。未来研究方向包括通过SU(1,1)离散序列将横向弦长算符（transverse string size operator）与Krylov数算子（Krylov number operator）联系起来。

Abstract: In spread complexity, the average position of an operator along its Krylov chain, recovers the right radial momentum of an infalling particle in AdS, yet it is a measure of the first moment, irrespective of the spread of the wavepacket away from its classical trajectory. The rate of a normalized Krylov-Wigner negativity can be proposed as a diagnostic of the second moment of the boundary state that captures this spreading. Starting with the \emph{seed-normalized} Krylov-Wigner distribution -- that is, the Wigner transform of the descendant cloud, with the decaying return amplitude divided out -- we obtain an analytic Bessel form in the macroscopic limit and compute its total negativity explicitly. Retaining the Bessel variable all the way through, we find that the negativity goes as $\sinh^{4Δ}(πt/β)$, while the raw, seed-normalized state negativity saturates, as dictated by the $O(\sqrt{D})$ bound. Using the exact negative binomial statistics of the Krylov chain and the momentum dictionary of Caputa et al.~\cite{Caputa:2024}, the rate of the negativity scales as the growth rate of the Krylov variance at late time asymptotics \emph{if and only if} $Δ=1$, the Breitenlohner-Freedman saturating dimension in $AdS_3$. This dimensionality is special in that the negativity rate is the product of the proper radial position and momentum, $\mathcal{R} \propto \mathcal{C} P_ρ$, i.e., the rate of the tidal stretch of nearby geodesic falling into the horizon. We comment on the direction for future research, in particular the interpretation of the transverse string size operator in terms of the Krylov number operator through the common $SU(1,1)$ discrete series.

### [353] [Infrared Divergences as Itinerant Vacua](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04115)
*Masahiro Morikawa*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出“游走真空”（itinerant vacuum）的构念，认为红外发散（infrared divergence）并非病理现象，而是真空在经典序参量（order parameter）演化过程中穿过一族不等价真空态的场论代价。通过闭时路径（closed-time-path, CTP）有效作用量中的精确分离，将红外发散的影响泛函（influence functional）转换为经典随机源，从而统一解释了软QED、德西特空间中的标量场、软引力子与非平衡相变中的1/f噪声、引力记忆（gravitational memory）及非高斯涨落等现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 红外发散通常被视为需要抵消或隐藏的病态；本文旨在发展一种互补的、建设性的视角，将其重新解释为游走真空的物理可观测信号，而非计算上的瑕疵。

Method: 在实时闭时路径（CTP）有效作用量中实现精确分离；将红外发散的影响泛函的虚部通过Hubbard–Stratonovich恒等式变换为经典随机源，该变换是生成泛函的代数恒等式，无需预先粗粒化或退相干假设。

Result: 该机制统一解释了软QED中的1/f电流噪声、德西特空间中的原初功率谱（primordial power spectrum）、软引力子中的引力记忆以及非平衡相变中的序参量动力学，证明这些现象均源于同一游走真空机制。

Conclusion: 红外发散是有序参量演化时真空游走的场论代价，其经典可观测残余包括1/f噪声、引力记忆与非高斯涨落；论文还展望了基于真空流形上的希尔伯特空间纤维丛（Hilbert-space bundle）的几何表述。

Abstract: Infrared divergences (IRDs) are usually treated as pathologies to be cancelled, regularized, or hidden in dressed asymptotic states. This paper develops a complementary and constructive viewpoint: an IRD is the signature of an \emph{itinerant vacuum} -- a quantum vacuum that wanders continuously through a family of inequivalent states as a classical order parameter evolves. Each value of the order parameter carries its own coherent vacuum, so moving the order parameter means traversing a succession of orthogonal vacua. The IRD is the field-theoretic cost of this wandering, and the $1/f$ noise, gravitational memory, and non-Gaussian fluctuations that emerge from it are its observable classical remnants.
  The technical core is an exact separation in the real-time closed-time-path (CTP) effective action. The infrared-divergent imaginary part of the influence functional must not be left as a divergent coefficient in a deterministic equation of motion; it is instead converted, by a Hubbard--Stratonovich identity, into a classical stochastic source. This step is an algebraic identity of the generating functional and requires no prior coarse graining or decoherence assumption: the retarded kernel encodes the memory of past vacuum transitions, while the noise kernel encodes the quantum uncertainty of the next one. We apply this construction to four parallel arenas -- soft QED, scalar fields in de Sitter space, soft gravitons, and non-equilibrium phase transitions -- and show that the same itinerant-vacuum mechanism underlies $1/f$ current noise, the primordial power spectrum, gravitational memory, and order-parameter dynamics. A geometric formulation in terms of a Hilbert-space bundle over the vacuum manifold is outlined as an outlook.

</details>


### [354] [Finite-$N$ Operator Algebras and the Hilbert Space of Bilocal Holography](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04143)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 延续arXiv:2602.20788[hep-th]中有限N希尔伯特空间的构造工作，旨在为有限N双局域全息对偶（bilocal holography）提供更严格的算子代数与表示论框架，解决单重态空间的数学描述问题。

Method: 利用算子代数（operator algebra）与表示论（representation theory），在Fock空间上构造颜色群（color group）与双局域李代数（bilocal Lie algebra）的交换作用；通过单重态投影（singlet projection）选出不变李代数（称为主代数/master algebra）的一个不可约表示；并借助正交、辛、酉三种情形下的卡西米尔算子（Casimir）与特征标（character）计算有限迹与配分函数。

Abstract: We give an operator-algebraic and representation-theoretic description of the Hilbert spaces finite-$N$ bilocal holography. This work is a sequel to the finite-$N$ Hilbert space construction of arXiv:2602.20788 [hep-th]. The central result is the establishment of an invariant dual-pair operator algebra: before imposing the singlet constraint the Fock space carries commuting actions of the color group and of a bilocal Lie algebra, while the projection to the singlet sector selects a single irreducible representation of the invariant Lie algebra, which we call a master algebra. The finite-$N$ trace relations, beginning with the quadratic identities studied here, are shown to become representation-theoretic identities of the selected irreducible representation. We summarize the orthogonal, symplectic and unitary cases, identify the corresponding finite-$N$ constraints, compute the singlet Casimirs, and explain how finite traces and partition functions are obtained through characters of the resulting irreducible representations. This provides a novel, previously unknown mathematical description of the singlet space.

Method: 后选择的测量结果由携带共形边界条件（conformal boundary condition）的狭缝表示，激发态通过在欧几里得路径积分（Euclidean path integral）中插入算子引入。通过将复制狭缝几何（replicated slit geometry）映射到圆盘，后测量Rényi熵中激发态的贡献被归一化为边界CFT关联函数。针对紧致自由玻色子CFT，分别分析了手征流激发、J与\bar J的相干叠加以及共轭紧致顶点算子（conjugate compact vertex operator）的激发情况。

Abstract: We study the entanglement of low-energy excited states after a fixed-outcome projective measurement on a spatial interval in a (1+1)-dimensional conformal field theory (CFT). The post-selected measurement outcome is represented by a slit carrying a conformal boundary condition, while excited states are introduced by operator insertions in the Euclidean path integral. After mapping the replicated slit geometry to a disk, the excited-state contribution to the post-measurement Rényi entropy is expressed as a normalized boundary-CFT correlation function.
  We apply this framework to the compact free boson CFT. For the chiral current excitation, the relevant ratios are given by current hafnians. We also study coherent superpositions of $J$ and $\bar J$, and of conjugate compact vertex operators. In the conjugate-vertex case, the ordinary-cylinder second Rényi ratio is independent of the relative phase, whereas the finite-slit post-measurement ratio contains phase-sensitive interference terms. ### [360] [Topological effects in the polarization of the Fulling-Rindler vacuum](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04483)

The phases of these conditions are interpreted in terms of the magnetic flux enclosed by the compact dimensions. For a general number of spatial dimensions, the components of the VEVs are explicitly separated, corresponding to the expectation values in the Minkowski vacuum. As a limiting case, the VEVs are retrieved in Rindler spacetime with trivial topology. We demonstrate that, for non-zero phases in the periodicity conditions, the vacuum energy-momentum tensor exhibits off-diagonal components with indices in the compact subspace. Near the Rindler horizon, the leading terms in the asymptotic expansions of the field squared and the diagonal components of the energy-momentum tensor coincide with the corresponding VEVs in Rindler spacetime with trivial topology. The off-diagonal components of the energy-momentum tensor vanish on the Rindler horizon. For small accelerations, the difference between the VEVs in the Fulling-Rindler and Minkowski vacua is exponentially small. The exception to this is a massless field with zero phases in the periodicity conditions. In this special case, the difference decays according to a power law as a function of acceleration. As an application, we consider the VEVs near the horizon of cylindrical black holes and topological black holes with toroidal horizons.

Abstract: Lie-Poisson electrodynamics (LPE) is a non-Abelian and nonlinear deformation of usual electrodynamics, where the gauge algebra is defined through a Lie-algebra-type Poisson bracket on space-time. We focus on the geometric approach to LPE in the absence of charged matter. We establish a non-trivial field redefinition which, under mild technical assumptions, maps the LPE dynamics to that of Maxwell theory. Using this map, for any symmetry of the Maxwell action, we construct generators of LPE symmetries and the corresponding conserved currents. In particular, we obtain deformed Poincaré transformations. ### [362] [Kaluza-Klein tower thresholds and scheme dependence of the species scale](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04602)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子引力中物种标度有两种常见但关系模糊的定义：一种是单圈引力子传播子修正推断出的微扰失效能量，另一种是引力有效作用量中高导数算符的抑制标度。该研究旨在通过有效场论分析厘清二者之间的关联。

Method: 通过分析单圈塔贡献对截断方案（cutoff scheme）的依赖性，区分局域修正（local correction）与对数贡献（logarithmic contribution）的不同角色，并以 Kaluza-Klein 塔（Kaluza-Klein tower）为具体案例计算完整的四导数（four-derivative）单圈修正。

Result: 对于大数量物种（large number of species），主导的塔增强局域修正依赖于调节子（regulator），应被解释为 EFT 匹配数据（matching data）；而次主导的对数贡献在考虑的 proper-time 截断轮廓类中是普适的。Kaluza-Klein 塔的实例明确分离了调节子稳定的对数数据与方案依赖的局域阈值贡献。

Conclusion: 研究提供了物种标度的微扰失效定义与高导数定义之间关系的可控 EFT 解释，并解释了为何两者的系数级识别（coefficient-level identification）并非调节子无关（regulator independent）的。

Abstract: We revisit the species scale in quantum gravity from the viewpoint of effective field theory (EFT). Two characterizations are commonly used: one defines it as the energy at which the perturbative description of quantum gravity breaks down, as inferred from the one-loop correction to the graviton propagator; the other identifies it with the suppression scale of higher-derivative operators in the gravitational effective action. We clarify the relation between these characterizations by analyzing the cutoff-scheme dependence of the one-loop tower contribution. For a large number of species, the leading tower-enhanced local correction is regulator dependent and should be interpreted as EFT matching data, while the subleading logarithmic contribution is universal within the class of proper-time cutoff profiles considered here. As a concrete application, we compute the full four-derivative one-loop corrections from Kaluza-Klein towers. Our results separate regulator-stable logarithmic data from scheme-dependent local threshold contributions, providing a controlled EFT interpretation of the relation between perturbative-breakdown and higher-derivative definitions of the species scale and explaining why their coefficient-level identification is not regulator independent.

</details>


### [363] [Multi-Particle Contributions to the Celestial Algebra in the ${\cal N}=8$ Supergravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04611)
*Changhyun Ahn*

Main category: hep-th

Result: 得到了九十五个单粒子贡献的（反）对易关系；建立了多粒子OPE与对应天体振幅（celestial amplitudes）之间的非平凡关系；通过三重共线极限验证了结果的自洽性；隐含地提出了将构造推广到单粒子顶角算子与$(N-1)$粒子顶角算子的多粒子OPE以及右侧包含线性项（即振幅中$N$粒子因子化道的单粒子交换项之和）的（反）对易关系的一般形式。

Conclusion: 多粒子OPE构造在${\cal N}=8$超引力中成功推广，所得（反）对易关系丰富了天体软流代数的结构，三重共线极限的校验进一步支持了该框架的正确性。该工作为更高粒子数的天体算子代数以及全息对偶中线性项的完整处理提供了隐含的推广路径。

Abstract: Recently, Calkins and Pate calculated the multi-particle operator product expansions (OPEs) of single-particle celestial operators with two-particle celestial operators in pure Einstein gravity. We apply their construction to the graviton, gravitinos, graviphotons, graviphotinos and scalars in ${\cal N}=8$ supergravity. By performing various contour integrals on these multi-particle OPEs, we obtain ninety-five (anti)commutators for the single-particle contributions from the celestial soft current algebra (derived from the single-particle OPEs) in a two-dimensional boundary. Moreover, these ninety-five multi-particle OPEs provide nontrivial relations between the corresponding celestial amplitudes. The triple-collinear limits between these bosonic and fermionic particles from the four-dimensional bulk are also described as a double check. Finally, we implicitly propose both the multi-particle OPEs of single-particle celestial operators with $(N-1)$-particle celestial operators and the corresponding (anti)commutators for the modes of celestial operators that have linear terms (or single-particle exchange terms due to the sum of $N$-particle factorization channels from amplitudes) on the right-hand sides.

### [364] [New insights on mutual information in the island approach to the Page curve](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04706)
*Anirban Roy Chowdhury,Souvik Paul,Sunandan Gangopadhyay*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文报告了关于Page时间后两套子系统互信息（mutual information）行为的关键观察，揭示了几何纠缠（geometrical entanglement）的守恒性质。研究发现，在scrambling time，$B_+$与$B_-$之间的互信息$I(B_{+}:B_{-})$消失，而$\mathcal{I}$与$R$之间的互信息$I(\mathcal{I}:R)$发散至无穷，表明后两者达到最大纠缠。此外，本文首次提出利用二分区域结果计算三分互信息（tripartite mutual information）$I(\mathcal{I}:R_+:R_-)$的方法，填补了此前文献的空白。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索Page时间（after Page time）后不同子系统间互信息的行为，以深入理解几何纠缠的守恒机制。

Method: 通过分析$B_+$与$B_-$之间互信息$I(B_{+}:B_{-})$在scrambling time归零，以及$\mathcal{I}$与$R$之间互信息$I(\mathcal{I}:R)$在该时刻发散至无穷的对比，揭示Cauchy面上不同区域间的几何关联守恒。并利用已有二分区域结果，计算三分互信息$I(\mathcal{I}:R_+:R_-)$。

Result: 在scrambling time，$I(B_{+}:B_{-})$为零，$I(\mathcal{I}:R)$为无穷大，表明$\mathcal{I}$与$R$达到最大纠缠（maximally entangled）。三分互信息$I(\mathcal{I}:R_+:R_-)$的计算方法被首次给出。

Conclusion: 互信息的特定行为为获得永恒黑洞（eternal black hole）的正确Page曲线（Page curve）提供了关键支持，并建立了几何纠缠在不同区域间的守恒观念。三分互信息的新计算方法补充了此前文献的缺失。

Abstract: In this article, we have presented one of the very important observations, regarding the behavior of mutual information of two different sets of subsystems in the after Page time scenario. This provides us with some deep insights about the conservation of geometrical entanglement. In our earlier works, we have shown how the saturation of mutual information between two specific subsystems plays a vital role in obtaining the correct Page curve for the eternal black hole. In those works, we have shown that the mutual information between $B_+$ and $B_-$, that is, $I(B_{+}: B_{-})$, vanishes at scrambling time, which leads to the correct Page curve. That means that at scrambling time, there is no correlation between $B_+$ and $B_-$. Remarkably, it is observed that at this particular value of observer's time, the mutual information between $\mathcal{I}$ and $R$, that is, $I(\mathcal{I}:R)$, becomes infinity. This indicates that the regions $\mathcal{I}$ and $R$ become maximally entangled. This provides us with a notion of conservation of geometric correlation between different regions on the Cauchy slice. In this work, we have also provided a way to calculate the tripartite mutual information of regions $\mathcal{I}$,$R_+$ and $R_-$, that is, $I(\mathcal{I}:R_+:R_-)$ on the Cauchy slice using the earlier results involving the bipartite regions. *Bijan Bagchi,Akshat Pandey,Parmest Roy,Sauvik Sen*

TL;DR: 本文基于Geroch过程，在广义不确定性原理（GUP）框架下研究了黑洞视界附近系统的形变对贝肯斯坦熵界（Bekenstein entropy bound）的影响，涵盖(3+1)维和(2+1)维情形，发现负GUP形变使熵界普遍放宽，正形变则使其收紧。

Abstract: Based on Geroch's process of dropping a system into a black hole from the vicinity of the horizon, we investigate in this paper the influence of deformation on the Bekenstein entropy bound both for (3+1) and (2+1) dimensions in the context of a generalized uncertainty principle (GUP). While providing a coherent framework for providing an upper limit on the entropy across dimensions we show, in the framework of a semiclassical treatment, that while a negative GUP deformation yields a universal relaxation of the bound, a positive deformation tightens it. Our results may be interpreted as a response to Planck-scale modifications of the near-horizon redshift.

Method: 引入电磁、重子数和同位旋背景规范场，分别对$N_f=2$和$N_f=3$两种味数情况写出中性介子（$π^0$、$η$、$η'$）的拓扑耦合项，并分析其中与磁场$\vec{B}$和旋转角速度$\vecΩ$成正比的梯度耦合贡献。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示的结果对于理解稠密旋转物质中的手征孤子晶格具有重要意义，为在复杂外部条件下QCD物质的手征反常效应提供了理论依据。

Abstract: We study anomalous Wess-Zumino-Witten terms associated with the chiral anomaly in dense QCD matter under magnetic fields and rotation. By introducing electromagnetic, baryon number, and isospin background gauge fields, we write down the topological couplings of neutral mesons for the $N_f=2$ and $N_f=3$ cases. The resulting terms contain characteristic contributions proportional to $\vec{B} \cdot \vec{\nabla} φ$ and $\vecΩ \cdot \vec{\nabla} φ$, where $φ$ denotes $π^0$, $η$, or $η'$. ### [367] [The causal set reduction formula](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.04980)
*Stav Zalel*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文在因果集（causal set）背景下推导了矩阵元的约化公式（reduction formula），并建立了关联函数间的无限层级关系（类似于连续时空中的Schwinger-Dyson方程）。结合这两项结果，作者将矩阵元表示为三种等价形式：路径积分（path integral）以及两种不同的关联函数求和。该方法绕过了显式使用微分运动方程算子，并在平坦连续时空中提供了标准LSZ公式的替代表达。

Method: 首先推导因果集背景下的矩阵元约化公式；其次建立关联函数间的无限层级关系，该关系类似于连续时空中的Schwinger-Dyson方程；最后结合上述两个结果，将矩阵元表达为三种形式：路径积分以及两种不同的关联函数求和。该方法的核心特点是绕过了对微分运动方程算子的显式使用。

Result: 得到了因果集上矩阵元的约化公式（reduction formula）以及关联函数间的无限层级关系（类似于Schwinger-Dyson方程）。矩阵元可表达为三种等价形式：路径积分形式和两种不同的关联函数求和形式。该方法在平坦连续时空中提供了标准LSZ约化公式的一种替代表达。

Conclusion: 该工作为因果集离散背景下的散射计算提供了新的理论工具，避开了连续时空方法对微分运动方程算子的依赖，为量子引力中的散射问题研究开辟了新的路径。

Abstract: We derive a reduction formula for matrix elements on a causal set background. We derive an infinite tower of relations between correlators, akin to the Schwinger-Dyson equations of the continuum. Combining these two results we are able to express matrix elements in three different forms: as a path integral and as two distinct sums of correlators. We sketch the form that our method - which circumvents explicit use of differential equation of motion operators - takes in flat continuum spacetime where it provides an alternative expression for the standard LSZ result.

### [368] [From Galilei to Euclidean Carroll and the Alice Particle: The Times They Are a-Changin'](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05115)
*Eric A. Bergshoeff,Luca Romano,Jan Rosseel,Elena Simón Félix,Sara Zeko*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出“欧几里得p-膜卡罗尔极限（Euclidean p-brane Carroll limit）”，将p-膜伽利略极限（Galilei limit）与卡罗尔极限（Carroll limit）统一起来，并针对p=0情况推导出Alice代数（Alice algebra）与Alice粒子（Alice particle）的概念，将其与巴格曼粒子（Bargmann particle）进行对比，揭示了二者在弦理论中的对应关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有文献中，p-膜伽利略极限（Galilei limit）与卡罗尔极限（Carroll limit）通常被分别处理，缺乏统一的极限框架。本文旨在通过允许世界体积（worldvolume）为欧几里得（Euclidean），将时间变为横向方向，从而统一这两种极限，并探索其在p=0情况下的物理后果。

Method: 通过将p-膜伽利略极限中世界体积的方向由洛伦兹（Lorentzian）改为欧几里得（Euclidean），使时间变为横向，从而将伽利略极限转变为卡罗尔极限（称为“欧几里得p-膜卡罗尔极限”）。对p=0情况，研究由此产生的时空对称性及其中心扩张，并通过对相对论性有质量粒子或快子（tachyon）作用量的统一极限，导出巴格曼（Bargmann）与Alice粒子的作用量。

Result: 发现欧几里得0-膜卡罗尔极限下的时空对称性可以中心扩张为Alice代数（Alice algebra），类似于巴格曼代数（Bargmann algebra）对伽利略对称性的中心扩张。宇宙学常数为负时巴格曼粒子运动稳定，为正时Alice粒子运动稳定。两者均可通过对一个或两个时间的相对论性无质量粒子作用量的零约化（null reduction）得到。

Conclusion: 在10维中，Alice粒子对应于Hull的IIA${}^*$型理论中D$0{}^*$-膜的退耦极限（decoupling limit），类似于巴格曼粒子与IIA型弦论中D0-膜的关系。这一统一框架为理解不同极限下的对称性及其弦论对应提供了新视角。

Abstract: In generalized, also known as $p$-brane Galilei limits, the speed of light $c$ becomes infinite in the directions transverse to a $(p+1)$-dimensional Lorentzian worldvolume. In this paper, we explain that allowing the worldvolume to be Euclidean, and thus time to be transversal, $p$-brane Galilei limits turn into Carrollian ones, that we refer to as "Euclidean $p$-brane Carroll limits", in which $c$ goes to zero in the $p+1$ worldvolume directions. This leads to a unified approach to taking Galilean and Carrollian limits, whose consequences we explore for $p=0$. We show that the spacetime symmetries that arise from the Euclidean 0-brane Carroll limit can be centrally extended to what we will call the Alice algebra, similar to how the Bargmann algebra centrally extends the Galilei symmetries. This gives rise to the novel notion of an Alice particle, and we obtain the Bargmann and Alice particle actions from a unified limit of the action of a relativistic massive particle or tachyon, suitably coupled to a one-form gauge potential. In the presence of a cosmological constant, we find that the Bargmann and Alice particles undergo stable motion for negative and positive cosmological constant, respectively. Finally, we show that the Bargmann and Alice particle actions can be obtained from null reduction of a massless particle action in a relativistic spacetime with one and two times. Our results indicate that in 10 dimensions, the Alice particle is a decoupling limit of a D$0{}^*$-brane in Hull's type IIA${}^*$ theory, similar to how the Bargmann particle is related to a D$0$-brane in type IIA string theory.

### [369] [Chern Character for Discrete Spectrum Partition Function](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05136)
*Shunrui Li,Yang Liu*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文建立了离散谱量子系统热配分函数与时空上“虚拟物理层”陈特征之间的严格几何对应，通过将哈密顿动力学解释为量子相空间上的U(1)-等变流并前推至时空，证明了有限温配分函数可作为陈特征的积分导出，并利用Grothendieck-Riemann-Roch形式体系证明了热紧致化下陈特征的前推不变性，为量子场论中的热迹提供了拓扑基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将哈密顿动力学（Hamiltonian dynamics）视为量子相空间$\mathbb{CP}^n$上的$U(1)$-等变流（equivariant flow），并前推（pushforward）至时空；借助Weyl渐近律（Weyl's asymptotic law）保证的迹类（trace class）推广至无穷维；利用Grothendieck-Riemann-Roch形式体系证明热紧致化（thermal compactification）下陈特征（Chern character）的前推不变性。

Result: 离散谱量子系统的有限温配分函数可表示为时空上“虚拟物理层”（virtual physical sheaf）陈特征的积分；该构造在无穷维情形下同样成立，且在任意流形的热紧致化下陈特征的前推具有不变性。

Conclusion: 该框架统一了谱理论与示性类理论，为基于算子代数方法（operator-algebraic approach）的配分函数提供了几何解释与拓扑基础。

Abstract: We establish a rigorous geometric correspondence between thermal partition functions of discrete-spectrum quantum systems with bounded ground energy and the Chern character of "virtual physical sheaf" over spacetime. By interpreting Hamiltonian dynamics as a $U(1)$-equivariant flow on the quantum phase space $\mathbb{CP}^n$ and pushforward to spacetime, we show that the finite-temperature partition function emerges as the integral of the Chern character of "virtual physical sheaf" over spacetime. The construction extends naturally to infinite dimensions through trace class guaranteed by Weyl's aspmtotic law. Using the Grothendieck-Riemann-Roch formalism, we prove pushforward invariance of the Chern character under thermal compactification on arbitrary manifolds, providing a topological foundation for thermal traces in quantum field theory. This framework unifies spectral theory with characteristic class theory, offering a geometric interpretation of partition functions based on operator-algebraic approach.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为双标度非相对论费米液体建立统一的余切轨道玻色化框架，进而为非临界M理论提供有效的时空引力描述，以加深对2维非临界弦（noncritical strings）景观和3维量子引力（quantum gravity）的理解。

Method: 采用余切轨道方法扩展至具有中心反转向谐振子势的双标度非相对论费米液体，在1+1维重现Das-Jevicki集体场理论，在2+1维得到Hořava-Keeler费米液体的有效场论；通过合适的规范选择将理论约化为连续族1+1维手征玻色子，并利用非临界M理论的可积性（integrability）进行微扰计算。

Result: 在1+1维重现了描述c=1矩阵模型准粒子激发的Das-Jevicki集体场理论；在2+1维得到了非临界M理论的有效场论，并可约化为连续族耦合手征玻色子；通过微扰计算给出了费米子密度关联函数的逐阶结果，并在半经典极限下证明了其与费米液体对应结果的一致性。

Conclusion: 该工作为建立非临界M理论的有效时空引力描述迈出了关键一步，预期将有助于理解2维非临界弦的景观以及3维量子引力的一般性质。

Abstract: We extend the coadjoint orbit approach to bosonization systematized by Delacretaz-Du-Mehta-Son to double-scaled non-relativistic Fermi liquids with central inverted harmonic oscillator potential. In 1+1d, this reproduces the Das-Jevicki collective field theory describing quasiparticle excitations of the $c=1$ matrix model. In 2+1d, this yields an effective field theory for noncritical M-theory, namely the 2+1d Fermi liquid proposed by Hořava and Keeler as a unified framework for characterizing noncritical string vacua. With a suitable gauge choice this theory reduces to a continuous family of 1+1d chiral bosons resembling Das-Jevicki collective fields coupled by additional interactions. Utilizing the underlying integrability of noncritical M-theory, we compute select fermion density correlation functions order-by-order in perturbation theory, and provide evidence that they agree with their Fermi liquid counterparts in a suitable semiclassical limit. This represents a step toward an effective spacetime gravity description of noncritical M-theory, which we expect to shed light on both the landscape of 2d noncritical strings and 3d quantum gravity in general.

</details>

Result: 群论对粒子物理的贡献尤为突出，其方法在统计物理等领域同样具有不可忽视的实用性，并对理论生物学可能具有参考价值。

Some of these aspects will be examined.

### [372] [Thermal two-point functions in SYK and complex-time singularities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05258)
*Ilija Burić,Chi-Ming Chang,Ivan Gusev,Elizabeth Helfenberger,Andrei Parnachev,Mukund Rangamani*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文分析了大N SYK模型在有限温度、中等耦合（intermediate coupling）下远离红外不动点区域的双点函数（two-point function），追踪了复时间平面中奇异点的温度演化，并将其与算子复杂性（operator complexity）及涌现的黑色几何结构联系起来。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: SYK模型在全息对偶（holographic duality）框架下是理解量子混沌、虫洞几何和黑洞信息问题的关键玩具模型。现有研究主要集中于红外（IR）不动点附近的共形极限，而中等耦合区域远离该不动点，其全时标动力学（full-time dynamics）及复时间奇异结构尚未被系统阐明。

Method: 采用解析方法研究大N SYK模型有限温度下中等耦合区域的双点函数，在复时间平面（complex time plane）上追踪奇异点的位置随温度的变化。

Result: 领先奇异点位于虚时间轴上，控制算子复杂性的短时动力学，为关联函数定义了一个“有效温度”（effective temperature）；次领先奇异点位于由有效温度确定的热条带（thermal strip）之外，且两个奇异点均持续存在直至零温。

Conclusion: 次领先奇异点的行为被解释为涌现黑洞几何（emergent black hole geometry）中的反弹零测地线（bouncing null geodesics）；作者从运动学空间（kinematic space）视角进一步论证了相关涌现几何的合理性。

Abstract: We analyze the finite-temperature two-point function of the large-$N$ SYK model at intermediate couplings away from the infrared fixed point. Specifically, we examine its analytic structure in the complex time plane, tracking the complex-time singularities over a range of temperatures. The location of the leading singularity lies on the imaginary axis. It controls the short-time dynamics of operator complexity, defining an `effective temperature' for the correlator. The next-to-leading singularity lies outside the thermal strip set by the above effective temperature. It has been argued that this could be interpreted in terms of bouncing null geodesics in the emergent black hole geometry. Both these singularities persist all the way down to zero temperature. We discuss our observations and motivate the related emergent geometry using a kinematic space perspective.

### [373] [Polynomial Initial-State Jumps and Christoffel Transforms in Krylov Complexity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05294)
*Abhishek Chowdhury,Ajit Prasad Mahapatra*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个解析框架，用于在固定哈密顿量（Hamiltonian）下计算初始态变化导致的 Krylov 复杂度（Krylov complexity）变化，通过多项式滤波（polynomial filtering）将初始态问题转化为有限和表达式，并推广至算子 Krylov 复杂度场景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Krylov（或 spread）复杂度是依赖于初始态 $\ket{K_0}$ 和哈密顿量 $H$ 这一对组合（pair）的性质，而非仅由哈密顿量决定。改变初始态通常会改变 Lanczos 系数和 Krylov 基，因此需要一种解析方法来处理这种“相对初始态问题”（relative initial-state problem）。

Method: 采用归一化多项式滤波器 $\ket{\psi_Q}=Q(H)\ket{K_0}/\sqrt{N_Q}$，将滤波后的谱测度（spectral measure）表示为正多项式修饰 $|Q(E)|^2\mathrm d\mu(E)/N_Q$。利用正交性将测度变化转化为从参考傅里叶正交多项式矩到移位 Krylov 振幅的有限带转移（finite-band transfer），推导出个体振幅的精确有限和公式，以及用于累积概率和 spread 复杂度的投影 Christoffel-Darboux 核（projected Christoffel-Darboux kernels）。该构造通过矩阵值父测度（matrix-valued parent measure）及其标量压缩（scalar compression）来组织有限种子族（finite seed families），并通过将 $H\mapsto\mathcal L$、$\ket{K_0}\mapsto O$ 推广至算子 Krylov 复杂度。

Result: 在三类经典 Jacobi 族——海森堡-外尔/Charlier 振子（Heisenberg–Weyl/Charlier oscillator）、紧致 $SU(2)$/Krawtchouk 自旋（compact $SU(2)$/Krawtchouk spin）以及常系数紧束缚/Chebyshev 链（constant-coefficient tight-binding/Chebyshev chain）上验证了该构造，并以 Charlier 的 Hermite 中心极限标度作为 Christoffel 跳跃机制（Christoffel jump machinery）的连续谱检验。公式涵盖共轭根（confluent roots）、复种子系数、支撑损失（support loss）和有限维终端商（terminal quotients）。

Conclusion: 该工作提供了一个精确的“相对演算”（relative calculus）：一个已求解的循环问题可以生成一族多项式相关的初始态动力学，而无需在原始希尔伯特空间中重复进行 Lanczos 算法。

Abstract: State Krylov, or spread, complexity is a property of a pair $(H,\ket{K_0})$ rather than of the Hamiltonian alone. Thus, changing the initial state at fixed $H$ generally changes the Lanczos coefficients and the ordered Krylov basis. We solve this relative initial-state problem for normalized polynomial filters, $\ket{ψ_Q}=Q(H)\ket{K_0}/\sqrt{N_Q}$ with $N_Q=\langle K_0|Q(H)^\dagger Q(H)|K_0\rangle$. The filtered spectral measure is the positive polynomial modification $|Q(E)|^2\mathrm dμ(E)/N_Q$, and orthogonality turns this measure change into a finite-band transfer from reference Fourier-orthogonal-polynomial moments to shifted Krylov amplitudes. We derive exact finite sums for individual amplitudes and projected Christoffel-Darboux kernels for cumulative probabilities and spread complexity. The formulae cover confluent roots, complex seed coefficients, support loss, and terminal quotients in finite dimensions. We evaluate the construction in three canonical Jacobi families, the Heisenberg--Weyl/Charlier oscillator, the compact $SU(2)$/Krawtchouk spin, and the constant-coefficient tight-binding/Chebyshev chain, with a Hermite central-limit scaling of Charlier as a continuous-spectrum check of this Christoffel jump machinery. Finite seed families are organized by a matrix-valued parent measure whose scalar compressions recover the individual shifted problems. The fixed-inner-product construction carries over to operator Krylov complexity after the replacement \(H\mapsto\mathcal L\) and \(\ket{K_0}\mapsto O\); polynomial seeds then become nested-commutator descendants \(Q(\mathcal L)O\). The result is an exact relative calculus in which a solved cyclic problem generates a family of polynomially related initial-state dynamics without repeating Lanczos in the original Hilbert space.

</details>


### [374] [Cosmological Correlators in KLF and the Double-Exchange](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05327)
*Nathan Belrhali,Arthur Poisson,Sébastien Renaux-Petel*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出了利用Kontorovich-Lebedev-Fourier（KLF）空间形式得到树级宇宙学关联函数（tree-level cosmological correlators）级数展开的方法，通过将嵌套时间积分转化为频率积分，并利用Lauricella函数分析传播子和顶点函数的解析性质，实现了无需微分方程的直接计算。以双交换图（double-exchange diagram）为例展示了该过程，最终结果以超几何函数（hypergeometric functions）的双重级数表示。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 树级宇宙学关联函数的计算通常涉及复杂的嵌套时间积分（in-in nested time integrals），现有方法往往依赖微分方程，计算过程繁琐且不直观。本文旨在提出一种更直接、系统化的计算框架，以简化推导过程并清晰地分离不同的物理贡献。

Method: 利用KLF空间形式将原有的in-in嵌套时间积分转化为对有理传播子（rational propagators）和顶点函数（vertex functions）的频率积分；通过Lauricella函数的积分表示和级数表示推导这些关键对象的解析性质，包括奇点位置、留数（residues）和大频率渐近行为（large-frequency asymptotic behaviour）。

Result: 获得了任意场数目顶点的奇点位置、留数和大频率渐近行为；通过对双交换图的完整计算，展示了该程序的有效性；最终关联函数表达式简化为至多由超几何函数构成的双重级数（double series over hypergeometric functions），显著简化了解析形式。

Conclusion: 本文提出的KLF空间方法能够系统性地计算树级宇宙学关联函数，无需依赖微分方程，计算过程中自然区分背景贡献（background contribution）和宇宙学对撞机信号（cosmological collider signal）贡献，为未来更复杂图的计算提供了通用框架。

Abstract: In this work, we present the procedure to find series representations of tree-level cosmological correlators using the Kontorovich-Lebedev-Fourier (KLF) space formalism. This framework allows us to trade the in-in nested time integrals for frequency integrals over rational propagators and vertex functions, which encode interactions among quantum fields on a de Sitter background. Because these functions are the key objects to understand in order to perform a diagrammatic computation, we derive their relevant analytic properties by using both their integral representation and series representation in terms of Lauricella functions. For a vertex involving any number of fields, we obtain the location of singularities, the corresponding residues and the large-frequency asymptotic behaviour. Gathering these properties at each frequency integration allows us to compute a tree-level correlator directly, without relying on the differential equations it satisfies. To illustrate this procedure, we provide a complete treatment of the double-exchange diagram. The computation naturally distinguishes the different physical contributions, whether to the background or to the cosmological collider signal. The newly derived result is expressed at most in terms of a double series over hypergeometric functions, which simplifies the analytical expression of the correlator.

Result: 发现 QCD 和 QED 等理论在复维度平面上存在分支割线（branch cuts），且低能 CFT 中许多算子的 OPE 和标度维度会随维度 $d$ 发生跳跃（jump）。

Abstract: We revisit the old problem of analytically continuing QFTs to fractional dimension $d\in\mathbb C$. ### [376] [Charge-Sector Construction of the Type-IIB Axion--Dilaton Wormhole Partition Function](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05385)

Method: 在给定的轴子电荷（即形式场通量）扇区中，通过长距离鞍点计算得到带有系数矩阵\(C^{ij}_ν\)的双端算符项；利用约化数据\(b\)将矩阵转化为标量系数\(W_ν[b]\)，进而将虫洞配分函数表示为\(Z_{\rm wh}(θ;b)=\sum_νW_ν[b]\e^{iνθ}\)。

Conclusion: 虫洞配分函数对θ的依赖关系是电荷扇区标量系数的傅里叶变换，该系数满足一系列严格的数学与对称性约束。

Abstract: I construct the Type-IIB axion--dilaton wormhole partition function from charge-sector data. In a chosen axion charge, equivalently form-field flux sector, the long-distance saddle calculation supplies a two-end operator term with coefficient matrix \(C^{ij}_ν\). The labels \(i,j\) label end-insertion operators; the labels \(A,B\) label parent universes. Reduction data \(b\) convert this matrix into scalar coefficients \(W_ν[b]\). The wormhole partition function in the theta variable is \(Z_{\rm wh}(θ;b)=\sum_νW_ν[b]\e^{iνθ}\). I analyze properties and constraints this coefficients satisfy: discrete-symmetry covariance, phase, absolute bounds, moment positivity, Cauchy--Schwarz inequalities for the unreduced coefficient matrix, complex-\(θ\) domains, charge-lattice tails, and the dilute Bessel/Skellam limit. The \(θ\)-dependence of the wormhole partition function is the Fourier transform of the charge-sector scalar coefficients.

### [377] [Liénard--Wiechert fields in AdS and flat-space antipodal matching from geodesic-centered Coulombic data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05395)
*Sarthak Duary*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过几何方法推导了平直时空和全局AdS时空中的李纳-维谢尔场（Liénard–Wiechert fields），重点揭示了反极点匹配（antipodal matching）的几何起源，并给出了从AdS到平直时空极限的统一图像。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 作者旨在从几何角度阐明反极点匹配条件的起源，并将平直时空中匀速运动电荷的李纳-维谢尔场构造推广到全局AdS时空，从而建立AdS与平直时空之间库仑场、反极点匹配和极限对应关系的统一理解。

Method: 采用以源粒子类时测地线（timelike geodesic）为中心的坐标系，使电荷静止从而直接得到库仑场（Coulomb field），再通过变换到非中心参考系导出平直时空的角依赖关系；在AdS中，利用测地线适配坐标和嵌入空间不变量（embedding-space invariants）重建一般全局坐标下的场，并借助镜像电荷（image-charge）解释库仑种子场。

Result: 在平直时空中，零无穷远（null infinity）处领头数据的非平凡角依赖源于坐标系的重新选取，反极点匹配条件自然透明；在全局AdS中，得到了封闭形式的AdS库仑型李纳-维谢尔场，包括规范不变分量$F_{ρτ}$，并证明体场满足精确的反极点协变性，其零边界极限恢复平直时空标准反极点匹配关系。

Conclusion: 反极点匹配是几何坐标变换的自然结果，而非附加条件；AdS中的库仑种子场可通过镜像电荷解释，从而将库仑场、反极点匹配与AdS到平直时空极限统一在一个框架中。

Abstract: We give a geometric derivation of Li'enard--Wiechert fields in flat space and in global AdS, emphasizing the origin of antipodal matching. In flat space, the field of a uniformly moving charge is obtained by using coordinates centered on the source timelike geodesic, where the charge is at rest and the solution is the ordinary Coulomb field. The nontrivial angular dependence of the leading data at null infinity arises only after rewriting this static solution in a non-centered frame, making the antipodal matching condition transparent. We extend the same construction to global AdS, where uniform motion is replaced by motion along a timelike geodesic. Starting from the static Maxwell solution at the AdS center, we use geodesic-adapted coordinates and embedding-space invariants to reconstruct the field in arbitrary global coordinates. This yields a closed-form AdS analogue of the Coulombic Li'enard--Wiechert field, including the gauge-invariant component $F_{ρτ}$. We show that the bulk field satisfies exact antipodal covariance, and that its null-fringe limit reproduces the standard flat-space antipodal matching relation between the Coulombic data at $\mathscr I^+*-$ and $\mathscr I^-*+$. We also describe an image-charge interpretation of the Coulomb seed, giving a unified picture of Coulombic fields, antipodal matching, and the AdS-to-flat-space limit.

</details>
